# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A Landscape of Cosmological Decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07663)
*S. Shajidul Haque,Bret Underwood*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文为早期宇宙原初扰动从量子到经典转变过程提出了一个统一的理论框架，揭示了混合态几何景观，并通过引力非线性性约束排除了退相干热态，限制了振幅对角退相干模型的暴胀时期长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前观测仅约束原初扰动为绝热、近似高斯且近乎尺度不变，但满足这些约束的混合态仍存在未被约束的自由度（状态纯度与动量方差）。作者旨在系统刻画这些自由度所对应的混合态几何景观，并建立退相干模型与其各自指针基之间的映射关系。

Method: 通过状态纯度（purity）和动量方差（momentum variance）参数化混合态未受约束的自由度，构建统一的几何景观框架。利用Glauber-Sudarshan P-函数的正则正定性条件界定环境对系统的作用方向，并分析退相干模型在辐射主导时期对引力势衰减模的动态影响。

Result: ①环境必须主动向系统注入动量（而非抑制动量）才能越过正则正定Glauber-Sudarshan P-函数阈值；②增强的动量方差在辐射时期动态源起引力势的衰减模（decaying mode）；③虽然衰减模衰减足够快以维持宇宙微波背景的时间相干性，但其初始振幅对退相干模型施加了严格的引力非线性性约束；④该约束排除了退相干热态，并将振幅对角退相干模型限制在少于70 e-fold的暴胀时期。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个评估早期宇宙量子-经典转变（quantum-to-classical transition）的统一框架，利用引力非线性性界限对现有退相干模型提供了决定性约束，为理解宇宙原初扰动的统计性质与退相干机制之间的关系奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Current observations constrain primordial perturbations to be adiabatic, approximately Gaussian, and nearly-scale invariant. However, a generic mixed state satisfying these constraints has additional unconstrained degrees of freedom, which can be parameterized by the purity of the state and its momentum variance. This allowable parameter space reveals a unified geometric landscape of mixed states, allowing us to map and relate distinct models of decoherence and their respective pointer bases. Crossing the threshold of a regular, positive-definite Glauber-Sudarshan $P$-function requires the environment to actively inject momentum into the system, rather than suppress it. This enhanced momentum variance dynamically sources the decaying mode of the gravitational potential in the radiation era. While the decaying mode vanishes fast enough to preserve the temporal coherence of the Cosmic Microwave Background, its initial amplitude places severe theoretical constraints on decoherence models to avoid gravitational non-linearities. These non-linearity bounds definitively rule out decohered thermal states, while long-wavelength divergences restrict amplitude-diagonal decoherence models to fewer than 70 $e$-folds of inflation. Altogether, we present a unifying framework for evaluating the quantum-to-classical transition of the early universe.

</details>


### [2] [Spacetime Bartnik Mass Positivity and Temporal Monotonicity for Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07781)
*Lars Andersson,Marcus Khuri,Marc Mars,Walter Simon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文定义了一种巴特尼克型（Bartnik type）的准局域质量（quasilocal mass），并针对两类黑洞相关区域证明了其正性（positivity）和时间单调性（temporal monotonicity）。具体而言，该准局域质量在两类特定时空超曲面（spacelike hypersurface）上严格为正，并在相关演化场景中随时间单调非减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为黑洞相关的准局域质量概念建立同时满足正性和时间单调性的严格数学框架，以弥补现有巴特尼克型准局域质量在这两方面性质的缺失。

Method: 定义一种巴特尼克型（Bartnik type）的准局域质量，并通过数学证明对其在两类黑洞相关区域上的正性和时间单调性进行严格论证。第一类区域为具有表观视界（apparent horizon）边界的紧致类空超曲面；第二类区域为具有渐近平直末端（asymptotically flat ends）且在任何允许延拓（admissible extension）中都包含表观视界的非紧致类空超曲面。

Result: 证明了该准局域质量在第一类和第二类类空超曲面上严格为正（strictly positive）；同时证明在该两类设置相关的演化场景中，该准局域质量随时间单调非减（monotonically nondecreasing）。

Conclusion: 所定义的巴特尼克型准局域质量在黑洞相关区域上同时具有正性和时间单调性，为经典广义相对论中准局域质量的若干核心期望性质提供了严格证明。

Abstract: We define a quasilocal mass of Bartnik type, and establish its positivity and temporal monotonicity properties for two classes of domains associated with black holes. More precisely, we first show that the quasilocal mass is strictly positive for spacelike hypersurfaces that are: compact with apparent horizon boundary or noncompact with asymptotically flat ends and containing an apparent horizon in any admissible extension. Secondly, we show that the quasilocal mass is monotonically nondecreasing in time within evolutionary scenarios related to the two aforementioned settings.

</details>


### [3] [Does Eternal Inflation Violate the Smeared Null Energy Condition?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08003)
*Dong-Hui Yu,Yong Cai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了永恒暴胀（eternal inflation）中的随机向上涨落是否会违反涂抹零能条件（SNEC）。通过福克-普朗克方程和单轨迹分析，证明在慢滚近似（slow-roll approximation）的半经典框架内，涨落并不会导致SNEC被违反，因为引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）会在SNEC边界被触及之前就破坏背景时空的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涂抹零能条件（SNEC）对沿零测地线（null geodesics）累积的负能量施加了半局域性约束。永恒暴胀中稀有的随机向上涨落会局域地提高哈勃参数（Hubble parameter），这似乎与SNEC存在矛盾。因此需要检验这种量子诱导的自再生过程是否真的会违反SNEC。

Method: 采用正则单场暴胀模型，利用福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）分析哈勃参数系综漂移（ensemble drift）的标度行为。同时进行了互补的单轨迹分析（single-trajectory analysis），考察两个时间尺度——SNEC时间尺度（N_SNEC）与背景辐射时间尺度（N_BR）之间的层级关系。

Result: 哈勃参数的系综漂移受到慢滚参数（slow-roll parameters）和半经典压低（semiclassical suppression）的参数化约束。单轨迹分析显示存在强烈的时间尺度层级：N_SNEC >> N_BR，表明即使在稀有的随机向上涨落中，引力反作用会在SNEC边界被数学上接近之前就已经使背景时空假设失效。

Conclusion: 在标准随机扩散（stochastic diffusion）驱动永恒暴胀的过程中，在半经典慢滚区域内不会固有地导致SNEC的违反。

Abstract: The smeared null energy condition (SNEC) imposes a semilocal bound on the negative energy accumulated along null geodesics. In eternal inflation, rare stochastic upward fluctuations of the inflaton locally increase the Hubble parameter, creating an apparent tension with the SNEC. Focusing on a canonical single-field model, we investigate whether this quantum-induced self-reproduction violates the SNEC. Using the Fokker-Planck equation, we demonstrate that the ensemble drift of the Hubble parameter is parametrically bounded by slow-roll parameters and semiclassical suppression. Furthermore, a complementary single-trajectory analysis reveals a strong timescale hierarchy, $N_{\rm SNEC} \gg N_{\rm BR}$. This indicates that even for rare upward stochastic excursions, gravitational backreaction invalidates the background spacetime assumption long before the SNEC bound can be mathematically approached. We conclude that while standard stochastic diffusion drives eternal inflation, it does not inherently lead to SNEC violations within the semiclassical slow-roll regime.

</details>


### [4] [Degenerate Geometries as Matter-Free Physical Configurations in General Relativity: Three Examples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08022)
*Juri Dimaschko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分支坐标变换构造了三种具有虫洞拓扑（wormhole topology）的退化时空构型（Rindler虫洞、Klinkhamer虫洞和Schwarzschild-Klinkhamer虫洞），并在爱因斯坦-帕拉蒂尼-嘉当（Einstein-Palatini-Cartan）框架下证明这些退化构型是无物质的，且无法通过非退化时空的极限过渡获得，表明退化几何构成广义相对论（general relativity）构型空间的一个独立扇区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的薄壳模型（thin shell model）中，非退化虫洞需要奇异物质（exotic matter）来维持。本研究旨在探索退化时空构型是否可以在没有物质场的情况下存在，并考察其与非退化虫洞之间的本质区别。

Method: 通过对Rindler、Minkowski和Schwarzschild真空度规进行分支坐标变换（branching coordinate transformations），构造三种退化虫洞时空构型。随后在爱因斯坦-帕拉蒂尼-嘉当（Einstein-Palatini-Cartan）形式框架下，检验这些构型是否含有物质场。

Result: 三种退化虫洞构型均被证明是无物质（matter-free）的，因此与需要奇异物质的非退化虫洞存在根本差异。这些构型表现出从纯拓扑结构到真实引力效应的不同物理表现。此外，在所有三个例子中，均不存在从非退化时空到无物质退化构型的极限过渡。

Conclusion: 退化几何构型构成广义相对论（general relativity）构型空间中的一个独立扇区（independent sector），不能通过非退化时空的极限过程获得。这一发现挑战了传统虫洞模型对奇异物质的依赖，并为理解时空拓扑与物质之间的关系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We examine three degenerate spacetime configurations with wormhole topology, obtained via branching coordinate transformations of the Rindler, Minkowski, and Schwarzschild vacuum metrics.These configurations are, respectively, a Rindler wormhole with a planar throat, and the Klinkhamer and Schwarzschild Klinkhamer wormholes with spherical throats. Within the framework of the Einstein Palatini Cartan formulation, we demonstrate that these degenerate configurations are matter free. In this regard, they differ fundamentally from their nondegenerate wormhole counterparts in the thin shell model, which require exotic matter. Nevertheless, the degenerate configurations considered here exhibit distinct physical manifestations, ranging from purely topological structures to genuine gravitational effects. Furthermore, in all three examples, we demonstrate the absence of a limiting transition from the non-degenerate spacetime to the matter free degenerate configuration. This suggests that degenerate geometries constitute an independent sector of the configuration space of general relativity.

</details>


### [5] [Warped Product Einstein Manifolds in Four Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08047)
*Jack C. M. Hughes,Joudy F. Jamal Beek,Fedor V. Kusmartsev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在四维（伪）黎曼流形上，通过曲率张量的手征6×6矩阵表示与积流形（warped product）的另一种矩阵表示之间的相似变换，系统分类了1+3、2+2和3+1积流形的爱因斯坦极限（Einstein limit），并给出了相应的Petrov分类（Petrov classification）：3+1为一般型I（type-I），2+2为型D（type-D），1+3受限于型O（type-O）。在闭黎曼情形下，半共形平坦（half-conformally flat）极限中的爱因斯坦积流形必为平坦流形（flat manifold）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 曲率张量在四维流形上存在手征6×6矩阵表示，其块状结构可判断流形是否为爱因斯坦流形（Einstein manifold）。当流形为积流形（warped product）时，2-形式可依据基空间与纤维空间的外代数分解，导出另一种矩阵表示。两种表示间存在相似变换，但尚未被系统构造与应用。

Method: 对于1+3、2+2和3+1三种积流形，分别构造曲率张量的两种矩阵表示及其之间的相似变换（similarity transformation）。利用该代数框架分析爱因斯坦极限条件，并进一步进行Petrov分类（Petrov classification）。

Result: 3+1积流形在爱因斯坦极限下一般为Petrov型I（type-I），2+2为型D（type-D），1+3受限于型O（type-O）。在闭黎曼（closed Riemannian）情形下，半共形平坦（half-conformally flat）极限中的爱因斯坦积流形必为平坦流形（flat manifold）。

Conclusion: 上述代数方法为爱因斯坦积流形的分类与Petrov分类提供了系统且简便的工具，并揭示了闭黎曼情形下的拓扑限制（topological restrictions）。

Abstract: On four-dimensional (pseudo-)Riemannian manifolds $\mathcal{M}$ the curvature tensor (viewed as an endomorphism on 2-forms) admits a chiral $6 \times 6$ matrix representation which decomposes into four $3 \times 3$ blocks. $\mathcal{M}$ is Einstein if and only if the off-diagonal blocks vanish. If the manifold is a warped product $\mathcal{M} = F \times_f B$, then there exists an alternative matrix representation relative to the decomposition of the 2-forms into spaces induced by the exterior algebra on both the base and the fiber. These two representations are not independent and a similarity transformation can be found between them. We construct these matrices and associated transformations for $1+3$, $2+2$ and $3+1$ warped products, giving classifications for the Einstein limits from this algebraic perspective. Using this, one can easily Petrov classify the Einstein warped products for each case considered: $3+1$ are generically type-\RNum{1}, $2+2$ are type-D while $1+3$ are constrained to be type-O. In the closed Riemannian case, there are a number of topological restrictions on these manifolds that we discuss: in the half-conformally flat limit, each of these Einstein warped products must be flat.

</details>


### [6] [Higher-dimensional quantum-corrected Oppenheimer-Snyder model with a cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08182)
*Shudi Jiang,Jianhui Lin,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将高维量子奥本海默-斯奈德模型（Oppenheimer-Snyder model）推广至包含宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的情形。在反德西特（AdS）情形下，在扩展相空间形式（extend phase space formalism）中讨论了其热力学性质，并与经典黑洞进行了比较。对于AdS时空中量子修正的小黑洞，温度不再发散而是趋于零。此外，热容表现出特征行为，表明量子修正诱导了额外的相变，凸显了量子效应对黑洞热力学的深刻影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将高维量子奥本海默-斯奈德模型推广到包含宇宙学常数的情形，以填补现有模型在处理宇宙学常数影响方面的空白，并探索量子修正对黑洞热力学行为的深层影响。

Method: 采用扩展相空间形式（extend phase space formalism）对推广后的量子奥本海默-斯奈德模型进行热力学分析；通过与经典黑洞的对比，揭示量子修正效应。

Result: 在AdS时空中，量子修正后的小黑洞温度不再发散，而是趋于零；热容表现出特征行为，指示存在由量子修正诱导的额外相变。

Conclusion: 量子效应对黑洞热力学具有深刻影响，特别是在量子修正下AdS小黑洞的热力学行为与经典黑洞存在显著差异，包括温度不发散以及出现额外的相变。

Abstract: We extended the higher-dimensional quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder model to the case with a cosmological constant. For AdS case, we discuss its thermodynamic properties in extend phase space formalism and make comparison with classical black holes. For quantum-corrected small black holes in AdS spacetime, the temperature no longer diverges but tends to zero. Additionally, the heat capacity exhibits characteristic behavior indicative of an extra phase transition induced by quantum corrections, highlighting the profound impact of quantum effects on black hole thermodynamics.

</details>


### [7] [Non conservative conformal Killing gravity: coupling the dark sector with curvature and matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08213)
*Salvatore Capozziello,Carlo Alberto Mantica,Luca Guido Molinari*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有非守恒能量-动量张量的Harada引力，该理论以Rastall引力为特例，并包含Unimodular引力。场方程通过共形Killing张量和与曲率及能量-动量迹相关的度规项引入暗区（dark sector）耦合。在Friedmann-Robertson-Walker（FRW）背景及宇宙微波背景（CMB）限制下，暗区仅与能量-动量张量的迹耦合，推导出连续方程并给出物质密度随尺度因子的修正演化指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展Rastall引力及Harada引力框架，为非守恒能量-动量张量理论提供统一的场方程形式，同时将暗区（dark sector）自然地纳入引力理论，解释其与物质内容的耦合机制。

Method: 将Harada引力的场方程改写为爱因斯坦方程形式，其中源项补充了无散度的共形Killing张量（conformal Killing tensor）以及一个与度规成正比、依赖于标量曲率（scalar curvature）和能量-动量张量迹（trace）的张量。在FRW度规背景下引入CMB观测约束，推导暗区张量的显式形式及修正的Friedmann方程与连续方程。

Result: CMB观测限制了参数，使得暗区仅通过与能量-动量张量的迹（trace）耦合。暗区张量的显式形式得以确定，修正后的连续方程显示：尘埃物质（dust matter）与暗流体（dark fluid）的总能量-动量张量守恒，尘埃能量密度随尺度因子（scale function）以指数 -3/(1+τ) 演化，其中 τ 为与暗流体的耦合参数。

Conclusion: Harada引力框架下的暗区耦合机制可为宇宙暗成分提供自然候选，但CMB观测将耦合限制为仅与能量-动量张量的迹相关。该理论统一了Rastall引力和Unimodular引力，并给出了可检验的宇宙学演化修正。

Abstract: The so called Harada gravity with non conserved energy-momentum tensor is here taken into account. It includes Rastall gravity as a special case. The field equations are written as Einstein equations where the source is supplemented by a divergence-free conformal Killing tensor and a tensor proportional to the metric, linear in the scalar curvature and the trace of the energy-momentum tensor. These terms can be natural candidates for dark sector and give rise to a coupling of the dark sector with the matter content. The field equations are the conformal Killing extension of Rastall gravity, and include Unimodular gravity. In a Friedmann-Robertson-Walker background, the Cosmic Microwave Background restricts parameters so that the dark sector only couples with the trace of the energy-momentum tensor. The explicit form of the tensor for the dark sector is found, and the Friedmann and continuity equations are presented, with a standard cosmological analysis. The sum of energy-momentum tensors of dust matter and of dark fluid is conserved, and the dust energy density evolves with the scale function with exponent -3/(1+tau), modified by the coupling tau with the dark fluid.

</details>


### [8] [Stimulated Emission from Boson Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08220)
*Yu An,Xian-Hui Ge,Yun-Gui Gong,Yun-Long Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，超辐射云（superradiant cloud）中的超轻玻色子（ultralight boson）可以通过受激辐射机制（stimulated emission mechanism）充当引力波（gravitational-wave）的自然放大器，其放大效率取决于玻色子质量，可能将信号增强数个数量级，从而弥合地面干涉仪与脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array）之间的灵敏度缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天体物理源发出的引力波极其微弱，这是当前及下一代探测器面临的主要障碍。尽管带有超辐射云的旋转黑洞被视为超出标准模型（Standard Model）物理的有前景探针，但这些系统主动发射和调制引力辐射的能力尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 将玻色子云与周围随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background）之间的相互作用形式化，建立了支配该放大过程的严格选择定则（selection rule）和阈值条件（threshold condition）。

Result: 分析表明，放大后的信号发射率关键依赖于玻色子质量，可能比自发过程（spontaneous process）增强数个数量级。对于代表性质量范围，这些信号能够弥合地面干涉仪与脉冲星计时阵列之间的灵敏度差距。

Conclusion: 超辐射云可以有效增强先前无法探测的引力波信号，为探索超轻场（ultralight field）及克尔时空（Kerr spacetime）环境提供新的观测前沿。

Abstract: Gravitational-waves from astrophysical sources are characterized by their extreme faintness, which remains a primary obstacle for both current and next generation detectors. While rotating black holes dressed in superradiant clouds of ultralight bosons are recognized as promising probes of physics beyond the Standard Model, their capacity to actively emit and modulate gravitational radiation remains largely unexamined. Here we demonstrate that these gravitational atoms can function as natural amplifiers of gravitational-waves via a stimulated emission mechanism analogous to astrophysical masers. By formalizing the interaction between the bosonic cloud and an ambient stochastic gravitational-wave background, we establish the rigorous selection rules and threshold conditions that govern this amplification. Our analysis reveals that the emission rate depends critically on the boson mass, potentially yielding an enhancement of several orders of magnitude over spontaneous processes. For representative mass ranges, these amplified signals bridge the sensitivity gap between ground-based interferometers and pulsar timing arrays. These findings suggest that superradiant clouds can effectively boost previously undetectable signals, offering a novel observational frontier for exploring ultralight fields and the Kerr spacetime environment.

### [9] [Hawking Emission from Black Holes Evaporating toward Wormholes and the Accuracy of the WKB Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08351)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过直接数值散射方法重新计算了两种趋近虫洞（wormhole）构型的黑洞的霍金辐射（Hawking radiation），发现WKB估计在远离史瓦西极限时误差可达数个数量级，直接数值灰体因子（greybody factor）对准确评估黑洞蒸发率至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对Simpson–Visser黑洞反弹（black-bounce）几何和Casadio–Fabbri–Mazzacurati膜世界（braneworld）几何的霍金辐射分析依赖于WKB灰体因子近似，该近似的误差范围和可靠性尚需定量评估。

Method: 针对光子和无质量狄拉克（Dirac）通道，采用直接数值散射计算替代原有的WKB灰体因子近似，重新计算发射谱（emission spectra）和积分光度（integrated luminosities）。

Result: 定性上，趋近虫洞端点时黑洞冷却、总通量被强烈抑制、剩余辐射日益以费米子为主；定量上，WKB估计在史瓦西极限附近较准确，但远离该极限时误差巨大，接近冷端点时可达数个数量级。在固定参数的Simpson–Visser半衰期估计中，直接灰体因子使WKB寿命系数增大约85倍。

Conclusion: 对于演化向虫洞状端点的黑洞，可靠的蒸发率计算必须采用直接数值灰体因子，而非仅依赖势垒顶部（barrier-top）WKB估计。

Abstract: We revisit Hawking radiation from two black-hole families that can approach macroscopic wormhole configurations: the Simpson--Visser black-bounce geometry and the Casadio--Fabbri--Mazzacurati braneworld geometry. The earlier analysis of these backgrounds relied on WKB greybody factors. Here we replace that approximation by direct numerical scattering for the photon and massless Dirac channels and then recompute the emission spectra and integrated luminosities. The qualitative picture remains the same: as the wormhole endpoint is approached the black holes cool, the total flux is strongly suppressed, and the residual emission becomes increasingly fermion dominated. The quantitative picture, however, changes substantially. Close to the Schwarzschild limit the WKB estimates are reasonably accurate, but far from that limit the error can be large, and near the cold endpoint it can reach orders of magnitude. In particular, the WKB calculation can substantially overestimate the remaining luminosity precisely in the regime where the evaporation rate is most sensitive to the low-frequency tail of the greybody factors. In a fixed-parameter Simpson--Visser half-decay estimate, the direct-greybody luminosities increase the WKB lifetime coefficient by a factor of about 85. These results show that reliable evaporation rates for black holes evolving toward wormhole-like endpoints require direct numerical greybody factors rather than barrier-top WKB estimates alone.

### [10] [Frenet-Serret equations with variable proper acceleration in Minkowski spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08456)
*Ivan Perez-Roman,Michael R. R. Good,Yen Chin Ong,Haret C. Rosu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中类时世界线（timelike worldlines）的Frenet-Serret方程，在曲率（curvature）和挠率（torsion）随固有时（proper time）变化的情况下，将内禀Frenet-Serret参数与四加速度（proper acceleration）、四急动度（four-jerk）和四跃度（four-snap）等运动学量建立联系，并通过解析实例阐明非恒定加速度和挠率如何改变加速相对论运动的几何特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Frenet-Serret框架通常假定曲率和挠率为常数，无法描述非均匀固有加速度（non-uniform proper acceleration）及加速平面之外框架旋转的轨迹。本文旨在将Frenet-Serret形式推广到含时变的曲率和挠率情形，从而更一般地刻画加速相对论运动的几何结构。

Method: 基于Gram-Schmidt正交化程序，从四速度（four-velocity）及其各阶导数构建标架（tetrad），从而将内禀Frenet-Serret参数与四加速度、四急动度、四跃度等运动学量直接关联。随后考虑急动度不变量（jerk invariant）和挠率的简单解析情形，推导出显式的曲率轮廓（curvature profiles）和约化Frenet-Serret方程。

Result: 得到了非恒定曲率和挠率下Frenet-Serret参数与多阶运动学量之间的解析关系；通过具体解析实例展示了曲率轮廓的显式形式，并获得了对应的约化Frenet-Serret方程。

Conclusion: 非恒定加速度和挠率的引入显著改变了加速相对论运动的几何行为；所建立的框架为研究更复杂的非均匀加速相对论轨迹提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study Frenet-Serret equations for timelike worldlines in Minkowski spacetime with proper-time-dependent curvature and torsion. This corresponds to relativistic motion with non-uniform proper acceleration and, when torsion is included, to trajectories whose Frenet-Serret frame rotates beyond the acceleration plane. Using the Gram-Schmidt construction of the tetrad from the four-velocity and its derivatives, we relate the intrinsic Frenet-Serret parameters to kinematic quantities such as proper acceleration, four-jerk, and four-snap. We then consider simple analytic cases for the jerk invariant and torsion, obtaining explicit curvature profiles and reduced Frenet-Serret equations. These examples clarify how non-constant acceleration and torsion modify the geometry of accelerated relativistic motion.

### [11] [Curvature-induced scalarization of charged AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08507)
*Chao-Ming Zhang,Yun Soo Myung,Lina Zhang,De-Cheng Zou,Fu-Wen Shu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了负宇宙常数对爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内理论中高斯-博内标量化的影响，发现标量化的出现受 Breitenlohner-Freedman 界约束而非仅由有效质量为负决定，并给出了不同耦合参数下 scalarized AdS 黑洞的分支结构及相变行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究负宇宙常数（cosmological constant）如何影响爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内理论（Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory）中的高斯-博内标量化（Gauss-Bonnet scalarization），重点关注其与渐近平坦时空情形的差异。

Method: 通过分析 Reissner-Nordström-AdS（RN-AdS）黑洞在标量扰动下的不稳定性，该扰动由高斯-博内项（GB term）贡献的有效质量 $μ^2_{\text{eff}}$ 控制；结合 Breitenlohner-Freedman 界（BF bound）和 Gibbs 自由能进行判定。

Result: 标量化的 onset 不仅取决于 $μ^2_{\text{eff}}<0$，还受 BF 界约束；当 BF 界被违反（$η>2.25$，$Λ=-0.5$）时出现 AdS 超不稳定性（AdS-tachyonic instability）。对于 $0<η<2.25$，GB$^+$ 标量化通过自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）实现；$η<0$ 时，GB$^-$ 标量化给出单一分支。在 $η_{th}\le η<2.25$ 范围内，GB$^+$ 标量化仅存在单分支（$n=0$ 基态分支），而非无限分支。Gibbs 自由能表明从 scalarized AdS 黑洞到 RN-AdS 黑洞的相变为二级相变（second-order phase transition）。

Conclusion: 负宇宙常数通过 BF 界对高斯-博内标量化的 onset 施加额外约束，改变了标量化黑洞的分支结构（仅存在单分支），并导致二级相变行为。

Abstract: We investigate how a negative cosmological constant affects the Gauss-Bonnet (GB) scalarization in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory with a scalar coupling constant $η$ to GB term. We focus on the instability of Reissner-Nordström-AdS (RN-AdS) black holes under a scalar perturbation governed by an effective mass $μ^2_{\text{eff}}$ sourced by the GB term. Unlike the asymptotically flat spacetime case, the onset of scalarization is not merely determined by $μ^2_{\text{eff}} < 0$, but it is constrained by the Breitenlohner-Freedman (BF) bound. In case that the BF bound is violated ($η>2.25$ with $Λ=-0.5$), one may find AdS-tachyoinic instability. We find that for $0<η<2.25$, the GB$^+$ scalarization may be performed through spontaneous scalarization, while for $η<0$ the GB$^-$ scalarization is found to give the single branch of scalarized AdS black holes. For the GB$^+$ scalarization in $η_{th}\leη<2.25$ with $η_{th}$ threshold instability, we obtain the single branch ($n=0$ fundamental branch) of scalarized AdS black holes, contradicting to infinite branches. Finally, it is observed from Gibbs free energy that a phase transition from scalarized AdS black holes to RNAdS black hole occur natually and it is confirmed to be second-order.

### [12] [Shadow of Rotating Black Hole Immersed in Dark Matter Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08616)
*Yong-You Liu,Tian-Yun Ye,Zhen Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）对黑洞阴影的观测，研究了一个浸没在广义双幂律暗物质晕（generalized double power law dark matter halo）中的旋转黑洞的时空结构、光子动力学和阴影性质，并通过Sgr A*的阴影观测约束了暗物质晕的参数空间。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从静态暗物质黑洞解出发，采用纽曼-贾尼斯算法（Newman--Janis algorithm）构造其旋转对应解，得到带有暗物质修正质量函数（dark matter-modified mass function）的类克尔度规（Kerr-like metric）。随后分析视界结构、能层（ergosphere）和不稳定球形光子轨道（unstable spherical photon orbits），并利用Sgr A*的阴影观测数据对暗物质晕参数空间进行约束。

Result: 暗物质晕通常扩大了视界（horizon），向外移动了光子球壳（photon shell），并改变了黑洞阴影；这些效应在快速旋转的黑洞中更加显著。通过Sgr A*的阴影观测进一步约束了暗物质晕参数空间，并识别出晕参数、黑洞自旋和观测者倾角（inclination angle）之间的相关性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，黑洞阴影观测为探测超大质量黑洞附近的暗物质分布提供了一种有前景的探针。

Abstract: The recent black hole shadow observations by the Event Horizon Telescope provide a unique opportunity to probe both the strong gravity regime and the environment surrounding supermassive black holes. Since dark matter halos are expected to exist around galactic-center black holes, they may leave observable signatures on black hole shadows. In this work, we investigate the spacetime structure, photon dynamics, and shadow properties of a rotating black hole immersed in a generalized double power law dark matter halo. Starting from a static dark matter black hole solution, we employ the Newman--Janis algorithm to construct its rotating counterpart and obtain a Kerr-like metric with a dark matter-modified mass function. We analyze the horizon structure, ergosphere, and unstable spherical photon orbits, and find that the dark matter halo generally enlarges the horizon, shifts the photon shell outward, and modifies the black hole shadow. The effects become more pronounced for rapidly rotating black holes. Using the shadow observation of Sgr A*, we further constrain the dark matter halo parameter space and identify correlations among the halo parameters, black hole spin, and observer inclination angle. Our results suggest that black hole shadow observations provide a promising probe of dark matter distributions near supermassive black holes.

### [13] [Hawking Radiation from the Dymnikova Regular Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08631)
*Milena Skvortsova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Dymnikova规则黑洞的霍金辐射，发现其主要效应并非灰体因子（greybody factor）的显著改变，而是霍金温度（Hawking temperature）的急剧下降极大地抑制了总光度（total luminosity），导致黑洞仅渐近趋近于冷的极值残余（cold extremal remnant），因此寿命估计应被视为近极端构型的截止时间而非完全蒸发时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dymnikova正则黑洞模型用平滑的德西特核心取代了中心奇点，且在远处近似于史瓦西黑洞，其黑洞分支终止于冷极值残余。研究该模型下标准模型测试场（test field）与引力子的霍金辐射，有助于理解奇点正则化对黑洞蒸发过程的影响。

Method: 计算标准模型测试场和引力子的灰体因子，将精确数值散射结果与WKB（Wentzel–Kramers–Brillouin）估计进行对比，并利用所得谱估计绝热蒸发历史。

Result: 主要效应并非透射概率的剧烈变化：当几何结构趋近残余时，灰体阈值仅轻微移动。霍金温度的快速下降显著抑制了总光度；光子、轻费米子和引力子通道在末端附近均衰减，引力子贡献始终处于次主导地位。无质量剩余通量（residual massless flux）逐渐以费米子主导，因为光子通道被更有效地抑制。

Conclusion: 黑洞仅渐近趋近冷残余，因此论文中的寿命估计应被解释为到达近极端构型的截止时间（cutoff time），而非完整的蒸发时间。

Abstract: We study Hawking radiation of the Dymnikova regular black hole. This model replaces the central singularity by a smooth de Sitter core while remaining Schwarzschild-like far from the hole, and its black-hole branch ends in a cold extremal remnant. We compute the greybody factors of the Standard Model test fields and gravitons, compare the precise numerical scattering results with WKB estimates, and use the resulting spectra to estimate an adiabatic evaporation history. The main effect is not a dramatic change in the transmission probabilities: the greybody thresholds move only slightly as the geometry approaches the remnant. Instead, the rapid decrease of the Hawking temperature strongly suppresses the total luminosity. The photon, light-fermion and graviton channels all fade near the endpoint, with the gravitational contribution remaining subdominant. The residual massless flux becomes increasingly fermion dominated because the photon channel is suppressed more efficiently. The black hole approaches the cold remnant only asymptotically, so the quoted lifetime estimates should be interpreted as cutoff times to near-extremal configurations rather than as complete evaporation times.

Method: 利用自由数据形式化方法（free data formalism）进行前向积分，并结合一种基于有效均匀化（effective uniformization）的新规范条件（gauge condition）。

Result: 成功构造了在类空无穷远处具有有限衰减的爱因斯坦真空约束方程的一般解，包括最小衰减和边界衰减情形。

Conclusion: 本文所发展的技术将为后续论文中构造导致陷获面（trapped surfaces）形成的一般短脉冲柯西数据类（short-pulse Cauchy data）提供基础，从而扩展 Li 和 Yu 的经典结果。

Abstract: We make use of the free data formalism developed in \cite{CK25} to construct solutions of the Einstein vacuum constraint equations by integrating in the forward direction. ### [15] [Non-Perturbative Bounds on Cosmological Backreaction, the Non-Linear Scale, and Gauge-Invariant Mutual Information from the Matter Power Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08764)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文应用介观粗粒化（mesoscopic coarse-graining）框架处理宇宙学微扰论（Cosmological Perturbation Theory）与反作用（backreaction）争论中的三个问题：基于吉布斯-玻戈留波夫不等式（Gibbs–Bogoliubov inequality）给出运动学反作用的非微扰下界；给出累积量展开的收敛半径与非线性尺度的关系，为标准微扰论的失效提供KAM定理式解释；导出高斯物质场下细胞间互信息的精确表达式，并给出可数据计算的FRW自由能反作用修正度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准宇宙学微扰论在非线性尺度（k>k_NL）失效，反作用（backreaction）效应在非线性阶段的定量刻画尚不清晰，需要建立非微扰的粗粒化分析框架来统一处理这三个问题。

Method: 采用Osano等人的介观粗粒化（mesoscopic coarse-graining）框架，运用吉布斯-玻戈留波夫不等式（Gibbs–Bogoliubov inequality）推导下界；通过累积量展开的收敛半径分析给出标准微扰论失效的KAM定理（KAM theorem）式解释；利用高斯场假设导出互信息（mutual information）的精确解析形式。

Result: (i) Buchert方程中的运动学反作用Q_D存在非微扰下界，在线性微扰理论值之上不可被进一步压制；(ii) 介观累积量展开的收敛半径为O(k_NL^{-1})，即物质功率谱的非线性尺度；(iii) 高斯物质场下细胞间互信息精确为I(i,j)=-(1/2)ln(1-r_ij^2)，在线性阶规范不变，ΛCDM模型下ℓ=50 Mpc h^{-1}时最邻近互信息约0.10。

Conclusion: 反作用下界成立依赖于所陈述的猜想；规范不变性的证明仅在线性阶成立；KAM定理的识别是精确的；总互信息可作为FRW自由能反作用修正的、可由数据直接计算的度量。

Abstract: We apply the mesoscopic coarse-graining framework of~\cite{OsanoMeso,OsanoExtensivity,OsanoPerturbation} to three problems in Cosmological Perturbation Theory and the backreaction debate. \textbf{(i)}~A non-perturbative lower bound on the kinematic backreaction $\QD$ in the Buchert equations, derived from the Gibbs--Bogoliubov inequality: $\QD$ cannot be suppressed below its linear-perturbation-theoryvalue, regardless of the degree of non-linearity, provided the system satisfies stability and temperedness. \textbf{(ii)}~The radius of convergence of the mesoscopic cumulant expansion equals $O(\kNL^{-1})$, the non-linear scale of the matter power spectrum, providing a KAM-theorem explanation for why standard perturbation theory fails at $k>\kNL$. \textbf{(iii)}~For a Gaussian matter field, the inter-cell mutual information is exactly $I(i,j)=-\tfrac{1}{2}\ln(1-r_{ij}^2)$, gauge-invariant at linear order and computable directly from the observed $P(k)$; for $Λ$CDM at $\ell=50\,\mathrm{Mpc}\,h^{-1}$, $I_{\rm NN}\approx 0.10$.The total mutual information gives a data-computable measure of the backreaction correction to the FRW free energy. The gauge proof holds at linear order; the KAM identification is exact; the backreaction bound rests on a stated conjecture.

</details>


### [16] [Line-of-sight acceleration in compact binaries with higher harmonics and eccentricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08838)
*Soumen Roy,Justin Janquart*

TL;DR: 本文重新推导了视线加速度（line-of-sight acceleration）效应，将其纳入包含进动和高阶模的准圆形引力波波形模型以及偏心波形模型中，并应用于LIGO/Virgo第三次观测运行的部分GWTC事件。分析未发现显著的视线加速度证据，并指出高阶谐波间不一致的处理会导致有偏结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波直接探测为研究致密双星并合的天体物理起源提供了独特机会。这些系统的形成通道（formation channels）仍然存在高度争议，其中部分可能起源于动力学环境或活动星系核。在这种环境中形成的双星会因周围环境的视线加速度而在引力波信号中留下特征印记。

Method: 本文重新推导了视线加速度效应，并将其实现于包含进动（precession）和高阶模（higher-order modes）的准圆形波形模型（quasi-circular waveform models）中。同时将修正一致地应用于偏心波形模型（eccentric waveform models）的所有贡献谐波。

Result: 基于该模型分析了LIGO/Virgo第三次观测运行中的部分感兴趣GWTC事件，未发现显著的视线加速度证据。研究同时表明，若在高阶谐波间不一致地处理视线加速度，会导致有偏的结论。

Conclusion: 该模型为在现有及未来的引力波观测中揭示视线加速度提供了稳健框架，能够更精确地探测致密双星形成过程中的环境特征（environmental signatures）。

Abstract: Direct detections of gravitational waves provide a unique opportunity to probe the astrophysical origin of compact binary mergers. The formation channels of these systems remain highly debated, and a fraction may originate in dynamical environments or active galactic nuclei. Binaries formed in such environments are expected to experience line-of-sight acceleration from their surroundings, which can imprint characteristic signatures on the observed gravitational-wave signal. Here, we re-derive the line-of-sight acceleration effects and implement them in state-of-the-art quasi-circular waveform models with precession and higher-order modes. We also implement the corrections in eccentric waveform models, applying them consistently to all contributing harmonics. Using this model, we investigate the impact of these effects on the inference of line-of-sight acceleration and analyze a few interesting GWTC events observed during the third observing run of LIGO and Virgo. We find no substantial evidence for line-of-sight acceleration in these events. We also show that an inconsistent treatment of line-of-sight acceleration between higher harmonics can lead to biased conclusions. Our model provides a robust framework for uncovering line-of-sight acceleration in current and future gravitational-wave observations, enabling more accurate probes of environmental signatures in compact-binary formation.

</details>


### [17] [Electromagnetism from two matter spaces: mutual helicity and the nondegenerate completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08917)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，一般麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field）可通过引入两个独立的物质空间流（matter-space flow）来表征，每个流各自携带一个退化的螺旋性扇区（helicity sector），而完整的非退化电磁场（nondegenerate electromagnetic field）则通过两个扇区的耦合重建，其总螺旋性（total helicity）包含自螺旋性与互螺旋性（mutual helicity）两项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单流（one-flow）物质空间框架仅能描述退化的螺旋性扇区，其场强满足 F∧F=0，无法涵盖一般（非退化）电磁场。本文旨在通过最小扩展——引入第二个独立流——来重建完整、非退化的麦克斯韦理论。

Method: 将电磁场强度 F 分解为两个扇区场 G^{(1)} 和 G^{(2)}，每个扇区场分别是独立物质空间流上的二形式（two-form）的拉回（pull-back）。每个扇区满足退化条件 G^{(I)}∧G^{(I)}=0，而完整场满足 F∧F = 2 G^{(1)}∧G^{(2)}。该方法将单流理论缺失的不变量恢复为两个流之间的互螺旋量（inter-flow quantity）。

Result: 总螺旋性分解为两个自螺旋性（self-helicity）与一个互螺旋性（mutual helicity）之和，其外微分为 F∧F。互螺旋性为零的构型对应于退化扇区，而非退化麦克斯韦场必然携带非平凡的互螺旋性。基于总场的变分原理可恢复有源麦克斯韦方程，前提是两个扇区核（kernel）的交集平凡。

Conclusion: 一般电磁学可被重建为两个独立退化物质空间扇区的最小耦合完备化（minimal coupled completion）。该框架为理解电磁场的螺旋性结构提供了一个新的几何视角。

Abstract: We show that generic Maxwell fields can be represented within the matter-space framework by introducing two independent matter-space flows. In the one-flow formulation the electromagnetic field strength is the pull-back of a two-form on a three-dimensional matter space and therefore satisfies $F\wedge F=0$, so that a single flow captures only a degenerate, helicity-carrying sector. The minimal completion is obtained by writing $$F=G^{(1)}+G^{(2)},$$ where each sector field $G^{(I)}$ is the pull-back of a matter-space two-form from an independent flow. Each sector is individually degenerate, $G^{(I)}\wedge G^{(I)}=0$, while the full field satisfies $F\wedge F=2G^{(1)}\wedge G^{(2)}$; the invariant excluded by the one-flow theory is thus recovered as an inter-flow quantity. We interpret this structure in terms of mutual helicity: the total helicity decomposes into two self-helicity contributions and a mutual term whose exterior derivative is $F\wedge F$. Hence a configuration with vanishing mutual helicity lies in the degenerate sector, whereas a nondegenerate Maxwell field necessarily carries a nontrivial mutual helicity. A variational principle for the total field recovers the sourced Maxwell equation, the two matter-space variations combining into the full equation whenever the sector kernels intersect trivially. Generic electromagnetism is thereby reconstructed as the minimal coupled completion of two individually degenerate matter-space sectors.

</details>


### [18] [Static axisymmetric Einstein spaces with a cosmological constant and the limitation of canonical Weyl coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09177)
*Sheref Nasereldin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明在四维静态轴对称真空度规中，标准 Weyl 形式（$W=ρ$）仅在宇宙学常数 $Λ=0$ 时局部允许；当 $Λ\neq 0$ 时，面积函数不再是调和函数，因此标准 Weyl 坐标无法推广到非零宇宙学常数的爱因斯坦空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 Weyl 形式通过将 Killing 轨道面积函数（area function）视为二维轨道空间上的调和坐标（harmonic coordinate）来构造，该构造在 Ricci 平坦真空（Ricci-flat vacuum）中有效，但在具有非零宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的爱因斯坦空间（Einstein spaces）中不再成立。本文旨在研究这一限制的精确数学来源。

Method: 考虑广义正交可迁静态轴对称线元（generalized orthogonally transitive static axisymmetric line element），推导约化后的 Einstein-Λ 场方程。通过检验标准 Weyl 选择 $W=ρ$ 的局部可容许性条件，分析宇宙学常数对该条件的影响。

Result: 标准 Weyl 坐标选择 $W=ρ$ 当且仅当 $Λ=0$ 时在局部可容许。Kottler 度规（Kottler metric）为面积函数所得方程提供了最简单的显式例子。因此，“Weyl 度规不允许 $Λ\neq 0$”这一论断仅当度规被假定采用标准 Weyl 坐标时才精确成立。

Conclusion: 问题的根源不在于静态性或轴对称性（staticity or axisymmetry），而在于当宇宙学常数非零时，面积函数不再是调和函数（harmonic function）。该结果澄清了 Weyl 形式在非零宇宙学常数情形下的适用边界。

Abstract: The canonical Weyl form for four-dimensional static axisymmetric vacuum metrics is obtained by identifying the area function of the two Killing orbits with a harmonic coordinate on the twodimensional orbit space. This construction is valid in Ricci-flat vacuum, but it is no longer available in Einstein spaces with nonzero cosmological constant. In this paper, we consider the generalized orthogonally transitive static axisymmetric line element and derive the reduced Einstein- $Λ$ field equations. We show that the canonical Weyl choice $W=ρ$ is locally admissible if and only if $Λ=0$. The Kottler metric gives the simplest explicit example of the resulting equation for the area function. Thus, the statement that "Weyl metrics do not allow $Λ\neq 0$ " is precise only when the metric is assumed to be in canonical Weyl coordinates. The issue is not staticity or axisymmetry, but rather the fact that the area function is no longer harmonic.

### [19] [Detectability to extreme mass ratio inspirals with alternative space-based detector networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09238)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋近（EMRI）是空间引力波（GW）探测器的重要目标，可用于研究恒星质量致密天体绕超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的运动并检验强场引力理论。随着LISA、TAIJI和天琴（TianQin）任务预计在2035年左右运行，多个探测器联合观测可能提供比单一任务更强的测量能力，因此有必要评估全局探测器网络对EMRI的探测与参数约束性能。

Method: 采用Fisher信息矩阵（Fisher information matrix）分析方法，针对由LISA、天琴（TianQin）以及两种替代TAIJI轨道构型组成的全局探测器网络，评估其对EMRI的探测能力与参数约束前景。研究涵盖单信号场景以及两种并发双信号场景：两颗EMRI绕同一SMBH运动，以及两颗具有相同内在参数但不同天区位置与取向的EMRI。

Result: 联合观测相比单独LISA任务可改善源定位，一个月观测期的天空定位不确定性降低最多两个数量级。三探测器网络（LISA-TAIJI-天琴）运行一个月的参数约束效果与LISA单独运行一年相当，部分情况下更优。在并发双信号场景中，源几何构型导致的探测器响应差异降低了重叠信号之间的相关性，使得源在单独任务下仍可区分；加入多个探测器星座进一步改善了源定位并收紧了参数约束。

Conclusion: 多探测器网络观测可在参数推断中部分补偿较短观测时长的不足；并发双EMRI信号在探测器响应中的几何差异使其保持可分辨性，而多探测器联合进一步增强了测量能力。

Abstract: Extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are among the primary targets for space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, providing valuable opportunities to study stellar-mass compact objects orbiting supermassive black holes (SMBHs) and to probe gravity in the strong-field regime. As the LISA, TAIJI, and TianQin missions are expected to operate around 2035, joint observations by multiple detectors may provide enhanced measurement capabilities compared to individual missions. In this work, we investigate the detectability and parameter-constraint prospects for EMRIs using global detector networks composed of LISA, TianQin, and two alternative TAIJI orbital configurations. Employing Fisher information matrix analysis, we find that joint observations improve source localization relative to a standalone LISA mission, with sky-localization uncertainties reduced by up to two orders of magnitude for a one-month observation period. We further find that a three-detector network (LISA-TAIJI-TianQin) operating for one month yields parameter constraints comparable to, and in some cases tighter than, those obtained from a one-year observation by LISA alone. This result indicates that network observations can partially compensate for shorter observation durations in parameter inference. Furthermore, we evaluate measurement uncertainties in concurrent dual-signal scenarios: (i) two EMRIs orbiting the same SMBH and (ii) two EMRIs with identical intrinsic parameters but different sky locations and orientations. The results indicate that differences in the detector responses associated with the source geometries reduce correlations between overlapping signals, allowing the sources to remain distinguishable even for a standalone mission. The inclusion of multiple detector constellations further improves source localization and tightens parameter constraints in these concurrent-source scenarios.

### [21] [Quantum Reference Fields Transformations in Linearized Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09344)
*Lin-Qing Chen,Flaminia Giacomini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在线性化量子引力（linearized quantum gravity）中引入量子参考场（quantum reference fields），即四个动力学标量场，使物质与引力自由度能够相对于物理量子系统进行关系性描述，并实现了量子参考系（quantum reference frames）的局域场论推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论的核心特征——微分同胚不变性（diffeomorphism invariance）要求物质与几何必须以关系性（relational）方式描述，且量子引力中参考系本身必须是量子的，这促使将量子参考系的概念推广到场论中的局域参考系统。

Method: 引入四个动力学标量场作为量子参考场，其应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）进入引力约束（gravitational constraints）；推广视角中立（perspective-neutral）的量子参考系构造，将关系性、规范不变可观测量（gauge invariant observables）约化到每个量子参考场的视角中，并推导出连接它们之间的幺正变换（unitary transformations）。

Result: 所得幺正映射实现了不同内部视角之间的局域量子坐标变换（local quantum coordinate changes），其作用于线性化引力场的结构与线性化微分同胚（linearized diffeomorphism）类似，但经典规范参数被替换为物理量子场；进一步构建了关系性冯·诺伊曼型测量方案（relational von Neumann-type measurement scheme），展示了相应的约化可观测量如何从量子参考场的视角被操作性地获取。

Conclusion: 本文建立了线性化量子引力中关系性描述的框架，将量子参考系从点粒子推广到场论系统，并为量子引力中的观测问题提供了操作性的关系性测量方案。

Abstract: Diffeomorphism invariance is a central feature of general relativity. Without external reference structures, matter and geometry must be specified relationally, with respect to internal subsystems serving as reference frames. In quantum gravity, these reference systems must themselves be treated as quantum, motivating the use of quantum reference frames. In this work, we address how such a relational description could be formulated within linearized quantum gravity. To this purpose, we introduce quantum reference fields, i.e. sets of four dynamical scalar fields whose stress-energy tensors enter the gravitational constraints. These fields extend the notion of quantum reference frames to local field-theoretic reference systems, allowing matter and gravitational degrees of freedom to be described relationally with respect to physical quantum systems. By generalizing the perspective-neutral construction of quantum reference frames, we show that relational, gauge invariant observables admit reduced descriptions in the perspective of each quantum reference field, and we derive the unitary transformations relating them. The resulting unitary maps implement local quantum coordinate changes between different internal perspectives, and act on the linearized gravitational field with an analogous structure to a linearized diffeomorphism, but with the classical gauge parameter replaced by a physical quantum field. Finally, we construct a relational von Neumann-type measurement scheme, showing how the corresponding reduced observables can be accessed operationally from the perspective of a quantum reference field.

Method: 在变形Kerr度规中引入基于质量比分析解的测地线运动作为Teukolsky方程的源项，将有限质量比轨道动力学与引力波发射直接关联；采用频域表述并结合Teukolsky齐次方程的高性能求解器，实现大量模式的快速计算。

Abstract: We present a full-relativistic waveform model for extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) by self-consistently combining the effective one-body (EOB) formalism with the Teukolsky equation. The model incorporates analytical, mass-ratio-informed geodesic solutions within a deformed Kerr metric into the source term of the Teukolsky equation, establishing a direct connection between finite-mass-ratio orbital dynamics and gravitational-wave emission. The resulting frequency-domain formulation is coupled to a high-performance solver for the homogeneous Teukolsky equation, enabling rapid evaluation of the tens of thousands of modes required for accurate EMRI waveforms. We generate waveforms and radiation fluxes for generic Kerr orbits and investigate the influence of finite-mass-ratio corrections beyond the test-particle limit. The results show that mass-ratio-dependent deformations produce measurable modifications to radiation fluxes, and accumulated waveform phases over observationally relevant timescales. Our framework provides a generic-orbit EOB--Teukolsky waveform model for future space-based GW data analysis.

Result: 协框架/自旋联络变量对提供了引力变量的一种替代性、几何上更精细的描述，能够自然地兼容局域洛伦兹对称性与费米子耦合。该框架并非完整的平行引力量子化方案，而是为未来量子引力研究识别了所需的几何与概念要素。

Conclusion: 本文的主要贡献不在于提出完整的平行引力量子化方案，而在于识别并阐明构建这样一种量子引力公式所需的几何与概念基础。协框架与自旋联络变量可作为未来探索量子引力理论的可行起点。

Abstract: We revisit quantum field theory in curved spacetime (QFTCS) as a semi-classical framework for quantum matter on classical geometries, emphasizing its limitations, including vacuum ambiguity and background dependence. We briefly review major approaches to quantum gravity (QG), including Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG), string theory, and asymptotic safety, highlighting their conceptual challenges. Motivated by these issues, we outline a teleparallel framework based on coframe and spin-connection variables, where gravity is encoded in torsion rather than curvature. This framework naturally incorporates local Lorentz symmetry and fermionic couplings while displaying a gauge-like structure. We argue that the coframe/spin-connection pair provides an alternative and geometrically refined description of gravitational variables, which may serve as a useful starting point for future investigations of QG. The purpose of this work is not to provide a complete quantization of teleparallel gravity but to identify the geometric and conceptual ingredients that such a formulation would require.

### [24] [Stationary scalar clouds around a rotating Kalb-Ramond BTZ black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09694)
*Rui Ding,Fangli Quan,Zhong-Wu Xia,Qiyuan Pan,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究罗宾边界条件（Robin boundary conditions）下旋转Kalb-Ramond（KR）BTZ黑洞周围的标量云（scalar clouds）。标量云在超辐射阈值（superradiant threshold）ω=mΩ_H处作为稳态束缚态存在，其存在性由KR参数、旋转和罗宾边界条件共同决定。KR参数会定性改变云的存在线：非正KR参数下存在线保持单调，正KR参数下存在线可变为非单调，导致固定边界条件可能在参数空间的不连通区域内容纳云。准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）和视界通量（horizon fluxes）被用作一致性检验，确认云解对应超辐射阈值处的非阻尼模式。KR参数还移动了云存在的临界罗宾参数。这些结果确立了稳态标量云可作为探测罗宾边界条件与KR引力之间相互作用的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究旋转KR BTZ黑洞在罗宾边界条件下标量云的存在性及其性质，揭示KR引力参数与边界条件如何共同影响超辐射束缚态的形成机制。

Method: 在超辐射阈值ω=mΩ_H处求解标量场的稳态束缚态解，分析KR参数、旋转参数和罗宾边界条件对云存在线的定性影响；利用准正则模和视界通量进行一致性检验，验证云解对应于超辐射阈值处能量通量变号时的非阻尼模式。

Result: KR参数定性改变云的存在线：非正KR参数下存在线保持单调，正KR参数下存在线可变为非单调，使得固定边界条件可能在参数空间的不连通区域内容纳云；KR参数同时移动了云存在的临界罗宾参数。

Conclusion: 稳态标量云可作为探测罗宾边界条件与KR引力之间相互作用的灵敏探针。

Abstract: We investigate the scalar clouds around a rotating Kalb-Ramond (KR) BTZ black hole under Robin boundary conditions. The clouds are obtained as stationary bound states at the superradiant threshold $ω=mΩ_H$, where the KR parameter, the rotation and the Robin boundary jointly determine their existence. It is shown that the KR parameter qualitatively changes the existence lines of clouds. For a nonpositive KR parameter, the lines remain monotonic, whereas for a positive KR parameter they can become nonmonotonic, so that a fixed boundary condition may admit clouds in disconnected regions of parameter space. Quasinormal modes (QNMs) and horizon fluxes are further used as consistency checks, confirming that the cloud solutions correspond to non-damping modes at the superradiant threshold where the energy flux changes sign. The KR parameter also shifts the critical Robin parameter at which the clouds exist. These results establish stationary scalar clouds as sensitive probes of the interplay between the Robin boundary conditions and KR gravity.

</details>


### [25] [Modified Teukolsky Formalism for Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals in Higher-Derivative Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09766)
*Chaoyi Yang,Neev Khera,Dongjun Li,Huan Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对高阶引力理论中质点螺旋落入非旋转黑洞的模型问题，发展了修正的Teukolsky形式化方法，用于描述质点激发的引力波，并以立方引力理论为例计算了向黑洞视界和无穷远的通量。该形式化方法可自然推广到旋转黑洞，为构建修正引力中的极端质量比旋近波形奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高阶引力理论（higher-derivative theories of gravity）中，背景时空以及引力波的产生与传播均与广义相对论（General Relativity）不同。为构建修正引力理论下的极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspiral, EMRI）波形，需要发展相应的理论框架。

Method: 发展了一种修正的Teukolsky形式化方法（modified Teukolsky formalism），用于描述由点粒子激发的引力波。该形式化方法以可自然推广至旋转黑洞的方式构建，并以立方引力理论（cubic gravity theory）为例进行了具体计算。

Result: 在立方引力理论中，计算了由质点螺旋落入非旋转黑洞所产生的向黑洞视界（black hole horizon）和类光无穷远（null infinity）的引力波通量（fluxes）。

Conclusion: 这些结果是为在修正引力理论中构建极端质量比旋近波形所迈出的关键步骤。此类波形还可通过尺度变换近似用于等质量双黑洞系统的波形，类似于广义相对论中的现有方法。

Abstract: In this work, we study a model problem involving a point particle inspiraling into a non-rotating black hole in higher-derivative theories of gravity. In such theories, both the background spacetime and the generation and propagation of gravitational waves differ from those in General Relativity. We develop a modified Teukolsky formalism to describe gravitational waves sourced by the point particle and, as an illustrative example, compute the resulting fluxes to the black hole horizon and null infinity for a cubic gravity theory. The formalism is constructed in a way that can be naturally extended to rotating black holes. These results represent essential steps to build extreme mass-ratio-inspiral waveforms in modified gravity theories, which may also be rescaled to approximate waveforms from comparable-mass binary black hole systems, analogous to existing approaches in General Relativity.

</details>


### [26] [Neutron stars in Poincaré gauge gravity with quadratic torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09786)
*Chaitanya Vashistha,Radouane Gannouji,Apratim Ganguly*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在庞加莱规范引力（Poincaré gauge gravity）的代数扇区中研究静态中子星，其中挠率（torsion）不传播，可通过自旋流（spin current）代数求解。利用满足 Frenkel 条件的 Weyssenhoff 流体，度规场方程退化为带有自旋平方修正的有效流体的黎曼爱因斯坦方程（Riemannian Einstein equations）。数值求解修正的 TOV 方程表明，正有效自旋-自旋耦合分支使恒星更致密、最大质量更低、结合能更小，而自旋关联各向异性对质量-半径关系影响可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在庞加莱规范引力框架下，此前工作多聚焦于挠率的传播特性或特定极限（如爱因斯坦-嘉当理论（Einstein–Cartan theory）），而本文旨在探索挠率不传播的代数扇区中，宇称偶和宇称奇二次挠率不变量如何影响静态中子星的结构，并考察自旋-自旋相互作用系数可调性带来的新效应。

Method: 采用满足 Frenkel 条件的 Weyssenhoff 流体模型描述自旋物质；将挠率不传播的 contorsion 方程代数求解为自旋流的函数；将度规场方程归约为由含自旋平方修正的有效流体驱动的标准黎曼爱因斯坦方程；推导有效能量密度、径向压强和切向压强（允许各向同性及各向异性自旋关联）；在爱因斯坦-嘉当极限下解析计算非极化自旋贡献；推导修正的 Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff（TOV）方程，并采用 DD2 状态方程进行数值求解。

Result: 在爱因斯坦-嘉当极限下，基于度规定义的应力-能量张量，非极化自旋贡献给出状态参数 w_spin = -1/3。数值求解表明，对于正有效自旋-自旋耦合分支，挠率修正使恒星构型更致密、最大质量降低、结合能小于广义相对论预言的结果。对于所考虑的平滑弱极化分布，自旋关联各向异性对质量-半径关系的影响可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 在庞加莱规范引力的代数扇区中，二次挠率不变量导致的自旋-自旋相互作用系数不再固定（不同于爱因斯坦-嘉当理论），从而提供了一组可调节的中子星修正方案。正耦合分支使中子星更紧凑且降低最大质量，但自旋极化各向异性对宏观可观测量的影响极小。

Abstract: We study static neutron stars in an algebraic sector of Poincaré gauge gravity with parity-even and parity-odd quadratic torsion invariants. Since torsion is non-propagating, the contorsion equation is algebraic and can be solved in terms of the spin current. For a Weyssenhoff fluid satisfying the Frenkel condition, the metric field equations reduce to ordinary Riemannian Einstein equations sourced by an effective fluid containing spin-squared corrections. We derive the effective energy density, radial pressure, and tangential pressure, allowing both isotropic and anisotropic spin correlations. In contrast with Einstein--Cartan theory, the coefficient of the effective spin-spin interaction is not fixed, but depends on the dimensionless quadratic-torsion couplings. In the Einstein--Cartan limit, using the metric definition of the stress-energy tensor, the unpolarized spin contribution gives $w_{\mathrm{spin}}=-1/3$. We then derive the corresponding modified Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equations and solve them numerically using the DD2 equation of state. For the positive effective spin-spin coupling branch considered here, the torsion correction makes the stellar configurations more compact, lowers the maximum mass, and reduces the binding energy relative to the general-relativistic sequence. For the smooth weak-polarization profiles considered, spin-correlation anisotropy has only a negligible effect on the mass--radius relation.

</details>


### [27] [Linear Ricci-Trace Deformations and Operational Equivalence in Rastall-Type Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09819)
*José A. C. Nogales,Karen-Luz Burgoa Rosso,Marcelo H. Alavarenga*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文对爱因斯坦场方程的一类线性Ricci-迹变形（Ricci–trace deformation）进行了结构化分类，澄清了Rastall引力文献中常用的参数化之间的代数等价性与操作等价性区别，并将该类模型与单模引力（Unimodular Gravity, UG）加以区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该分析以结构性而非现象学为目的，旨在对Ricci-迹变形所对应的场方程类别进行分类，固定Rastall引力文献中常用的参数变换字典，并识别在牛顿极限标定之后哪些等价关系仍然成立。

Method: 通过代数比较两种常用参数化形式，证明它们仅当形变参数和裸引力耦合（bare gravitational coupling）同时变换时才代数同构；进一步在固定实验室应力张量（stress tensor）和测得的牛顿常数（Newton constant）条件下检验这种等价是否为操作等价（operational equivalence）。

Result: 两种常用参数化仅在爱因斯坦点（Einstein point）处为被动重参数化；将λ-代表式识别为标准Rastall方程，推导了FLRW（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker）理想流体（perfect-fluid）扇区，讨论了真空、无迹物质（trace-free matter）、辐射、尘埃以及奇异无迹点（singular traceless point）等退化情形；明确区分了Ricci-迹类与单模引力——后者源于受限变分原理（restricted variational principle），将宇宙学常数作为积分常数产生，而非来自代数Ricci-迹变形。

Conclusion: 该工作为Rastall型Ricci-迹模型提供了一个紧凑的操作性分类框架。

Abstract: We analyze a class of linear Ricci--trace deformations of Einstein's field equations in which the relative weight between the Ricci tensor and the scalar-curvature trace sector is modified while the metric remains the only gravitational field. The purpose of the analysis is structural rather than phenomenological: we classify the corresponding field-equation class, fix the parameter dictionaries commonly used in the Rastall-gravity literature, and identify which equivalence statements survive after Newtonian calibration. We show that two frequently used parametrizations, \[ (1-ε)R_{μν}-\frac12 g_{μν}R=κ_εT_{μν}, \qquad R_{μν}-\frac{1-λ}{2}g_{μν}R=κ_λT_{μν}, \] are algebraically isomorphic only if both the deformation parameter and the bare gravitational coupling are transformed simultaneously. This algebraic equivalence, however, is not automatically an operational equivalence. Once the same laboratory stress tensor and the same measured Newton constant are fixed, the parameter map is a passive reparametrization only at the Einstein point. We further identify the \(λ\)-representative with the standard Rastall equation, clarify the role of the conserved effective source, derive the corresponding FLRW perfect-fluid sector, and discuss degenerate cases including vacuum, trace-free matter, radiation, dust, and the singular traceless point. Finally, we distinguish the Ricci--trace class from Unimodular Gravity (UG): although both involve the trace sector, UG follows from a restricted variational principle and produces the cosmological constant as an integration constant, rather than from an algebraic Ricci--trace deformation. The result is a compact operational classification of Rastall-type Ricci--trace models.

</details>

### [28] [Global Ab initio Neutrino Mass Limits from Neutrinoless Double-Beta Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09288)
*T. Shickele,L. Jokiniemi,A. Belley,J. D. Holt*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本研究结合最新无中微子双β衰变（$0νββ$-decay）实验数据与基于手征有效场论（chiral effective field theory）和介质内相似性重整化群（in-medium similarity renormalization group, IMSRG）的从头算核理论（ab initio nuclear theory），在贝叶斯框架（Bayesian framework）下给出马约拉纳中微子质量（Majorana neutrino mass）的全局上限。结果显示，当前实验灵敏度尚不足以探测中微子振荡数据所允许的质量区间，且联合约束显著强于单一实验；未来通过四种关键同位素的联合贡献可覆盖反质量顺序（inverted mass ordering）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无中微子双β衰变实验是探测马约拉纳中微子质量的关键途径，但此前核矩阵元（nuclear matrix elements）的计算依赖传统核模型，不确定性较大，且各实验结果单独给出的质量上限存在差异。本研究旨在利用更精确的从头算核理论结合多实验联合分析，给出更可靠的全局质量上限，并评估当前及下一代实验的探测能力。

Method: 采用贝叶斯框架（Bayesian framework），利用多个$0νββ$衰变实验的似然函数（likelihood functions）与核矩阵元（nuclear matrix elements）相结合。其中核矩阵元基于手征有效场论（chiral effective field theory）衍生的核力与弱力，通过介质内相似性重整化群（in-medium similarity renormalization group, IMSRG）多体方法计算得到。

Result: 与核模型（nuclear models）相比，从头算结果（ab initio results）表明当前一代$0νββ$衰变实验的灵敏度可能尚未达到探测中微子振荡数据（neutrino-oscillation data）所允许质量区间的水平；多实验联合给出的约束（combined bounds）显著强于任一单一实验。此外，对于下一代实验，没有任何单个实验能完全覆盖反质量顺序（inverted mass ordering），但通过$^{76}$Ge、$^{100}$Mo、$^{130}$Te和$^{136}$Xe四种关键同位素的联合贡献可以实现这一目标。

Conclusion: 基于从头算核理论的全局联合分析给出了马约拉纳中微子质量的当前最严格上限，并揭示了现有实验灵敏度的不足。未来需要多种同位素实验的联合贡献，才能全面覆盖反质量顺序对应的质量区间。

Abstract: We present global limits for Majorana neutrino masses by combining latest results from neutrinoless double-beta ($0νββ$) decay searches and ab initio nuclear theory. Limits are derived in a Bayesian framework utilizing likelihood functions from a suite of $0νββ$-decay experiments in conjunction with nuclear matrix elements calculated from nuclear and electroweak forces derived from chiral effective field theory and implemented in the in-medium similarity renormalization group many-body approach. In contrast to nuclear models, ab initio results indicate that the current generation of $0νββ$-decay experiments have likely \textit{not} yet reached sensitivities required to probe the mass regime allowed by neutrino-oscillation data, where the combined bounds are notably stronger than those given by individual experiments. Finally, from predicted sensitivities of next-generation searches, we show that, while no one individual experiment fully covers the inverted mass ordering, this can be achieved from combined contributions from the four key isotopes: $^{76}$Ge, $^{100}$Mo, $^{130}$Te, and $^{136}$Xe.

</details>


### [29] [On the effect of higher order symmetry energy corrections in Skyrme models for neutron star matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08250)
*Md. Emanuel Hoque,Arunava Mukherjee*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本研究在Skyrme类有效核相互作用框架下，系统考察了对称能的高阶同位旋修正对中子星内部物质的影响。结果表明，高阶修正对β平衡下的物质组分敏感量（如质子分数、直接Urca过程等）有显著影响，但对整体热力学状态（状态方程、能量密度、压强、声速）影响较小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大多数核状态方程（equation of state, EOS）研究采用对称能的二次/抛物线近似来描述非对称核物质的同位旋依赖性，然而该近似在高度富中子的中子星内核（inner core）中的有效性尚不明确。因此，有必要系统检验高阶同位旋修正的作用。

Method: 在Skyrme类有效核相互作用（Skyrme-like effective nuclear interactions）框架下，首先分析标准SLy4参数化中逐次高阶项引起的偏差，然后扩展分析至大量物理上可行的Skyrme EOS样本，这些样本由常规核饱和密度约束、热力学稳定性、因果性（causality）以及支持超过2倍太阳质量的中子星观测质量等条件共同筛选。

Result: 高阶同位旋修正（higher-order isospin corrections）在超高核密度下变得愈发重要，并可显著改变β平衡（β-equilibrium）下与物质组分敏感的量，包括中子-质子化学势差、质子分数（proton fraction）、轻子区性质及直接Urca过程（direct-Urca process）；但对β平衡状态方程、能量密度、压强和声速的影响相对较小。

Conclusion: 二次近似虽然能较好地捕捉整体热力学行为，但高阶同位旋贡献在中子星内部致密物质的详细组分和微观性质确定中扮演着不可忽视的角色。

Abstract: Neutron stars consist of cold, dense, neutron-rich nuclear matter under charge neutrality and $β$-equilibrium. In most nuclear equation of state (EOS) studies, the isospin dependence of asymmetric nuclear matter is described using the conventional quadratic/parabolic approximation to the nuclear symmetry energy. However, its validity in the highly neutron-rich inner core of neutron stars remains uncertain. In this work, we systematically investigate the role of higher-order isospin corrections to the symmetry energy within the framework of Skyrme-like effective nuclear interactions. We first analyze the standard SLy4 parametrization and quantify deviations arising from successive higher-order terms in the expansion of the energy per nucleon with respect to the isospin asymmetry parameter. We then extend the analysis to a large population of physically viable Skyrme EOSs sampled over a broad parameter space constrained by conventional nuclear saturation density bounds, thermodynamic stability, and causality, as well as the requirement to support astrophysical neutron-star mass observations exceeding $2\text{M}_{\odot}$. We find that higher-order isospin corrections become increasingly important at supra-nuclear densities and can significantly modify composition-sensitive quantities under $β$-equilibrium, including the neutron-proton chemical potential difference, proton fraction, leptonic sector properties, and the direct-Urca process. In contrast, the $β$-equilibrated EOS, energy density, pressure, and sound speed remain comparatively insensitive to these corrections for most viable EOSs. Our results demonstrate that while the quadratic approximation captures bulk thermodynamic behavior reasonably well, higher-order isospin contributions play a non-negligible role in determining the detailed composition and microscopic properties of dense matter in neutron-star interiors.

</details>

### [30] [Post-Merger Gravitational-Wave Uncertainties of Binary Neutron Stars under Multi-Messenger EOS Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08522)
*Yong-Jia Huang,Luca Baiotti*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过结合多信使约束（multimessenger constraints）的冷核物质态方程（EOS）和广义相对论流体动力学模拟，系统量化了双中子星并合残骸主导后并合频率$f_{2,\rm mean}$的不确定性。结果表明，在固定双星质量与恒星紧致度参数后，该频率的残余散布仅约100 Hz，远低于被数据剔除的EOS模型所覆盖的范围；未来若高频引力波探测偏离此校准预测，则直接指向有限温度下的额外物理（如强子-夸克相变）。此外，研究确认了$(f_1+f_3)/2 \approx f_{2,\rm mean}$的准普适关系，误差约116 Hz。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星并合残骸发射的高频引力波携带着孤立中子星无法达到的密度与温度下的物质信息。当前需要量化已有观测约束如何紧密地确定主导后并合频率$f_{2,\rm mean}$，以便识别偏离该预测所对应的新物理。

Method: 采用受引力波潮汐形变测量、NICER质量-半径测量、大质量脉冲星质量、低密度手征有效场论（chiral effective field theory）及渐近高密度微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）等多信使约束联合限定的冷态方程集合；对每种双星质量选择最软和最硬的模型，执行完全广义相对论流体动力学（fully general-relativistic hydrodynamics）模拟。此外，从文献中收集82种态方程模型进行对比分析。

Result: 在固定双星质量和单一恒星紧致度参数（$Λ$或$R$）的条件下，$f_{2,\rm mean}$的残余散布仅约100 Hz，远低于包含已被数据排除的态方程模型所覆盖的$≥$500 Hz范围。$(f_1+f_3)/2 \approx f_{2,\rm mean}$的准普适关系得到确认，偏差约116 Hz。

Conclusion: 多信使约束已显著缩小冷物质后并合频率预测的不确定性；未来高频引力波探测若偏离此校准预测，将直接指向有限温度下的额外物理机制，如强子-夸克相变（hadron–quark transition）。

Abstract: The high-frequency gravitational waves emitted by a binary neutron star merger remnant carry information on matter at densities and temperatures beyond those reached in isolated neutron stars. We quantify how tightly current multi-messenger constraints already determine the dominant post-merger frequency $f_{2,\rm mean}$. Adopting a set of cold equations of state (EOSs) constrained jointly by gravitational-wave tidal deformability, NICER mass--radius measurements, massive-pulsar masses, chiral effective field theory at low density, and perturbative QCD at asymptotically high density, for each binary mass we select the softest and stiffest models of the multi-messenger posterior and follow their coalescence with fully general-relativistic hydrodynamics simulations. Together with a broad set of EOSs drawn from the literature ($82$ models in total), these simulations show that, once the binary mass and a single measure of the stellar compactness ($Λ$ or $R$) are held fixed, the residual spread of $f_{2,\rm mean}$ is only $\sim 100\,{\rm Hz}$, a factor of several below the $\gtrsim 500\,{\rm Hz}$ range spanned by an EOSs set including those already disfavored by the data. This tight calibration of the cold-matter prediction implies that a future high-frequency detection departing from it would point directly to additional physics, such as a hadron--quark transition occurring at finite temperature. We further confirm the quasi-universal relation $(f_1+f_3)/2 \approx f_{2,\rm mean}$ to within $\sim 116\,{\rm Hz}$, which provides a model-independent estimate of $f_{2,\rm mean}$ from the secondary spectral peaks.

</details>


### [31] [Relativistic Thermal Emission from Accretion Disks in Kerr-MOG Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08910)
*Cheng Liu,Xu-fan Hu,Yosuke Mizuno,Tao Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在标量-张量-矢量引力（STVG/MOG）框架下，研究旋转Kerr-MOG黑洞中矢量场耦合对薄盘热连续谱的影响，发现第五力电荷会外推最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、降低盘温并软化热谱，且该效应与减小Kerr黑洞自旋几乎不可区分；通过XMM-Newton对LMC X-1的观测给出耦合参数α<0.044（90%置信度），与广义相对论（GR）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨STVG/MOG理论中矢量场（vector field）产生的排斥性第五力（repulsive fifth force）如何通过单一变形参数α修改旋转黑洞的近视界几何，并进一步影响吸积盘的热连续谱（thermal continuum emission），从而检验该引力理论是否与观测一致。

Method: 重新推导Kerr-MOG时空下的最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、Novikov-Thorne辐射通量、相对论能量移动以及零测地线结构；利用专用XSPEC谱模型（kmspec）在宽范围的自旋、倾角和第五力强度下计算完全相对论性的盘谱。

Result: 第五力电荷使ISCO外推、峰值盘温降低、热连续谱系统性软化（softening），且偏差在高倾角观测时更显著；该谱型变化与纯Kerr框架中减小自旋参数的效果高度相似；当α=0时完全恢复标准Kerr黑洞预言；模型经独立解析与数值基准验证达到机器精度；对LMC X-1的XMM-Newton数据拟合给出α<0.044（90%置信度）。

Conclusion: STVG/MOG的矢量场效应与Kerr黑洞低自旋态高度简并，需要独立的自旋测量手段（如铁线反射谱学（iron-line reflection spectroscopy））才能解耦第五力贡献；当前观测对LMC X-1的约束与Kerr度规及广义相对论（GR）相容。

Abstract: In Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG, also known as MOG), a massive vector field $φ_μ$ generates a repulsive fifth force that endows rotating black holes with a gravitational charge $Q \propto \sqrtα\,M$, modifying the near-horizon geometry through a single deformation parameter $α$. We investigate how this vector-field coupling imprints itself on the thermal continuum emission of geometrically thin, optically thick accretion disks in the Kerr-MOG black hole. By re-deriving the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), the Novikov-Thorne radiative flux, the relativistic energy shift, and the null geodesic structure for the Kerr-MOG spacetime, we compute fully relativistic disk spectra across a broad range of spins, inclinations, and fifth-force strengths using a dedicated \textsc{xspec} spectral model (\texttt{kmspec}). We find that the fifth-force charge pushes the ISCO outward, lowers the peak disk temperature, and systematically softens the thermal continuum relative to its Kerr black hole counterpart at the same spin, with the deviation amplified at high observer inclinations. The resulting spectral modification closely mimics a reduction of spin in the pure Kerr black hole framework, indicating that independent spin measurements from, e.g., iron-line reflection spectroscopy are indispensable for disentangling the vector-field contribution. All results recover the standard Kerr black hole predictions when $α= 0$, and the model is validated against independent analytic and numerical benchmarks to machine precision. Application to a 69.6~ks \textit{XMM-Newton} observation of LMC~X-1 yields $α< 0.044$ at 90\% confidence, consistent with the Kerr metric and general relativity.

</details>

### [32] [A Finite-Lattice Model from a Reciprocal Cost Action: Spectral and Reflection-Positivity Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07922)
*Jonathan Washburn,Megan Simons*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种由d'Alembert泛函方程选定的有限格点统计力学模型，其键势能为$\cosh\varepsilon-1$。主要结果包括一个负向结论：连续非紧致模型因核函数$K(u)=\exp[-(\cosh u-1)]$未通过Bochner正定性检验，从而无法建立Osterwalder-Schrader反射正性（reflection positivity）；以及一个正向结论：在有限字母变体中，当有限交叉键Toeplitz矩阵半正定时反射正性成立，并通过对角占优（diagonal-dominance）判据在特定参数下给出严格证明。这些有限体积结果不直接提供连续统的Wightman理论、Osterwalder-Schrader重构、LSZ散射或连续统质量间隙（mass gap）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是在明确的规律性和标定假设下，通过d'Alembert泛函方程选定一个具体的有限格点统计力学模型，并严格分析其反射正性是否成立，从而探讨该模型是否能通向连续量子场论的核心性质（如Osterwalder-Schrader反射正性）。

Method: 研究方法以严格数学分析为主：首先明确模型的结构输入，包括$\mathbb Z^3\times\mathbb Z/8\mathbb Z$上的键作用量$V(Δφ)=\cosh(Δφ)-1$；然后针对连续非紧致模型，通过区间验证的求积（interval-certified quadrature）计算核函数的傅里叶变换$\widetilde K(3)<0$来检验Bochner正定性；针对有限字母变体，构造Toeplitz矩阵并利用对角占优判据（diagonal-dominance certificate）在特定$v_0$值下证明反射正性。

Result: 主要结果有二：（1）连续非紧致模型中，时间核$K(u)=\exp[-(\cosh u-1)]$未通过Bochner正定性检验（$\widetilde K(3)<0$），标准Bochner途径到Osterwalder-Schrader反射正性被阻断；（2）在有限字母变体中，当Toeplitz矩阵$(K_{Φ(v_0,N)})_{a,b}$半正定时反射正性成立；对$v_0\in\{1.2,1.5,2.5\}$，通过严格的对角占优判据（与$N$无关）予以证明，相应的单步转移算子（transfer operator）在显式反射正性内积下是正且自伴的。

Conclusion: 本文的有限体积结果虽确立了特定参数下反射正性成立，但明确指出这些结果并不直接导出连续统的Wightman理论、Osterwalder-Schrader重构、LSZ散射或连续统质量间隙，表明该模型距构造完整连续量子场论仍有显著距离。

Abstract: We study the finite-lattice statistical-mechanical model whose nearest-neighbor bond potential is the reciprocal cost $J(e^\varepsilon)=\cosh\varepsilon-1$, selected by the d'Alembert functional equation under the stated regularity and calibration assumptions. The structural inputs are stated explicitly; once they are fixed, the analysis is rigorous mathematics about the bond action $V(Δφ)=\cosh(Δφ)-1$ on finite boxes in $\mathbb Z^3\times\mathbb Z/8\mathbb Z$. Our main result pairs a negative and a positive statement about reflection positivity. For the continuous noncompact model the natural temporal kernel $K(u)=\exp[-(\cosh u-1)]$ fails the Bochner positive-definiteness test: an interval-certified quadrature gives $\widetilde K(3)<0$. Thus the standard Bochner route to Osterwalder-Schrader reflection positivity is obstructed. For a finite-alphabet variant, with field values restricted to a finite symmetric set $Φ=v_0\{-N,\ldots,N\}$, reflection positivity holds whenever the finite crossing-bond Toeplitz matrix $(K_{Φ(v_0,N)})_{a,b}:=K(b-a), a,b\inΦ$, is positive semidefinite. For $v_0\in\{1.2,1.5,2.5\}$, this is discharged by a rigorous diagonal-dominance certificate uniform in $N$, and the associated one-step transfer operator is then positive and self-adjoint in an explicit reflection-positivity inner product. These finite-volume results do not provide a continuum Wightman theory, Osterwalder-Schrader reconstruction, LSZ scattering, or a continuum mass gap.

</details>


### [33] [Tracking metastable phases by complex Lee-Yang zeros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08004)
*Yi-Hua Dong,Ling Liu,Fang-Cheng Wang,Qi-Jun Ye,Xin-Zheng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过将亚稳相（metastable phases, MPs）映射到热场复平面中由李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zeros, LYZs）界定的区域，揭示了亚稳相并非“隐藏”状态，并利用玩具模型和周期驱动系统进行数值验证，表明驱动强度与LYZs虚部相关，为理解与调控非平衡集体态提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚稳相（metastable phases, MPs）在平衡相图中通常被抑制，被视为能量不利的状态而“隐藏”。本文旨在揭示并形式化描述这些亚稳相的存在位置与稳定化条件。

Method: 采用数值方法，在一个具有三个高斯峰的可调态密度（density of states）玩具模型和一个更现实的周期驱动系统中进行分析。通过追踪李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zeros, LYZs）在热场复平面中的运动，考察其随人工参数或驱动幅值的变化行为。

Result: 在两种模型中，随着人工参数或驱动幅值增大，界定亚稳相（MP）的LYZs向实轴靠近并分裂为独立分支，标志着MP在相邻两个稳定相之间增大的能隙中出现并稳定。在驱动系统中，LYZs的虚部与驱动强度相关。

Conclusion: 该发现提供了一种将亚稳相（MP）纳入相图分析的方案，揭示了亚稳相在复平面中的结构本质。将周期驱动视为复热场（complex thermal fields），为非平衡集体态的理解与工程调控开辟了新视角。

Abstract: Metastable phases (MPs) are energetically unfavorable states typically suppressed in equilibrium phase diagrams. Rather than remaining ''hidden'', we show that they exist in the complex plane of thermal fields, as regions delineated by Lee-Yang zeros (LYZs). We demonstrate this numerically in a toy model with a tunable density of states featuring three Gaussian peaks and in a more realistic periodically driven system. In both cases, as artificial parameters or drive amplitudes increase, the LYZs bounding the MP approach the real axis and split into separated branches, signaling the emergence and stabilization of the MP within the enlarged gap between two adjacent stable phases. In the driven system, the imaginary part of LYZs correlates with drive strength, linking Lee-Yang theory to terahertz matter manipulation. These findings provide a scheme to describe MPs in phase diagram analysis. By viewing periodic drives as complex thermal fields, it also offers a new perspective for understanding and engineering non-equilibrium collective states.

### [34] [Enhanced dumbbell diffusion in a periodic potential by the elevator effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08334)
*B. A. Kiang,H. Schiessel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过分子动力学模拟研究了弹簧连接的双珠哑铃模型在一维周期势中的随机行走，发现当哑铃的平衡距离与势周期不可公度且弹簧常数足够大时，会出现增强扩散（enhanced diffusion），其扩散常数可超过单珠体系，并将其类比为“牵引电梯效应（elevator effect）”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究哑铃状分子（dumbbell）在一维周期势（one-dimensional periodic potential）中的扩散行为，特别是弹簧参数与势场周期之间的匹配关系对输运性质的影响。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）对由弹簧连接的两个珠子组成的哑铃模型在一维周期势中的随机行走进行数值计算，并在极限情形下与理论解析方程进行对比验证。

Result: 当哑铃的平衡距离（equilibrium distance）与势场周期（periodicity of the potential）不可公度（incommensurate）且弹簧常数（spring constant）足够大时，体系表现出增强扩散，扩散常数（diffusion constant）可超过单珠在相同势场中的扩散常数。

Conclusion: 该增强扩散机制可类比为“牵引电梯效应”（elevator effect），即两个珠子分别扮演电梯轿厢和对重（counterweight）的角色，相互协作以克服势垒实现更高效的输运。

Abstract: We present molecular dynamics simulations of the random walk of a dumbbell - two beads connected by a spring - in a one-dimensional periodic potential and compare our results in limiting cases to theoretical analytical equations. The relevant parameters in this system are the spring constant, the equilibrium distance of the spring (relative to the periodicity of the potential), and the amplitude of the potential. Dumbbells with equilibrium distances incommensurate with the potential periodicity and with a sufficiently large spring constant exhibit enhanced diffusion. The diffusion constant can exceed that of a single bead in the same potential landscape. In this case, the dumbbell resembles a traction elevator, with the two connected beads acting as the elevator car and counterweight: the ''elevator effect''.

</details>


### [35] [A spectral model of power-law decay in natural and engineered systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08342)
*Balázs Sándor,Márk Honti,Henrique Santos Lima*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从第一性原理出发，提出了一种非广延q-指数稀释与幂律弛豫的涌现机制，通过将不完全混合反应器建模为具有吸收边界的层状扩散矩阵，证明宏观幂律尾部依赖于初始示踪物位置与边界配置的几何相互作用，并在特定条件下推导出q=5/3的非广延q-指数衰减函数及其对空间维度的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非理想输运系统中，重尾弛豫（heavy-tailed relaxation）与非广延统计力学（nonextensive statistical mechanics）现象普遍存在，但其微观物理机制尚不明确。本文旨在建立线性扩散输运与非广延统计力学之间的第一性原理联系，揭示边界几何与谱维数如何产生非广延行为。

Method: 将不完全混合反应器建模为具有吸收边界（absorbing boundary）的层状扩散矩阵（layered diffusion matrix）。在一维系统中，通过非对称、体积分布的初始浓度剖面投影到低波数本征模（low-wavenumber eigenmodes），生成弛豫率的Gamma分布（Gamma distribution）；在$d$维系统采用高度局域化、紧邻边界的奇异初始条件，分析不同空间配置下的标度指数。

Result: 在边界层厚度趋于零（$Δz \to 0$）的一维极限下，初始浓度剖面在整个时域上精确产生非广延$q$-指数衰减函数（$q$-exponential decay function），其中$q = 5/3$。在$d$维扩展中，标度指数与对应的$q$值依赖于吸收边界的空间构型；但在$d=1$极限下，$q=5/3$指数具有几何不变性（geometrically invariant）。

Conclusion: 建立了线性扩散输运与非广延统计力学之间的明确联系，表明重尾输运行为可以从边界几何与谱维数（spectral dimensionality）推导得出，为理解非理想输运系统中的非广延现象提供了第一性原理框架。

Abstract: We present a first-principles spectral mechanism for the emergence of nonextensive $q$-exponential dilution and power-law relaxation in non-ideal transport systems. By modeling an incompletely mixed reactor as a layered diffusion matrix with an absorbing boundary, we demonstrate that macroscopic power-law tails depend on the geometric interaction between the initial tracer placement and the domain's boundary configuration. For a one-dimensional system, an asymmetric, volumetrically distributed initial concentration profile projects onto the low-wavenumber eigenmodes, generating an emergent Gamma distribution of relaxation rates; at an infinitesimal boundary layer thickness ($Δz \to 0$), this profile yields the nonextensive $q$-exponential decay function exactly across the entire temporal domain with $q = 5/3$. Extended to $d$ dimensions under a highly localized, boundary-adjacent singular initial condition, the resulting scaling exponents and corresponding $q$ values depend explicitly on the spatial configuration of the absorbing boundaries. However, in the one-dimensional limit ($d=1$), these distinct initial states and boundary formulations intersect, rendering the $q=5/3$ exponent geometrically invariant. Our approach establishes a clear connection between linear diffusion transport and nonextensive statistical mechanics, showing how heavy-tailed transport can be derived from boundary geometry and spectral dimensionality.

</details>


### [36] [What Is a Pattern in Statistical Mechanics? Formalizing Structure and Patterns in One-Dimensional Spin Lattice Models with Computational Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08509)
*Omar Aguilar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用信息论和计算论方法，对三种一维自旋晶格模型（有限程Ising模型、solid-on-solid模型和三体模型）中的结构与模式概念进行了形式化定义，并将玻尔兹曼分布重构为随机过程，借助计算力学中的过剩熵、统计复杂度和epsilon-机进行分析，结果与统计力学预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在对一维自旋晶格模型中"结构"与"模式"的概念进行严格的形式化定义，并建立计算力学（computational mechanics）与统计力学（statistical mechanics）之间的桥梁，以统一两种理论框架对系统复杂性的描述。

Method: 首先对嵌入无限自旋构型中的有限一维自旋构型，提出玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的新型推导；然后将该分布重构为随机过程（stochastic process），从而利用计算力学理论分析每个自旋晶格模型；通过过剩熵（excess entropy）量化过程的可预测信息，通过统计复杂度（statistical complexity）量化过程存储的信息，并通过epsilon-机（epsilon-machine）指定结构生成机制；最后将信息测度与epsilon-机联合确定的构型与玻尔兹曼分布的典型构型进行比较，以评估一致性。

Result: 信息测度与epsilon-机联合确定的构型与从玻尔兹曼分布抽取的典型构型之间吻合，表明计算力学方法与统计力学在该问题框架下具有相容性。此外，论文还提供了计算力学的自包含入门指南以及实现信息测度和自旋模型分布的代码。

Conclusion: 计算力学为自旋晶格模型中的结构与模式提供了一种形式化且与统计力学相容的描述框架，过剩熵、统计复杂度和epsilon-机能够有效刻画系统的可预测性与结构生成机制。

Abstract: This work formalizes the notions of structure and pattern for three distinct one-dimensional spin-lattice models (finite-range Ising, solid-on-solid, and three-body), using information-theoretic and computation-theoretic methods. We begin by presenting a novel derivation of the Boltzmann distribution for finite one-dimensional spin configurations embedded in infinite ones. We next recast this distribution as a stochastic process, thereby enabling us to analyze each spin-lattice model within the theory of computational mechanics. In this framework, the process's structure is quantified by excess entropy (predictable information) and statistical complexity (stored information), and the process's structure-generating mechanism is specified by its epsilon-machine. To assess compatibility with statistical mechanics, we compare the configurations jointly determined by the information measures and epsilon-machines to typical configurations drawn from the Boltzmann distribution, and we find agreement. We also include a self-contained primer on computational mechanics and provide code implementing the information measures and spin-model distributions.

</details>


### [37] [Wave Resistance for Stochastic Motion at Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08732)
*Maxence Arutkin,Shlomi Reuveni,Elie Raphael*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究了随机轨迹下运动源在流体界面产生的波阻（wave resistance），发现低于确定性辐射阈值时存在有限阻力，并推导了布朗轨迹和Lévy飞行（Lévy flight）的标度律与闭合解，将波阻理论推广至非高斯轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统波阻理论主要关注确定性轨迹下的波辐射阻力，但在随机或噪声驱动轨迹下的平均阻力行为尚不明确，特别是低于确定性辐射阈值（deterministic radiation threshold）以及奇异性正则化（regularization）的机制有待探索。

Method: 通过系综平均表面轮廓（ensemble-averaged surface profile）控制随机轨迹下的平均阻力，对漂移布朗轨迹（drifted Brownian trajectories）推导显式标度律（scaling laws），并对漂移Lévy飞行（drifted Lévy flight）导出闭合形式（closed-form）的平均波阻表达式。

Result: 在确定性辐射阈值以下存在有限阻力（finite resistance）；在毛细-重力波（capillary-gravity waves）的最小相速度处，奇异响应被正则化；布朗轨迹显示出普适的高扩散衰减（universal high-diffusivity decay）；Lévy飞行轨迹的波阻可解析表达。

Conclusion: 该工作将经典波阻理论从确定性轨迹扩展至随机与非高斯轨迹，揭示了噪声诱导的有限阻力与正则化机制，为理解复杂运动下的流体界面阻力提供了新视角。

Abstract: Wave resistance is the drag generated by the wave radiation that a source moving at a fluid interface sustains. Under stochastic trajectories, the mean drag is controlled by the ensemble-averaged surface profile built from the trajectory history. We show that the result is a finite resistance below the deterministic radiation threshold and a regularization of the singular response at the minimum phase velocity of the capillary-gravity waves. We derive explicit scaling laws for drifted Brownian trajectories, including a universal high-diffusivity decay. For drifted Lévy flight, we find the mean wave resistance in closed-form, extending wave-drag theory to non-Gaussian trajectories.
