### [38] [Fluctuation-stable generalized entropy probes of spectral heterogeneity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08801)
*Arpita Goswami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了广义熵（generalized entropy）诊断的涨落-稳定性（fluctuation-stability）框架，从理论上解释了为何 q>1 区域数值更稳定，并引入熵梯度磁化率（entropy-gradient susceptibility）作为粗粒化探针，利用 Aubry-André 模型证明其能清晰区分均匀局域化转变与迁移率边共存区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义熵测度被广泛用于表征局域化（localization）与多重分形（multifractality），经验发现 q>1 区域数值稳定性和标度行为更优，但缺乏理论解释。

Method: 建立涨落-稳定性框架，进行热力学标度分析（thermodynamic scaling analysis），并引入熵梯度磁化率 χ_q 作为粗粒化（coarse-grained）谱异质性探针。

Result: 弱振幅谱涨落（weak-amplitude spectral fluctuations）在 q<1 时被放大，在 q>1 时被抑制；存在一个临界阈值之上的渐近稳定区域；χ_q 能清晰区分 Aubry-André 模型与广义 Aubry-André 模型中的均匀局域化转变与迁移率边共存区域。

Conclusion: 涨落稳定性（fluctuation stability）可作为准周期系统（quasiperiodic systems）中广义熵诊断的指导性原则。

Abstract: Generalized entropy measures are widely used to characterize localization and multifractality, and the regime \(q>1\) is often empirically found to exhibit improved numerical stability and cleaner scaling behavior. Here, we develop a fluctuation-stability framework for generalized entropy diagnostics and show that weak-amplitude spectral fluctuations are amplified for \(q<1\) and suppressed for \(q>1\), thereby providing a theoretical basis for the physically robust \(q>1\) regime. A thermodynamic scaling analysis further identifies an asymptotically stable regime beyond a critical threshold. As an application, we introduce the entropy-gradient susceptibility \(χ_q\) as a coarse-grained probe of spectral heterogeneity. Using the Aubry-André and generalized Aubry-André models, we demonstrate that \(χ_q\) sharply distinguishes homogeneous localization transitions from mobility-edge coexistence regimes. Our results establish fluctuation stability as a guiding principle for generalized entropy diagnostics in quasiperiodic systems.

</details>


### [39] [Time Evolution of Heat Conduction in a Generalized Model of Brownian Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08839)
*T. Koide,F. Nicacio*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一类包含动量与位置噪声及耗散项的广义谐振子网络热传导模型（基于GKSL方程的一致性要求），推导了稳态热流的解析表达式，验证了傅里叶定律并捕捉到微观热边界电阻（类似卡皮查电阻），同时发现该模型生成连续但处处不可微的轨迹，并展示了相互作用开启时的瞬时热流行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准热流定义（基于速度）在广义布朗运动框架下存在数学不一致性，且现有模型难以同时满足GKSL方程、傅里叶定律及微观热边界电阻等物理约束。因此需要发展一个自洽的广义模型，以弥合随机热力学与量子热力学之间的形式化鸿沟。

Method: 基于广义布朗运动模型构建谐振子网络，在动量与位置方程中同时引入噪声与耗散项以确保与GKSL方程兼容；利用随机能量学（stochastic energetics）的扩展框架推导稳态热流的解析表达式；通过对关联函数的微分方程进行数值求解，分析热传导的时间演化。

Result: 该模型满足傅里叶定律（线性热响应），并自然捕获了微观热边界电阻（类比卡皮查电阻）；广义模型生成了动量与位置均连续但处处不可微的轨迹（过阻尼动力学特征）；当粒子间相互作用突然开启时，热流呈现瞬态行为，且瞬时热流方向严格由相互作用是吸引还是排斥决定，与标准模型预测显著不同。

Conclusion: 该广义谐振子网络模型是一个有效的非平衡过程模拟现象学框架，为随机热力学与量子热力学的统一表述迈出了关键一步。

Abstract: We investigate the properties of heat conduction in a network of harmonic oscillators interacting with heat baths, described by a generalized model of Brownian motion. This model includes noise and dissipation terms in both the momentum and position equations. This generalization is motivated by the requirement of consistency with the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) equation. Because standard definitions of heat current based on velocity become mathematically inconsistent in this framework, we derive an analytical expression for the steady-state heat flow based on an extended framework of stochastic energetics. We confirm that Fourier's law (linear thermal response) is satisfied and that the model naturally captures microscopic thermal boundary resistance, analogous to Kapitza resistance. This demonstrates that our generalized model functions as a valid phenomenological framework for simulating non-equilibrium processes, marking a crucial step toward a unified formulation of stochastic and quantum thermodynamics. Furthermore, we analyze the time evolution of heat conduction by numerically solving the corresponding differential equations for the correlation functions. Unlike standard Brownian motion, the generalized model generates continuous and nowhere differentiable trajectories for both momentum and position (as is characteristic of overdamped dynamics). Finally, we show that the heat current exhibits characteristic transient behavior when the inter-particle interaction is switched on. Specifically, an instantaneous heat flow emerges, whose direction is strictly governed by whether the interaction is attractive or repulsive, significantly differing from the predictions of the standard model.

</details>


### [40] [Control transition in a temporally random classical spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09297)
*Elisha Shmalo,J. H. Pixley,Manas Kulkarni,Sarang Gopalakrishnan,David A. Huse*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文在经典自旋链模型中探讨了受控动力学与混沌动力学之间的相变。研究交替施加混沌哈密顿动力学与收缩性“控制映射”，发现当控制足够强时系统趋向全局稳定不动点，而控制弱时则保持混沌。该相变具有混合特征，且其普适类与存在时间随机性的有向逾渗（directed percolation）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解经典多体系统中受控动力学与混沌动力学之间的竞争机制，探究是否存在从混沌行为向受控行为的相变，以及该相变的临界性质。

Method: 采用交替施加混沌哈密顿动力学（chaotic Hamiltonian dynamics）与收缩性控制映射（contractive control map）的经典自旋链模型，通过理论分析考察控制强度变化时系统从混沌相向受控相的转变。

Result: 发现相变具有混合特征：从混沌侧接近转变点时，远离目标构型的自旋占比连续趋于零，空间与时间关联长度发散；但主导李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）在相变点处不连续，从混沌相的正值跳变为受控相的负值。此外，该相变属于存在时间随机性的有向逾渗（directed percolation）普适类。

Conclusion: 该相变的普适类与存在时间随机性的有向逾渗一致，且结果符合动力学哈里斯判据（dynamical Harris criterion）但未饱和该界限。

Abstract: We theoretically explore a phase transition between controlled and chaotic dynamics in a classical spin chain model subject to chaotic Hamiltonian dynamics and a contractive "control map", which alternate in time. The control map drives the system toward a target configuration that is an unstable fixed point under the chaotic dynamics. When the control is strong enough, the target configuration is the globally attracting stable fixed point of the dynamics; for weaker control, the many-body dynamics remains chaotic for almost all initial states. The phase transition between controlled and chaotic phases has a mixed character: As the transition is approached from the chaotic phase, the fraction of the spins that are far from the target configuration goes continuously to zero, and there are diverging spatial and temporal correlation lengths; however, the leading Lyapunov exponent is discontinuous across the transition, jumping from a positive value in the chaotic phase to a negative value in the controlled phase. We present evidence that this transition is in the same universality class as directed percolation in the presence of temporal randomness, a universality class for which we obtain results that are consistent with the dynamical Harris criterion but do not saturate the bound.

</details>


### [41] [Free fermions in disguise without exponential degeneracies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09462)
*Balázs Pozsgay*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现了一类可通过“伪装自由费米子”（free fermions in disguise, FFD）方法求解的自旋链模型，其谱在一般耦合常数下不存在指数级简并，从而区别于先前所有同类模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通过隐藏自由费米子结构可解的自旋链模型普遍存在随系统体积指数增长的能谱简并，且该简并在所有能级上均匀分布。作者希望构造一个可解模型，摆脱这种指数级简并的限制。

Method: 作者构造了一个可视为两条伊辛链（Ising chains）受特定微扰的模型，也可视为标准Jordan-Wigner可解链与Fendley原始FFD模型之间的插值。此外，作者在研究中使用了ChatGPT Pro 5.4和5.5作为研究助手，并在补充材料中详细说明了AI与人类作者的合作过程。

Result: 该模型可通过“伪装自由费米子”（FFD）方法求解，且在一般耦合常数下，其能谱不存在指数级简并。这一结果打破了此前同类模型中简并度随体积指数增长且谱均匀简并的模式。

Conclusion: 该工作为可解自旋链模型家族增添了新成员，展示了超越Jordan-Wigner范式的自由费米子可解结构中打破指数简并的可能性，并为AI辅助理论物理研究提供了一个具体案例。

Abstract: Recently, a number of spin chain models have been discovered that are solvable via hidden free-fermionic structures, going beyond the Jordan-Wigner paradigm. However, all examples in the literature displayed degeneracies that grow exponentially with the volume and that are homogeneous in the spectrum (identical degeneracies for all energy levels). In this note we present a model that can be solved by ``free fermions in disguise'' (FFD), such that the spectrum is free from exponential degeneracies for generic coupling constants. The model can be seen as a particular perturbation of two Ising chains. Alternatively, it can be realized as an interpolation between a standard Jordan-Wigner solvable chain and the original FFD model of Fendley. We used ChatGPT Pro 5.4 and 5.5 as a research assistant; in the Supplemental Material we provide details about the collaboration between the AI and the human author.

</details>


### [42] [Scaling Behaviors of Work Cumulants in Slow Isothermal Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09552)
*Ruohan Xu,Yanbo Qiao,H. T. Quan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究利用MSRDJ形式体系和连通关联函数性质，证明在有能隙系统的慢速等温过程中，功的第n阶累积量按1/T^{n-1}标度，且其系数与热力学几何张量相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统分析有能隙系统在慢速等温过程中功的累积量（cumulants of work）的行为，揭示其标度律及其与平衡性质的定量关系。

Method: 采用Martin-Siggia-Rose-De Dominicis-Janssen（MSRDJ）形式体系，并结合连通关联函数（connected correlation functions）的性质，对任意光滑协议（smooth protocols）下的慢速等温过程进行分析。

Result: 证明了慢速等温过程中功的第n阶累积量按1/T^{n-1}标度，其中T为过程持续时间；并推导出累积量的系数，发现这些系数与热力学几何张量（thermodynamic geometric tensors）相关。

Conclusion: 功累积量的标度律对任意光滑协议普遍成立，且其系数可由平衡性质确定并关联至热力学几何结构，为理解非平衡功涨落提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study the cumulants of work in a slow isothermal process for gapped systems. Using the Martin-Siggia-Rose-De Dominicis-Janssen (MSRDJ) formalism and the properties of connected correlation functions, we show that in this process, the $n$-th cumulant of work scales as $1/T^{n-1}$ , where $T$ is the time duration. This result holds generally for arbitrary smooth protocols. Furthermore, we derive the coefficients of the cumulants from equilibrium properties. These coefficients are found to be relevant to thermodynamic geometric tensors.

### [43] [Deviations from Debye's specific heat due to excess energy fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09566)
*Ralph V. Chamberlin,Sumiyoshi Abe*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过时间-相位-热平均的顺序，建立了一个理论框架来解释晶体比热超出德拜T³定律的过剩能量涨落，并将非广延性与反常扩散类比，修正了能量涨落与比热之间的标准关系，与分子动力学模拟及多种实验吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验测量发现，即使是高纯度单晶，其比热（specific heat）也常常超过德拜T³定律（Debye's T³-law）。同时，无缺陷晶体的分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟中也存在类似的过剩能量涨落，其来源涉及次近邻原子间的快速能量调制。现有理论无法解释这一现象。

Method: 基于模拟和实验证据（局域激发与热库退耦合），该理论采用独特的平均顺序：先进行时间平均（time-averaging）和相位平均（phase-averaging），再进行热平均（thermal averaging）。通过类比反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）来解释由此产生的非广延性（nonextensivity）。

Result: 该理论修正了能量涨落与比热之间的标准关系，与分子动力学模拟结果取得了良好的一致，并为大量实验测量提供了新的理解视角。

Conclusion: 该理论不仅解释了晶体中的过剩比热，还可能为理解非晶材料（amorphous materials）中的过剩比热以及量子器件（quantum devices）中的反常噪声（anomalous noise）提供理论基础。

Abstract: Measured specific heats often exceed Debye's T^3-law, even in high-purity single crystals. Analogous excess energy fluctuations in molecular dynamics (MD) simulations of crystals with no defects come from fast energy modulations involving next-nearest-neighbor atoms. Here, a theory is developed for these modulations, based on time- and phase-averaging followed by thermal averaging. This order of averaging is guided by evidence from the simulations and various experimental techniques showing that localized excitations are decoupled from the heat bath. Emergent nonextensivity is interpreted by analogy with anomalous diffusion. The theory modifies the standard relation between energy fluctuations and specific heat, giving good agreement with the simulations and new insight into many measurements. The theory may also provide a basis for understanding excess specific heat in amorphous materials and anomalous noise in quantum devices.

</details>


### [44] [Geometric Dissipation Constraints in Stochastic Reaction Dynamics: A Variational Observable for Hidden Kinetic Structure in Energy Landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09684)
*Shlomo Segal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种几何框架，用于刻画随机反应动力学（stochastic reaction dynamics）中隐藏的动力学约束（hidden kinetic constraints）。通过从Wasserstein空间的梯度流出发，推导出一个变分泛函（variational functional），其渐近结构定义了局域耗散-几何耦合可观测量（local dissipation-geometry coupling observable），能够区分传统自由能分析无法分辨的反应通道，并在Muller-Brown势、波纹周期势以及丙氨酸二肽（Alanine Dipeptide）的构象转变等基准系统中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热力学描述（如自由能势垒和熵产生）对构型空间（configuration space）中的局域几何结构不敏感，无法捕捉路径选择（pathway selection）背后的动力学约束。现有方法缺乏能够反映能量景观二阶几何特征的可观测量（observable）。

Method: 从过阻尼朗之万动力学（overdamped Langevin dynamics）出发，将其表述为Wasserstein空间（Wasserstein space）中的梯度流（gradient flow）；推导一个变分泛函，其主导阶渐近结构定义一个局域标量场；该标量场结合力-漂移对齐（force-drift alignment）与由漂移场散度诱导的相空间收缩（phase-space contraction），反映能量景观的第二阶几何特征。

Result: 该可观测量能够区分在传统自由能分析下简并的动力学反应通道（kinetically distinct reaction channels）。在Muller-Brown势、波纹周期势（corrugated periodic landscapes）及丙氨酸二肽（Alanine Dipeptide）构象转变的数值实验中，该可观测量实现了路径的稳健分离，并在高频均匀化（high-frequency homogenization）区域表现出二次标度（quadratic scaling）行为。

Conclusion: 随机反应动力学中存在额外的几何动力学控制层（geometric layer of kinetic control），该层未被标准热力学描述或反应坐标（reaction-coordinate）描述所捕捉。

Abstract: We propose a geometric framework for characterizing hidden kinetic constraints in stochastic reaction dynamics. While free-energy barriers and entropy production provide global descriptors of thermodynamic behavior, they are largely insensitive to local geometric structure in configuration space that governs pathway selection. Starting from overdamped Langevin dynamics formulated as a gradient flow in Wasserstein space, we derive a variational functional whose leading-order asymptotic structure defines a local dissipation-geometry coupling observable. This quantity combines force-drift alignment with phase-space contraction induced by the divergence of the drift field, yielding a scalar field that reflects second-order geometric features of the underlying energy landscape. We demonstrate that this observable distinguishes kinetically distinct reaction channels that are degenerate under conventional free-energy analysis, as shown through numerical experiments on benchmark systems including the Muller-Brown potential, corrugated periodic landscapes, and the conformational transitions of Alanine Dipeptide. These experiments demonstrate robust separation of pathways and are consistent with a quadratic scaling behavior in the high-frequency homogenization regime. Our results suggest that stochastic reaction dynamics contain an additional geometric layer of kinetic control in molecular motion not captured by standard thermodynamic or reaction-coordinate descriptions.

</details>

### [45] [Polyethylene-based thermo-mechanically recyclable stretchable yarns for circular sustainable textiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07652)
*SeongHyeon Kim,Duo Xu,Volodymyr Korolovych,Domingo R. Flores-Hernandez,Kaniz Moriam,Daniel J. Braconnier,Svetlana V. Boriskina*

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种完全可热机械回收的弹性纱线，由聚乙烯（PE）家族材料制成，通过调控结晶度和链取向设计出一系列熔纺PE纤维，组装成芯鞘结构纱线，其机械性能超过商用PET-氨纶纱线，且可与现有PE回收流兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能弹性纺织品多依赖化学性质不同的聚合物组成（如PET-氨纶混纺纱线），导致回收困难；亟需开发兼具高性能与可回收性的弹性纱线。

Method: 从天然材料的结构-性能关系中汲取灵感，通过调控聚合物结晶度（crystallinity）和链取向（chain orientation），设计熔纺PE纤维库使其力学性质覆盖从弹性体到功能化范围；随后将烯烃嵌段共聚物弹性芯与高强度PE鞘层组装成螺旋结构芯鞘纱线。

Result: 所制芯鞘纱线在机械性能上超越商用PET-氨纶纱线，同时保持完全可回收性；PE均聚物与共聚物可共同熔融加工和回收，不发生相分离或性能损失。

Conclusion: 该方案实现了兼具冷却、吸湿排汗和抗污性能的可回收弹性纺织品，为与现有聚乙烯回收流兼容的循环服装提供了可规模化路径。

Abstract: Most high-performance elastic textiles rely on yarns composed of chemically dissimilar polymers, rendering them difficult to recycle. Here, we demonstrate fully thermo-mechanically recyclable stretchable yarns composed of polyethylene (PE) family materials. Inspired by structure-property relationships in natural materials, we engineer a library of melt-spun PE fibers spanning mechanical properties from elastomeric to functional by tuning polymer crystallinity and chain orientation. These fibers are assembled into core-sheath yarns comprising an olefin block copolymer elastic core and a high-strength PE sheath, forming a helical architecture. The resulting yarns exceed mechanical performance of commercial PET-spandex yarns while maintaining full recyclability. We further show that PE homopolymers and copolymers can be jointly melt-processed and recycled without phase separation or loss of performance. This approach enables stretchable recyclable textiles from fibers with previously demonstrated cooling, moisture-wicking and stain-resisting performance and provides a scalable pathway toward circular garments compatible with existing polyethylene recycling streams.

### [46] [Shear-Induced Structural Convergence but Formation-History-Dependent Yielding in Sequentially Gelled Binary Colloidal Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07672)
*Alexander Kaltashov,Safa Jamali*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过粒子模拟研究二元胶体凝胶（binary colloidal gels）的稳态剪切形变，发现顺序凝胶化（sequential gelation）过程可在体系中留下持久的流变记忆（rheological memory），即使剪切作用已显著抹平常见的结构描述符差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分胶体凝胶的力学响应不仅取决于相互作用强度，还取决于网络形成的时间路径（temporal pathway），因此需要系统探究凝胶化时序对后续流变行为的影响。

Method: 采用基于粒子的模拟（particle-based simulations），通过可调延迟时间（delay time）和主导种间吸引（dominant interspecies attractions）的顺序凝胶化过程组装二元胶体凝胶，并对其施加稳态剪切变形（steady-shear deformation）。

Result: 改变凝胶化延迟产生显著不同的静态形貌（从混合良好网络到粗壳核结构），但稳态剪切驱动体系向结构收敛的混合态演化；然而，瞬态应力响应仍强烈依赖于凝胶化延迟和种间吸引强度。中等种间吸引下，增加延迟增强应力过冲；强种间吸引下，初始异质凝胶在低剪切速率下呈现两步屈服（two-step yielding）。

Conclusion: 顺序凝胶化能够在二元胶体凝胶中印刻持久的流变记忆，即使剪切作用显著抹平了常见结构描述符上的差异。

Abstract: Multicomponent colloidal gels can exhibit mechanical responses that depend not only on interaction strengths but also on the temporal pathway by which their networks form. Here, we use particle-based simulations to investigate the steady-shear deformation of binary colloidal gels assembled by sequential gelation with tunable delay time and dominant interspecies attractions. Although varying the gelation delay produces markedly different quiescent morphologies, ranging from well-mixed networks to coarse shell-core structures, steady shear drives the systems toward structurally convergent, mixed states as quantified by cluster, connected-component, and coordination analyses. This structural convergence, however, does not imply rheological equivalence. The transient stress response remains strongly dependent on gelation delay and interspecies attraction strength. For moderate interspecies attractions, increasing delay enhances the stress overshoot, particularly at high shear rates. For stronger interspecies attractions, initially heterogeneous gels exhibit two-step yielding at low shear rates, indicating distinct deformation and restructuring processes. These results show that sequential gelation can imprint a persistent rheological memory in binary colloidal gels, even when shear substantially erases differences in common structural descriptors.

### [47] [Exact mean-field phase diagram for self-avoiding active particles in a lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07823)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用平均场近似下的主方程形式（master-equation formalism），线性化均匀稳态附近的主方程，结合布洛赫定理（Bloch's theorem）将稳定性分析转化为z维紧束缚本征值问题（tight-binding eigenvalue problem），再对波数（wavenumber）在零附近做微扰展开，得到六种布拉维晶格（Bravais lattices）的旋节线表面闭式解析解。

Result: 推导出线性、正方、六角、简单立方、体心立方和面心立方六种晶格的旋节线表面闭式解析表达式；晶格几何的影响完全通过单一系数$\mathcal{A}$体现；平移扩散会平滑致密相与稀疏相之间的界面；非均匀稳态中存在旋转概率流（rotational probability currents），这是活性系统精细平衡破坏（broken detailed balance）的独特特征。

Conclusion: 平均场主方程形式可有效解析活性粒子系统的相分离行为，晶格几何通过一个系数决定稳定性，旋转概率流可作为活性系统非平衡性的可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate motility-induced phase separation in a lattice gas of self-propelled particles with hard-core exclusion, where an internal director biases particle hopping along the lattice coordination directions while undergoing rotational diffusion, together with a thermal-like translational diffusion. Rather than employing stochastic simulations, we adopt a master-equation formalism within a general mean-field approximation. By linearizing the mean-field master equation around the homogeneous stationary state and applying Bloch's theorem, the stability analysis is reduced to a $z$-dimensional tight-binding eigenvalue problem. A perturbation expansion in the wavenumber near $\vk = 0$ then yields the spinodal surface in closed analytical form for six Bravais lattices: linear, square, hexagonal, simple cubic, body-centered cubic, and face-centered cubic. The influence of lattice geometry is shown to enter exclusively through a single coefficient $\mathcal{A}$ which we evaluate exactly for each case. We further show that translational diffusion smooths the interface between the dense and dilute phases. Finally, we determine the rotational probability currents associated with the inhomogeneous stationary states, a distinctive signature of the broken detailed balance underlying active-system dynamics.

### [48] [The fluid-lattice gas isomorphism with application to liquid-vapor equilibrium in physisorbed monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08178)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于序参量（order parameter）恢复双节线（binodal）的对称性，将流体系统映射为晶格气体（lattice gas）即Ising模型（Ising model），并在二维Lennard-Jones流体及分子流体单层（monolayers）的双节线数据上进行验证；同时从微观层面将连续流体模型哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）过渡到有效准自旋晶格模型（effective quasi-spin lattice model）。

Result: 该方法在二维Lennard-Jones流体和分子流体单层的数据上得到了验证，据此推测了此类系统中存在Kramers-Wannier对偶性（Kramers-Wannier duality），并给出了临界点饱和曲线上 $dp/dT$ 的理论估计值。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够将流体液-气平衡与晶格气体（Ising模型）在全局共存区建立映射，不仅为理解临界点的热力学行为提供了理论估计，也为进一步探索流体系统中的对偶性（duality）关系奠定了基础。

Abstract: Liquid-gas equilibrium for a simple molecular fluid is considered in view of the existence of the order parameter, in terms of which the symmetry of the binodal is restored not only in the vicinity of the critical point (critical isomorphism) but also globally in the whole coexistence region. This leads to the mapping between fluid and lattice gas (Ising model). We test this approach against the data on the liquid-gas binodal of a two-dimensional Lennard-Jones fluid and monolayers of molecular fluids. The obtained results allow us to speculate about the analog of the Kramers-Wannier duality in such systems and provide the theoretical estimate for $dp/dT$ on the saturation curve at the critical point. The microscopic grounds of the proposed approach are also discussed, and the transition from the continuous fluid model Hamiltonian to the effective quasi-spin lattice model is outlined.

### [49] [Shear Banding in Amorphous Solids as a Nonlinear Screened Soft Mode Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08540)
*Yang Fu,Yuliang Jin,Avanish Kumar,Itamar Procaccia*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟验证了一种基于拓扑荷（topological charges）的非线性弹性理论对剪切带（shear banding）不稳定性机制的预测，表明剪切带源自塑性变形屏蔽的弹性场的非线性不稳定性，而非断裂（fracture）过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 剪切带是应变固体中广泛存在的失稳现象，对其建立正确的理论描述是理解固体材料力学失效（mechanical failure）的关键。近期提出了一种将塑性变形视为拓扑荷的非线性理论，但该理论尚缺乏数值验证。

Method: 本文采用数值模拟方法，对上述非线性弹性理论在非平衡准静态变形（athermal quasistatic deformation）条件下的预测进行检验。通过计算位移场分布，分析屏蔽参数（screening parameter）和非线性系数（nonlinear coefficient）的影响。

Result: 数值结果定量验证了理论预测：剪切带周围的位移场分布直接由屏蔽参数和非线性系数决定。在失稳起始点，Hessian算子的最低本征值（lowest eigenvalue）消失，对应的临界本征模（critical eigenmode）描述了跨越剪切带的位移场，该软模（soft mode）具有特定的局域化尺度并饱和形成有限宽度的剪切带。

Conclusion: 剪切带与断裂存在本质区别：剪切带源于受塑性变形屏蔽的弹性场的非线性不稳定性。拓扑屏蔽（topological screening）是控制非晶固体（amorphous solids）中剪切带形成的关键机制。

Abstract: Shear banding is a well-known and widespread instability in strained solids: under external strain, the deformation localizes along a line in two dimensions or a plane in three dimensions. Developing a proper theoretical description of this phenomenon is key to understanding mechanical failure in solid materials. Very recently, a nonlinear theory extending classical elasticity to include plastic deformations as topological charges was proposed, offering detailed predictions on the nature and consequences of the shear-banding instability. The theory derives a Hessian operator whose lowest eigenvalue vanishes at the onset of instability, and the corresponding critical eigenmode describes the displacement field across the shear band. The resulting soft mode possesses the selected localization scale and subsequently saturates into a finite-width shear band. The aim of this Letter is to examine this theory numerically, establishing the role of topological screening and nonlinear instability as the mechanisms governing shear banding during athermal quasistatic deformation. We show that the displacement profile around the shear band is directly determined by the screening parameter and the nonlinear coefficient, thereby quantitatively verifying the theoretical predictions. Our results demonstrate that shear banding differs fundamentally from fracture: it arises from a nonlinear instability of an elastic field screened by plastic deformations. This establishes topological screening as the essential mechanism governing shear banding in amorphous solids.

### [50] [On the correlation lengths of confined spheres in a cylindrical pore](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08549)
*Ana M. Montero*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文基于拉普拉斯空间方法，研究准一维窄圆柱孔道中硬球流体的结构关联，发现全局径向分布函数（global RDF）与横向分辨径向分布函数（transverse-resolved RDF）虽共享相同的极点谱（pole spectrum），但因残余（residue）的对称性消失，不同粒子对构型可由不同主导极点主导，表现出不同的关联长度和振荡频率；在强受限极限下，系统趋近于Tonks气体行为，各RDF差异消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准一维受限系统中硬球流体（hard spheres）的结构关联尚未被充分理解，尤其在窄圆柱孔道中，全局与局域关联的差异及其对密度和受限强度的依赖关系需要系统研究。

Method: 采用拉普拉斯空间形式（Laplace-space formulation）推导径向分布函数（radial distribution function, RDF），并引入横向分辨RDF（transverse-resolved RDF）以考虑粒子对在孔道横截面上的位置分布；通过极点分析（pole analysis）提取关联长度（correlation length）与振荡频率（oscillation frequency）。

Result: 全局RDF与横向分辨RDF共享相同的极点谱，但其残余依赖于横向构型并可能因对称性而消失，导致不同粒子对构型由不同主导极点（leading pole）控制，从而呈现不同的关联长度和振荡频率；全局RDF并不总是反映横向分辨可观测量中最长程的关联。

Conclusion: 在准一维硬球受限系统中，全局与横向分辨的关联结构存在本质差异，该差异随密度和受限强度变化；在强受限极限下，系统退化为Tonks气体（Tonks gas）行为，RDF间的差异消失。

Abstract: We investigate the structural correlations of hard spheres confined within a narrow cylindrical pore in the quasi-one-dimensional regime, where interactions are restricted to nearest neighbors. Using a Laplace-space formulation of the radial distribution function (RDF), we determine the correlation lengths and oscillation frequencies associated with its long-distance decay. In addition to the global RDF, we analyze transverse-resolved RDFs that account for the positions of particle pairs across the pore cross section. While these observables are associated with the same underlying pole spectrum, their residues depend on the transverse configuration and can vanish due to symmetry. As a result, different particle-pair configurations may be governed by different leading poles and display different correlation lengths and oscillation frequencies. In particular, the global RDF does not always reflect the longest-ranged correlations found in transverse-resolved observables. We examine how this behavior depends on density and confinement. In the strong-confinement limit, the system approaches the Tonks-gas behavior at finite pressure, and the differences between the RDFs disappear.

### [51] [Discovering and decoding latent mean-field structure with variational autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08694)
*Marco Biroli,Max Welling,Vincenzo Vitelli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过建立变分自编码器（VAE）容量与数据二分互信息之间的界限，揭示了成功VAE的条件独立解码器在结构上等价于有限尺寸平均场分解（finite-size mean-field factorization），从而将生成模型的潜在表示与统计力学中的平均场理论直接联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成模型虽然被广泛用于捕捉多体系统（many-body systems）中的关联，但其学习到的表示在物理上缺乏可解释性。本文旨在建立一个直观的标准，量化VAE忠实重建多体系统联合概率分布（joint probability distribution）的能力，并揭示其潜在的物理结构。

Method: 通过比较潜在通道的速率（rate of the latent channel）与数据的二分互信息（bipartite mutual information），推导出一个关于VAE容量的界限。利用该界限证明，成功的VAE其条件独立解码器在结构上与有限尺寸平均场分解相同。

Result: 在标量（Curie-Weiss）、矢量（Hopfield）和张量（Maier-Saupe）序参数的层级可解模型上验证了结论，从平衡样本中恢复了完整的Hopfield模式矩阵。应用于蝾螈视网膜记录数据时，一个双潜在变量的VAE仅用两个有效集体变量就重现了种群统计量，恢复了神经种群的“存储模式”（stored patterns）。

Conclusion: 成功的VAE重建直接证明了存在一个潜在的平均场理论（latent mean-field theory），且该理论的微观参数可以从训练好的解码器中直接读出。这为物理学家提供了一种从数据中自动推断平均场模型的新工具。

Abstract: Generative models are increasingly used to capture correlations in many-body systems, but the representations they learn remain largely opaque to physical interpretation. Here, we establish an intuitive criterion that quantifies the capacity of a variational autoencoder (VAE) to faithfully reconstruct the joint probability distribution of a many body system. In a nutshell, a bound on the VAE capacity is obtained by comparing the rate of the latent channel to the bipartite mutual information of the data. Using this bound, we show that the conditionally independent decoder of any successful VAE is structurally identical to a finite-size mean-field factorization. Hence, a successful reconstruction is direct evidence for a latent mean-field theory and the microscopic parameters of that theory can be read off the trained decoder. We validate these conclusions on a hierarchy of solvable models with scalar (Curie-Weiss), vector (Hopfield) and tensor (Maier-Saupe) order parameters, recovering the full Hopfield pattern matrix from equilibrium samples alone. We find that, when applied to Salamander retinal recordings, a two-latent VAE reproduces the population statistics with only two effective collective variables allowing us to recover the `stored patterns' of the neural population and write a generalized Hopfield model which correctly models the experimental data.

### [52] [Energy Barriers for Reversible Chain Scission and Healing under Tension with Displacement Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08763)
*Mohammad A. Ansari,Kenneth M. Liechti,Dmitrii E. Makarov,Rui Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统链断裂动力学模型假设力控制条件，导致断裂不可逆，无法解释软材料中观察到的自愈合现象。本文旨在探索位移控制条件下聚合物链断裂的可逆性。

Method: 建立可断裂的自由连接链模型，假设链中一个键断裂而其他键保持近似刚性。通过计算自由能曲线获得两个局部极小值（对应断裂与愈合状态）和一个过渡态（transition state），进而采用动力学方法（积分速率方程和动力学蒙特卡洛模拟）预测单链的统计与动力学行为。

Result: 模型预测了依赖于加载速率的链断裂行为，断裂力（rupture force）存在下界，该下界可能比上界（接近共价键的理论强度）低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 在位移控制条件下，聚合物链断裂是可逆的，能量势垒随施加位移、链长和键势能变化，为解释软材料中的自愈合现象提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Polymer chain scission is a key mechanism for fracture of soft materials. It is well known from single-molecule force spectroscopy experiments that the critical condition for chain scission depends on the loading rate and other environmental effects (e.g., temperature and solvent). Common approaches to describing the kinetics of chain scission often assume force-controlled conditions, that is, when a polymer chain is stretched by a prescribed force. As a result of this assumption, chain scission is irreversible, excluding the possibility of healing. In many soft materials, however, self-healing has been observed after fracture, suggesting possibly reversible chain scission. Here, we show that reversible chain scission is possible under displacement-controlled conditions, that is, when a polymer chain is stretched with a prescribed end-to-end distance. We present a breakable freely-jointed chain model, assuming that a polymer chain breaks when one of its links breaks while the other links remain nearly rigid. At a prescribed end-to-end distance, the free energy of the chain has two local minima and a local maximum (the transition state), giving rise to energy barriers for chain scission and healing. As the prescribed displacement increases, the energy barrier decreases for scission but increases for healing, depending on the chain length (number of links) and the potential energy of the link. With the energy barriers, we adopt a kinetic approach to predict the statistics and kinetics of a single polymer chain under tension, first by integrating the rate equation and then by kinetic Monte Carlo simulations. Notably, the present model predicts rate-dependent chain scission, with a lower bound for the rupture force that could be several orders of magnitude lower than the upper bound (which is close to the theoretical strength of the covalent bonds).

Abstract: The hydrodynamic response of Brownian particles in liquids is fundamentally altered by inertial forces arising from unsteady momentum transport in the surrounding fluid. These forces are of two distinct types\,: the added mass and the history effect. While both are well understood in bulk and weakly-confined geometries, under deterministic driving, their respective behaviours under strong confinement and thermal fluctuations remain scarcely addressed, unclear and often entangled together. The goal of the present study is thus to fill this fundamental gap. The behaviours of the two distinct inertial contributions are quantitatively investigated in the vicinity of a flat, rigid wall, using a combination of broadrange thermal colloidal-probe atomic-force-microscopy experiments, advanced numerical simulations and theory. The separation of the added-mass and history-force contributions is achieved through their different frequency-scaling signatures within the measured high-resolution thermal spectra. Our results establish a complete picture of Brownian motion at interfaces, in the lubrication regime, with direct relevance to nanofluidics and interfacial biophysics.

### [55] [Curvature-guided topology and self-assembly in chiral nematics and liquid-crystal colloids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09265)
*Ivan I. Smalyukh,Mykola Tasinkevych*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了在软凝聚态物质（soft condensed matter）中，曲率（curvature）、拓扑（topology）和手性（chirality）如何通过液晶胶体（liquid-crystal colloids）和受限向列相（confined nematics）中的缺陷结构与局域孤子织构（solitonic textures）来调控介观尺度自组装行为，并提出了一个基于亏格（genus）、欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）、锚定（anchoring）和手性的统一分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 曲率在软凝聚态中不仅扭曲有序介质，还能选择缺陷结构、重新分布弹性应力、偏置手性以及引导自组装。理解这些机制对设计可编程的软物质有序结构至关重要。

Method: 作者提出了一个基于亏格、欧拉示性数、锚定条件和手性的统一框架，用以分析球形、环柄体及带边界的胶体粒子，以及非平凡拓扑的液滴和聚合物分散向列相（polymer-dispersed nematics）。

Result: 着重分析了boojums、向错环（disclination loops）、hedgehog电荷以及链接和打结的缺陷结构；在手性体系中，讨论了skyrmions、torons、hopfions及其相关局域织构，揭示了手性和受限如何稳定三维拓扑态。

Conclusion: 这些概念可以转化为可控自组装、模板化和功能性复合材料的设�设计原则；液晶胶体和受限向列相提供了实验上易操作、可编程的模型系统，用于设计有组织的软物质。建议将全文结论扩展为1–2句完整总结。

Abstract: In soft condensed matter, curvature does more than simply distort an ordered medium: it helps select defect structures, redistribute elastic stress, bias chirality, and guide self-assembly. This review examines how curved, multiply connected, and knotted boundaries in liquid-crystal colloids and confined nematics generate topological defects and localized solitonic textures, and how these structures mediate interactions between mesoscale building blocks. We introduce a unifying framework based on genus, Euler characteristic, anchoring, and chirality, and use it to discuss spherical, handlebody, and boundary-bearing colloids, together with droplets and polymer-dispersed nematics of nontrivial topology. Particular emphasis is placed on the interplay of geometry and topology in determining boojums, disclination loops, hedgehog charges, and linked and knotted defect structures. We then turn to chiral systems hosting skyrmions, torons, hopfions, and related localized textures, highlighting how chirality and confinement stabilize three-dimensional topological states. Finally, we discuss how these concepts translate into design principles for controlled self-assembly, templating, and functional composite materials. More broadly, we argue that liquid-crystal colloids and confined nematics provide experimentally accessible model systems in which curvature, topology, and chirality can be harnessed as programmable tools for designing organized soft matter.

### [56] [ARTGEL: A temperature-regulated electrophoresis platform for quantitative studies of reversible association in gels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09597)
*Rupam Saha,Seth Fraden*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出ARTGEL——一种主动调控温度的凝胶电泳平台，可在独立控制的热和电条件下进行长时间实验。该平台通过热电调控、循环缓冲液和自动电极擦拭机制稳定电压超过24小时。相比传统电泳迁移率变动分析（EMSA）试图通过稀释、竞争剂或降温来“淬灭”反应，ARTGEL允许在与互补体相测量相同温度下进行电泳，从而直接在凝胶中量化可逆结合。利用DNA折纸组装体，展示了其保留温度依赖结合态、解析反应引起的条带变形，并支持从反应-扩散-平流模型中提取凝胶内动力学和热力学参数的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电泳迁移率变动分析（EMSA）用于分析可逆生物分子结合时，通常通过稀释、竞争剂或低温来抑制反应，以使凝胶反映预平衡体相溶液状态。对于温度敏感系统，这些策略可能在进样和迁移过程中改变化学状态，导致无法判断观测到的条带模式反映的是原始体相样品还是多孔凝胶内重新平衡后的状态。因此需要一种能够在实验全程维持可控温度条件的电泳平台。

Method: ARTGEL平台集成了三个关键技术组件：凝胶温度的半导体热电调控（thermoelectric regulation）、大型加热循环缓冲液储液槽，以及自动电极擦拭（electrode-wiping）机构。这三者协同作用，可在超过24小时的电泳运行中稳定凝胶两端的电压。实验采用DNA折纸（DNA origami）组装体作为测试体系，并在独立控制的热和电条件下进行长时间电泳运行。

Result: 实验结果表明，ARTGEL能够保留DNA折纸组装体中不同的温度依赖结合状态，可以解析由反应引起的迁移条带变形（reaction-dependent distortions）。进一步地，通过反应-扩散-平流模型（reaction-diffusion-advection modeling），可以从凝胶内条带数据中提取动力学（kinetic）和热力学参数（thermodynamic parameters）。

Conclusion: ARTGEL平台解决了传统EMSA中温度控制这一关键限制，使得可逆生物分子结合能在与体相测量相同的温度下直接于凝胶内量化，并可与溶液中的匹配测量进行比较。该工作建立了一种新的实验框架，用于在凝胶基质中直接研究可逆结合反应的动力学和热力学。

Abstract: Here we present ARTGEL, an actively regulated-temperature gel electrophoresis platform designed for long-duration experiments under independently controlled thermal and electrical conditions. ARTGEL combines thermoelectric regulation of the gel temperature, a large heated and circulated buffer reservoir, and an automated electrode-wiping mechanism that stabilizes the voltage across the gel during runs exceeding 24 h. The platform was developed to address a limitation of conventional electrophoretic mobility shift assays, which are commonly used to analyze reversible biomolecular association but usually aim to suppress reaction during electrophoresis by dilution, competitors, or reduced temperature so that the gel reports a pre-equilibrated bulk solution. For temperature-sensitive systems, these strategies can alter the chemical state during loading and migration and obscure whether the measured band pattern reflects the original bulk sample or a re-equilibrated state inside the porous gel. Rather than attempting to quench reactions, ARTGEL enables electrophoresis to be performed at the same temperature as complementary bulk measurements, so that reversible association can be quantified directly in the gel and compared with matched measurements in solution. Using DNA origami assemblies, we show that ARTGEL preserves distinct temperature-dependent association states, resolves reaction-dependent distortions of migrating bands, and supports extraction of in-gel kinetic and thermodynamic parameters from reaction-diffusion-advection modeling.

</details>


### [57] [Elastoinertial effects govern dynamic response of soft hair beds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09703)
*Jonas Smucker,Naiesa Freeman,Eric Caballero,Philip J. Morrison,José Alvarado*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过大振幅振荡剪切流实验，研究了弹性毛发床（elastic hair beds）在低至中等雷诺数下的瞬态流变学响应，发现流体与弹性毛发之间的耦合作用会产生依赖于驱动频率和幅度的动态非线性响应，并识别出从应力滞后（stress-lagging）到应力超前（stress-leading）的交叉行为，为理解生物毛发床在机械转导（mechanotransduction）过程中如何优化动态信息传递建立了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管生物体中广泛存在浸没于流体中的毛发床结构（如内皮糖萼、初级纤毛、肠微绒毛等）并充当机械传感器，但它们在时变条件下的动态力学特性尚未得到充分表征。

Method: 研究采用大振幅振荡剪切流（large-amplitude oscillatory shear flows）对弹性毛发床进行实验，在低至中等雷诺数范围内观察其瞬态流变学响应，并引入简化的刚性梁模型（rigid-beam model）对交叉行为进行定性捕捉。

Result: 毛发和流体本身服从线性本构关系，但耦合相互作用产生动态非线性响应，该响应敏感地依赖于驱动频率和幅度；研究识别出一个由流体粘度、流体惯性和毛发弹性共同决定的从应力滞后到应力超前的交叉行为。

Conclusion: 动态流动响应的表征具有直接的生物学意义，因为滞后时间敏感地决定了机械感觉信号在反馈回路中的稳定性，这些反馈回路是血管舒张、纤毛重塑和肾小管重吸收等关键生物过程的基础；研究结果为理解生物毛发床的物理性质如何优化机械转导中的动态信息传递提供了框架。

Abstract: Fluid-immersed hair beds are ubiquitous in biology-from the endothelial glycocalyx and primary cilia to intestinal microvilli-where they serve as mechanosensors that transduce dynamic flow signals into biochemical regulatory responses. Despite the inherently dynamic nature of physiological flows, the dynamic mechanical properties of fluid-immersed hair beds under time-varying conditions remain poorly characterized. Here we investigate the transient rheological response of elastic hair beds to large-amplitude oscillatory shear flows at low to intermediate Reynolds number. While the hairs and fluid themselves obey linear constitutive laws, their coupled interaction produces a dynamic nonlinear response that depends sensitively on driving frequency and amplitude. We identify a crossover from a stress-lagging regime to a stress-leading regime, which is governed by an interplay between fluid viscosity, fluid inertia, and hair elasticity. A simplified rigid-beam model qualitatively captures the crossover behavior. Characterizing the dynamic flow response of soft hair beds has direct biological implications, since the lag time sensitively determines the stability of mechanosensory signaling in the feedback loops underlying essential biological processes such as vasodilation, ciliary remodeling, and tubular reabsorption. Our results establish a framework for understanding how the physical properties of biological hair beds optimize dynamic information transmission during mechanotransduction.

</details>

### [58] [Simplest Nontrivial Maxwellian Random Field Models for Stochastic LoS MIMO Using the Dyadic Green's Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08463)
*Lumeng Xu,Said Mikki*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于全波、物理自洽的随机并矢格林函数（SDGF）框架，用于在波数不确定性下建模电磁MIMO信道。该框架提供了同时满足麦克斯韦方程组的最简精确随机场模型（称为麦克斯韦随机场理论模型），包含解析可处理的波数高斯模型和更一般的随机平面波（SPW）模型，并分析了遍历容量与自由度（DoF），揭示了复杂SPW模型的关键结果可由更简单的高斯模型复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统MIMO信道建模多基于唯象的衰落模型（phenomenological fading models），缺乏对电磁场基本物理定律（麦克斯韦方程组）的严格遵从，导致无法准确描述波数不确定性下的随机传播行为。

Method: 提出随机并矢格林函数（stochastic dyadic Green's function, SDGF）框架，构建两种精确随机场模型：解析可处理的波数高斯模型（wavenumber Gaussian model）和更一般的随机平面波（stochastic plane wave, SPW）模型。模型通过保持麦克斯韦方程组的矢量结构和色散关系（dispersion relation），自然包含传播模式（propagating modes）和倏逝模式（evanescent modes）。

Result: 遍历容量（ergodic capacity）与自由度（degrees of freedom, DoF）分析表明，复杂SPW模型的关键结果可由更简单的波数高斯模型在有限方差条件下复现。在二维连续MIMO系统中，该麦克斯韦自洽的随机性可解释信道容量和DoF相对于确定性MIMO容量基线的增加。

Conclusion: 所提出的麦克斯韦随机场理论模型（Maxwellian random field theoretic models）为理解随机视距（line-of-sight, LoS）传播环境中的基本极限提供了物理上自洽的基准参考点。

Abstract: This letter introduces a novel, full-wave, physics-compliant stochastic dyadic Green's function (SDGF) framework for modeling electromagnetic (EM) multiple-input-multiple-output (MIMO) channels under wavenumber uncertainty. Unlike conventional phenomenological fading models, the proposed approach provides what appear to be the simplest exact random field models of electromagnetic line-of-sight (LoS) propagation that are also exact solutions of Maxwell's equations. Hence, we dub them Maxwellian random field theoretic models. These physically consistent stochastic models, including an analytically tractable wavenumber Gaussian model and a more general stochastic plane wave (SPW) model, serve as fundamental baseline models for stochastic LoS channel characterization. By preserving the vectorial structure of Maxwell's equations and the dispersion relation, the framework naturally incorporates both propagating and evanescent modes. Our analysis of ergodic capacity and degrees of freedom (DoF) reveals that the key results of the complex SPW model can be reproduced by the simpler Gaussian model with limited variance. Furthermore, we provide examples using 2D continuous MIMO systems, illustrating how the model's Maxwell-consistent stochasticity explains observed increases in channel capacity and DoF over the deterministic MIMO capacity baseline. These idealized Maxwellian random field theoretic models offer a physically grounded reference point for understanding fundamental limits in stochastic LoS propagation environments.

### [59] [Length-resolved Operator Growth and Path-Entropy Obstructions to Many-Body Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07774)
*J. Sirker*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文证明无序横纵场伊辛链中局域算子的算符权重在支撑长度 ℓ_k ∼ k/ln k 上呈现近乎阶乘增长，排除了任意 Disorder 强度下的动力学局域性（dynamical locality），并建立了有限尺寸交叉标度 L∼(W/J)²，同时指出一种结构性的路径熵障碍阻碍了微扰 LIOM 构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无序量子多体系统中，多体局域化（many-body localization, MBL）是否能在任意 Disorder 强度下存在仍是一个核心问题。作者旨在通过分析局域算符在空间支撑长度上的权重增长，检验动力学局域性（dynamical locality）——MBL 的最强形式——是否可能成立。

Method: 作者将算符范数按照支撑长度（support length）进行分解，解析求解了在严格正分布下的无序横纵场伊辛链中局域算符嵌套对易子（nested commutator）的范数增长与空间展宽行为，并利用路径计数（path-counting）与随机振幅分析揭示路径熵障碍（path-entropy obstruction）。

Result: 算符在支撑长度 ℓ_k ∼ k/ln k 上的权重已呈现近乎阶乘增长 ‖[H,σ_z⁰]^{(k)}_{ℓ_k}‖₂ ≳ (k/ln k)^k。这排除了任意 Disorder 下的动力学局域性。同时严格建立了有限尺寸交叉标度 L∼(W/J)²，并识别出一种不依赖于共振效应（resonance effects）的结构性路径熵障碍，该机制强烈提示弹道式的实时算符扩展（ballistic real-time operator spreading）。

Conclusion: 在无序横纵场伊辛链中，局域算符的展宽达到最大允许速率（maximal allowed rate），表明不存在动力学局域性；数值研究在 L≲(W/J)² 范围内仅能观察到一个预渐近（pre-asymptotic）行为。亚弹道或局域化动力学若要存在，需要一个尚未发现的抵消原理（cancellation principle）作用于近乎阶乘多个 Disorder 依赖的路径上。

Abstract: For the disordered Ising chain with transverse and longitudinal fields, where couplings and fields are drawn from strictly positive distributions, Cao~\cite{Cao} has shown that the moments $μ_{2k} = \|[H,σ^z_0]^{(k)}\|_2^2$ grow almost factorially, $μ_{2k}^{1/(2k)}\sim k/\ln k$, and thus asymptotically at the maximal allowed rate. We generalize this result by resolving the operator norm in support length and show that the weight at length $\ell_k \sim k/\ln k$ already exhibits almost factorial growth, $\|[H,σ^z_0]^{(k)}_{\ell_k}\|_2 \gtrsim (k/\ln k)^k$. This implies maximal spatial delocalization of local operators and, in particular, rules out dynamical locality -- the strongest form of many-body localization -- at any disorder strength. We further establish rigorously a finite-size crossover scale $L\sim (W/J)^2$, where $W$ is the disorder and $J$ the coupling strength. For $L\lesssim (W/J)^2$ numerical studies only access a pre-asymptotic regime. Finally, we identify a structural path-entropy obstruction to perturbative LIOM constructions, based on the almost factorial branching of operator content and independent of resonance effects; the same mechanism strongly suggests ballistic real-time operator spreading, so sub-ballistic or localized dynamics would require a presently unidentified cancellation principle acting on almost factorially many disorder-dependent paths with random amplitudes.

</details>


### [60] [Dynamical cavity method for continuous-time complex systems on sparse random graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08689)
*Fernando L. Metz,Isaac Pérez Castillo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过连续时间腔方法（cavity method）发展了稀疏网络动力平均场理论（sparse-network DMFT），给出了稀疏随机图上一般成对相互作用随机动力学的路径测度（path measure）描述，阐明了有向图与互易图在动态闭包机制上的根本区别，并建立了有限记忆数值闭包与高连接极限下的理论联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的动力平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）适用于稠密高维无序动力学，但在稀疏异质网络中，局部场仅包含有限数量的强输入，因此稠密DMFT的高斯闭包（Gaussian closure）机制不再适用。本文旨在为稀疏网络建立严格且通用的DMFT路径测度框架。

Method: 采用连续时间腔方法，在路径测度层面上推导稀疏随机图上一般成对相互作用随机动力学的DMFT方程；该方法在树上精确成立，并推广到局部树状图（locally tree-like graphs）。通过因果离散时间推导获得相应的群体动力学表示（population-dynamics representation），区分有向图与互易图的不同闭包结构。还提出了有限记忆数值闭包方案。

Result: 推导出了稀疏网络的精确腔方程，表明互易性（reciprocity）从根本上改变了动态闭包结构：有向图恢复稀疏有向路径概率方程，而互易/双向边需要由接收节点历史驱动的条件路径核（conditional path kernel）。群体动力学表示中，有向图对应轨迹群体，互易图对应条件分支律或有限深度树群体。高连接极限下，稀疏路径测度理论可投影还原为标准的低维DMFT。

Conclusion: 稀疏DMFT路径测度框架统一了有向与互易网络的动力学描述，澄清了高连接极限下稠密与稀疏DMFT的适用条件，为实际应用（如加法输入递归神经网络）提供了理论支撑和数值闭包方法。

Abstract: Dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) reduces dense high-dimensional disordered dynamics to a self-consistent effective stochastic process. For sparse and heterogeneous networks, however, local fields contain finitely many strong inputs, so the Gaussian closure mechanisms of dense DMFT need not apply. We develop a continuous-time cavity derivation of sparse-network DMFT at the level of path measures for stochastic dynamics with general pairwise interactions on sparse random graphs. The cavity equations are exact on trees and yield the finite-time thermodynamic description on locally tree-like graphs. They show explicitly how reciprocity changes dynamical closure: fully directed graphs recover the sparse directed path-probability equation, whereas reciprocal or bidirected edges require conditional path kernels driven by the imposed history of the receiving node. Ensemble averaging gives laws over path-probability messages, with barycenters and higher-message moments closing by multilinearity and independence of incoming branches. A causal discrete-time derivation yields the corresponding population-dynamics representation, distinguishing trajectory populations for directed graphs from conditional branch-law or finite-depth tree populations for reciprocal graphs. We also formulate finite-memory numerical closures and test them in an additive-input recurrent neural network specialization. Finally, high-connectivity limits are obtained as projections of the sparse path-measure theory, clarifying when dense drift, noise, and response channels reduce to standard low-dimensional DMFT and when path-level descriptions remain essential.

</details>


### [61] [Statistical Mechanics of Random Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08706)
*Isaac Pérez Castillo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文是基于2024年在阿卜杜斯·萨拉姆国际理论物理中心（ICTP）举办的春季学院讲义，系统介绍了稀疏随机矩阵（sparse and diluted random matrices）谱理论的统计力学方法，重点涵盖空穴与复制方法（cavity and replica methods）、预解式技巧、种群动力学、典型谱密度、谱计数涨落与大偏差、条件谱以及非厄米拓展等内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 讲义旨在从统计力学（statistical mechanics）的视角为稀疏随机矩阵的谱理论提供系统性教学路径，弥补黑板讲授的局限性，并在讲义形式中更全面地展开方法框架及其自然延伸。

Method: 主要采用统计力学方法，包括空穴方法（cavity method）与复制方法（replica method）、预解式（resolvent）技术、种群动力学（population dynamics）以及大偏差理论（large deviations）等工具，对稀疏随机矩阵的谱性质进行分析。

Result: 讲义在内容上扩展了实际授课范围，涵盖了典型谱密度（typical spectral densities）、谱计数涨落（spectral-count fluctuations）和大偏差、受条件约束的谱（conditioned spectra）以及非厄米随机矩阵（non-Hermitian random matrices）拓展等专题。

Conclusion: 作为教学性讲义，本文在选择性选题的基础上兼顾与更广泛文献的衔接，力图在教材性框架内公平呈现该领域的研究现状，并为未来更深入的讲授提供方向性指引。

Abstract: These lecture notes are based on the lectures on \emph{Statistical Mechanics of Random Matrices} delivered at the Spring College on the Physics of Complex Systems, held at the Abdus Salam International Centre for Theoretical Physics, Trieste, Italy, from 19 February to 15 March 2024. Their aim is to present a statistical-mechanics route to the spectral theory of sparse and diluted random matrices, with emphasis on cavity and replica methods, resolvent techniques, population dynamics, typical spectral densities, spectral-count fluctuations and large deviations, conditioned spectra, and non-Hermitian extensions. The written form of the notes has been deliberately expanded beyond the material actually covered during the lectures. This is partly because a set of lecture notes can afford a more systematic development than a sequence of blackboard lectures, and partly because several natural continuations of the material become clearer once the central methods have been introduced. Consequently, not every topic discussed here was presented during the College. The additional material is included to give a more coherent account of the subject and to indicate directions that, hopefully, can be covered in greater detail in future lectures or schools. Since these are lecture notes rather than a state-of-the-art review, the choice of topics is necessarily selective and is naturally tilted towards the author's own work and collaborations on this subject. I have nevertheless tried, within the limits of this format, to place the material in contact with the broader literature and to represent the surrounding state of the art as fairly as possible. Inevitably, some relevant contributions may be missing or treated too briefly; such omissions are unintentional and reflect the pedagogical scope of the notes rather than a judgement on their importance.

</details>


### [62] [Predictable Mean-Field Chaos in Random Recurrent Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08805)
*Alkesh Yadav,Vladimir Shaidurov,Jonathan Kadmon*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文证明，对于具有足够快傅里叶衰减（Fourier decay）的解析非线性函数，随机循环网络（random recurrent networks）中平均场理论（mean-field theory）的混沌行为表面上是随机的，实际上由其连续过去唯一决定，从而将平均场理论从系综描述提升为个体轨迹的条件预测理论。研究通过将功率谱展开为Krylov状态空间（Krylov state space），揭示了隐性确定性在时间模式层级中的组织方式，并表明Krylov增长率（Krylov growth rate）限制了有限分辨率预测的复杂度，上界约束了最大李雅普诺夫指数（largest Lyapunov exponent），从而区分了微观敏感性与预测复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将动态平均场理论从系综层面的统计描述，重新解释为对个体混沌轨迹具有条件预测能力的确定性理论，并厘清微观敏感性与预测复杂性之间的关系。

Method: 利用解析非线性的快速傅里叶衰减性质，证明平均场轨迹的过去连续历史唯一决定其未来；通过将功率谱展开为Krylov状态空间，构建无限时间模式层级来组织结构化预测。

Result: Krylov增长率设定了有限分辨率预测的复杂度上限，并对该网络类别中的最大李雅普诺夫指数给出了上界约束。

Conclusion: 微观敏感性（microscopic sensitivity）与预测复杂性（predictive complexity）是平均场混沌（mean-field chaos）的两个不同方面；本文将针对哈密顿混沌动力学（Hamiltonian chaotic dynamics）的Krylov增长思想推广到了经典耗散系统（classical dissipative systems）中。

Abstract: Dynamical mean-field theory recasts deterministic chaos in random recurrent networks as an effective stochastic process. We show that for analytic nonlinearities with sufficiently fast Fourier decay, this stochasticity is only apparent: the continuous past of a realized mean-field trajectory uniquely determines its future. The mean-field theory is therefore not merely an ensemble description, but a conditional prediction theory for individual trajectories. Unfolding the power spectrum into a Krylov state space exposes how this latent determinism is organized across an infinite hierarchy of temporal modes. The associated Krylov growth rate sets the complexity of finite-resolution prediction and upper-bounds the largest Lyapunov exponent in this class of networks. Thus, microscopic sensitivity and predictive complexity are distinct aspects of mean-field chaos. Our results extend Krylov growth ideas developed for Hamiltonian chaotic dynamics to classical dissipative systems.

### [63] [Search for new physics using single-lepton events with high multiplicities of jets and b jets in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09567)

TL;DR: 基于CMS探测器在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中收集的138 fb$^{-1}$数据，利用单轻子多喷注（含底夸克喷注）事件搜索超出标准模型的新物理。未发现显著超出，在R宇称破坏超对称模型下，胶微子质量被排除至1890 GeV以下（95%置信水平）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在13 TeV质心能量下利用高亮度LHC数据，搜索超出标准模型（beyond the standard model）的新物理信号，重点关注R宇称破坏（R-parity violating, RPV）超对称（supersymmetry, SUSY）模型中胶微子（gluino）对的产生与衰变。

Method: 采用单轻子（single-lepton）事件样本，要求高喷注多重度（high multiplicity of jets），包含由底夸克喷注（bottom quark jets）标记的喷注，但不要求缺失横动量（missing transverse momentum）。信号鉴别基于大半径喷注（large-radius jet）质量之和，以有效捕捉高喷注多重度与高相互作用能量的特征。

Result: 观测数据与标准模型背景预测之间无显著超出。在RPV超对称模型框架下，假设胶微子衰变至顶、底和奇异夸克，胶微子质量在95%置信水平（confidence level）下被排除至1890 GeV以下。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现超出标准模型的新物理迹象，并对RPV超对称模型中胶微子质量设定了新的严格排除界限（m<1890 GeV），进一步限制了相关新物理模型参数空间。

Abstract: This paper presents a search for beyond the standard model physics using single-lepton events with a high multiplicity of jets, including those identified as bottom quark jets, without a requirement on missing transverse momentum. The analysis is based on proton-proton collision data collected with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. This search is sensitive to $R$-parity violating supersymmetry models, where supersymmetric particles can decay into standard-model particles through interactions that violate baryon number conservation. In particular, the signal model considered is gluino pair production, where each gluino decays into top, bottom, and strange quarks. The sum of large-radius jet masses is used to distinguish the signal from background, as it effectively captures the features of high jet multiplicity and high interaction energy. No significant excess of data over the background predictions is observed. Gluinos in this model have been excluded for masses below 1890 GeV at 95% confidence level.

### [64] [Atmospheric Neutrino Oscillations: the Full Picture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09714)
*Philipp Eller*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究首次对多个大气中微子数据集（Super-Kamiokande、IceCube-DeepCore、KM3NeT/ORCA）与反应堆数据（Daya Bay）进行联合振荡分析，证明统一物理模型可同时描述所有数据集且无显著参数张力，在大型参数空间中给出了中微子混合参数的竞争性测量，并倾向于正常质量顺序（Normal Mass Ordering）且不支持CP守恒（CP conservation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，跨实验合作的多大气中微子数据集联合振荡分析被认为在合作外部不可行；本文旨在证明统一的物理模型能够同时拟合这些数据集，从而获得更精确的中微子振荡参数测量。

Method: 对来自Super-Kamiokande、IceCube-DeepCore、KM3NeT/ORCA的大气中微子数据集与Daya Bay反应堆数据进行了首次联合振荡分析（combined oscillation analysis）；拟合了1536个能箱（bin）中的839048个事件，模型包含91个参数。

Result: 联合分析获得了中微子混合参数（neutrino mixing parameters）的竞争性测量值；结果不支持CP守恒（CP conservation），并倾向于正常质量顺序（Normal Mass Ordering）而非倒转质量顺序（Inverted Mass Ordering）。所有数据集之间未发现显著的参数张力（parameter tensions）。

Conclusion: 跨实验联合分析大气中微子及反应堆数据集在技术上是可行的，且可提供一致的物理图像；该方法为未来开展更大规模的中微子振荡联合研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present the first combined oscillation analysis of multiple atmospheric neutrino datasets, featuring data from Super-Kamiokande, IceCube-DeepCore, and KM3NeT/ORCA together with reactor data from Daya Bay. Such combinations have long been considered infeasible outside experimental collaborations; we demonstrate that a unified physics model can simultaneously describe all datasets with no significant parameter tensions. Fitting 839\,048 events across 1536 bins with 91 parameters, our combined analysis yields competitive measurements of the neutrino mixing parameters, disfavors CP conservation, and prefers the Normal over the Inverted Mass Ordering.

### [65] [No need to stay positive: a practical approach to direct numerical simulations of elastic turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09468)
*Damiano Capocci,Moritz Linkmann,Alexander Morozov*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在高分子流体直接数值模拟中，违反物理约束条件 Tr c>3（即构象张量失去正定性）的模拟是否仍能提供有意义的物理洞察。结果显示，在一定分辨率区间内，即使局部违反该约束，模拟仍能保持稳定且混沌，且速度、速度梯度及高分子拉伸的中平面统计量与完全正定性模拟的结果一致，从而可能降低研究弹性湍流（elastic turbulence）的计算门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分子流体（polymeric flows）的直接数值模拟面临维持构象张量（conformation tensor）正定性的挑战，现有防止违反 Tr c>3 的方法计算成本高昂，使得弹性湍流等混沌流动的模拟严重依赖高性能计算。因此，研究能否在放松该约束的条件下仍获得有意义的物理结果。

Method: 在低雷诺数（Reynolds number）条件下，对通过平面通道的稀聚合物溶液（dilute polymer solution）模型进行模拟，观察其向弹性湍流的转变过程。通过调整分辨率，识别出两个阈值分辨率，并分析介于两者之间、局部违反 Tr c>3 但保持稳定的模拟结果。

Result: 发现存在两个阈值分辨率：低于第一阈值时模拟出现数值不稳定和有限时间爆裂（finite-time blow-up）；高于第二阈值时保持正定性。在两者之间的分辨率下，模拟尽管局部违反 Tr c>3，仍保持稳定和混沌特性；且中平面（mid-plane）的速度、速度梯度及高分子拉伸统计量与完全正定性模拟的结果一致。

Conclusion: 局部违反构象张量正定性并未显著影响关键流动统计量，表明解析流动结构或关键统计量可能不需要维持正定性所需的极端分辨率，这有望降低研究弹性湍流的计算障碍。

Abstract: Successfully performing direct numerical simulations of polymeric flows remains a major challenge in computational fluid mechanics. In addition to the velocity field, such simulations must resolve polymeric degrees of freedom, often expressed via the conformation tensor, $\mathbf{c}$, which captures the local stretch of polymer molecules. A key difficulty here lies in maintaining the physical requirement $\mathrm{Tr}\, \mathbf{c}>3$, which is not explicitly enforced by the governing equations. Consequently, simulations initiated from physical conditions may silently drift into unphysical states with $\mathrm{Tr}\, \mathbf{c}<0$, indicating a loss of positive-definiteness of the conformation tensor. Existing numerical methods to prevent this are costly, making direct numerical simulations of chaotic polymer flows, such as elastic turbulence, heavily reliant on high-performance computing.
  Here, we ask whether simulations that violate $\mathrm{Tr}\, \mathbf{c}>3$ can still yield meaningful physical insight into the underlying dynamics. We simulate a model dilute polymer solution driven through a plane channel at low Reynolds number and observe the transition to elastic turbulence. Our simulations exhibit two threshold resolutions: below the first, they become numerically unstable and exhibit a finite-time blow-up; above the second, they maintain positive-definiteness. In between, simulations remain stable and chaotic despite local violations of $\mathrm{Tr}\, \mathbf{c}>3$. Surprisingly, these violations do not affect mid-plane statistics of velocity, its gradients, or polymer stretch, which match results from fully positive-definite simulations. This suggests that resolving flow structures or key flow statistics may not require the extreme resolutions needed to preserve positive-definiteness, potentially lowering computational barriers for studying elastic turbulence.

</details>

### [66] [Finite-temperature formation of magnetic plateaus and simplex liquid states on the frustrated ruby lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07609)
*Antonio Francesco Mello,E. Miles Stoudenmire,Joseph Tindall*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用基于置信传播（belief propagation）的无限张量网络态（iTNS）方法，绘制了具有次近邻相互作用的红宝石晶格上自旋-1/2海森堡反铁磁体的有限温度相图，发现了低温柔磁化平台及其中存在的“单纯形液态”（simplex liquid state）——一种具有非零残余熵的无序相，并证明系统在降温过程中未经历相变即可进入该状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统中的几何阻挫（geometric frustration）可稳定非常规物相，避免低温下的传统磁有序，但如何在有限温度下准确描述此类阻挫量子磁体的相行为仍是挑战。

Method: 采用无限张量网络态（infinite tensor network state, iTNS），结合置信传播（belief propagation, BP）及其修正算法进行优化和测量，绘制红宝石晶格上次近邻自旋-1/2海森堡反铁磁体的有限温度相图。

Result: 观察到不同磁场强度下低温稳定磁化平台的形成；这些平台中存在一种称为“单纯形液态”（simplex liquid state）的无序相，其特征是强配对的自旋单纯形（spin simplex）构成、由于指数大的晶格构型子空间而保留非零残余熵（non-zero residual entropy）。

Conclusion: 系统降温至磁化平台态的过程中未经历相变，热容（heat capacity）在所有观测温度下保持有限且连续；基于BP的张量网络技术为理解有限温度下阻挫量子磁体提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Geometric frustration in quantum systems can stabilize unconventional phases of matter that avoid traditional magnetic ordering at low temperatures. Here, we observe this phenomenon while mapping out the finite temperature phase diagram of the spin-1/2 Heisenberg antiferromagnet on the ruby lattice with next-nearest-neighbor interactions. Using an infinite tensor network state (iTNS) optimized and measured with belief propagation (BP) and corrections to BP, we observe the low temperature formation of stable magnetic plateaus at various magnetic field strengths. We find these plateaus host a novel `simplex liquid state' -- a disordered phase involving strongly paired spin simplices that retains non-zero residual entropy due to an exponentially large subspace of crystalline configurations. We accurately quantify the energy gap associated with these states and show that, as the temperature of the system is lowered, it does not go through a phase transition to reach them: the heat capacity remains finite and continuous at all observed temperatures. Our work demonstrates how BP-based tensor network techniques provide a powerful route to understanding frustrated quantum magnets at finite temperature.

### [67] [Topological Melting of Magnetic Stripes and the Emergence of Macroscopic d-wave Superconductivity in the 2D Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07634)
*Jin Hyung Cho*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过约束路径辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（constrained-path auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo）方法对高达24×24格点的各向同性二维哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）进行数值研究，证明静态条带是边界伪影，而真实的二维热力学极限表现为拓扑熔化的动态磁畴流体，并揭示了铜氧化物（cuprate）中空穴掺杂与电子掺杂的非对称机制，最终无参数地恢复了倾斜的超导穹顶（superconducting dome），表明稳健的d波超导是纯哈伯德哈密顿量的内禀基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维哈伯德模型的精确基态对于理解铜氧化物超导电性（cuprate superconductivity）至关重要。此前在窄圆柱上的数值研究发现了绝缘的静态条带（static stripes），这本质上抑制了超导，因此需要在大尺寸各向同性晶格上重新检验这些结论。

Method: 采用约束路径辅助场量子蒙特卡洛方法（constrained-path auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo），在各向同性晶格（isotropic lattice）上对最大24×24格点进行数值模拟，提取宏观的非对角长程序（off-diagonal long-range order）来刻画超导序。

Result: 静态条带是边界伪影，真实二维热力学极限是拓扑熔化的动态磁畴流体。空穴掺杂（hole doping）主动熔融磁背景，驱动Lifshitz相变（Lifshitz transition），在最优掺杂x≈0.150–0.200处释放宏观d_{x^2-y^2}相位相干性；电子掺杂（electron doping）则保持刚性反铁磁畴，载流子被限制在狭窄断层线中，最优掺杂提前至x≈0.100。恢复的穹顶曲线与Uemura和Božović标度关系一致，捕捉到欠掺杂出现、不同最优峰、1/8异常抑制和过掺杂塌缩。

Conclusion: 稳健的d波超导电性是纯哈伯德哈密顿量的内禀基态，铜氧化物空穴-电子掺杂不对称性在微观实空间层面得到解释。

Abstract: The exact ground state of the two-dimensional Hubbard model is critical for understanding cuprate superconductivity. Previous numerical studies on narrow cylinders found insulating, static stripes that inherently suppress superconductivity. Here, using constrained-path auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo on isotropic lattices up to $24 \times 24$ sites, we show static stripes are boundary artifacts. The true 2D thermodynamic limit yields a topologically melted fluid of dynamically fluctuating magnetic pockets. Furthermore, we reveal the microscopic real-space origin of cuprate particle-hole asymmetry. Hole doping actively melts the magnetic background, driving a Lifshitz transition that unleashes macroscopic $d_{x^2-y^2}$ phase coherence at an optimal $x \approx 0.150-0.200$. Conversely, electron doping preserves rigid antiferromagnetic domains, confining carriers to narrow fault lines that optimally saturate early at $x \approx 0.100$. By extracting the macroscopic off-diagonal long-range order across both regimes, we perfectly recover the skewed phenomenological superconducting dome. Our parameter-free theoretical curve aligns with empirical Uemura and Božović scaling relations, capturing the underdoped emergence, distinct optimal peaks, the 1/8 anomaly suppression, and overdoped collapse. These results prove that robust d-wave superconductivity is the intrinsic ground state of the pure Hubbard Hamiltonian.

</details>


### [68] [Stability and thermodynamic properties of bound magnetic polarons in ferromagnetic semiconductors: Beyond the Gaussian approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07671)
*Henryk Bednarski*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过超越高斯近似的金兹堡-朗道-威尔逊泛函（Ginzburg-Landau-Wilson functional）方法，扩展了束缚磁极化子（bound magnetic polaron, BMP）理论，消除了传统高斯近似在居里温度（Curie temperature, Tc）附近发散的不稳定性，并成功应用于铁磁半导体GdN，预测了Tc以上持续存在的BMP介导铁磁性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统束缚磁极化子（BMP）理论采用高斯近似描述宿主磁化涨落，这虽适用于稀磁半导体，但在接近居里温度（Tc）的铁磁半导体（如GdN）中，磁化率发散导致非物理解的不稳定性。因此需要超越高斯近似的方法来扩展BMP理论。

Method: 通过严格纳入金兹堡-朗道-威尔逊泛函（Ginzburg-Landau-Wilson functional）的三次和四次涨落项来扩展BMP理论。提出两种Dietl-Spalek框架的一致扩展：(i) 有限自旋关联长度ξ下的非局域处理（λ一阶），(ii) 严格局域极限ξ→0下主导局域涨落的非微扰重求和，化为闭合指数形式。后者通过一个新的极化子金兹堡判据（polaronic Ginzburg criterion）证明非局域性被O(1/N_eff)（N_eff>>1）所压制。理论还包含施主轨道尺寸的变分优化，从而捕获磁自陷效应。

Result: 当应用于GdN（Tc=55 K）时，该模型消除了高斯发散，预测在顺磁相深处存在具有非零自发自旋分裂Δ0的铁磁有序BMP。对于实际交换耦合Jc=400 meV，有效极化子有序温度T*达到155-160 K。模型还表明在金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）附近存在一个最佳施主浓度窗口，该窗口内增强的介电屏蔽能使T*最大化。

Conclusion: 该模型建立了一个在Tc以上持续存在的BMP介导铁磁性的微观机制，为理解远离热力学临界点的铁磁有序行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The formation of bound magnetic polarons (BMPs) is traditionally described using a Gaussian approximation for host magnetization fluctuations. While successful for diluted magnetic semiconductors, this approach fails for ferromagnetic semiconductors like GdN near their Curie temperature Tc, where diverging susceptibility yields unphysical instabilities. We extend the BMP theory beyond the Gaussian approximation by rigorously incorporating cubic and quartic fluctuations of the Ginzburg-Landau-Wilson functional. Two consistent extensions of the Dietl-Spalek framework are presented: (i) a non-local treatment valid for finite spin correlation lengths xi (to first order in lambda) and (ii) a non-perturbative resummation of dominant local fluctuations to a closed exponential form in the strict local limit xi to 0. The latter is justified by a novel polaronic Ginzburg criterion showing that constraint-induced non-localities are suppressed by O(1/N_eff) with N_eff >> 1. Crucially, the theory incorporates variational optimization of the donor orbital size, capturing magnetic self-trapping even above Tc. When applied to GdN (Tc = 55 K), the model eliminates the Gaussian divergence and predicts stable, ferromagnetically ordered BMPs with a non-zero spontaneous spin splitting Delta_0 deep into the paramagnetic phase. For a realistic exchange coupling Jc = 400 meV, the effective polaron ordering temperature reaches T* = 155-160 K. The model further suggests an optimal donor-concentration window near the metal-insulator transition where enhanced dielectric screening maximizes T*. These results establish a microscopic mechanism for persistent BMP-mediated ferromagnetism well above Tc.

</details>


### [69] [Translationally Covariant Modulated Symmetries: Classification and Goldstone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07952)
*Bo-Ting Chen,Zihan Zhou,Biao Lian*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了调制对称性（modulated symmetries）与平移对称哈密顿量的兼容性问题，定义了平移协变调制对称性（TCMS），并对其分类、电荷单元形式以及自发对称性破缺（SSB）后的戈德斯通模式（Goldstone modes）行为给出了完整刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调制对称性（如偶极对称性、指数对称性）是电荷单位具有空间依赖性的全局对称性，但此类对称性与平移对称哈密顿量之间的兼容条件尚不清楚，其自发破缺后的低能激发模式也缺乏统一理解。

Method: 首先给出调制对称性与平移对称哈密顿量兼容的普适条件，定义平移协变调制对称性（translationally covariant modulated symmetry, TCMS）。对于阿贝尔（Abelian）TCMS，利用实若尔当标准形（real Jordan normal form）对一维情形进行完全分类，并推导连续TCMS自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking, SSB）相下的普适戈德斯通作用量（Goldstone action）。

Result: 阿贝尔TCMS的电荷单元仅包含多极（multipole）、指数（exponential）和谐波（harmonic）三种分量。一维TCMS可由实若尔当标准形块完全分类。多极对称性破缺产生高阶无带隙戈德斯通模式，谐波对称性破缺产生有限动量处的无带隙戈德斯通模式，指数对称性破缺不产生无带隙戈德斯通模式，从而修改了传统的戈德斯通定理（Goldstone theorem）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了调制对称性的系统理论框架，揭示了其对戈德斯通定理的修正，为理解具有空间依赖电荷单位的广义对称性及其低能物理提供了统一分类方案。

Abstract: Modulated symmetries are global symmetries with a spatially dependent unit of charge, such as the dipole symmetry and the exponential symmetry. We give the generic condition for a modulated symmetry to be compatible with translationally symmetric Hamiltonians, which we define as a translationally covariant modulated symmetry (TCMS). For Abelian TCMSs, we prove that their units of charge can only contain multipole, exponential and harmonic components. Particularly, we classify all the one-dimensional TCMSs by real Jordan normal form blocks. We further derive the generic Goldstone action for SSB phases of continuous TCMSs, by which we show that a broken multipole symmetry gives higher-order gapless Goldstone modes, a broken harmonic symmetry gives gapless Goldstone modes at finite momenta, and a broken exponential symmetry gives no gapless Goldstone modes, modifying the conventional Goldstone theorem.

</details>


### [70] [Microscopic universal theory of symmetry-enriched topological quantum spin liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08558)
*Yingcheng Li,Liujun Zou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于微观可测量量的二维对称性赋义拓扑量子自旋液体的普适微观理论，建立了晶体等价性原理（crystalline equivalence principle），并在超导量子比特、离子阱和里德伯原子量子处理器上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为对称性赋义拓扑量子自旋液体（symmetry-enriched topological quantum spin liquids, TQSLs）建立一种终极理论，使其所有普适性质都能通过数值和实验可测量的量来描述，从而填补现有理论在微观可测量性方面的空白。

Method: 该理论以包含任意子（anyons）的微观态、控制任意子动力学的算符以及TQSL中的对称性作用为输入，输出一套刻画普适性质的数据集，其底层数学结构是范畴论（category theory）的推广。基于此理论，建立了对称性群$G$下包含晶格与内部对称性的TQSL与仅含内部对称性的TQSL之间的显式双射映射，即晶体等价性原理。

Result: 该理论适用于阿贝尔（Abelian）与非阿贝尔、手征（chiral）与非手征的通用TQSL，支持内部对称性、晶格对称性、幺正（unitary）与反幺正（anti-unitary）对称性、离散与连续对称性，并且允许自旋-轨道耦合、对称性下的投影表示以及任意子的对称性置换。在超导量子比特、离子阱和里德伯原子量子处理器上实现了对称性赋义TQSL，并验证了Lieb-Schultz-Mattis反常匹配条件（Lieb-Schultz-Mattis anomaly matching condition）。

Conclusion: 该理论为对称性赋义TQSL的识别和操控提供了坚实基础，进而为基于这些系统的容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computation）铺平了道路。

Abstract: An ultimate theory of a phase of matter should describe all its universal properties via quantities that are measurable numerically and experimentally. In this work, we present a microscopic universal theory of symmetry-enriched topological quantum spin liquids (TQSLs) in two spatial dimensions, which directly utilizes microscopically measurable quantities to describe the universal properties. This theory applies to generic TQSLs, which can be Abelian or non-Abelian, chiral or non-chiral. The symmetries are also general, which can include both internal and lattice symmetries, unitary and anti-unitary symmetries, and discrete and continuous symmetries. There can be spin-orbit coupling, the microscopic degrees of freedom may transform linearly or projectively under the symmetries, and the symmetries can permute anyons. The input of the theory is some microscopic states with anyons, operators that control the dynamics of anyons, and symmetry actions in the TQSL, and its output is a set of data characterizing the universal properties, whose underlying mathematical structure is a generalization of category theory. Based on this theory, we find an explicit bijective map between the universal data characterizing a TQSL with a symmetry described by a group $G$, where the symmetry actions may include both lattice and internal symmetries, and the corresponding universal data for a TQSL with only an internal symmetry group $G$, and thus establish a precise crystalline equivalence principle. We demonstrate our theory in symmetry-enriched TQSLs realized on quantum processors based on superconducting qubits, trapped ions, and Rydberg atoms, and in each example we verify the Lieb-Schultz-Mattis anomaly matching condition. Our theory provides a solid basis for identifying and manipulating symmetry-enriched TQSLs, which further paves the way for fault-tolerant quantum computation based on these systems.

*T. Takayama,K. Ishii,S. Bette,J. Nuss,Y. Matsumoto,K. Fürsich,M. Minola,D. P. Sari,I. Watanabe,A. Krajewska,R. Dinnebier,B. Keimer,H. Takagi*

Method: 通过实验测量A₂WCl₆（A = Cs, Rb, K）的电子、磁性和结构性质，结合反萤石型（antifluorite-type）结构中W⁴⁺离子构成的面心立方（face-centered cubic）晶格及5d²电子构型在立方环境下的自旋-轨道纠缠J = 2态进行分析。

Conclusion: J = 2态的局域四极分量（quadrupolar component）驱动了微弱的局域结构畸变，但受挫的四极相互作用（frustrated quadrupolar interaction）和化学无序（chemical disorder）抑制了长程四极有序的形成。

Abstract: Heavy transition metal compounds with strong spin-orbit coupling appeared as a platform for $d$-electron multipolar physics. We report the electronic, magnetic, and structural properties of antifluorite-type tungsten chloride A$_2$WCl$_6$ (A = Cs, Rb, and K), comprising a face-centered cubic lattice of W$^{4+}$ ions. The 5$d^2$ configuration of W$^{4+}$ ions in a cubic environment yields a spin-orbit-entangled $J$ = 2 state, which has been discussed to give rise to multipolar ordering such as charge quadrupolar or magnetic octupolar ordering. We found that K$_2$WCl$_6$ undergoes a cubic-to-tetragonal structural transition which lifts the degeneracy of the $J$ = 2 state, leading to a non-magnetic singlet ground state. By contrast, Rb$_2$WCl$_6$ and Cs$_2$WCl$_6$ show no signs of phase transition and remain non-magnetic down to the lowest temperature measured. At low temperatures, signatures of weak structural anomalies were revealed, which may point to the presence of local distortions of the WCl$_6$ octahedra. We argue that the subtle structural distortion arises from the local quadrupolar component of the $J$ = 2 state but the frustrated quadrupolar interaction, together with chemical disorder, inhibits the formation of long-range quadrupolar ordering.

*Soshun Ozaki,Hironobu Yoshida,Hosho Katsura*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用干净SYK模型的可积性（integrability），在GKSL形式下对Liouvillian超算符进行谱分解，得到任意系统尺寸N下的精确本征值和对应的投影超算符（projection superoperators）。

Result: 谱隙（gap）在热力学极限先于耗散极限时不为零，呈现反常弛豫；Liouvillian谱从复本征值到实本征值的相变随耗散强度增大而发生；耗散形状因子在耗散极限下收敛至谱形状因子（spectral form factor）。

Conclusion: 该模型为研究多体量子系统的非平凡开放动力学提供了一个有用平台，并可能与混沌动力学及量子Ruelle-Pollicott共振存在深层联系。

Abstract: We study a disorder-free variant of the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model with dissipation within the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad formalism. By utilizing the integrability of the clean SYK model, we derive an exact solution in a spectrum-resolved form, i.e., the eigenvalues and corresponding projection superoperators of the Liouvillian for arbitrary system size $N$. We determine the scaling of the gap that governs the long-time decay of the two-point correlation functions. Importantly, the gap does not vanish in the dissipationless limit when the thermodynamic limit is taken first, despite the integrability of the model. This phenomenon, known as anomalous relaxation, suggests a possible connection with chaotic dynamics and quantum Ruelle-Pollicott resonances. We also find several spectral features, such as transitions in the Liouvillian spectrum from complex to real eigenvalues with increasing dissipation strength, as well as the convergence of the dissipative form factor to the spectral form factor in the dissipationless limit. These findings indicate that the present model offers a useful platform for exploring nontrivial open dynamics of many-body quantum systems.

### [73] [Inhomogeneous Coulomb Models Without Defects are Sick: Domain Wall Energies Scaling as Volume (not Boundary Area)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08613)
*Garry Goldstein*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，服从散度为零约束的库仑模型（Coulomb models）若不包含缺陷（defects），将导致病态行为：在边界通量不抵消的情形下，不同相之间的锐利畴壁（domain walls）能量与系统尺寸成正比而非边界面积；同时，边界条件即使满足总通量为零，也会对亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）产生广延性（extensive）代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究服从 $\nabla\cdot\langle\mathbf{B}\rangle=0$ 约束的库仑模型（Coulomb models）在边界与畴壁行为上的内在病态问题，揭示不引入缺陷（defects）时模型在热力学与畴壁标度上的物理矛盾。

Method: 通过理论分析，考虑一般边界条件下赝磁场（pseudo-magnetic fields）通量不抵消的情形，结合平方格点六顶点模型（square lattice six vertex model）、量子二聚体模型（quantum dimers）以及磁场中的经典自旋冰（classical spin ice）等多个实例进行论证。

Result: 在边界通量不抵消时，不包含缺陷的库仑模型中锐利畴壁的能量随系统尺寸（而非边界面积）增长；通量抵消条件 $(\langle\mathbf{B}_R\rangle-\langle\mathbf{B}_L\rangle)\cdot\mathbf{n}=0$ 是边界兼容的必要但非充分条件；即便满足总通量为零的边界，仍对亥姆霍兹自由能产生广延性代价。

Conclusion: 库仑模型必须包含缺陷才能克服边界与畴壁的病态标度行为；边界条件在库仑系统中具有重要的热力学后果，即使宏观总通量为零也不能忽略。

Abstract: In this work we show that coulomb models, ones that obey a $\nabla\cdot\left\langle \mathbf{B}\right\rangle =0$ divergence free constraint - for $\left\langle \mathbf{B}\right\rangle $ being some coarse grained variables related to the microscopic degrees of freedom of the lattice system - are sick without the inclusion of defects with $\nabla\cdot\mathbf{B}\neq0$. We show that for generic boundaries (ones where the fluxes of the pseudo-magnetic fields on the boundary do not cancel: $\left(\left\langle \mathbf{B}_{R}\right\rangle -\left\langle \mathbf{B}_{L}\right\rangle \right)\cdot\mathbf{n}\neq0$ - here $\mathbf{n}$ is the unit normal and $\left\langle \mathbf{B}_{R/L}\right\rangle $ are the two ground state pseudo-magnetic fields on either side of the domain wall) without the inclusion of defects, sharp domain walls (on the order of the width of a unit cell) between different phases of the system cost energy proportional to system size (not boundary area). We present several different examples of this phenomena in the square lattice six vertex model, in quantum dimers and in classical spin ice in the presence of magnetic fields. We also show by example that the condition $\left(\left\langle \mathbf{B}_{R}\right\rangle -\left\langle \mathbf{B}_{L}\right\rangle \right)\cdot\mathbf{n}=0$ is a necessary but not sufficient condition for the boundaries to be compatible - that is domain wall energy to scale with domain wall area and not system size. To further present the importance of boundary conditions in Coulomb systems we show that system boundaries, even ones that satisfy $\int_{\partial V}\mathbf{B}\cdot\mathbf{n}=0$, have thermodynamic consequences - that is there is a cost, extensive in system size, to the Helmholtz free energy.
