### [74] [Dynamic scaling and Family-Vicsek universality in the Hubbard model at infinite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09106)
*Cătălin Paşcu Moca,Doru Sticlet,Balázs Dóra*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文利用量子生成函数方法，研究了无穷温度下一维哈伯德模型中电荷、自旋和能量的Family-Vicsek标度行为，发现长时标度行为由可积性控制：自由极限下所有输运均为弹道型；可积相互作用下电荷与自旋进入KPZ标度区而能量保持弹道型；破坏可积性后所有扇区变为扩散型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究一维哈伯德模型在无穷温度下，电荷、自旋和能量涨落的Family-Vicsek标度行为，以及可积性如何控制长时标度动力学。

Method: 采用量子生成函数方法（quantum generating function approach）计算转移守恒量的时间依赖累积量（time-dependent cumulants），并基于Family-Vicsek标度框架分析粗糙度随子系统和时间的依赖关系。

Result: 长时标度行为由可积性控制：自由极限下电荷、自旋和能量均为弹道输运（ballistic transport）；可积相互作用下电荷与自旋交叉至KPZ标度（KPZ scaling regime）区，能量仍为弹道型；加入次近邻密度相互作用破坏可积性后，所有扇区变为扩散型（diffusive）。所有情形均观察到短时微观弹道增长窗口。

Conclusion: Family-Vicsek标度框架能有效提取一维哈伯德模型中的生长、饱和与动力学指数，揭示可积性对涨落标度行为的决定性影响。

Abstract: We study Family-Vicsek scaling of charge, spin, and energy fluctuations in the one-dimensional Hubbard model at infinite temperature. Using a quantum generating function approach, we compute time-dependent cumulants of transferred conserved quantities and analyze how the corresponding roughness depends on subsystem size and time. We start by focusing on a single interface at half the chain and determine the transport exponents. Then we turn to fluctuations of a small finite interval and study the Family-Vicsek universality of fluctuations over an extended timescale. We find that the long-time scaling behavior is controlled by integrability. In the free limit, charge, spin, and energy all display ballistic transport. In the interacting integrable Hubbard chain, charge and spin cross over to a KPZ scaling regime, while the energy sector remains ballistic. Once integrability is broken by a next-nearest-neighbor density interaction, the long-time dynamics becomes diffusive in all sectors. In every case we also observe a short-time microscopic regime with apparently universal ballistic growth before the hydrodynamic scaling window sets in. The Family-Vicsek setup allows us to determine the growth, the saturation as well as the dynamical exponents.

Abstract: Magnetoelectric (ME) phenomena are commonly driven by spin-lattice coupling. Here we demonstrate a different route based on frustrated quantum spin trimers that intrinsically intertwine magnetic moments and electric dipoles. Using molecular design principles, we realize a weakly coupled lattice of equilateral $S=1/2$ spin trimers in the organic radical crystal TNN$\cdot$CH$_3$CN. In this material, correlated electronic fluctuations within each trimer generate electric dipoles, while geometrically frustrated intertrimer interactions organize them into collective ME states. Magnetization, thermodynamic, and dielectric measurements reveal multiple magnetic-field-induced phases, including the $1/3$-magnetization plateau marked by pronounced dielectric anomalies. Effective low-energy theories and numerical simulations show that these phenomena are driven by electronically generated trimer dipoles whose collective order is stabilized by frustration relief of the intertrimer interactions, establishing a direct connection between geometric frustration and emergent magnetoelectricity. Our results identify quantum spin trimers as multifunctional building blocks, providing a bottom-up route for designing correlated ME materials from electronically active quantum spin clusters.

### [76] [Order parameters and ground-state phase diagram of the interacting topological Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with extended-range hoppings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09201)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 相互作用与扩展范围跳跃共同导致了SSH模型中更丰富的相行为，打破了无相互作用情形下的单向跳跃限制。

Abstract: Topological insulators have attracted numerous attentions recent years, where the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model is one of the most studied models. While the interacting version of it has been explored recently, the interplay between interactions and long-range hoppings merit further investigations. In this work, we uncover a rich phase diagram of the interacting SSH model with extended-range hoppings, in which it consists of several topological phases, two novel superconducting-like (SC-like) phases and five distinct charge-density-wave (CDW) phases. We substantiate that the SC-like and two CDW phases are direct consequences of imbalanced interactions and extended-range hoppings. We derive the order parameters (OPs) for each of the phases and verify them in large-system simulations, finding consistency with the entanglement entropy and the fidelity in capturing the phase transitions. In contrast to the non-interacting case where the favored hoppings are unidirectional in the topological phases, the derived OPs suggest non-unidirectional hoppings are possible under the influence of interactions.

</details>


### [77] [Evolution of terahertz third harmonic response across rare-earth nickelate phase-diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09622)
*Gulloo Lal Prajapati,Igor Ilyakov,Alexey Ponomaryov,Atiqa Arshad,Sanjeev Kumar,Jayaprakash Sahoo,Dhanvir Singh Rana,Abdelrahman Azab,Friedemann Queisser,Ralf Schützhold,Jan-Christoph Deinert*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在稀土镍酸盐（rare-earth nickelates）中观测到的太赫兹三次谐波产生（THz third harmonic generation, THG），这是一种负电荷转移绝缘体（negative charge-transfer insulators），并揭示了THG振幅对电子相和磁相强度的高度敏感性，同时发展了一个广义理论以描述强关联材料中的太赫兹高次谐波产生（THz HHG）并提出了增强太赫兹非线性的策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太赫兹高次谐波产生（THz HHG）是探测关联材料中由低能多体相互作用引发的非线性响应的有力手段，然而目前相关研究主要集中在拓扑材料和超导体上，尚未充分探索其他可能成为高效THz HHG源的材料体系。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索稀土镍酸盐这一典型的Mott绝缘体-金属转变材料体系中的THz非线性行为。

Method: 本研究在稀土镍酸盐薄膜中测量了温度依赖的太赫兹三次谐波产生（THG）振幅，并对比了具有尖锐相变和较弱相变的薄膜样品。同时，作者发展了一个广义理论框架，用于描述负电荷转移绝缘体（negative charge-transfer insulators）中的太赫兹谐波产生过程。

Result: 研究发现THG振幅对镍酸盐的电子相和磁相强度高度敏感。在具有尖锐相变的薄膜中，温度依赖的THG振幅的局部最大值和最小值分别对应于绝缘体-金属转变温度和磁转变温度。而在相变较弱的薄膜中，这些特征向低温方向移动，甚至观察到单调的THG增强直至低温。

Conclusion: 本研究将太赫兹高次谐波产生（THz HHG）的研究范围拓展到了强关联材料体系，提供了稀土镍酸盐作为高效THz非线性源的实验和理论依据，并为未来增强太赫兹非线性效应提供了设计策略。

Abstract: High harmonic generation (HHG) is a sensitive probe for investigating electronic structures and dynamics of materials and a source for attosecond pulses. In particular, HHG with terahertz (THz) light can enable probing of nonlinear responses in correlated materials arising from low-energy many-body interactions. However, THz HHG studies have so far largely focused on topological materials and superconductors, leaving out other potential material systems which could also become efficient THz HHG sources. Here, we report THz third harmonic generation (THG) in rare-earth nickelates -- a prototype material for exploring the Mott insulator-metal transition and related technological applications. We find that the THG amplitude is highly sensitive to the strengths of electronic and magnetic phases of nickelates. In films with sharp phase-transitions, the local maximum and minimum in the temperature-dependent THG amplitude coincide with insulator-metal and magnetic transition temperatures, respectively. While in films with weaker transitions, these features shift toward lower temperatures or even monotonous THG enhancement is observed down to low temperatures. We developed a generalized theory for THz harmonic generation in negative charge-transfer insulators and outlined strategies to enhance the THz nonlinearities further. Our study broadens the scope of THz HHG studies and related applications to strongly correlated materials.

### [78] [Uniaxial-Stress-Induced Magnetic Transitions in the Triangular-Lattice Antiferromagnet PdCrO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09628)
*Nina Stilkerich,Tobias Ritschel,Hilary M. L. Noad,Richard Waite,Dmitry Khalyavin,Kousuke Ishida,Pascal Manuel,Fabio Orlandi,Seunghyun Khim,Elena Gati,Andrew P. Mackenzie,Jochen Geck,Clifford W. Hicks*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过单轴应力（uniaxial stress）调控三角晶格反铁磁体（triangular-lattice antiferromagnet）PdCrO₂的磁阻挫效应，发现应力可诱导一级磁相变（first-order magnetic transition），导致晶格常数缩减0.21%、杨氏模量（Young's modulus）增加约80 GPa、泊松比（Poisson ratio）从约1降至约0.4，表明磁有序进入“锁定”状态，且该行为可能与费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单轴应力是一种有望精确调控磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）的方法，而PdCrO₂中Cr-Cr磁相互作用对原子间距高度敏感，使得实验室可实现的应力足以显著改变其磁结构，因此本文旨在通过应力手段探索该材料的磁弹性耦合行为。

Method: 对三角晶格反铁磁体PdCrO₂施加单轴应力，综合采用三种测量手段：X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）、应力-应变关系（stress-strain relationship）以及中子衍射（neutron diffraction）。

Result: 联合数据表明，PdCrO₂的弹性模量（elastic moduli）受应力诱导的磁结构变化强烈影响；观测到一个新的应力诱导的一级磁相变，相变时晶格常数收缩0.21%；晶格明显硬化：杨氏模量增加约80 GPa，泊松比从约1降至约0.4。

Conclusion: 磁有序在相变后进入“锁定”状态，即对晶格应变不再敏感，这可能源于应力诱导的磁有序对Pd层费米面产生嵌套（nesting）效应。其他阻挫磁体（包括候选自旋液体材料）可能同样表现出磁与弹性自由度之间的强耦合。

Abstract: Uniaxial stress is a promising method to tune magnetic frustration, allowing its effects to be studied in a precise way. In this work, uniaxial stress is applied to the triangular-lattice antiferromagnet PdCrO2. The Cr-Cr magnetic interaction is very sensitive to interatomic separation, so laboratory-achievable stress can induce substantial changes in magnetic structure. Results from three types of measurement are presented: X-ray diffraction, the stress-strain relationship, and neutron diffraction. The combined data show that the elastic moduli of PdCrO2 are strongly affected by stress-induced changes in magnetic structure. A new, first-order stress-induced magnetic transition is observed, at which the lattice constant shrinks by 0.21%. The lattice stiffens dramatically across this transition: the Young's modulus increases by about 80 GPa, and the Poisson ratio falls from about 1 to about 0.4. This stiffening indicates that the magnetic order "locks," that is, becomes insensitive to lattice strain. This locking might occur because the new stress-induced magnetic order nests the Fermi surface of the Pd sheets. Other frustrated magnets, including candidate spin liquids, may show similarly strong coupling between magnetic and elastic degrees of freedom.

Method: 采用键算符平均场理论（bond-operator mean-field theory）计算三重子能带结构、动力学结构因子、贝里曲率及热霍尔电导率。

Abstract: We investigate the triplon excitations of the pinwheel valence-bond-solid phase on the deformed kagome lattice compound Rb2Cu3SnF12. We show that the presence of Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions and an external magnetic field are key for endowing triplon bands with nontrivial Chern numbers. We find good qualitative agreement of the low-energy dynamical structure factor with neutron-scattering experiments. An applied magnetic field can isolate the lowest triplon Chern band leading to a tunable thermal Hall conductivity for accessible temperature and field regimes. Our results establish the deformed kagome pinwheel valence-bond solid as a promising platform for topological triplon physics and for observing the associated thermal Hall effect.

Abstract: For dynamical systems in the plane, there can be many periodic attractors coexisting in a bounded region. That is the vague question we start with. For a test study, we chose the Hénon map with a tiny dissipation. We tuned the other parameter to yield a case with 50 attracting periodic orbits. They have a total of 4259 periodic points. We describe how these orbits can be organized into families. In addition to two low-period orbits, the remaining 48 orbits can be classified into three families, which we describe in detail.

### [81] [Data-driven discovery of governing differential equations across physical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09638)
*Siyu Lou,Hao Xu,Wenguan Wang,Lu Lu,Hao Sun,Yang Liu,Linfeng Zhang,Dongxiao Zhang,Yuntian Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种以问题为导向的数据驱动微分方程发现视角，通过二维结构-系数复杂度相图（phase diagram）和表示-评估-优化（REO）框架（representation-evaluation-optimization framework），系统梳理了该领域的方法演进与核心原理，并指出未来的挑战在于利用发现的方程修正现有理论、提炼机制与形成新科学概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微分方程（differential equations）在科学发现中至关重要，但数据驱动的方程发现领域随AI方法兴起而快速扩展，方向多样且缺乏清晰的组织视角。本文旨在提供一个系统性的问题导向框架，以厘清不同方法的适用条件与根本挑战。

Method: 首先构建了一个二维相图，按结构复杂度（structural complexity）和系数复杂度（coefficient complexity）组织方程发现问题；随后提出了REO框架，将发现过程抽象为表示（representation）、评估（evaluation）和优化（optimization）三个核心步骤，从而将讨论从具体算法提升至决定可发现性（discoverability）的基本原理层面。

Result: 相图展示了该领域从发现稀疏方程（sparse equations）与简单系数向更复杂结构及灵活参数化的发展轨迹，并解释了不同方法族在不同问题场景下成败的原因。REO框架则识别出跨算法变化持续存在的核心问题。

Conclusion: 数据驱动微分方程发现的下一挑战不在于单纯的方程恢复，而在于利用这些方程来修正现有理论、提炼机制（distill mechanisms）并形成新的科学概念，从而推动物理学及相关科学领域的理论进步。

Abstract: Differential equations play a critical role in scientific discovery because they provide a mathematical framework to describe the behaviour of physical phenomena. As a promising alternative to traditional first principles, data-driven differential equation discovery has attracted increasing attention for its ability to infer governing laws directly from experimental or simulated data, especially when the underlying physics is unclear. However, the field has expanded rapidly along diverse methodological directions, particularly with the emergence of AI-based approaches, and still lacks a clear organizing perspective. In this Review, we propose a problem-oriented perspective on data-driven differential equation discovery. We first introduce a two-dimensional phase diagram of equation discoverability, where discovery problems are organized according to structural complexity and coefficient complexity. This phase diagram shows how the field has moved from the discovery of sparse equations with simple coefficients toward more complex governing laws with richer structures and more flexible parameterizations. It also clarifies why different methodological families succeed or fail in different problem settings. We then present the representation-evaluation-optimization (REO) framework as a fundamental abstraction of the discovery process. By identifying the core problems of equation discovery that persist across algorithmic variations, REO shifts the discussion from individual algorithms to the fundamental principles that determine discoverability. We connect these perspectives to applications across physics and adjacent sciences, and argue that the next challenge is not merely recovering equations, but using them to revise existing theories, distil mechanisms and form new scientific concepts.

</details>


### [82] [Mesh Graph Neural Network Framework for Accelerating Finite Element Simulation for Arbitrary Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08287)
*Josiah D. Kunz,Kamal Choudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种网格图网络（mesh graph network, MGN），用于预测具有任意孔洞几何形状的二维结构部件的 von Mises 应力场。该模型通过编码节点类型、相对边特征和全局特征实现平移与旋转不变性，从而无需重新训练即可泛化到未见几何形状。在最优情况下，MGN 在未见几何和未见载荷上达到 $R^2 \geq 0.97$，显著优于传统机器学习模型（$R^2 \approx 0.01$–$0.86$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限元分析（finite element analysis, FEA）在结构设计中不可或缺，但在评估多个设计迭代或载荷场景时计算成本高昂。机器学习替代模型大多难以泛化到不同几何形状，这一关键局限亟需解决。

Method: 基于 Pfaff 等人的网格图网络（MGN）框架进行扩展，编码三类特征：节点类型（如固定边界、自由表面、孔洞边缘）、相对边特征（相邻节点之间的距离）和全局特征（施加的载荷）。该架构不使用绝对节点坐标，因而具备平移不变性（translation invariance）和旋转不变性（rotation invariance），可在不重新训练的情况下泛化到未见几何形状。

Result: 在 11 种板几何形状、20 种载荷条件下训练 MGN，在 7 种未见几何形状和 3 种未见载荷上评估。最优情况下 MGN 在未见几何和未见载荷上达到 $R^2 \geq 0.97$，而传统模型（随机森林、梯度提升、K近邻）的 $R^2$ 仅为约 $0.01$–$0.86$。即使在较不理想的情况下，MGN 仍优于传统模型。

Conclusion: 这项工作将 Pfaff 等人的网格仿真框架扩展到结构力学领域，证明图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）可以在不同几何形状下作为有限元分析的高效替代模型。

Abstract: Finite element analysis (FEA) is essential for structural design but remains computationally expensive, particularly when evaluating multiple design iterations or load scenarios. Machine learning surrogate models offer a promising alternative, yet most approaches struggle with a critical limitation: generalizing across varying geometries. This work presents a mesh graph network (MGN) for predicting von Mises stress fields in 2D structural components with arbitrary hole geometries. Unlike traditional machine learning approaches that use absolute node coordinates as features, the proposed model builds on existing MGN frameworks that encode node types (e.g., fixed boundary, free surface, hole edge), relative edge features (distance between neighbors), and global features (applied load). This architecture is inherently translation- and rotation-invariant, enabling generalization to unseen geometries without retraining. The MGN was trained on 11 plate geometries under 20 load conditions and evaluated on 7 unseen geometries and 3 unseen loads. In the most favorable case, the model achieves $R^2 \geq 0.97$ on an unseen geometry and unseen load, compared to $R^2 \approx 0.01$--$0.86$ for conventional models (Random Forest, Gradient Boosting , K-Nearest Neighbors) trained on identical data. However, even in less favorable cases, the MGN model still outperforms conventional models. This work extends the mesh-based simulation framework of Pfaff et al. (arXiv:2010.03409) to structural mechanics, demonstrating that graph neural networks can serve as efficient surrogates for finite element analysis across varying geometries.

</details>


### [83] [When Do Local Score Models Extrapolate Across Size? A Diagnostic Theory and Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09705)
*Wenjie Xi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明，科学生成建模中的尺寸迁移（size transfer）稳定性不取决于架构的局部性（locality），而取决于高斯平滑得分（Gaussian-smoothed score）的准局部性（quasi-locality）。论文提出了有限深度局部流（FDLF）诊断基准，并证明在空间混合（spatial mixing）条件下，平滑得分保持准局部性，从而实现稳定外推。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学生成建模中经常需要将小系统上训练的模型应用于大系统（即尺寸迁移），但现有研究对于何种因素决定了稳定尺寸外推（size extrapolation）的理解尚不充分。

Method: 通过Tweedie公式揭示远距离扰动通过后验协方差（posterior covariance）影响局部得分分量；证明了一个关于反向扩散（reverse diffusion）下局部边缘分布（local marginals）的尺寸一致比较定理；并引入FDLF（有限深度局部流）白盒诊断基准，提供精确的得分、密度和可控的响应范围。

Result: 平移不变架构（translation-invariant architectures）本身不能保证稳定尺寸外推；稳定外推取决于高斯平滑得分的准局部性；在空间混合条件下，平滑得分相对于感受野（receptive field）保持准局部性，支持稳定外推；而当空间混合减弱时，得分局部性快速退化，导致尺寸迁移失败。

Conclusion: 架构局部性并非尺寸迁移稳定性的充分条件，平滑得分的准局部性才是关键机制；FDLF可作为诊断和验证该机制的基准工具。

Abstract: Scientific generative modeling often requires size transfer, where models trained on small systems are evaluated on larger ones. While translation-invariant architectures enable this evaluation, we show that architectural locality alone does not guarantee stable size extrapolation. Instead, stable extrapolation is governed by the quasi-locality of the Gaussian-smoothed score. Through Tweedie's formula, far-away perturbations can influence local score components via posterior covariance, meaning a local model succeeds only if its receptive field covers the smoothed score's response range. We formalize this mechanism, proving a size-uniform comparison theorem for local marginals under reverse diffusion. We also introduce Finite-Depth Local Flow (FDLF), a white-box diagnostic benchmark with exact scores, densities, and controllable response ranges. Empirically, we validate the interplay between spatial mixing, smoothed-score quasi-locality, and model receptive fields. Under spatial mixing, the smoothed score remains quasi-local relative to the receptive field, enabling stable extrapolation. Conversely, when spatial mixing weakens, the score's locality rapidly degrades, causing size transfer to fail.

</details>


### [84] [Learning Dynamics Reveal a Hierarchy of Weight-Induced Layerwise Gram Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09744)
*Claudio Nordio*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究将前馈ReLU网络在固定读出层与二次损失下的梯度下降重写为训练集空间上场量的集体动力学，揭示了残差动力学的核结构及其随网络深度增加的层次化闭合条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多将梯度下降视为权重空间（weight space）中的动力学过程，但较少直接从训练集空间（training-set space）中的场量出发构建闭合的集体动力学方程。本文旨在填补这一视角空白。

Method: 针对单隐层网络，从激活动力学中消去权重变量，得到由输入几何矩阵（input-geometric matrix）与动态共激活矩阵（dynamical co-activation matrix）因式分解的集体核（collective kernel）所主导的残差闭合方程。对于更深网络，保留了逐层的核结构（layer-wise kernel structure），但从三层深度起，闭合需要引入权重诱导的Gram算子（weight-induced Gram operators）层次结构以实现层间信息传输。

Result: 单隐层网络中残差动力学可实现完全闭合，核矩阵分解为输入几何部分与动态共激活部分。对于更深网络，逐层核结构保持清晰；但深度≥3时，必须引入层次化的权重诱导Gram算子才能实现闭合。

Conclusion: 梯度下降在前馈ReLU网络中可以表述为训练集空间上的集体动力学，而不仅仅是权重空间的运动。该视角为理解深度网络的训练动态提供了新的理论框架，尤其揭示了深度增加后核结构闭合所需额外算子。

Abstract: We study feed-forward ReLU networks with fixed readout and quadratic loss. The aim is to rewrite gradient descent not primarily as a dynamics in weight space, but as a collective dynamics closed in terms of fields defined on the training-set space. For a single hidden layer, the weight variables can be eliminated from the activation dynamics, yielding a closed equation for the residuals governed by a collective kernel that factorizes into an input-geometric matrix and a dynamical co-activation matrix. For deeper networks, the residual dynamics retains a clean layer-wise kernel structure. However, from depth three onward, closure requires a hierarchy of weight-induced Gram operators that mediate information transport across layers.

</details>


### [85] [Perturbative Contrastive Physical Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09756)
*Kyungeun Kim,Amanuel Anteneh,Israel Klich,Olivier Pfister,J. M. Schwarz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出扰动对比物理学习（Perturbative Contrastive Physical Learning, PCPL），一个统一的理论框架，通过测量物理系统在不同条件下的响应对比来实现学习，无需外部处理器或显式反向传播（backpropagation），并在弹簧网络和光子电路中验证了分类与模拟乘法任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理系统对扰动的响应是理解其行为的关键；若能对比系统在略微不同条件下的响应差异，便为学习提供了一种机制。现有方法（如平衡传播（Equilibrium Propagation）和频率传播（Frequency Propagation））各自局限于特定系统类型，缺乏统一的理论框架。

Method: PCPL通过对比物理系统在受控变化（输入、边界条件、参数或解释器函数）下产生的可测量状态差异来实现学习。更新规则可反映局部敏感性（local sensitivities）或全局逆问题结构（global inverse-problem structure），但无需集中式梯度计算（centralized gradient computation），有效学习几何（learning geometry）由系统自身的物理响应隐式涌现。

Result: 在两种平台上验证了PCPL：(i) 弹簧网络（spring networks）利用测量位移和力更新键刚度；(ii) 连续变量光子电路（continuous-variable photonic circuits）通过x正交测量和雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）的有限差分估计进行训练。两个平台均成功完成分类任务；光子电路还被训练实现模拟乘法（analog multiplication）。

Conclusion: PCPL统一并扩展了平衡传播与频率传播等先前方法，提供了一种无需外部处理器或显式反向传播的物理学习机制，朝更自主的物理学习系统迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: Responses to perturbations are key to understanding physical systems. The ability to contrast such responses by comparing how a system reacts under slightly different conditions provides a mechanism for learning. Here, we introduce Perturbative Contrastive Physical Learning (PCPL), a general framework in which learning emerges from measurable contrasts between physical states produced by controlled changes to inputs, boundary conditions, parameters, or interpreter functions. PCPL unifies and extends prior approaches: Equilibrium Propagation is rooted in contrasts between free and nudged equilibria in energy-based systems, while Frequency Propagation corresponds to contrasts extracted from sinusoidally driven, frequency-demodulated responses. We show that contrast-driven updates can reflect either local sensitivities or global inverse-problem structure, yet do not require centralized gradient computation. Instead, effective learning geometry emerges implicitly from the system's own physical response, allowing learning behavior to arise without an external processor or explicit backpropagation. We demonstrate PCPL in two platforms: (i) spring networks that update bond stiffness using measured displacements and forces, and (ii) continuous-variable photonic circuits trained via x quadrature measurements and finite-difference estimates of the Jacobian. Both platforms successfully learn classification tasks. We further show that a continuous-variable photonic circuit can be trained to implement analog multiplication, illustrating a step toward more autonomous physical learning systems.

</details>

### [86] [From Simulations to Surveys: Domain Adaptation for Galaxy Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.18590)
*Kaley Brauer,Aditya Prasad Dash,Meet J. Vyas,Ahmed Salim,Stiven Briand Massala*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向星系图像物理属性推断的领域适配（domain adaptation）流程，利用模拟TNG50数据训练，结合基于最优传输（optimal transport）的top-k软匹配损失与多种特征级领域损失，在真实SDSS星系数据上将宏F1分数从约46%提升至约87%，显著缩小模拟域与真实域之间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模光度巡天（photometric survey）将观测数十亿星系，但缺乏快速、可靠的自动化方法推断其形态、恒星质量、恒星形成率等物理属性。模拟数据虽提供真实标签，但由于点扩散函数（PSF）、噪声、背景、选择效应及标签先验等方面的领域偏移（domain shift），模型难以直接迁移到真实巡天数据。

Method: 构建了一个基于TNG50模拟数据训练、在SDSS真实数据上评估的领域适配流程。采用三种骨干网络（CNN、E(2)-steerable CNN、ResNet-18），配合焦点损失（focal loss）和有效样本数类别加权。在特征层面引入由GeomLoss构建的领域损失$L_D$，包括熵化Sinkhorn最优传输（entropic Sinkhorn OT）、能量距离（energy distance）、高斯最大均值差异（Gaussian MMD）等指标，并进一步提出基于最优传输的“top-k软匹配”损失，将$L_D$聚焦于最不匹配的源-目标样本对。

Result: 结合欧氏距离、调度式对齐权重（scheduled alignment weights）和top-k匹配后，目标域准确率（宏F1）从无领域适配时的约46%（约30%）提升至约87%（约62.6%），领域AUC接近0.5，表明潜在空间（latent space）实现了充分混合。

Conclusion: 所提出的领域适配流程能显著缓解模拟域与真实域之间的分布偏移，为大规模星系物理属性自动推断提供了可行方案，尤其适用于缺乏真实标签的海量巡天数据。

Abstract: Large photometric surveys will image billions of galaxies, but we currently lack quick, reliable automated ways to infer their physical properties like morphology, stellar mass, and star formation rates. Simulations provide galaxy images with ground-truth physical labels, but domain shifts in PSF, noise, backgrounds, selection, and label priors degrade transfer to real surveys. We present a preliminary domain adaptation pipeline that trains on simulated TNG50 galaxies and evaluates on real SDSS galaxies with morphology labels (elliptical/spiral/irregular). We train three backbones (CNN, $E(2)$-steerable CNN, ResNet-18) with focal loss and effective-number class weighting, and a feature-level domain loss $L_D$ built from GeomLoss (entropic Sinkhorn OT, energy distance, Gaussian MMD, and related metrics). We show that a combination of these losses with an OT-based "top_$k$ soft matching" loss that focuses $L_D$ on the worst-matched source-target pairs can further enhance domain alignment. With Euclidean distance, scheduled alignment weights, and top-$k$ matching, target accuracy (macro F1) rises from $\sim$46% ($\sim$30%) at no adaptation to $\sim$87% ($\sim$62.6%), with a domain AUC near 0.5, indicating strong latent-space mixing.

</details>

### [87] [Phase Formation and Thermal Stability of Superconducting Platinum Silicide Thin Films on Silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07848)
*Tharanga R. Nanayakkara,Ananya Chattaraj,Mingzhao Liu,Charles T. Black*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了铂硅化物（PtSi）薄膜的物相形成、微观结构和界面质量随退火温度与时间的变化规律，发现相纯PtSi可在600 °C下快速形成并保持稳定，且界面粗糙化源于Pt2Si-to-PtSi转变过程而非高温或长时间退火，从而为硅基超导量子器件的制备确立了稳健的工艺窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用掠入射X射线衍射（grazing-incidence X-ray diffraction）、X射线反射率（X-ray reflectivity）和电输运测量（electrical transport measurements），对不同退火温度与时间的PtSi薄膜进行表征。

Result: 相纯PtSi可在600 °C下经快速热处理（rapid thermal processing）在分钟级时间内形成，且长时间退火后仍保持稳定；300–600 °C区间内30秒退火即可获得等效的薄膜质量与一致的超导性能。X射线反射率表明界面粗糙化是Pt2Si向PtSi转变的固有效应，而非高温或长时间退火导致。

Conclusion: 上述结果确立了PtSi在硅基超导器件制造流程中的稳健工艺窗口（robust processing window），为推进其实际应用提供了工艺依据。

Abstract: Platinum silicide (PtSi) thin films are promising for silicon-based superconducting quantum devices due to their compatibility with CMOS fabrication, air stability, and superconducting transition temperature near 1 K. We report a systematic study of PtSi phase formation, microstructure, and interface quality as a function of annealing temperature and duration, characterizing films using grazing-incidence X-ray diffraction, X-ray reflectivity, and electrical transport measurements. Phase-pure PtSi forms within minutes by rapid thermal processing at 600 °C and is stable under extended annealing, while 30 s anneals across 300-600 °C yield equivalent film quality with consistent microstructure and superconducting properties. X-ray reflectivity reveals that interfacial roughening is an intrinsic consequence of the Pt2Si-to-PtSi conversion step rather than a result of elevated temperature or prolonged annealing. These results establish a robust processing window for PtSi formation in silicon-based superconducting device fabrication flows.

### [88] [Superconductivity in the high-pressure tetragonal phase of UTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07903)
*Yuhang Deng,Gabriel Mee,Tyler Wannamaker,Keke Feng,Mingyu Xu,Weiwei Xie,M. Brian Maple*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过电输运和磁性测量，确定了高压下正交相转变为四方相后UTe2的超导电性：四方相中Tc最高约4 K，上临界场较小（Hc2(0)≈1.2 T），表现出更常规的超导行为；而正交相的超导具有自旋三重态（spin-triplet）配对特征，二者呈现出明显的二分性，且与U二聚体（U-dimer）的存在与否相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定UTe2在高压四方相中超导转变温度Tc随压力P变化的相图，并对比正交相与四方相中超导电性的差异，以揭示不同晶体结构下超导配对机制的转变。

Method: 对UTe2施加最高约16 GPa的压力，进行电输运（electrical transport）和磁性测量（magnetic measurements），系统测量不同压力下的超导转变温度Tc和上临界场Hc2。

Result: 超导电性在约5 GPa处随正交-四方相变出现；四方相中Tc在6 GPa时达到最大值约4 K，随后随压力升高而下降，约18 GPa时消失。四方相的上临界场Hc2(0)约为1.2 T（5.3 GPa），小于泡利顺磁极限（Pauli paramagnetic limit），相干长度ξtetra≈16.5 nm，表现为轨道限制（orbitally limited）行为。正交相则在所有晶向上Hc2均超过泡利顺磁极限；正常态电阻率ρ(T)在200–240 K区间出现拐点（knee），可能标志着与超导共存的磁有序相变。

Conclusion: UTe2的温度-压力相图呈现显著二分性：正交相为狭窄、脆弱的非常规超导区域（自旋三重态配对），而四方相为宽泛、稳健的更常规超导穹顶（conventional superconducting dome）。该二分性与U二聚体在正交相中存在、在四方相中缺失的假设一致，表明U二聚体可能在自旋三重态超导中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: Electrical transport and magnetic measurements have been made on UTe2 under pressure P up to approximately 16 GPa to determine the superconducting transition temperature Tc vs P phase diagram in the high-pressure tetragonal phase. Superconductivity emerges near 5 GPa, coincident with the orthorhombic to tetragonal phase transition; in the tetragonal phase, Tc reaches a maximum value of approximately 4 K at 6 GPa and then decreases with P and appears to vanish near 18 GPa. Tetragonal UTe2 has a relatively small upper critical field Hc2(0) $\approx$ 1.2 T at 5.3 GPa, smaller than the Pauli paramagnetic limit, and is orbitally limited with a coherence length $ξ$tetra $\approx$ 16.5 nm. This small value of Hc2(0) favors more conventional superconductivity; in contrast, the large values of Hc2(T) for orthorhombic UTe2 exceed the Pauli paramagnetic limit in all three crystallographic directions and have been attributed to unconventional superconductivity, widely believed to involve spin-triplet pairing. The temperature-pressure phase diagram of UTe2 shows a striking dichotomy: a narrow, fragile, unconventional superconducting region in the orthorhombic phase vs a broad, robust, and more conventional superconducting dome in the tetragonal phase. This dichotomy is consistent with the proposal that U-dimers, present (absent) in the orthorhombic (tetragonal) phase, may play a role in spin-triplet superconductivity of orthorhombic UTe2. In the tetragonal phase, the normal-state electrical resistivity $ρ$(T) exhibits metallic behavior with a knee between 200 and 240 K that depends weakly on P and most likely marks the onset of a transition to a magnetically ordered phase that coexists with superconductivity.

### [89] [Fragile electron-phonon superconductivity in MnB4 under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07930)
*Renhai Wang,Shiya Chen,Feng Zheng,Zhen Zhang,Xingzhi Wang,Huafeng Dong,Cai-Zhuang Wang,Vladimir Antropov,Kai-Ming Ho,Yang Sun*

TL;DR: 本文通过将结构空间映射到体积和二聚体距离两个关键参数，揭示了MnB4在压力下超导电性的起源来自电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling），并发现二聚体距离的微小变化显著影响电子和声子性质，使计算出的超导转变温度（Tc）与实验一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnB4中压力诱导超导电性（pressure-induced superconductivity）的形成机制尚不明确，研究者希望澄清其物理起源。

Method: 使用体积（volume）和Mn二聚体距离（Mn dimer distance）作为两个关键结构参数，系统映射压缩下的结构空间，并基于电子-声子耦合理论进行计算分析。

Result: Mn二聚体距离的微小变化会显著影响电子性质和声子性质，使得计算得到的超导转变温度（Tc）与实验观测值一致。

Conclusion: MnB4是一个高度响应的体系，为探究结构不稳定性（structural instability）、超导电性（superconductivity）与磁性（magnetism）之间微妙的相互作用提供了一个理想平台。

Abstract: The origin of pressure-induced superconductivity in MnB4 remains unclear. Here we show that it can be explained by electron-phonon coupling once the structural space is mapped using both volume and the Mn dimer distance as key structural parameters under compression. Minor changes in the dimer distance significantly affect electronic and phonon properties, bringing the calculated Tc into agreement with experiment. Our results suggest that MnB4 is a highly responsive system, providing a platform for probing the subtle interplay between structural instability, superconductivity and magnetism.

</details>


### [90] [Microscopic mechanism of high-temperature superconductivity revealed by ab initio studies on hole-doped multilayer cuprates HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_8$ under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08181)
*Ryui Kaneko,Masatoshi Imada*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过神经网络辅助的变分求解器对三层铜酸盐超导体 HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈ (Hg1223) 进行从头算（ab initio）哈密顿量求解，揭示了其高压下高达 160 K 的超导临界温度（critical temperature, Tc）的微观机制：强局域库仑排斥 U 在掺杂载流子驱动下转化为“局域吸引”（emergent local attraction），其本质为“来自减弱排斥的吸引”（attraction from reduced repulsion），与常规 BCS 超导的玻色子胶水（bosonic glue）机制截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hg1223 在常压下保持最高超导临界温度 Tc ~ 134 K 的记录，加压后 Tc 可进一步提升至约 160 K，但其微观机理尚不明确。本文旨在通过第一性原理方法揭示其超高 Tc 的起源及压力依赖关系。

Method: 采用变分求解器（variational solver）结合神经网络（neural network）对 Hg1223 的从头算（ab initio）哈密顿量进行求解，分析压力下电子跃迁 t、局域库仑排斥 U 和离位库仑排斥 V 的变化对 d 波超导序参量（d-wave SC order parameter）及 Tc 的影响。

Result: d 波超导序参量和 Tc 的压力依赖呈现穹顶状（dome-like）结构，与实验定性一致。常压下强超导振幅源于屏蔽不足导致的强局域库仑排斥 U；加压后 Tc 进一步提升归因于电子跃迁 t 增加、U 减小以及更重要的离位库仑排斥 V 大幅降低。研究发现配对机制为从原本的强局域排斥 U 逆直觉产生的局域吸引（emergent local attraction），其本质为“来自减弱排斥的吸引”——掺杂载流子使莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）中“假真空”（false vacuum）特征的双占据涨落释放到无双占据的 d 波超导态。论文还展示了超导与反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）共存。

Conclusion: Hg1223 的超高 Tc 微观机制源于局域排斥在掺杂下转化为局域瞬时吸引（instantaneous attraction），与依赖玻色子胶水（bosonic glue）的常规 BCS 超导不同，且与实验分析支持的电子分数化（electron fractionalization）一致。该机制为利用这种局域吸引设计和优化超导材料提供了新路径。

Abstract: Triple-layer cuprate superconductor $\mathrm{HgBa_2Ca_2Cu_3O_8}$ (Hg1223) keeps the record of the highest superconducting (SC) critical temperature $T_{c}\sim 134$K among all the existing materials at ambient pressure. $T_{c}$ further increases under pressure up to $T_{c}\sim 160$K. However, its microscopic mechanism remains to be elucidated. We solve {\it ab initio} Hamiltonians for Hg1223 using a variational solver supplemented by a neural network. The pressure dependence of the $d$-wave SC order parameter and estimated $T_{c}$ show a dome-like structure in essential agreement with the experimental indications. The origin of the strong SC amplitude at ambient pressure is identified as strong local Coulomb repulsion $U$ attributed to poor screening. Further increase in $T_{c}$ under pressure is understood from interplay of three elements, namely increased electron hopping $t$, decreased $U$ and more importantly, strongly reduced offsite Coulomb repulsion $V$ with increasing pressure. Pairing mechanism is identified as the emergent local attraction counterintuitively generated from the originally strong local repulsion $U$. The emergent attraction is interpreted from ``attraction from reduced repulsion'', originating from the release of the fluctuating doubly-occupied sites characterized from the ``false vacuum'' in the Mott insulator to the double-occupation-free $d$-wave SC states upon carrier doping. This instantaneous attraction is in contrast with the conventional BCS SC mediated by bosonic glues. The local attraction is consistent with the electron fractionalization supported in experimental analyses. The coexistence of the SC and antiferromagnetic order is also demonstrated as a characteristic feature of the multi-layer system. The microscopic understanding of Hg1223 offers a new route explicitly using this emergent attraction to design and optimize SC materials.

</details>


### [91] [Nearly ballistic transport and high magnetic-field sensitivity in a $\text{Bi}_4\text{Br}_4$ topological Josephson weak link](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08333)
*Enamul Haque,Javier Cerrillo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Nb-1D Bi₄Br₄-Nb约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）的超导弱链接（superconducting weak link）器件，用于高效磁传感。通过第一性原理紧束缚哈密顿量和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，发现其安德烈夫束缚态（ABS）谱导致非正弦电流-相位关系（CPR），具有高前向偏斜度和磁场相位灵敏度，表明该平台在片上超导磁传感器中具有应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高透明度的超导弱链接因相位相关的安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound-state, ABS）谱能产生强磁通-信号响应且耗散极小，是设计紧凑磁传感器的理想途径。利用拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）边缘态实现弹道输运，可抗背散射，为开发高效磁传感的弱链接器件提供独特路径。

Method: 基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，构建第一性原理紧束缚哈密顿量（first-principles tight-binding Hamiltonian）和瓦尼尔基（Wannier basis）中的轨道分辨界面耦合，包含自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）。通过密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory, DFPT）计算体相Nb的Eliashberg谱函数（Eliashberg spectral function），得到电子-声子耦合强度1.19和转变温度约9 K。

Result: 体相Nb的Eliashberg谱函数计算表明电子-声子耦合强度为1.19，超导转变温度约9 K，与常规超导电性吻合。亚间隙电导（subgap conductance）主要受安德烈夫过程（Andreev processes）影响。ABS谱导致非正弦电流-相位关系（current-phase relation, CPR），前向偏斜度（forward skewness）为+1.74，并表现出对磁场的相位灵敏度。

Conclusion: Nb-1D Bi₄Br₄-Nb弱链接是可用于片上超导磁传感器（on-chip superconducting magnetic sensor）的有前景的平台，兼容可扩展的纳米加工（scalable nanofabrication）和拓扑-超导混合电子学的进一步发展。

Abstract: Superconducting weak links with high transparency offer an appealing approach for designing compact magnetic-field sensors, as their phase-dependent Andreev bound-state (ABS) spectrum produces a strong flux-to-signal response with minimal dissipation. One way to achieve ballistic transport in the weak link is to use the edge states of topological insulators, since these states resist backscattering and provide a unique path to developing topological insulator-based weak-link devices for highly efficient magnetic-field sensing. Building on this, we propose a weak-link device using superconducting Nb electrodes and a nanoribbon of $\text{Bi}_4\text{Br}_4$ as the normal region, forming a Nb-1D (one-dimensional) $\text{Bi}_4\text{Br}_4$-Nb Josephson junction. We develop first-principles tight-binding Hamiltonians and orbital-resolved interface couplings in the Wannier basis, including spin-orbit coupling, based on density functional theory (DFT) calculations. The Eliashberg spectral function of bulk Nb, obtained via density functional perturbation theory (DFPT), indicates an electron-phonon coupling strength of 1.19 and a transition temperature of about 9 K, aligning well with conventional superconductivity in Nb. The subgap conductance is primarily influenced by Andreev processes. The ABS spectrum leads to a non-sinusoidal current-phase relation (CPR) with high forward skewness ($+$1.74) and phase sensitivity to the magnetic field. Overall, our findings suggest that the Nb-1D $\text{Bi}_4\text{Br}_4$-Nb weak link is a promising platform for on-chip superconducting magnetic sensors, compatible with scalable nanofabrication and broader development of topological-superconductor hybrid electronics.

</details>


### [92] [First-Principles Investigation of Electron--Phonon Coupling and Intrinsic Two-Gap Superconductivity in Hexagonal BAs3 Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08423)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算结合密度泛函微扰理论与完全各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg理论，研究了六方BAs₃单层膜的结构、电子、振动与超导性质，发现其为内禀的各向异性双能隙超导体，超导临界温度T_c=3.4 K，呈现无节点的全能隙超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多能带电子结构的二维超导体为探索降维极限下的各向异性超导与多能隙超导提供了理想平台。该研究旨在通过理论计算揭示六方BAs₃单层膜的超导特性，扩充硼基二维超导体家族。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory, DFPT）与完全各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg理论（fully anisotropic Migdal–Eliashberg theory）进行计算；通过声子计算与从头算分子动力学模拟（ab initio molecular dynamics simulations）验证结构稳定性。

Result: 优化结构具有动力学与热力学稳定性。电子结构显示内禀金属态，多条能带穿越费米面，费米面主要由杂化的B-p与As-p轨道贡献。电声子耦合（electron–phonon coupling）常数λ=0.75，超导临界温度T_c=3.4 K。超导能隙呈现双能隙特征（Δ₁=0.75 meV, Δ₂=0.51 meV, T=1 K），为无节点全能隙超导态。双能隙超导电性源于与不同费米面条带相关的依赖片层配对相互作用。

Conclusion: 单层BAs₃是一种内禀的各向异性双能隙超导体，扩展了硼基二维超导体家族。

Abstract: Two-dimensional superconductors with multiband electronic structures provide an ideal platform for exploring anisotropic and multigap superconductivity in the reduced-dimensionality limit. Here, we investigate the structural, electronic, vibrational, and superconducting properties of a hexagonal BAs$_3$ monolayer using first-principles calculations combined with density functional perturbation theory and fully anisotropic Migdal--Eliashberg theory. The optimized structure is found to be dynamically and thermally stable, as confirmed by phonon calculations and ab initio molecular dynamics simulations. Electronic structure calculations reveal an intrinsic metallic state with multiple bands crossing the Fermi level and several disconnected Fermi-surface sheets derived primarily from hybridized B-$p$ and As-$p$ orbitals. The electron--phonon interaction is dominated by low-frequency As-derived phonon modes, yielding a total electron--phonon coupling constant of $λ=0.75$. Solving the anisotropic Eliashberg equations predicts a superconducting critical temperature of $T_c=3.4$ K. The momentum-resolved superconducting gap exhibits a pronounced two-gap character with gap magnitudes of $Δ_1=0.75$ meV and $Δ_2=0.51$ meV at $T=1$ K. The superconducting gaps remain finite over the entire Fermi surface, demonstrating a fully gapped nodeless superconducting state. Analysis of the momentum-dependent electron--phonon coupling reveals that the two-gap superconductivity originates from sheet-dependent pairing interactions associated with distinct Fermi-surface sheets. Our results establish monolayer BAs$_3$ as an intrinsic anisotropic two-gap superconductor and expand the growing family of boron-based two-dimensional superconductors.

### [93] [Coexistence of High Temperature Superconductivity and Antiferromagnetic Order in a Cuprate with Multiple Hole Fermi Pockets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08643)
*Xiangyu Luo,Yinghao Li,Hao Chen,Yiwen Chen,Jumin Shi,Taimin Miao,Bo Liang,Wenpei Zhu,Neng Cai,Xiaolin Ren,Yingjie Shu,Chaohui Yin,Jiuxiang Zhang,Chengtian Lin,Shenjin Zhang,Zhimin Wang,Fengfeng Zhang,Feng Yang,Qinjun Peng,Zuyan Xu,Guodong Liu,Xintong Li,Hanqing Mao,Tao Xiang,Lin Zhao,X. J. Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用高分辨率激光基空间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（spatially-resolved ARPES）研究七层铜氧化物Bi2267，发现该系统存在多个空穴费米口袋（hole Fermi pockets），并观测到在这些费米口袋上出现了显著的动量、温度和费米面依赖的能隙（energy gaps）。关键发现是：在具有多个费米口袋且存在强反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）的体系中，仍可产生高温超导电性（$T_{\mathrm{c}}\sim$75 K），且在轻掺杂CuO$_2$面（$p\sim$0.05）上观测到高达约42 meV的电子配对能隙。这些结果挑战了关于节点（nodal）和反节点（antinodal）电子态驱动高温超导的传统理解，揭示了超导与反铁磁可在多费米口袋铜氧化物中共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温超导电性与反铁磁序之间的复杂关系，以及电子配对的根本起源，是铜氧化物超导领域尚未解决的关键问题。本研究旨在通过探索具有多费米口袋结构的铜氧化物体系，揭示超导与反铁磁共存的可能性，从而为理解高温超导配对机制提供新的实验依据。

Method: 采用高分辨率激光基空间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（laser-based spatially-resolved ARPES），对七层铜氧化物Bi2267进行电子结构表征，系统分析了费米口袋的能隙特征及其对动量、温度和费米面的依赖关系。

Result: 在Bi2267中识别出由多个空穴费米口袋构成的铜氧化物体系；观测到费米口袋上存在显著的动量、温度和费米面依赖的能隙；在具有强反铁磁序和关联的多费米口袋体系中，发现了临界温度$T_{\mathrm{c}}\sim$75 K的高温超导电性；在轻掺杂CuO$_2$面（$p\sim$0.05）上，沿费米口袋观测到高达约42 meV的电子配对能隙。

Conclusion: 上述发现挑战了关于节点（nodal）和反节点（antinodal）电子态在驱动高温超导中作用的传统认识，表明超导电性与反铁磁性可以在多费米口袋铜氧化物中共存，为深入理解铜氧化物超导体的配对机制提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The intricate relationship between high temperature superconductivity and antiferromagnetic order in cuprates, and the fundamental origin of electron pairing remain open questions. By utilizing high-resolution laser-based spatially-resolved angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we investigate the seven-layer $Bi_{2}Sr_{2}Ca_{6}Cu_{7}O_{18+δ}$ (Bi2267) and identify a cuprate system that consists of multiple hole Fermi pockets. The observed Fermi pockets exhibit pronounced momentum-, temperature- and Fermi surface-dependent energy gaps. Crucially, high temperature superconductivity with a critical temperature ($T_{\mathrm{c}}$) of $\sim$75 K emerges in a system with multiple Fermi pockets and the presence of strong antiferromagnetic order and correlations. In particular, substantial electron pairing is observed along the Fermi pocket with an energy gap up to $\sim$42 meV in lightly-doped CuO$_{2}$ planes ($p\sim$0.05). These findings challenge the conventional understanding of the roles of the nodal and antinodal electronic states in driving high-temperature superconductivity. They show that superconductivity and antiferromagnetism can coexist in a cuprate with multiple Fermi pockets, offering further insights into the pairing mechanism in cuprate superconductors.

</details>


### [94] [Superconducting diode effect in magnetic superconductors realized by nonreciprocal domain-wall dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08999)
*Dong Hui Han,Suk Bum Chung,Se Kwon Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示铁磁超导体（ferromagnetic superconductors）中磁畴壁（magnetic domain walls）的非互易动力学可产生超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect），通过将畴壁的非互易Walker击穿映射到超导相位滑移，并在均匀材料中利用拓扑缺陷实现纳米尺度的非线性非互易超导功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在单一均匀材料中实现超导二极管效应的本征机制，避免传统方法依赖复杂人工异质结（heterostructures）的局限性，并为超导器件的小型化（miniaturization）提供新途径。

Method: 利用铁磁超导体中磁畴壁的电流驱动动力学，分析其在外场下表现出的非互易Walker击穿（nonreciprocal Walker breakdown）——即两个方向依赖的临界电流。当超过临界电流时畴壁持续进动（precession），该旋转在铁磁超导体中引发相位滑移（phase slips）从而打开耗散通道，由此将非互易Walker击穿映射为超导二极管效应。通过解析分析考察磁场和Gilbert阻尼（Gilbert damping）的影响，并用微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）验证；随后纳入超导电性附加效应，扩展分析至铁磁超导体并确定实验条件。

Result: 揭示了磁畴壁的非互易Walker击穿与超导二极管效应之间的定量映射关系；解析获得了该效应对外磁场和Gilbert阻尼的依赖关系，并通过微磁模拟加以验证；确定了在铁磁超导体中实现该超导二极管效应的实验判据。

Conclusion: 磁超导体中的拓扑缺陷（如畴壁）可作为内在的纳米尺度平台，在单一均匀材料中实现非线性非互易超导功能，避免了复杂人工异质结的工程需求，使得超导器件的小型化达到传统约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）难以实现的纳米尺度。

Abstract: A superconducting diode effect is shown to arise in ferromagnetic superconductors through the nonreciprocal dynamics of magnetic domain walls. Specifically, we show that current-driven dynamics of a magnetic domain wall under a certain external field can exhibit a nonreciprocal Walker breakdown, possessing two distinct direction-dependent critical currents beyond which the domain wall precesses continuously. In ferromagnetic superconductors, the constant rotation of a domain wall is shown to give rise to phase slips, opening up dissipation channels, whereby the nonreciprocal Walker breakdown is mapped to the superconducting diode effect. For the nonreciprocal Walker breakdown of a magnetic domain wall, we analytically examine its dependence on the magnetic field and the Gilbert damping and verify the theoretical results with micromagnetic simulations. We then extend the analysis to ferromagnetic superconductors by considering additional effects from the superconductivity and identify criteria for experimental conditions to realize the predicted superconducting diode effect. Our work demonstrates that topological defects, such as domain walls, in magnetic superconductors can serve as an intrinsic nanoscale platform for nonlinear nonreciprocal superconducting functionalities within a single homogeneous material, circumventing the need for complicated engineered heterostructures and thereby enabling the miniaturization of superconducting devices down to the nanometer scale that is challenging to achieve with conventional Josephson junctions.

</details>


### [95] [Proximity-induced orbital antiferromagnetism in Ising superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09797)
*G. A. Bobkov,V. A. Bobkov,T. Karabassov,I. V. Bobkova,A. A. Golubov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文预测了具有Ising自旋–轨道耦合的超导体/反铁磁异质结构中存在一种全新的超导态——近邻诱导的轨道反铁磁性（proximity-induced orbital antiferromagnetism），其序参量具有锁定于磁晶格的周期性相位调制，产生原子尺度的环流，并通过NbSe₂/MnPS₃的first-principles和Bogoliubov–de Gennes计算验证了其稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超导体与反铁磁体异质结构中可能存在的全新超导态，特别是当体系具有Ising自旋–轨道耦合（Ising spin–orbit coupling）时，序参量是否会出现不同于已知超导态（如FFLO态、螺旋态）的新型相位调制行为。

Method: 以NbSe₂/MnPS₃异质结构为具体研究对象，结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）方程计算，分析近邻效应诱导的交换场（exchange field）如何导致超导序参量产生鲁棒的相位调制。

Result: 该超导态的出现要求每个原胞至少包含三个不等价磁子格（nonequivalent magnetic sublattices）以及有限的自旋–轨道耦合。与FFLO态和螺旋态（helical states）不同，该态的相位梯度是原子尺度的，且在整个参数范围内保持唯一稳定；态本身携带电流，并在局域态密度（local density of states, LDOS）中表现为特征性的有限能量凹陷，可通过扫描隧道显微镜（STM）观测。

Conclusion: 预测了一种基于近邻诱导轨道反铁磁性的新型超导态，其原子尺度的相位调制和电流携带特性使其区别于所有已知超导态，为在超导/反铁磁异质结构中探索新奇量子态提供了理论依据，并给出了实验可观测的STM特征信号。

Abstract: We predict a fundamentally new superconducting state in superconductor/antiferromagnet heterostructures with Ising spin--orbit coupling: proximity-induced orbital antiferromagnetism. In this state, the order parameter acquires a periodic phase modulation locked to the magnetic lattice, generating atomic-scale loop currents with opposite orbital moments on neighboring unit cells. Its emergence requires at least three nonequivalent magnetic sublattices per unit cell and finite spin--orbit coupling. Using NbSe$_2$/MnPS$_3$ as a concrete example, we combine first-principles and Bogoliubov--de Gennes calculations to demonstrate that the proximity-induced exchange field leads to robust phase modulation. Unlike FFLO and helical states, the phase gradient is atomic-scale, the state is current-carrying, and it remains uniquely stable over the full parameter range. The state manifests as characteristic finite-energy dips in the local density of states, accessible by STM.

### [96] [Injection-rate effects on failure in a fluid-saturated granular fault gouge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08766)
*Pritom Sarma,Stanislav Parez,Einat Aharonov,Renaud Toussaint*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过解析理论与耦合流体-颗粒（离散元）数值模拟，揭示了流体注入速率控制断层-断层泥破坏的机制：慢速注入使孔隙压力均匀扩散，导致均匀弱化；快速注入产生压力梯度，使远端区域保持强度。该框架将颗粒尺度物理与断层尺度破坏联系起来，为涉及颗粒岩土材料的注入方案设计提供定量指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向地下注入流体的工程操作会激活充填断层泥的断层并诱发地震活动，但注入速率如何控制断层-断层泥的破坏机制尚不明确。

Method: 首先假设一个预应力的充填断层泥断层（pre-stressed gouge-filled fault）受流体注入作用，推导了带有膨胀汇项（dilative sink）的孔隙压力扩散方程；然后通过耦合流体-颗粒（离散元，discrete element）数值模拟对理论进行验证。

Result: 该扩散方程的解析解预测了一个速率依赖性破坏准则（rate-dependent failure criterion），其根源在于断层泥层内的压力不均匀性：慢速注入使压力均匀扩散，促进均匀弱化；快速注入产生强压力梯度，使远端区域保持较强状态。数值模拟证实了该理论，并重现了经典均匀压有效应力理论（uniform-pressure effective-stress theory）无法捕捉的实验观测结果。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了从颗粒尺度物理到断层尺度破坏的联系，为涉及颗粒岩土材料（granular geomaterials）的工程注液方案设计提供了定量指导。

Abstract: Fluid injection into the Earth's subsurface, performed for energy extraction, waste disposal, and resource development, is known to reactivate gouge-filled faults and induce seismicity, a key hazard in modern geotechnical operations. Nevertheless, the role of injection rate in controlling fault-gouge failure remains poorly understood. Here we present both an analytical theory and coupled fluid--granular (discrete element) numerical simulations to explain this rate dependence. Assuming a pre-stressed gouge-filled fault subject to fluid injection, we derive a pore-pressure diffusion equation with a dilative sink. Its solution predicts a rate-dependent failure criterion, arising from pressure heterogeneity within the layer: slow injection allows pressure to diffuse uniformly throughout the layer, promoting uniform weakening, whereas rapid injection produces strong gradients, leaving distal regions stronger. The numerical simulations confirm the theory and reproduce experimental observations not captured by classical, uniform-pressure effective-stress theory. The framework links grain-scale physics to fault-scale failure and provides quantitative guidance for the design of injection protocols in geotechnical operations involving granular geomaterials.

</details>

### [97] [Phase diagram of magnetic $S^3$ Skyrmions on three-dimensional lattices and the toroidal antiSkyrmion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07740)
*Niccolò Francini,Stefano Bolognesi,Sven Bjarke Gudnason,Roberto Menta*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了磁斯格明子（magnetic Skyrmion）的三维推广：由广义Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）稳定的从$\mathbb{R}^3$到$S^3$的sigma模型，发现了一种称为"反禁闭"（anti-confinement）的磁弦分裂现象，并通过蒙特卡罗模拟绘制了有限温度相图，首次报道了单位电荷的环形（反）孤子（toroidal (anti-)soliton）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将已被广泛研究的二维磁斯格明子推广到三维空间，探索由广义DMI稳定的三维拓扑磁结构（three-dimensional topological magnetic textures）及其丰富的相行为。

Method: 利用两个SO(3)不变的广义DMI（α项和β项）构建从$\mathbb{R}^3$到$S^3$的sigma模型；推导出在长波长极限下重现连续理论的立方晶格离散化方案；采用蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟绘制有限温度相图。

Result: 识别出自旋螺旋（spin-spiral）、磁弦晶格（magnetic-string-lattice）、斯格明子晶格（Skyrmion-lattice）和反斯格明子晶格（antiSkyrmion-lattice）等相，以及具有分数$S^3$荷的混合拓扑区；首次发现单位电荷的环形（反）孤子。

Conclusion: 建立了序参量流形为$S^3$的系统中三维拓扑磁结构的理论与计算框架。

Abstract: Magnetic Skyrmions are planar solitons stabilized by the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI) and realized in chiral magnets. We study their natural three-dimensional generalization: a sigma model from $\mathbb{R}^3$ to $S^3$ with a four-component magnetization vector, stabilized by a one-derivative term which is a generalized DMI. We utilize two SO(3)-invariant generalized DMIs discovered recently: an "$α$-term" supporting a spherically symmetric hedgehog Skyrmion and a "$β$-term" supporting an axially symmetric Skyrmion that splits into two half-Skyrmions connected by a magnetic string of negative tension, a phenomenon we call "anti-confinement". We derive a cubic-lattice discretization that reproduces both continuum theories at long wavelengths and use Monte Carlo simulations to map the finite-temperature phase diagram. We identify spin-spiral, magnetic-string-lattice, Skyrmion-lattice, and antiSkyrmion-lattice phases, as well as a mixed-topology regime with fractional $S^3$ charges localized at string bends. We find, for the first time in the literature to the best of our knowledge, a toroidal (anti-)soliton of unit charge. Our results establish a theoretical and computational framework for three-dimensional topological magnetic textures in systems whose order-parameter manifold is $S^3$.

</details>

Here, we show that tailored two-colour light fields break this symmetry and enable selective excitation of individual Weyl nodes. The interference between a circularly-polarised $ω$ field and a phase-locked linearly-polarised $2ω$ field generates a chirality-dependent redistribution of carriers in momentum space, resulting in a nonzero controllable photocurrent. We demonstrate that both the magnitude and sign of the photocurrent can be tuned via the relative phase and field strength of the two colours, and identify an optimal regime in which chiral selectivity is maximised. Our results establish a general route to optically-controlled chiral charge dynamics in Weyl semimetals using polarisation-structured light.

### [100] [Equilibrium spin currents in altermagnet junctions: Josephson-like and anomalous transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07983)
*Abhiram Soori*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用紧束缚晶格模型（tight-binding lattice model）理论研究了二维交错磁体（altermagnet）异质结中的平衡自旋电流（equilibrium spin current），揭示了约瑟夫森类行为、反向平行磁矩导致的反常自旋输运，以及能带填充引起的临界自旋电流量子振荡现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用紧束缚晶格模型，构建二维AM-NM-AM（交错磁体-普通金属-交错磁体）结以及将中心层替换为$p$-波磁体（$p$-wave magnet, PM）的异质结构，通过理论分析研究平衡自旋电流的行为。

Result: 发现$σ_y$极化的平衡自旋电流在AM-NM-AM结中表现出类似约瑟夫森效应（Josephson-like behavior）的特征，受两AM奈尔矢量（Néel vectors）相对角度$θ$调控；在PM中心层体系中观测到反常平衡自旋电流（anomalous ESC），即$θ=0$时仍存在有限无耗散自旋电流；临界自旋电流随能带填充呈现显著涨落，归因于介观量子尺寸效应（mesoscopic quantum size effects）。

Conclusion: 交错磁体异质结有望用于设计无耗散、相位可调的自旋电子学器件（phase-tunable spintronic devices）。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) offer a compelling platform for exploring novel spin-dependent phenomena in materials with zero net macroscopic magnetization. In this work, we theoretically investigate the emergence of equilibrium spin currents (ESCs) in two-dimensional AM heterostructures using a tight-binding lattice model. We first study an AM-normal metal-AM (AM-NM-AM) junction and demonstrate that the $σ_y$-polarized ESC exhibits a characteristic Josephson-like behavior, fundamentally governed by the relative angle ($θ$) between the Néel vectors of the two AMs pointing in $xz$-plane. Crucially, we show that replacing the central normal metal with a $p$-wave magnet (PM) induces an anomalous ESC. Analogous to the anomalous Josephson effect, the breaking of spatial inversion symmetry by the PM allows a finite, dissipationless spin current to flow even when the Néel vectors are perfectly aligned ($θ=0$). We establish that this anomalous transport is driven by an asymmetry in the quantum phases accumulated by right- and left-moving electrons undergoing spin-flip reflections. Finally, we show that the critical ESC exhibits pronounced fluctuations as a function of band filling, which we attribute to mesoscopic quantum size effects, including transverse subband quantization and longitudinal Fabry-Pérot resonances. Our findings highlight the potential of altermagnet junctions for designing dissipationless, phase-tunable spintronic devices.

### [101] [DC conductivity of tilted Dirac Fermions across the Lifshitz Transition: short- versus long-range impurities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08010)
*Mohammad H. Pakzamir,Zahra Faraei,Ali G. Moghaddam*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Kubo形式主义系统研究了二维倾斜狄拉克系统在短程和长程杂质散射下的直流电导率，揭示了从亚临界（Type I）到过临界（Type II）倾斜区间的输运行为，并证明了倾斜参数可作为调控狄拉克材料宏观输运的有效手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解倾斜狄拉克系统中杂质散射对输运性质的影响，特别是跨越不同倾斜区间（subcritical、critical、overcritical）时短程与长程杂质散射的物理差异与机制。

Method: 采用Kubo形式主义（Kubo formalism）进行理论分析，系统研究亚临界（Type I）、临界和过临界（Type II）倾斜区间内的直流电导率（DC conductivity），并引入紫外动量截断（ultraviolet momentum cutoff）以正则化过临界区域的开放费米面（open Fermi surface）。

Result: 短程杂质在亚临界区间产生随倾斜单调递减的频率无关电导率；长程库仑散射则产生由倾斜无关散射率控制的强能量依赖电导率。在Lifshitz转变点（t=1），态密度的van Hove奇点对短程无序产生局域电导率谷，对库仑杂质则产生显著宏观峰。过临界区间，垂直于倾斜方向电导率σ_xx对短程缺陷在t≈√2处出现截断依赖的非单调峰，对长程散射则单调递减；沿倾斜轴电导率σ_yy均无界增长。长程杂质下，电导率能量依赖在Type I和II区间分别近似为二次和线性。顶点修正（vertex corrections）在Lifshitz转变点对两类杂质均严格为零。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一的几何框架（geometric framework），确立了倾斜参数（tilt parameter）可作为工程调控狄拉克材料（Dirac materials）宏观输运的有效手段。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the DC conductivity of two-dimensional tilted Dirac systems subject to short- and long-range impurity scattering. Using the Kubo formalism, we systematically study transport across the subcritical (Type I), critical, and overcritical (Type II) tilt regimes. In the subcritical phase, short-range impurities yield a frequency-independent conductivity that decreases monotonically with tilt. Conversely, long-range Coulomb scattering results in a strongly energy-dependent conductivity governed by a tilt-independent scattering rate. At the Lifshitz transition ($t = 1$), the transport signatures of these impurities diverge fundamentally: the van Hove singularity in the density of states induces a localized conductivity dip for short-range disorder, but a pronounced macroscopic peak for Coulomb impurities. In the overcritical regime, an ultraviolet momentum cutoff is required to regularize the open Fermi surface, leading to distinct behaviors for each impurity type. Notably, the conductivity perpendicular to the tilt direction ($σ_{xx}$) exhibits a cutoff-dependent, non-monotonic peak near $t = \sqrt{2}$ for short-range defects, while it decays monotonically with increasing tilt for long-range scattering. For both potentials, the conductivity along the tilt axis ($σ_{yy}$) increases without bound, revealing extreme transport anisotropy. For long-range impurities, the energy dependence of the conductivity becomes nearly quadratic and linear for Type I and II, respectively. Furthermore, vertex corrections vanish identically at the Lifshitz transition for both impurity types. Finally, we provide a unified geometric framework for these phenomena, establishing the tilt parameter as a powerful knob for engineering macroscopic transport in Dirac materials.

Abstract: Topological states in antiferromagnets (AFMs) offer a promising platform for exploring novel physical phenomena and advancing the applications of AFM spintronics. The AFM topological insulator (TI) state stands out as one of the most representative and prominent cases. Unlike the previously proposed AFM-TI states in noninteracting systems, here we employ an extended Kane-Mele-Hubbard model to demonstrate that electron correlations can give rise to a $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric AFM-TI state. This state breaks both spatial inversion symmetry $\mathcal{P}$ and time-reversal symmetry $\mathcal{T}$, and enables intrinsic topological nonlinear responses to dominate the leading-order dynamics of the system. The competition between electron correlations and spin-orbit coupling drives the system across a topological phase transition, where the closure of the bulk band gap induces singular behaviors in higher-order quantum geometric tensors. Such microscopic singular characteristics manifest macroscopically as pronounced enhancements in thermoelectric performance, charge conductivity, and thermal conductivity. These giant tunable transport signatures, which can be effectively modulated by mechanical strain and electrostatic gating, provide a feasible experimental route to probe and understand correlated topological materials.

These insights enable the construction of a comprehensive quantum Hall phase diagram. Our results demonstrate SCCM's capability in decoding complex quantum phenomena, establishing it as a versatile nanoscale probe for electron correlation and topology.

### [104] [Fidelity susceptibility and geometric response in flux-tuned Dirac systems: exact results from a low-energy two-level reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08280)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究利用Bures度规（保真度灵敏度）作为统计力学响应函数，分析了二维大质量狄拉克费米子在阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆通量插入下的参量灵敏度，导出了基态Bures度规的精确闭式表达式（呈洛伦兹线型），并建立了信息几何与介观狄拉克系统中可测响应函数（如持续电流灵敏度）之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二维大质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermions）在阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（Aharonov-Bohm, AB）通量插入下的参量灵敏度（parametric sensitivity），以Bures度规（Bures metric，又称保真度灵敏度fidelity susceptibility）为统计力学（statistical mechanics）中心响应函数。

Method: 将完整的狄拉克-AB（Dirac-Aharonov-Bohm）算子在整数值通量附近有效投影到一个两能级（two-level）子空间，推导出基态Bures度规的精确闭式表达式；同时引入积分几何灵敏度（integrated geometric susceptibility）χ(m)=π/(8m)，并采用布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）上的基态流形曲率进行几何解释。

Result: 基态Bures度规呈现以整数值通量为中心、质量参数设定宽度的通用洛伦兹线型（Lorentzian profile），峰值按 g^{max}_{λλ}∼m^{-2} 缩放，在手征极限（chiral limit）下发散。该几何响应独立于贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和拓扑不变量（topological invariants），源自普适的局部谱机制。Bures度规可识别为持续电流灵敏度（persistent current susceptibility）中的几何（顺磁）贡献。

Conclusion: 狄拉克质量（Dirac mass）扮演相关耦合（relevant coupling）的角色，控制到手征固定点（chiral fixed point）的距离；逆质量标度χ(m)∼m^{-1}构成信息几何（information geometry）中幂律临界行为（power-law critical behavior）的对应物。信息几何与介观狄拉克系统中的可测响应函数（持续电流、轨道磁化）之间存在直接联系。

Abstract: We study the parametric sensitivity of two-dimensional massive Dirac fermions subject to Aharonov-Bohm flux insertion, using the Bures metric (fidelity susceptibility) as the central statistical-mechanical response function. Near integer values of the reduced flux, the low-energy spectrum undergoes a flux-induced avoided crossing whose structure is controlled by the Dirac mass. Through a controlled low-energy projection of the full Dirac=Aharonov-Bohm operator onto an effective two-level subspace, valid near integer flux, we derive an exact closed-form expression for the ground-state Bures metric, which takes a universal Lorentzian profile centered at integer flux with width set by the mass parameter. The peak value scales as $g^{\max}_{λλ}\sim m^{-2}$, diverging in the chiral limit in direct analogy with the divergence of thermodynamic susceptibilities near critical points. We introduce an integrated geometric susceptibility $χ(m) = π/(8m)$, whose inverse-mass scaling is the information-geometric counterpart of power-law critical behavior, with the Dirac mass playing the role of a relevant coupling controlling the distance from the chiral fixed point. The Lorentzian profile is shown to arise from the curvature of the ground-state manifold on the Bloch sphere, requiring no dynamical input beyond the spectral structure. Importantly, this geometric response is independent of Berry curvature and topological invariants, emerging instead from a universal local spectral mechanism. Through its spectral representation, the Bures metric is identified as the geometric (paramagnetic) contribution to the persistent current susceptibility, encoding the sensitivity of persistent currents and orbital magnetization to flux variations and connecting information geometry to measurable response functions in mesoscopic Dirac systems.

### [105] [Topological bound states in the continuum with controllable multiplicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08510)
*Ya-Ping Lou,Wei Jia*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在广义呼吸型烧绿石晶格（generalized breathing pyrochlore lattice）中实现角局域拓扑连续谱束缚态（corner-localized topological BICs），并证明可通过调控胞间跳跃（inter-cell hoppings）参数任意调节每个角上BICs的数量。通过极化拓扑荷（polarized topological charges）——布里渊区中具有拓扑属性的可实验测量节点——准确表征这些态，并揭示了三种类型的拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管边界局域拓扑BICs已在二维系统中被广泛研究，但在三维体系中实现角局域拓扑BICs仍面临缺乏现实理论模型和有效拓扑表征方案的挑战，特别是如何调控其数量尚未解决。

Method: 提出一类具有一般胞间跳跃的广义呼吸型烧绿石晶格模型，通过调节胞间跳跃参数实现角局域拓扑BICs，并利用极化拓扑荷这一布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中的拓扑节点进行表征。

Result: 每个角上BICs的数量可通过改变胞间跳跃参数任意调节；虽然这些BICs与大量体态（bulk modes）交织，但可通过极化拓扑荷精确表征；揭示三种与体能隙（bulk energy gap）闭合方式相关的拓扑相变。

Conclusion: 本工作推进了角局域拓扑BICs的理论研究，并为其未来实验观测开辟了途径。

Abstract: Bound states in the continuum (BICs) are spatially localized states embedded in the continuous spectrum without hybridizing with extended bulk modes. Recent advances in topological band theory have greatly enriched the understanding of BICs, which gives rise to boundary-localized topological BICs with extremely high robustness against disorders. However, there remains a challenge in realizing corner-localized topological BICs in a three-dimensional system due to the absence of both realistic theoretical models and effective topological characterization schemes. In particular, how to engineer a controllable number of corner-localized topological BIC is still an open question. Here, we propose that the corner-localized topological BICs can emerge in a class of generalized breathing pyrochlore lattice with general inter-cell hoppings. We further show that the number of BICs at each corner can be arbitrarily adjusted by changing the parameters of inter-cell hoppings. Remarkably, although these corner-localized topological BICs are intertwined with a substantial number of bulk modes, we can accurately characterize them through the polarized topological charges, which are nodal points with topological properties in Brillouin zone and are measurable in experiments. We also reveal three types of topological phase transitions of corner-localized BICs, which are associated with the different ways of closing the bulk energy gap and can be intuitively captured by the polarized topological charges. This work not only promotes the theoretical research of corner-localized topological BICs, but also opens an avenue for their experimental observation in the future.

</details>


### [106] [Novel 2D Altermagnetic Vanadium Oxide with a Buckled Lieb Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08637)
*Tamer Taşkıran,Soheil Ershadrad,Biplab Sanyal,Cüneyt Şahin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理计算，识别出处于翘曲Lieb晶格（buckled Lieb lattice）中的单层V₂O晶体是一种有前景的二维交变磁（altermagnetic）材料。该材料具有负泊松比的拉胀行为、面外易磁化轴、1.2 eV的动量依赖自旋劈裂以及~40 (ℏ/e) S·cm⁻¹的本征自旋霍尔电导率，表明其是一个稳健的室温交变磁平台。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理分析，对单层V₂O晶体进行结构优化和稳定性验证；通过形成能、声子结构、室温从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）以及刚度矩阵计算确认其结构和热稳定性。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has recently emerged as a highly promising phase for spintronics, offering the combined advantages of both antiferromagnets and ferromagnets. Here, using a first-principles analysis based on density functional theory (DFT), we identify a monolayer V$_2$O crystal in a buckled Lieb lattice as a promising two-dimensional altermagnetic material. Our calculations indicate an antiferromagnetic ground state with a local magnetic moment of $2.79\,μ_{\mathrm{B}}$ per V atom and a magnetocrystalline anisotropy that favors an out-of-plane easy axis. The electronic structure exhibits a momentum-dependent spin splitting of 1.2 eV, which is a characteristic of altermagnets. Inclusion of spin-orbit coupling breaks the symmetry of the quadratic band crossing near the Fermi level, resulting in a large Berry curvature and significant intrinsic spin Hall conductivity around $40\,(\hbar/e)\,\mathrm{S\,cm^{-1}}$. The results demonstrate that monolayer V$_2$O serves as a robust room-temperature altermagnetic platform, exhibiting magnetic anisotropy and spin-dependent transport responses.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将两点电子松原格林函数（Matsubara Green function）的维格纳变换（Wigner transformation）引入拓扑不变量 $\mathcal{N}_3$ 的表达式，并将该不变量重新表述为 $K^{-1}$ 群（由格林函数生成）与循环上同调群 $HC^3$ 特定元素之间的配对（pairing）。

Result: 研究表明，该拓扑不变量 $\mathcal{N}_3$ 的整数性可以通过局部指标定理证明，但这一结论仅适用于一类有限范围的紧束缚模型。

Conclusion: 论文为二维非均匀紧束缚模型中霍尔电导率的量子化提供了基于非交换几何（noncommutative geometry）的拓扑解释，揭示了格林函数拓扑性质与循环上同调之间的内在联系，并明确了该整数性结论的适用范围限制。

Abstract: We consider a wide class of $2D$ tight - binding models of solid state physics. These models are, in the most general case, non - homogeneous. The topological invariant ${\cal N}_3$ responsible for the quantization of the Hall conductivity, for the specific case of the integer quantum Hall effect in $2D$, is expressed through the Wigner transformation of the two-point electron Matsubara Green function. We express this invariant as a pairing of the element of the $K^{-1}$ group (generated by the Green function) with the specific element of the cyclic cohomology group $HC^3$. According to a set of local index theorems the values of ${\cal N}_3$ can be shown to be integer for a limited class of tight - binding models.

### [108] [Valley Engineering in Bilayer WSe$_2$ Gate-All-Around Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08955)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi,Souren Adhikary,Kazuhito Tsukagoshi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究双层WSe₂中K–Γ谷分裂（Δ_{KΓ} ≈ k_BT）在室温下对栅极全环绕（GAA）场效应晶体管中空穴输运的影响。通过密度泛函理论（DFT）结合自旋–轨道耦合及解析双谷器件模型，揭示了近简并态如何调控开关特性：亚阈值摆幅受量子电容屏蔽保护维持在60 mV/dec附近；有效迁移率由K到Γ的谷占据比决定并随层数单调下降；双轴压缩应变可同时提升导通电流、抑制关断电流并将开关比从≈69提升至≈156，同时保持亚阈值摆幅接近热离子极限。这种导通性能与开关斜率的解耦建立了谷工程（valley engineering）的设计原则：当Δ_{KΓ} ≈ k_BT时灵敏度最大化，而双层WSe₂在室温零应变下天然满足该条件，是谷工程GAA晶体管的最优沟道材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双层WSe₂中，层间耦合使室温下的K–Γ谷分裂（valley splitting）降至Δ_{KΓ} ≈ k_BT，使得两个有效质量显著不同的空穴输运通道处于近热平衡状态。现有迁移率工程（mobility engineering）无法解耦导通性能与开关斜率，因此需要探索能够同时优化导通电流、关断电流和开关比的新机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）结合自旋–轨道耦合（spin–orbit coupling）进行第一性原理计算，并构建解析的双谷器件模型（two-valley device model），对栅极全环绕（gate-all-around, GAA）场效应晶体管中的空穴输运进行量化分析。

Result: (i) 亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold swing）通过量子电容屏蔽（quantum-capacitance screening）维持在约60 mV/dec，且与层数无关；(ii) 有效迁移率（effective mobility）由K谷到Γ谷的占据比决定，随层数增加单调下降；(iii) 在双层结构中，双轴压缩应变（compressive biaxial strain）同时提升导通电流、抑制关断电流，并将开关比（on/off ratio）从约69提升至约156，同时亚阈值摆幅保持在热离子极限附近。

Conclusion: 导通性能与开关斜率的解耦是传统迁移率工程无法实现的。本文建立了谷工程（valley engineering）的具体设计原则：当Δ_{KΓ} ≈ k_BT时，谷工程的灵敏度最大化；双层WSe₂在室温零应变下最自然地满足该条件，因此是谷工程GAA晶体管的最优沟道材料。

Abstract: In bilayer WSe$_2$, interlayer coupling reduces the K--$Γ$ valley splitting to $Δ_{KΓ} \approx k_BT$ at room temperature, placing two hole-transport channels of markedly different effective mass in near-thermal equilibrium. We combine density functional theory (DFT) with spin--orbit coupling and an analytical two-valley device model to quantify how this near-degeneracy governs hole transport in gate-all-around (GAA) field-effect transistors. Three main results are obtained: (i)~the subthreshold swing is protected near $60$~mV~dec$^{-1}$ by quantum-capacitance screening independently of layer number; (ii)~the effective mobility is set by the K-to-$Γ$ valley occupation ratio and decreases monotonically with layer number; and (iii)~in the bilayer, compressive biaxial strain \emph{simultaneously} enhances the on-current, suppresses the off-current, and improves the on/off ratio from ${\approx}69$ to ${\approx}156$, while the subthreshold swing remains near the thermionic limit. This decoupling of on-state performance from switching slope is inaccessible through conventional mobility engineering and establishes a concrete design principle: \emph{valley-engineering sensitivity is maximized when $Δ_{KΓ} \approx k_BT$}, the condition most naturally satisfied by bilayer WSe$_2$ at room temperature and zero strain, making it the optimal channel for valley-engineered GAA transistors.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和半导体布洛赫方程（semiconductor Bloch equations），对单层黑磷烯施加沿armchair（x）、zigzag（y）和out-of-plane（z）方向的单轴及双轴应变，系统分析THG响应。

Conclusion: 应变工程可作为动态调控二维材料非线性光学过程的有效策略，为高性能可重构红外光子器件（reconfigurable infrared photonic devices）的发展奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Based on the tight-binding model and the semiconductor Bloch equations, this work systematically reveals the microscopic mechanism of strain engineering in turning of third-harmonic generation (THG) in monolayer black phosphorene (BP). %
The results show that under strain-free conditions, monolayer BP exhibits significant in-plane anisotropy, and its dominant susceptibility component reaches a maximum of $χ^{(3);xxxx} = 1.8 \times 10^{-17} \, \text{m}^2/\text{V}^2$, agreeing well with the experimental results. %
By applying uniaxial and biaxial strains along the armchair ($x$), zigzag ($y$), and out-of-plane ($z$) directions, we find that the THG response presents strong direction dependence and unique spectral shifting behaviors: in-plane compressive strain and out-of-plane tensile strain both significantly enhance the THG conductivity and induce a redshift, whereas in-plane tensile strain and out-of-plane compression lead to suppression and a blueshift, with the tuning efficiency following the order of $z > y > x$. The microscopic origin of these phenomena is identified as the synergistic modulation of the bandgap and Berry connection by strain. %
Furthermore, the synergistic or competitive effects of biaxial strain further enrich the manipulation of THG signals. %
Strain engineering can serve as an effective strategy for dynamically controlling nonlinear optical processes in two-dimensional materials, and it also lays a theoretical foundation for the development of high-performance reconfigurable infrared photonic devices.

Temperature and displacement field dependence further confirms the correlation-enhanced nature of the hysteresis. ### [111] [Non-Bloch band theory of boundary-controlled magnon edge modes in an antiferromagnetic chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09267)
*Suman Debnath,Sonu Verma,Rohit Mukherjee,Arijit Kundu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在非布洛赫能带理论（Non-Bloch band theory）框架下定义了一个绕数（winding number），成功预测了一维反铁磁自旋链中在传统布洛赫绕数平庸时仍出现的磁振子边缘模（magnon edge modes），并通过边界微扰实现了对这些边缘模的控制，解决了体-边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）的失效问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统布洛赫绕数（Bloch winding number）在该体系中表现为平庸的拓扑不变量，但有限系统中仍然出现边缘局域模，表明常规的体-边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence）被破坏；因此需要发展新的理论框架来解释和预言这一现象。

Method: 在线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）框架下，将磁振子激发（magnon excitations）描述为由非厄米动力学矩阵（non-Hermitian dynamic matrix）支配，尽管原始哈密顿量是厄米的。基于广义布里渊区（generalized Brillouin zone）构建非布洛赫绕数（non-Bloch winding number），重新建立体-边对应关系。

Result: 非布洛赫绕数正确预测了一维反铁磁自旋链中边缘模的存在。通过调节边界势（boundary potential），可以使边缘模进入或离开体态谱（bulk spectrum），实现边界可控的拓扑转变（boundary-controlled topological transitions）。

Conclusion: 边界可控的拓扑转变在实验上可通过局域塞曼场（local Zeeman fields）或修改边缘各向异性（edge anisotropy）在反铁磁范德瓦尔斯纳米结构（antiferromagnetic van der Waals nanostructures）中实现。

Abstract: We define a winding number within the Non-Bloch band theory framework that captures the emergence of magnon edge modes in a one-dimensional antiferromagnetic spin chain, even when the conventional Bloch winding number is trivial. Within linear spin-wave theory, magnon excitations are governed by a non-Hermitian dynamic matrix, despite the underlying Hamiltonian being Hermitian. The symmetry classification of this matrix yields a trivial bulk invariant, however, finite systems exhibit boundary-localized modes, signaling a breakdown of the conventional bulk-boundary correspondence. We further show that these edge modes can be controlled via boundary perturbations. By tuning the boundary potential, the modes can be driven into or out of the bulk spectrum. To resolve the bulk-boundary mismatch, we develop a non-Bloch framework based on a generalized Brillouin zone and a winding number that correctly predicts the presence of edge states. Our results establish boundary-controlled topological transitions that are experimentally accessible through local Zeeman fields or modified edge anisotropy in antiferromagnetic van der Waals nanostructures.

### [112] [Unconventional incommensurate epitaxy of superconducting FeSe films on SrTiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09281)

  <summary>Details</summary>
