Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）在SrTiO₃(001)衬底上生长FeSe/FeTe多层膜，结合X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction, XRD）和扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy, STEM）对界面结构进行表征。

Result: XRD证实FeSe、FeTe与衬底之间具有完美的面内外延对齐；但STEM显示FeSe/SrTiO₃界面处缺乏原子级点阵匹配，FeSe保持自身面内晶格间距，且与SrTiO₃之间存在周期性的横向原子位置偏移，偏移的重复长度与XRD测得的晶格失配度一致。界面未观察到失配位错或其他弛豫特征。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了一种非常规外延生长模式，即晶向对齐与原子级匹配缺失共存，为分层系统中的应变容纳机制提供了新见解，并可能对铁基超导体的界面工程具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We present a combined X-ray diffraction and transmission electron microscopy study of superconducting FeSe/FeTe multilayers grown by molecular beam epitaxy on SrTiO$_3$(001) substrates. While X-ray diffraction confirms perfect in-plane epitaxial alignment between FeSe, FeTe, and the substrate, scanning transmission electron microscopy reveals a surprising lack of atomic registry at the FeSe/SrTiO$_3$ interface. Instead of adapting to the substrate lattice, FeSe retains its own in-plane lattice spacing. A periodic lateral shift between the atomic positions of FeSe and SrTiO$_3$ is observed, with a registry recurrence length that matches the lattice mismatch determined by X-ray diffraction. No misfit dislocations or other relaxation features are detected at the interface. This coexistence of directional alignment and registry-free growth suggests an unconventional regime of epitaxy in which crystallographic orientation is maintained without atomic matching. The findings offer insight into strain accommodation in layered systems and may have implications for interface engineering in Fe-based superconductors.

</details>


### [113] [Planar Hall effect in single and bilayer Rashba systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09506)
*Rahul Biswas,Sunit Das,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了存在Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的单层和双层二维电子气（2DEG）中的平面霍尔效应（planar Hall effect, PHE），识别出两种不同机制：塞曼耦合（Zeeman coupling）通道和能带几何（band geometric）通道。利用半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论（Boltzmann transport theory），计算了两种机制下的平面霍尔电导率，并揭示了不对称Rashba双层体系中平面霍尔效应的微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面霍尔效应是共面电场和磁场产生的各向异性磁输运现象，其微观机制在自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）系统中的起源尚需进一步澄清。

Method: 采用半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论（semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory）对单层和双层二维电子气（2DEG）中Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）系统的平面霍尔效应（PHE）进行理论分析，通过能带结构和对称性分析区分了塞曼耦合（Zeeman coupling）与能带几何（band geometric）两种贡献通道。

Result: 塞曼通道中，面内磁场扭曲Rashba自旋-轨道耦合能带色散产生各向异性载流子速度，导致有限平面霍尔效应（PHE）；在不对称Rashba双层中，层间电子退定域化产生有限平面贝里曲率（planar Berry curvature）和轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment），贡献能带几何通道。主导响应对磁场呈二次依赖且具有π周期角依赖性，塞曼贡献占主导，能带几何通道提供了不对称Rashba双层特有的对称性允许的贡献。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了自旋-轨道耦合二维材料中各向异性磁输运的微观起源，识别出塞曼耦合（Zeeman coupling）和能带几何（band geometric）两种独立的平面霍尔效应（PHE）机制，为理解相关体系中的磁输运行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The planar Hall effect (PHE) is an anisotropic magnetotransport response generated by coplanar electric and magnetic fields. We investigate the PHE in single- and bilayer two-dimensional electron gases (2DEGs) with Rashba spin-orbit coupling and identify two distinct mechanisms: Zeeman coupling and a band geometric channel. In the Zeeman channel, an in-plane magnetic field distorts the Rashba spin-orbit-coupled band dispersion and generates anisotropic carrier velocities, producing a finite PHE. In an asymmetric Rashba bilayer, interlayer electronic delocalization generates finite planar Berry curvature and orbital magnetic moment components, giving rise to a band geometric PHE channel. Using semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory, we calculate the chemical potential and angular dependence of the planar Hall conductivity for both mechanisms. Symmetry analysis shows that the leading response is quadratic in the magnetic field and exhibits the characteristic $π$-periodic angular dependence. For the parameter regime considered here, the Zeeman-induced contribution dominates, while the band geometric channel provides a distinct symmetry-allowed contribution unique to asymmetric Rashba bilayers. Our results reveal microscopic origins of anisotropic magnetotransport in spin-orbit-coupled two-dimensional materials.

</details>


### [114] [Frequency-resolved decoherence spectroscopy of a semiconductor charge qubit coupled to a high-impedance resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09722)
*Ekaterina Al-Tavil,Wonjin Jang,David J. van Woerkom,Ville Maisi,Stefano Bosco,Jan A. Krzywda,Jeroen Danon,Christian Reichl,Werner Wegscheider,Thomas Ihn,Klaus Ensslin,Andreas Wallraff,Pasquale Scarlino*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过将GaAs双量子点电荷量子比特（charge qubit）与高阻抗、频率可调的超导干涉阵列谐振器（SQUID-array resonator）电容耦合，构建了混合电路量子电动力学（circuit quantum electrodynamics, circuit QED）架构，利用频率分辨解耦光谱学（frequency-resolved decoherence spectroscopy）在宽带能量窗口内系统研究了电荷量子比特的退相干机制。研究发现，低频段（≤4.5 GHz）退相干以纯退相位（pure dephasing）为主，高频段则以能量弛豫（energy relaxation）为主；弛豫率随频率呈立方标度（cubic scaling），揭示了压电声子库（piezoelectric phonon bath）耦合的主导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导谐振器与半导体量子点的耦合平台为研究固态量子系统中的光-物质相互作用及退相干机制提供了有力工具。本文旨在利用混合半导体-超导电路，通过频率分辨手段系统探测电荷量子比特在不同频率下的退相干来源。

Method: 构建了由GaAs双量子点电荷量子比特与频率可调的高阻抗SQUID-阵列谐振器构成的混合电路QED架构。通过将量子比特跃迁频率调谐至ω_q/2π~3–6 GHz范围，进行宽带频率分辨解耦光谱学测量，并采用时间分辨测量区分弛豫（relaxation）与纯退相位过程。

Result: 低频段（≤4.5 GHz）量子比特线宽（linewidth）以退相位为主导，高频段则以能量弛豫为主导。弛豫率的频率依赖性呈立方标度，与电荷量子比特通过压电声子库耦合衰变的预期一致，从而获得了频率分辨的声子诱导谱密度（phonon-induced spectral density）。

Conclusion: 混合半导体-超导电路可作为灵敏的光谱工具，用于探测与多种混合量子器件相关的微观退相干机制。

Abstract: Superconducting resonators coupled to semiconductor quantum dots provide a powerful platform to investigate light-matter interaction and decoherence mechanisms in solid-state quantum systems. Here we study a hybrid circuit quantum electrodynamics architecture consisting of a GaAs double-quantum-dot charge qubit capacitively coupled to a high-impedance, frequency-tunable SQUID-array resonator. By tuning the qubit transition frequency over the range $ω_\mathrm{q}/2π\sim 3$-$6$ GHz, we perform frequency-resolved decoherence spectroscopy of the charge qubit across a broad energy window. Time-resolved measurements enable us to disentangle relaxation and pure dephasing processes and to identify distinct decoherence regimes as a function of qubit frequency. We find that at lower frequencies ($\leq 4.5$ GHz) dephasing dominates the qubit linewidth, whereas at higher frequencies energy relaxation becomes the leading contribution. The measured frequency dependence of the relaxation rate exhibits a cubic scaling, consistent with charge-qubit decay dominated by coupling to a piezoelectric phonon bath and providing frequency-resolved access to the corresponding phonon-induced spectral density. Our results show that hybrid semiconductor--superconducting circuits can serve as sensitive spectroscopic tools to probe microscopic decoherence mechanisms relevant for a wide range of hybrid quantum devices.

</details>


### [115] [Radiowave-induced Resistance Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09755)
*E. Bell,C. Hnatovsky,K. W. Baldwin,L. N. Pfeiffer,K. W. West,S. Studenikin,M. A. Zudov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一类新型的由射频辐射（UHF波段）诱导的磁阻振荡，其特性显著区别于已知的微波诱导电阻振荡（MIROs），并且这些振荡可以通过短程无序（short-range disorder）极限下的位移模型（displacement model）来解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的微波诱导电阻振荡（MIROs）已在二维电子气（2D electron gas）中得到广泛研究，但其特征是在回旋共振低频侧（ω_c ≲ ω）出现。本文旨在探索并报道另一类在极高频率比（ω_c ≫ ω）条件下出现的、由射频辐射诱导的磁阻振荡，并揭示其与MIROs的本质区别。

Method: 本文采用实验观测方法，在二维电子气中施加射频（UHF波段）辐射，并在不同的磁场强度B和辐射电场条件下测量磁阻振荡行为。通过改变辐射功率、频率和磁场，系统性地分析振荡的周期、幅度及其对辐射电场的依赖关系。

Result: 实验发现了一类新型射频诱导磁阻振荡，其主要特征包括：(i) 发生在 ω_c ≫ ω 的条件下；(ii) 振荡幅度不依赖于辐射功率；(iii) 振荡周期由辐射电场控制而非辐射频率 ω；(iv) 周期形式可为 1/B 或 1/B^2 周期性，取决于磁场 B 的大小。

Conclusion: 这类新型振荡与已知的MIROs存在本质差异，无法用单光子跃迁机制解释。该现象可以通过短程无序极限下的位移模型得到合理解释，表明该振荡源于辐射电场引起的电子位移效应，而非Landau能级间的光子吸收过程。

Abstract: Microwave-induced resistance oscillations (MIROs) \cite{zudov:2001a} occur when a 2D electron gas is subjected to radiation of frequency $ω= 2 πf$ and varying magnetic field $B$. MIROs are periodic in $1/B$, with the period determined by the radiation frequency $ω$, and their amplitude scales with the radiation power. Stepping from single-photon transitions between Landau levels, MIROs are found on the lower-field side of the cyclotron resonance, $ω_c \lesssim ω$, where $ω_c$ is the cyclotron frequency. Here, we report on experimental observation of another class of magneto resistance oscillations, which are also induced by radiation, but in the radio frequency (UHF band) range. These oscillations are distinct from MIROs in the following aspects: (i) they occur at $ω_c \gg ω$, (ii) their amplitude is independent of radiation power, (iii) their period is controlled by the radiation electric field, rather than by $ω$, and (iv) they can be either $1/B$ or $1/B^2$-periodic, depending on $B$. We further show that these oscillations can be explained by a displacement model in the limit of short-range disorder.

</details>


### [116] [Persistent currents, whirlpools, and local Chern markers in twisted TMD Chern insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09812)
*Francesco Cioni,Lorenzo Cavicchi,Nazzareno Africani,Giacomo Mazza,Fabio Taddei,Amir Yacoby,Marco Polini*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先对这些自发时间反演对称性破缺产生的持久电流（persistent currents）进行定量分析；然后论证体相电流密度幅值的最大值可作为拓扑序的精确跟踪器（accurate tracker）。

Result: 定量描述了莫尔尺度上具有涡旋结构的自旋极化持久电流；证明体相电流密度幅值的最大值能精确反映拓扑有序；给出了有限尺寸效应下霍尔电导量子化的修正规律。

Conclusion: 扭曲过渡金属二硫族化物同质双层中的持久电流可通过扫描探针方法（scanning probe methods）测量；体相电流密度最大值是实验上探测拓扑有序的可靠指标；有限尺寸效应会改变霍尔电导的理想量子化行为。

Abstract: Recent materials advances have made it possible to fabricate twisted transition metal dichalcogenide homobilayers. These systems have been shown to host integer and fractional Chern insulating states. Because of spontaneous time reversal symmetry breaking, their ground state harbors intriguing spin-polarized currents with whirlpools on the moiré length scale that can be measured by scanning probe methods. We first provide a quantitative analysis of these persistent currents and then show that the maximum of the amplitude of the current density in the bulk of the sample is an accurate tracker of topological order. We conclude by calculating how the quantization of the Hall conductance is affected by finite-size effects.

### [117] [The classical boundaries of the EPR argument and quantum ontology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07826)
*Vincenzo Chilla*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于冯·诺伊曼的希尔伯特空间形式体系，提出将量子-经典过渡重新表述为希尔伯特空间经典力学（HCM），以布尔性（Booleanity）的逻辑约束而非动力学极限（ħ→0）来奠定经典性基础。作者通过EPR论证揭示其本身隐含的经典边界，并构建了一种本体论框架，将客观测量现象与非客观观测干涉统一于情境依赖的语境中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典性（classicality）通常被视为量子力学在动力学极限（ħ→0）下的近似结果，但这一做法未能揭示经典性在形式体系内部的逻辑根源。本文旨在通过逻辑约束而非动力学极限来重新理解量子-经典过渡，并澄清玻尔与爱因斯坦之间长期存在的历史歧义。

Method: 作者引入希尔伯特空间经典力学（Hilbert-space classical mechanics, HCM），以布尔性（Booleanity）——即可制备态（preparable states）的相互对易性（mutual commutativity）——作为经典性的判定条件。在此基础上，应用爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森（EPR）判据，结合定域性（locality）与测量独立性（measurement independence），将标准量子力学约化至HCM模型。随后提出一种细化的量子本体论（quantum ontology），区分观察环境与观察对象之间的结构性二分，包含存在者（ontic）、过程性（processional）与殊相存在（tropos-existential）三类范畴。

Result: EPR论证揭示的不是量子力学的不完备性，而是其自身前提中的隐含经典边界。通过提出客观实在性（objective reality）的判据——将描述客观性（descriptive objectivity）仅视为物理实在性的充分条件而非必要条件——量子形式体系能够在情境依赖（context-dependent）的框架内，从本体论层面统一客观测量现象与非客观的观测干涉。

Conclusion: 本文从逻辑约束出发重新定义了量子-经典过渡，为理解经典性提供了不同于传统动力学极限的新视角。该框架有望调和玻尔与爱因斯坦在本体论上的分歧，并为量子力学中的实在性问题提供一种情境依赖的解决方案。

Abstract: Von Neumann's Hilbert-space formalism of quantum mechanics constitutes a logico-physical theory of observed or measured reality. Imposing the logical constraint of Booleanity, essential for objectively shareable descriptions among observers, reveals the physical meaning of classicality inherently embedded within the formalism itself. Starting from this consideration, the present work reformulates the quantum-classical transition via Hilbert-space classical mechanics (HCM), grounding classicality not in the dynamical limit ($\hbar \to 0$), but in the logical constraint of Booleanity (i.e., the mutual commutativity of preparable states). Within this state-centric framework, applying the Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen (EPR) criterion alongside locality and measurement independence reduces standard quantum mechanics to the HCM model. Thus, the EPR argument reveals not quantum incompleteness, but the implicit classical boundaries of its own premises. To resolve this impasse, we articulate a nuanced quantum ontology grounded in a fundamental structural bipartition between the observational environment and the observed object, which accommodates three categorical distinctions: ontic, processional, and tropos-existential. Building on this, we propose a criterion of objective reality wherein descriptive objectivity is treated as merely a sufficient condition for physical reality. This addresses the historical Bohr-Einstein ambiguity, enabling the quantum formalism to ontologically unify objective measured phenomena and non-objective observed interference within a context-dependent framework.

</details>


### [118] [Mathematical crystal chemistry: A formal theory for crystal structure prediction by generalized disjunctive programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07927)
*Ryotaro Koshoji*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 基于广义析取规划（generalized disjunctive programming, GDP）形式化描述无机结构化学，通过连续变量与布尔变量的迭代优化，并引入子图可行性在线学习（on-the-fly learning），实现仅依赖原子半径（atomic radii）和配位数（coordination number）的晶体结构预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无机结构化学天然导向晶体结构预测理论，但现有方法在连续变量与离散拓扑信息耦合时面临可行性剧烈变化的问题，亟需一种能够显式刻画结构组合骨架（combinatorial backbone）并高效搜索最优解的理论框架。

Method: 将晶体结构预测形式化为广义析取规划（GDP），同时使用连续变量与布尔变量（Boolean variables）描述代数方程、析取（disjunctions）和逻辑命题（logic propositions）。通过连续变量与布尔变量的迭代优化，将随机初始结构转化为最优解；在优化过程中实时学习子图（subgraphs）可行性，加速最优解的发现。

Result: 该方法仅需原子的原子半径和可行配位数作为输入，即可通过少量计算设计多种晶体结构。优化过程中从大量生成结构中发现的子图具有清晰的化学含义，对应晶体结构的图描述（graphs）。

Conclusion: 该理论提供了一种高效、低计算成本的晶体结构设计方法，其核心在于通过布尔变量揭示连续优化问题的组合骨架，并利用子图可行性的在线学习加速搜索，为无机晶体结构预测奠定了形式化基础。

Abstract: Inorganic structural chemistry leads naturally to a theory for crystal structure prediction formalized by a generalized disjunctive programming (GDP), which is formulated using continuous and Boolean variables to involve the algebraic equations, disjunctions, and logic propositions. Since the feasibilities of continuous variables change drastically depending on Boolean variables and vice versa, iterative optimization of continuous and Boolean variables efficiently transforms a randomly generated initial structure into an optimal solution. Boolean variables are introduced to elucidate the ``combinatorial backbone'' of the original continuous optimization problem, which corresponds to the graphs describing crystal structures with clear chemical meanings. Since many subgraphs are discovered in numerous graphs generated through structural optimizations, on-the-fly learning of the feasibilities of them accelerates the discovery of the optimal solutions. This theory enables designing a wide variety of crystal structures with small computations based on only the atomic radii and feasible coordination numbers of each atom.

</details>


### [119] [Structure of Clifford groups of composite finite quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08215)
*Miroslav Korbelář,Jiří Tolar*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了配置空间为 $\mathbb{Z}_{n_1}\oplus\cdots\oplus\mathbb{Z}_{n_k}$ 的多部分量子系统的克利福德群（Clifford group），证明了当总维数 $N=n_1\cdots n_k$ 为偶数但不被4整除时，克利福德群及其射影版本均可表示为自然的半直积（semidirect product）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往文献中，克利福德群（Clifford group）在奇数维希尔伯特空间中已被证明是自然的半直积结构，而偶数维情况虽有零散结果，但未涉及半直积结构。本文旨在填补该空白，明确偶数维下克利福德群何时仍具备半直积形式。

Method: 利用关联辛群 $\mathrm{Sp}_{[n_1,\dots,n_k]}$ 生成元之间的关系，对偶数总维数 $N=n_1\cdots n_k$ 的情形进行系统分析，推导克利福德群（Clifford group）及其射影版本（projective Clifford group）是否构成半直积（semidirect product）的充要条件。

Result: 克利福德群（Clifford group）和射影克利福德群（projective Clifford group）在偶数 $N$ 下构成自然的半直积（semidirect product）当且仅当总维数 $N=n_1\cdots n_k$ 不被4整除。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了多部分量子系统中克利福德群的半直积结构条件，将奇数维与偶数维情形统一纳入同一理论框架，并澄清了偶数维下该结构存在的精确数论判定准则。

Abstract: In this paper the Clifford groups of general multipartite quantum systems with configuration space $\mathbb{Z}_{n_1}\oplus\cdots\oplus\mathbb{Z}_{n_k}$, $k\geq 1$ are studied. It is known that the Clifford group is a natural semidirect product provided the dimension $N=n_1\cdots n_k$ of the corresponding Hilbert space is an odd number.
  For even $N$ special results on the Clifford groups are scattered in the mathematical literature, but they do not concern the semidirect product structure. Using the relation of generators of the associated symplectic group $\mathrm{Sp}_{[n_1,\dots,n_k]}$ we prove that for even $N=n_1\cdots n_k$ both Clifford group and the projective Clifford group are natural semidirect products if and only if $N$ is not divisible by four.

</details>


### [120] [A Unified Framework for Virtual Wave Transform: From Generalized Formulation to Excitation-Specific Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08747)
*Pengfei Zhu,Julien Lecompagnon,Philipp Daniel Hirsch,Mathias Ziegler*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的理论框架，通过复频率平面上的解析延拓，将扩散动力学（diffusive dynamics）与波动动力学（wave-like dynamics）之间的映射形式化为一个作用于时间场的谱积分算子（spectral integral operator）。该算子作为一个因果、紧致的弗雷德霍姆算子（Fredholm operator）和非平稳低通滤波器，揭示了扩散过程的内在信息损失及反问题重构的本质病态性。在此框架下，多种激励方案被统一为同一变换在不同子空间上的投影，对应不同的谱采样策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散过程与波动过程在物理上本质不同，尽管已有多种虚拟波场（virtual wave field）方法将热扩散映射为波动方程，但这些方法彼此孤立、缺乏统一的理论基础。本文旨在构建一个普适的算子理论框架，从谱积分算子的角度统一解释扩散-波动映射，并揭示其内在的信息损失机制与反问题的病态性（ill-posedness）。

Method: 通过引入复频率平面（complex frequency plane）上的解析延拓（analytic continuation），建立热扩散与双曲型波动方程所描述虚拟波场之间的显式对应关系，并将该映射形式化定义为一个作用于时间场的谱积分算子。在该算子框架下，分析其因果性、紧致性和非平稳低通滤波特性，并展示脉冲、锁相、啁啾和编码等多种激励方案如何作为该变换在不同子空间上的投影而涌现。

Result: 所构造的映射算子被证明是因果、紧致的弗雷德霍姆算子，充当非平稳低通滤波器，因此扩散过程本质上是信息损失的，逆重建（inverse reconstruction）是病态的。脉冲、锁相（lock-in）、啁啾（chirped）和编码（coded）等常见激励方案被统一为单一变换在不同子空间上的投影，对应不同的谱结构采样策略。该框架进一步推广至矩阵值系统，并暗示了一种跨扩散与传播过程的谱几何（spectral-geometric）时间演化解释。

Conclusion: 本文统一了此前分散的虚拟波场公式，为激励设计提供了基于算子采样与信息编码的系统性解释。该框架不仅适用于标量扩散场，还可推广至矩阵值系统，并为理解扩散与传播过程中的时间演化提供了一种谱几何视角。

Abstract: We present a unified theoretical framework for the mapping between diffusive and wave-like dynamics, formulated as a spectral integral operator acting on temporal fields. By introducing an analytic continuation in the complex frequency plane, we establish an explicit correspondence between thermal diffusion and a virtual wave field governed by a hyperbolic equation. This mapping is shown to define a causal, compact Fredholm operator that acts as a nonstationary low-pass filter, thereby revealing the intrinsic information loss of diffusive processes and the fundamental ill-posedness of the inverse reconstruction. Within this operator framework, we demonstrate that commonly used excitation schemes-including pulse, lock-in, chirped, and coded excitations-emerge as distinct projections onto subspaces of a single underlying transformation, corresponding to different sampling strategies of its spectral structure. This unifies previously disparate virtual wave formulations and provides a systematic interpretation of excitation design in terms of operator sampling and information encoding. The framework further generalizes to matrix-valued systems and suggests a spectral-geometric interpretation of temporal evolution across diffusive and propagative regimes.

Conclusion: 有限几何构型的几何嵌入特性直接决定了量子系统的谱行为，从局域化到 Bloch 波传播再到零能平带；这些离散紧束缚模型与粒子物理标准模型之间存在精确的形式同构，为理解高能物理中的对称性结构提供了几何视角。

Abstract: We investigate the spectral properties of tight-binding quantum Hamiltonians defined on the bipartite Levi graphs of finite geometric configurations. In Part I, we analyze the $10_3$ Desargues and Kantor configurations, demonstrating how deterministic spatial deformations induced by real planar embeddings ($\mathbb{R}\mathbb{P}^2$) destroy translational symmetry, leading to structural wave localization. We show how embedding in the complex projective plane ($\mathbb{C}\mathbb{P}^2$) restores Bloch wave propagation via synthetic gauge phases. In Part II, we evaluate the Schläfli double six ($12_5, 30_2$) and the Cremona-Richmond ($15_3$) configurations in $\mathbb{R}^3$. We analytically derive their exact spectral decompositions, confirming the existence of macroscopic zero-energy flat bands ($E=0$) driven entirely by geometric frustration. In Part III, we establish a formal structural isomorphism between these discrete tight-binding networks and the flavor symmetry sector of the Standard Model. We map the Schläfli graph to the $SU(6)$ flavor multiplets, where the flat band corresponds to the kinematic freezing of ultra-heavy baryons. Finally, we discuss the complementary Cremona-Richmond $15_3$ topology, demonstrating how its distinct geometric nature (based on tritangent planes rather than point intersections) provides a purely algebraic, topological completion to the $W(E_6)$ symmetry of the 27 lines.

*Yury Grabovsky,Lev Truskinovsky*

TL;DR: 本篇论文将Emmy Noether的经典变分方法推广到含有激波（shocks）的奇异极值，推导出广义积分关系，并应用于弹性动力学（elastodynamics）的激波极值问题，获得涉及动能与弹性能的新关系；对于满足热力学容许性的熵解，Noether的经典等式转化为不等式；并发现即便存在激波，动能仍可从动态储存弹性能的表达式中完全消去。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Emmy Noether的经典方法并加以调整，针对奇异极值推导出广义化的积分关系，再应用于含激波的弹性动力学极值，获得涉及动能与弹性能的新积分关系。

Conclusion: 通过将Noether方法推广到含激波的奇异极值，论文建立了新的积分关系并揭示了动能可在动态储存弹性能表达式中被消去的非平凡结论，为理解激波下的能量结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: As it is well known, solutions of equations of nonlinear elastodynamics, representing extremals of the action functional, can form shocks. We adapt the classical approach of Emmy Noether to such singular extremals and derive the appropriately generalized integral relations within Calculus of Variations. We apply them to elastodynamical extremals with shocks, obtaining new integral relations involving kinetic and elastic energies. For the extremals representing thermodynamically admissible (entropy) solutions of the corresponding hyperbolic Euler-Lagrange equations, the classical equalities, characterizing the variational approach of Noether, expectedly transform into ineqalities. We show that, rather remarkably, despite the crucial role of material velocity in the fully inertial energy redistribution processes, the corresponding kinetic energy can be completely eliminated from the expression for the dynamically stored elastic energy, even in the presence of shocks.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典线性弹性力学中的克拉贝龙定理提供了用边界力做功显式表达平衡构型中存储能量的方法。将该定理推广到非线性弹性力学的框架下，需要更一般的数学工具与变分对称性概念。

Method: 在变分法框架下，定义了比经典变分对称性（classical variational symmetries）更广义的“部分变分对称性”（partial variational symmetries），例如标度不变性（scale invariance）或标度齐次性（scaling homogeneity）。利用诺特分析，将这些对称性转化为新的积分关系，从而导出克拉贝龙定理的非线性类比。

Result: 推导出若干新的积分关系，这些关系是经典克拉贝龙定理的非线性类比，能够将物理力（physical forces）与构型力（configurational forces）的功自然地结合在一起。通过非线性弹性力学中的若干示例，验证了所获一般结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 部分变分对称性为非线性弹性力学中能量-做功关系提供了统一的理论框架；所导出的非线性克拉贝龙型积分关系具有广泛的适用性与有效性。

Abstract: Clapeyron's Theorem of classical linear elasticity provides a way to explicitly express the energy stored in an equilibrium configuration in terms of the work of the forces applied on the boundary. We derive several new integral relations which can be viewed as nonlinear analogs of this classical result, reinterpreting them as rather general statements within Calculus of Variations. These relations reflect specific properties of Lagrangians, that we call ``partial variational symmetries'', since they are more general than classical variational symmetries. In the framework of nonlinear elasticity, partial variational symmetries, such as scale invariance, or scaling homogeneity, lead, via Noether's analysis to different nonlinear generalizations of Clapeyron's Theorem that combine naturally the work of physical and configurational forces. We present a series of illuminating examples showing the effectiveness of the obtained general results in different problems of nonlinear elasticity.

### [125] [On an $n-$Dimensional Travel Time Tomography Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09020)
*Michael V. Klibanov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次针对具有形式确定不完全输入数据的n维（n≥2）走时层析成像问题（TTTP），在半离散情形下证明了Lipschitz稳定性估计与唯一性定理，关键工具是新的Carleman估计及Carleman加权空间的引入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑半离散情形，即由程函方程（eikonal equation）生成的偏微分方程对n-1个变量进行有限差分处理。假设半离散PDE的解可表示为关于点源位置的特定正交函数基的截断傅里叶型级数。在上述条件下，利用一种新的Carleman估计（Carleman estimate）并引入Carleman加权空间（Carleman Weighted Spaces）来证明稳定性与唯一性。

Result: 证明了Lipschitz稳定性估计（Lipschitz stability estimate），该估计直接蕴含唯一性（uniqueness）结论。

Conclusion: 本文是首篇系统处理n维TTTP稳定性与唯一性理论问题的文献。新建立的Carleman估计及其加权空间为此类反问题的理论分析提供了有效工具，填补了该领域长期存在的理论空白。

Abstract: In their seminal works Herglotz (1905) and Wiechert and Zoeppritz (1907) have solved the so-called Travel Time Tomography Problem (TTTP) in the 1-D case. However, the question about stability estimates and uniqueness theorems for an n-D n>= 2 TTTP with formally determined incomplete input data still mostly stands open after more than one hundred years period. \textquotedblleft Formally determined input data" means that the number p of free variables in the input data equals the number $n$ of free variables in the unknown right hand side of the governing nonliniear eikonal PDE, p=n. Some previous publications demonstrate that it is possible to develop well performed numerical methods for the TTTP with formally determined input data, which indicates the importance of such data for practical applications.
  This is the first publication in which the above question is addressed. More precisely, we consider a semi-discrete case, in which a PDE generated by the eikonal equation is written in finite differences with respect to n-1 variables. In addition, it is assumed that the solution of that semi-discrete PDE is represented via a truncated Fourier-like series with respect to a special orthonormal basis of functions, which depend only on the position of the point source. Under these conditions, Lipschitz stability estimate is proven, and this estimate implies uniqueness. An important tool of this paper is a new Carleman estimate. Carleman Weighted Spaces are introduced. Carleman estimates were not applied previously to address questions about stability estimates and uniqueness theorems for the TTTP.

### [127] [Engineering classical waves with quantized energy spectra in periodic media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09695)

TL;DR: 本文证明，通过适当设计的线性周期介质（periodic media），可以在不引入非线性约束或随机背景场等额外要素的情况下，复现量子力学中能量量子化（energy quantization）的核心特征。其关键在于构建波传播被强烈抑制、仅允许离散窄通带（narrow pass bands）存在的周期结构，使得驻波解展现出离散的能量与频率谱。该机制具有普适性，可在力学、电学或电磁波系统中实现，为设计控制离散波态的超材料（metamaterials）提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典线性波动方程通常被认为无法在不引入非线性约束、共振粒子-波耦合或随机背景场等额外机制的情况下，复现量子系统中的量子化（quantization）现象。本文旨在探索是否可以通过适当设计的线性波介质，在保持动力学线性不变的前提下，重现量子力学中能量量子化的基本特征。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于周期性介质（periodic media）的工程化方案，核心在于构建波传播被强烈抑制、仅存在离散窄通带（narrow pass bands）的波导结构。在这种结构中，驻波解（stationary wave solutions）在保持系统动力学完全线性的条件下，自然地展现出离散的能量和频率谱。

Result: 研究表明，在适当设计的线性周期介质中，驻波解能够产生与量子力学中类似的离散能量谱（discrete energy spectra）和频率谱（frequency spectra），尽管其底层动力学仍然是线性的。该机制具有普适性，可在力学、电学和电磁波等多种物理系统中实现。

Conclusion: 这项工作为设计能够控制离散波态的超材料（metamaterials）开辟了新途径，同时强化了经典波动物理与量子波动物理之间的概念桥梁（conceptual bridge）。

Abstract: Field quantization is a central feature of modern physics, that underpins the concept of photons and forms the foundation of quantum electrodynamics as well as much of solid-state theory. Classical linear wave equations are not generally expected to reproduce the quantization arising in quantum systems without introducing additional ingredients such as ad hoc nonlinear constraints, resonant particle-wave couplings or stochastic background fields. Here, we show that appropriately engineered linear wave media can recover fundamental features evocative of energy quantization in quantum mechanics. The key is to tailor periodic media in which wave propagation is strongly suppressed, except over a discrete set of narrow pass bands. In this regime, stationary wave solutions exhibit discrete energy and frequency spectra analogous to those arising in quantum mechanics despite the underlying dynamics remaining linear. Owing to the universality of the proposed mechanism, these effects may be realized experimentally using mechanical, electrical, or electromagnetic waves in appropriately designed periodic media. This work opens new avenues for designing metamaterials that enable control over discrete wave states while strengthening the conceptual bridge between classical and quantum wave physics.

</details>

# hep-lat [[Back]](#toc)

### [128] [Certified spectral functions from lattice Monte Carlo data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09791)
*Sophie Mutzel,Antoine Tilloy*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于半定规划（semidefinite programming）层次松弛的框架，在格点量子场论（lattice quantum field theory）中从蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）数据中严格约束谱密度（spectral density）的线性泛函，避免了传统启发式方法对误差的失控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格点量子场论中，蒙特卡罗方法能计算欧几里得关联函数（Euclidean correlation functions）并给出可靠的误差棒，但从中恢复谱密度这一反问题（inverse problem）通常是病态的（ill-posed）。现有方法依赖启发式（heuristics）手段，无法严格控制误差。

Method: 将问题转化为寻找谱密度线性泛函的上下界——在给定蒙特卡罗数据与格点作用量反射正性（reflection positivity）约束下的凸但无限维优化问题。通过求解其对偶问题的有限维半定规划层次松弛（hierarchical relaxation）来严格近似原问题，并使用标准求解器求解。

Result: 该松弛方法即使未达到紧致（tight）状态，给出的界也是严格的；且收敛快速，误差最终完全由蒙特卡罗统计误差主导。此外，该方法能通过不可行性证书（infeasibility certificate）识别不可靠的蒙特卡罗数据（例如低估的误差棒）。在二维格点φ⁴理论上的数值实验验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架为从蒙特色卡罗数据中提取谱信息提供了一种严格、可求解且具有强收敛保证的新途径，兼具理论严谨性和实际可行性。

Abstract: The Monte Carlo method, applied to lattice quantum field theory, gives access to Euclidean correlation functions with well-understood error bars. Recovering the observables one cares about, such as the spectral density, requires solving an ill-posed inverse problem, usually tackled with heuristics that lose rigorous control of the error. Instead of trying to find the ``best'' spectral density $ρ(ω)$, we ask how small or large linear functionals $\int_{\mathbb{R}^+} G(ω) ρ(ω) \mathrm{d} ω$ of it can be, given the Monte Carlo data and the reflection positivity of the lattice action. This is a convex but infinite-dimensional problem. We show how its dual can be rigorously relaxed into a hierarchy of finite semidefinite programs, solvable with standard solvers and enjoying strong convergence guarantees. The resulting bounds are rigorous even when the relaxation is not tight, and converge quickly to the regime where the error is entirely dominated by Monte Carlo statistics. The method also flags implausible Monte Carlo data, for instance underestimated error bars, through an infeasibility certificate. We demonstrate it on lattice $φ^4$ theory in two dimensions.

</details>

### [129] [Protein Dynamics Beyond Structure Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08647)
*Juliette Griffié,Sviatlana Shashkova,Antonio Ciarlo,Sreekanth K. Manikandan,Claes Andréasson,Malin Bäckström,Tristan Bereau,Hjalmar Brismar,Carlos Bustamante,Marta Carroni,Roberto Covino,Andreas Dahlin,Sebastian Deindl,Lucie Delemotte,Arne Elofsson,John Eriksson,Giovanna Fragneto,Anders Gunnarsson,Per Hammarström,Caroline Ingre,Christian Kaiser,Petronella Kettunen,Mark C. M.,Tijms,Gunnar von Heijne,Björn Wallner,Vitali Zhaunerchyk,Simon Olsson,Joana B. Pereira,Julia Fernandez-Rodriguez,Fredrik Westerlund,Giovanni Volpe*

TL;DR: 本文回顾了蛋白质折叠领域的现状，指出现有深度学习如AlphaFold虽能预测静态三维结构，但蛋白质折叠的动态构象变化与高阶组装机制仍未被定量理解。文章提出通过单分子实验、多尺度建模和数据驱动方法整合异构数据，构建蛋白质折叠动力学、构象动力学与大分子自组装的定量预测科学，以实现对健康和疾病中折叠与错误折叠的理性调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AlphaFold等深度学习技术能够从氨基酸序列预测蛋白质三维结构，但蛋白质序列如何引发动态构象变化（conformational changes）和高阶组装（higher-order assemblies）的定量理解仍未解决。折叠与构象状态是动态的、随机的过程，受序列、能量、共翻译约束、分子伴侣（chaperone machineries）及细胞环境理化条件共同影响。现有研究亟需超越静态结构终点，建立对活体中折叠动力学的机制性理解。

Method: 本文采用路线图（Roadmap）综述形式，整合了单分子技术（single-molecule techniques）、计算创新与数据驱动方法，通过高分辨率测量与多尺度建模（multiscale modeling）的融合，实现对折叠轨迹与中间态的时间分辨观测，并整合跨尺度的异构数据。

Result: 本文识别了当前蛋白质折叠领域的实验与理论空白，并讨论了将高分辨率测量与多尺度建模整合的新兴策略。文中勾勒了一条通向蛋白质折叠动力学、构象动力学（conformational kinetics）及大分子自组装（macromolecular self-assembly）定量预测科学的路线图。

Conclusion: 实现上述愿景将变革对分子自组织动力学的理解——从单个多肽链折叠到动态大分子复合物（macromolecular complexes）的涌现，进而实现对健康和疾病中折叠与错误折叠的理性控制，将蛋白质工程原则从静态结构设计拓展至新领域，并为蛋白质稳态相关疾病（proteostasis-related disorders）的预测性与个性化干预建立机制基础。

Abstract: The ability to predict protein three-dimensional structures from amino acid sequences is a landmark achievement in molecular biology, where recent deep learning approaches such as AlphaFold are the culmination of decades of work. Yet, the quantitative understanding of how protein sequences give rise to dynamic conformational changes and higher-order assemblies remains unsolved. Folding and conformational states are dynamic, stochastic processes, shaped by sequence, energy, co-translational constraints, chaperone machineries, and the physicochemical conditions of the cellular environment. Recent advances now position the field to move beyond static structural endpoints toward a mechanistic understanding of folding dynamics in living systems. Single-molecule techniques enable time-resolved observation of folding trajectories and intermediate states hitherto hidden by traditional structural biology approaches, while computational innovations and data-driven approaches offer new ways to integrate heterogeneous data across scales. In this Roadmap, we review the current conceptual landscape of protein folding, examine the experimental and theoretical gaps that remain, and discuss emerging strategies that integrate high-resolution measurements with multiscale modeling. We outline a roadmap toward a quantitative and predictive science of protein folding dynamics, conformational kinetics, and macromolecular self-assembly. Realizing this vision would transform our understanding of the dynamics of molecular self-organization, from the folding of individual polypeptides to the emergence of dynamic macromolecular complexes. This will enable rational control of folding and misfolding in health and disease, extend protein engineering principles beyond static structural design, and establish a mechanistic foundation for predictive and personalized interventions in proteostasis-related disorders.

### [130] [Area and water-capacity statistics for upper hulls of Dyck paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08834)
*Aleksander L. Owczarek,Thomas Prellberg*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究 Dyck 路径（Dyck paths）在适当面积（proper area）和水容量（water capacity）双重权重下的枚举与生成函数性质，提出了四变量高度展开（four-variable height expansion），并证明了在单位正方形内长度半径（length radius）由分母分支的最小值决定，在特殊对角线上得到支点交叉与临界标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓展 Dyck 路径的面积统计到水容量维度，探索两者耦合下的枚举结构与生成函数的解析性质，填补了经典有界高度面积多项式与连分数方法在组合多变量设置中的空白。

Method: 采用上包络分解（upper-hull decomposition）导出耦合的面积-容量替换关系（coupled area--capacity substitution），构建四变量高度展开；利用一致正态收敛性（uniform normal convergence）、Perron根表示（Perron-root representation）以及区间对数-子模性定理（interval log-submodularity theorem）进行半径分析；在特殊对角线上使用经典 Chebyshev 特殊化（Chebyshev specialisation）处理支点行为。

Result: 生成函数对面积与容量两个权重表现出不对称性，但高度求和项在权重互换下具有对称的未约化分母表示。长度半径由正实数分母分支的最小值给出，在 p=q=s 对角线上支点（branch crossings）显式出现，并服从 (1−s)^{2/3} 的分支包络累积律（branch-envelope accumulation law）在 Dyck 临界点处。

Conclusion: 上包络分解框架有效统一了 Dyck 路径的面积与水容量统计，揭示了高度展开的分支结构与临界标度行为，为组合枚举与解析组合学（analytic combinatorics）的交叉研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: We study Dyck paths refined simultaneously by proper area and water capacity, where water capacity is measured above the path and below its lattice-path upper hull. The finite-height ingredients used in the enumeration are classical bounded-height area-polynomial and continued-fraction objects. The upper-hull decomposition produces a coupled area--capacity substitution, which gives an exact four-variable height expansion with denominator branches indexed by the height levels. The full generating function is asymmetric in the two weights, while the height summands admit a symmetric unreduced denominator representation under interchange of the area and capacity weights. In the open square $0<p,q<1$, we prove that the length radius of $G(x,1,p,q)$ is the minimum of the positive real denominator branches. The proof combines uniform normal convergence of the height expansion below this first branch with a Perron-root representation of the branch locations and an interval log-submodularity theorem for spectral radii of weighted paths. On the diagonal $p=q=s$, the classical Chebyshev specialisation gives explicit branch crossings and a $(1-s)^{2/3}$ branch-envelope accumulation law at the Dyck critical point.

### [131] [Finite-n Estimate of Dedekind Numbers by Layer-Ratio Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09795)
*Tian-Shun Chen,Hao Feng,Haozhe Wang,Kilar Zhang*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文将Dedekind问题（计算单调布尔函数个数）重新表述为分层比率重建问题，利用可逆固定层马尔可夫链估计Whitney数序列，进而估计Dedekind数M(n)。研究发现n=9时Whitney数序列呈浅双肩特征，修正了此前单峰性的经验描述；给出了M(10)的估计值(8.9360±0.0010)×10⁷⁸。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dedekind问题旨在计数单调布尔函数（monotone Boolean functions），等价于布尔格（Boolean lattice）的下集（downsets）个数。该问题缺乏精确高效的计算方法，尤其是当n增大时计算复杂度急剧上升，因此需要发展统计估计方法。

Method: 将枚举问题重新表述为带秩理想格（ranked ideal lattice）上Whitney数（Whitney numbers）的有限层比率重建问题。通过精确的相邻层双计数关系，将每个层比率表示为可添加元素数和可移除元素数的局部平均值。利用可逆固定层马尔可夫链（reversible fixed-layer Markov chains）估计这些平均值，进而估计Dedekind数M(n)。

Result: 在M(8)和M(9)上进行回测（backtest），校准了固定协议下的种子层变异性并测量了蒙特卡洛预算缩放行为。高精度n=9估计显示Whitney数序列在中心秩附近具有浅双肩（shallow two-shoulder）特征，与以往单峰性经验描述不符；n=11和n=13的估计显示更大对比度的类似模式。M(10)的估计值为(8.9360±0.0010)×10⁷⁸。

Conclusion: 所提出的分层比率重建方法与马尔可夫链估计框架能够有效估计Dedekind数，并揭示了Whitney数序列在中心秩附近的双肩结构，修正了此前关于其单峰性的经验认知。给出的M(10)估计值附带基于预算的交叉n缩放律预测的不确定度。

Abstract: Dedekind's problem counts monotone Boolean functions, equivalently downsets of a Boolean lattice. We recast this enumeration as a finite layer-ratio reconstruction problem for the Whitney numbers of the ranked ideal lattice. An exact adjacent-layer double count expresses each layer ratio through local averages of the number of addable elements and the number of removable elements. Reversible fixed-layer Markov chains estimate these averages and hence estimate the Dedekind number M(n). Backtests at M(8) and M(9) calibrate seed-level variability under the fixed protocol and measure the observed Monte Carlo budget scaling. The resulting estimate probes the Whitney-number sequence of the ideal lattice. Although these rows have previously been described empirically as unimodal, the high-precision n=9 estimate has a shallow two-shoulder feature around the central rank, contrary to that empirical description; n=11 and n=13 center-window estimates show a larger-contrast analogous pattern. The protocol estimate for M(10) is \[
  \widehat M(10)=(8.9360\pm0.0010)\times 10^{78}, \] where the displayed uncertainty is the budget-based forecast scale from the cross-n scaling law under the production budget.

</details>

### [132] [PyCBC Live Search for Compact Binary Mergers in Advanced LIGO and Virgo's Fourth Observing Run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07679)
*Max Trevor,Gareth S. Cabourn Davies,Tito Dal Canton,Thomas Dent,Ian Harry,Stephanie Hoang,Arthur Tolley*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍了PyCBC Live低延迟引力波搜索流水线在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四轮观测运行（O4）中的改进，包括增强的排名统计量、改进的后随观测能力、早期预警搜索以及自动门控过程的扩展。在Mock Data Challenge中，与O3配置相比，O4配置在双探测器时间下的注入识别率从50.6%提升至79.3%，单探测器时间下的识别率从14.5%提升至18.6%，中位延迟保持在15.94秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA网络第四轮观测运行（O4）改进PyCBC Live低延迟搜索流水线，以提升引力波事件的探测灵敏度、降低延迟并增强电磁后随观测能力。

Method: 通过引入时间依赖背景建模（time-dependent background modeling）和数据质量流（data quality streams）来增强排名统计量；优化了天体物理起源概率计算和信噪比恢复算法；实现了早期预警搜索（Early Warning search），在中点前2.5-3.5秒发出预警，最长可提前60秒；将自动门控过程（autogating）扩展至整个应变数据缓冲（strain buffer）以提升对强瞬态噪声的抑制能力。

Result: Mock Data Challenge显示，在逆虚警率10年条件下，符合搜索灵敏度提升1.7-2.3倍（取决于源质量），单探测器搜索提升1.3-1.7倍。双探测器时间下，O4配置识别1979/2495次注入（79.3%），优于O3的1262次（50.6%）；单探测器时间下，O4识别218/1174次（18.6%），优于O3的170次（14.5%）。中位延迟为15.94秒。

Conclusion: PyCBC Live在O4配置中的改进显著提升了引力波探测的灵敏度和效率，尤其是在双探测器符合搜索中实现了近30个百分点的识别率提升，同时保持了低延迟特性，为电磁后随观测提供了更及时有效的警报。

Abstract: PyCBC Live is a low-latency search pipeline that identifies gravitational waves from compact binary coalescences and provides alerts for electromagnetic follow-up. This paper presents improvements to PyCBC Live that were implemented for the fourth observing run (O4) of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network, which operated from May 2023 to November 2025. The ranking statistic was enhanced to incorporate time-dependent background modeling using data quality streams and daily updates of the noise model. Follow-up capabilities were improved through refined probability of astrophysical origin calculations, optimized SNR recovery with reduced computational cost, and a method to incorporate Virgo as a sky-map-only detector. An Early Warning search was implemented to detect binary neutron star and neutron star-black hole systems before merger, providing pre-merger alerts with a pipeline latency of 2.5-3.5 seconds and warning times up to 60 seconds before coalescence. The autogating procedure was extended to apply to the full strain buffer rather than individual analysis segments, improving rejection of loud and rapidly successive glitches. Performance validation using the Mock Data Challenge showed sensitivity improvements of factors of 1.7 to 2.3 for the coincident search depending on source mass at an inverse false alarm rate of 10 years, and factors of 1.3 to 1.7 for the single-detector search. For injections in two-detector time, the O4 configuration identified 1979 of 2495 injections with a decisive SNR greater than 6 at a false alarm rate below one per year (79.3%), compared to 1262 (50.6%) with the O3 configuration. For injections in single-detector time, the O4 configuration identified 218 of 1174 injections (18.6%), compared to 170 (14.5%) with the O3 configuration. The search maintained a median latency of 15.94 seconds from merger to candidate upload.

### [133] [Statistical Estimation and Correction of Model-Measurement Bias in Time-Dependent Correction Factors of KAGRA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09010)
*Shingo Hido,Takahiro Yamamoto,Dan Chen,Takahiro Sawada,Shinji Miyoki*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种统计框架，用于估计并纠正引力波探测器标定中因模型-测量偏差（model-measurement bias）导致的系统误差。该方法基于限制性最大似然估计（REML）的滚动随机效应模型计算偏差校正因子，并将其纳入时间相关校正因子（TDCF）估计中。在KAGRA O4c数据上的应用表明，该方法能有效减小响应偏差，同时仅适度增加传播不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器的标定（calibration）过程中，从探测器输出重建应变h(t)时存在的偏差和不确定性会直接影响下游分析。当地面干涉仪使用时间相关校正因子（time-dependent correction factors, TDCFs）跟踪探测器响应的时变特性时，如果测量传递函数与参考模型之间存在模型-测量偏差（model-measurement bias），则从标定线（calibration lines）推断出的TDCFs会在重建应变中引入系统性偏差，因此需要提出方法来估计和纠正此偏差。

Method: 提出一个统计框架：使用重复的测量-模型比值（measurement-to-model ratios）在标定线频率处估计偏差。偏差校正因子通过基于限制性最大似然估计（restricted maximum likelihood, REML）的滚动随机效应模型（rolling random-effects model）进行估计，并纳入TDCF估计中，其不确定性传播至重建响应。

Result: 将该方法应用于KAGRA O4c数据，在代表性示例中发现：未经校正的响应相对于基于扫频标定测量（swept-sine calibration measurements, SSCMs）的参考存在幅度约7%、相位约5度的偏差。校正后偏差减小，由于包含校正因子不确定性，传播不确定性仅适度增加。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种在实际存在模型-测量偏差时，将宽带参考模型（broadband reference models）与基于标定线的跟踪方法（calibration-line-based tracking）相结合的有效手段。

Abstract: Calibration of gravitational-wave detectors reconstructs the strain h(t) from the detector output, and bias and uncertainty in this reconstruction directly affect downstream analyses. In ground-based interferometers, time-dependent correction factors (TDCFs) are estimated from calibration lines to track temporal variations of the detector response, while the underlying model parameters are periodically updated using broadband swept-sine calibration measurements (SSCMs). However, if a model-measurement bias exists between the measured transfer function and the reference model, the TDCFs inferred from calibration lines can introduce a systematic deviation into the reconstructed strain. We propose a statistical framework to estimate and correct this bias using repeated measurement-to-model ratios at the calibration-line frequencies. The bias correction factors are estimated with a rolling random-effects model based on restricted maximum likelihood (REML) and incorporated into the TDCF estimation, with their uncertainty propagated to the reconstructed response. Applying the method to KAGRA O4c data, we find that the uncorrected response shows deviations of up to approximately 7% in magnitude and 5 degrees in phase relative to the SSCM-based reference in representative examples. The correction reduces these deviations, with a modest increase in the propagated uncertainty due to the included correction-factor uncertainty. This framework provides a practical way to combine broadband reference models with calibration-line-based tracking when model-measurement bias is present.

</details>

### [134] [Collective dynamics in a one-dimensional Heisenberg ferromagnetic spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08149)
*R. Arun,M. Lakshmanan,Avadh Saxena*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维各向异性海森堡铁磁自旋链（one-dimensional anisotropic Heisenberg ferromagnetic spin chain）中的多种振荡模式，包括完全同步、同相同步、反相同步和去同步。通过求解Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert-Slonczewski方程，发现这些模式可在自旋系统中共存。当自旋数量较大时同步性丧失，但场类扭矩（field-like torque）能重新诱导同步振荡。数值得到的同相振荡频率与解析结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大量自旋组成的一维各向异性海森堡铁磁自旋链中不同的振荡模式及其同步行为，尤其是场类扭矩对同步恢复的作用。

Method: 求解与自旋系统相关联的Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert-Slonczewski方程，通过数值方法分析多种振荡模式的共存与转变。

Result: 在大量自旋的情况下，同步性会丧失；但场类扭矩能够重新诱导自旋之间的同步振荡。同相同步振荡的频率数值结果与解析结果吻合。

Conclusion: 一维各向异性海森堡铁磁自旋链中存在多种振荡模式的共存，且场类扭矩在恢复大自旋系统中的同步行为中起关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the different oscillatory modes, namely, complete synchronization, inphase synchronization, antiphase synchronization and desynchronization in a one-dimensional anisotropic Heisenberg ferromagnetic spin chain consisting of a large number of spins. By solving the associated Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert-Slonczewski equation for the spins we show the simultaneous existence of the above mentioned oscillatory modes in the spins. We observe that when the number of the spins is large the synchronization is lost between the spins; however, we identify that the field-like torque is able to induce synchronous oscillations of the spins in the chain again. We also confirm the agreement of the numerically obtained values of the frequency of the inphase synchronized oscillations with the analytically obtained values.

</details>

### [135] [Measurements of the Angular Homogeneity Scale from DESI DR1](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07854)

TL;DR: 该研究利用暗能量光谱巡天（DESI）第一批数据（DR1）中的发光红星系（LRGs）观测数据，在二维空间中探测宇宙学原理（Cosmological Principle）所预言的角向均匀性尺度（angular homogeneity scale, θ_H），结果在所有红移区间均识别出该尺度，并与ΛCDM模型模拟及先前SDSS-IV eBOSS DR16的测量结果高度一致，从而支持了宇宙在大尺度上统计均匀各向同性的基本假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标准宇宙学模型（ΛCDM）的两大基础之一——宇宙学原理，即宇宙在大尺度上统计均匀且各向同性的假设。该原理是使用FLRW度规进行距离和年龄测量的前提。

Method: 利用DESI DR1中LRGs的观测数据，在二维空间中（不引入第三维）对方位角均匀性尺度θ_H进行测量；分析覆盖0.4 < z < 1.1的窄红移区间，并分别处理北银冠和南银冠两个天区，以最小化对底层宇宙学模型的事先依赖。

Result: 在所有红移区间内均识别出角向均匀性尺度θ_H；测量结果与ΛCDM模型的模拟数据一致；结果与SDSS-IV eBOSS DR16的先期测量及DESI DR1南北银冠之间的测量均吻合良好。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持宇宙统计各向同性和均匀性作为物理上有效的假设，与标准宇宙学模型的基本支柱之一一致，并为即将开展的第四阶段红移巡天（stage-IV redshift surveys）提供了基础验证。

Abstract: The study of the large-scale distribution of galaxies provides essential information for testing the standard cosmological model, namely the $Λ$CDM paradigm. This scenario is based upon two foundations: General Relativity as the theory of gravity, and the Cosmological Principle, which states that the Universe is statistically homogeneous and isotropic on large scales -- so that we can measure distances and ages in the Universe assuming the FLRW metric.
  In this work, we perform a test of the Cosmological Principle by probing the angular homogeneity scale, $θ_H$, using the state-of-the-art observational data of Luminous Red Galaxies (LRGs) from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 1 (DESI DR1). Our analysis is performed exclusively in two dimensions, across narrow redshift ranges inside a larger redshift sample of $0.4 < z < 1.1$, in two different surveyed regions of the sky (North and South Galactic Caps), as we want to minimize a priori dependences on an underlying cosmological model.
  We obtain that such a scale is indeed identified in all redshift ranges, and that they are consistent with mock simulations assuming the $Λ$CDM model. Moreover, our results are in great agreement with previous measurements using Sloan Digital Sky Survey IV extended Baryon Oscillation Spectroscopic Survey Data Release 16 (SDSS-IV eBOSS DR16), as well as between the north and south galactic caps of the DESI DR1 survey. These findings help underpinning statistical isotropy and homogeneity of the Universe as a physically valid hypothesis in light of upcoming stage-IV redshift surveys, hence are consistent with one of the fundamental pillars of the standard cosmological model.

</details>


### [136] [Optimising ultra-light dark matter searches with ground-based interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09210)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用光谱形态中的恒星日调制（sidereal modulation）特征，在频率低于约30 Hz时区分自旋-1与自旋-2极轻暗物质信号；在Band-Sampled-Data框架内提出交叉相关统计量（cross-correlation statistics）的优化实现方案。

Result: 在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA搜索技术背景下，融入恒星日调制特征可使低频过剩功率约束提升约36%；优化的交叉相关统计量在低频段灵敏度提升约42%，在高频段提升约35%。

Conclusion: 恒星日调制特征为区分不同自旋类型的极轻暗物质信号提供了有效途径，所提出的优化方法可显著提升现有引力波探测器对极轻暗物质的搜索灵敏度。

Abstract: Ultra-light dark matter fields induce nearly monochromatic signals in gravitational-wave detectors through their coupling to the Standard Model. Their spectral morphology exhibits features caused by sidereal modulation that, for frequencies below $\sim 30~$Hz, enable discrimination between spin-1 and spin-2 ultra-light dark matter signals, provided sufficient signal-to-noise ratio. In the context of LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA search techniques, we show that incorporating these spectral features can improve current excess-power constraints at low frequencies by up to $\sim36\%$. Additionally, we propose an optimised implementation of the cross-correlation statistics within the Band-Sampled-Data framework, enhancing the sensitivity of cross-correlation searches across nearly the entire frequency range, reaching up to $\sim42\%$ at low frequencies and $\sim35\%$ at high frequencies.

### [137] [Modifying $Λ$CDM dynamics via out-of-equilibrium axions: reconciling SH0ES and DESI $H_0$ values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09427)
*Giovanni Montani,Luis A. Escamilla,Nakia Carlevaro,Francesco Cianfrani*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个由轴子（axion）粒子描述暗物质成分的晚期宇宙动力学模型，该模型在红移 z ≲ 1 时偏离标准 ΛCDM 模型，并能够同时兼容 SH0ES 本地校准给出的高哈勃常数（H₀ ≈ 73 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹）与 DESI 合作的重子声学振荡（BAO）数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 ΛCDM 模型在解释晚期宇宙观测（尤其是哈勃常数局域测量与早期宇宙推断值之间的“哈勃张力”（Hubble tension））时面临挑战。本文旨在探索由轴子粒子描述暗物质、且因少量轴子偏离热平衡而引发的非标准晚期宇宙动力学，以缓解上述张力。

Method: 分别采用动理学（kinetic）途径和经典场（classical field）途径分析轴子能量密度的演化，两种方法推导出暗物质密度满足相同的宏观演化方程。随后将理论预测与一套综合的晚期宇宙数据集进行统计比较。

Result: 当纳入 SH0ES 局域距离阶梯校准数据时，该碰撞轴子模型（collisional axion model）在统计上显著优于 ΛCDM 模型，最佳拟合哈勃常数 H₀ ≈ 73 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹。该模型还能与 DESI 的重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation, BAO）数据保持高度一致。

Conclusion: 该轴子暗物质框架在晚期宇宙（z ≲ 1）有效修正了 ΛCDM 动力学，而在更早宇宙时期渐近恢复标准基线，因此能够成功兼容局域距离阶梯测量与 BAO 观测，为解决哈勃张力提供了一种可行的模型方案。

Abstract: We investigate late-Universe dynamics in which the dark matter component is described by axion particles. The proposed framework departs from the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm due to a small fraction of axions driving the system away from thermal equilibrium. We analyze the evolution of the axion energy density using both a kinetic and a classical field approach, yielding an identical macroscopic evolution equation for the dark matter density. The resulting scenario modifies $Λ$CDM dynamics in the late Universe (specifically at $z \lesssim 1$), while asymptotically recovering the standard baseline at earlier cosmic epochs. We compare the theoretical predictions of our formulation against a comprehensive suite of late-Universe datasets. Our statistical analysis reveals that when the SH0ES local calibration is included, the collisional axion model becomes significantly favored over $Λ$CDM, yielding a best-fit Hubble constant of $H_0 \simeq 73~{\rm km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$. Ultimately, this cosmological scenario successfully accommodates local distance-ladder measurements while maintaining excellent agreement with Baryon Acoustic Oscillation data from the DESI Collaboration.

### [138] [Spectral distortion anisotropies from photon to dark photon conversions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09491)
*Sara Evangelista,Jens Chluba,Bryce Cyr*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究暗光子（dark photon）通过共振光子-暗光子转换在宇宙微波背景（CMB）中产生的各向异性谱畸变（anisotropic spectral distortions），利用频率层级（Frequency Hierarchy, FH）框架计算转移函数和畸变交叉功率谱，发现暗光子质量控制信号功率谱的多极依赖形状而动力学混合参数决定总体振幅，并基于Planck数据给出了互补约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗光子是暗扇区（dark sector）的规范玻色子，代表了标准模型（Standard Model）最受关注的极小扩展之一，具有广泛的理论和观测意义。本文旨在利用CMB谱畸变来约束这一模型，并将研究从单极（monopole）谱拓展到各向异性（anisotropic）谱畸变。

Method: 考虑初始未布居的暗光子扇区通过共振光子-暗光子转换（resonant photon to dark photon conversions）被布居的过程。利用CosmoTherm中新开发的频率层级（Frequency Hierarchy, FH）框架计算光子转移函数（transfer functions）和畸变交叉功率谱（distortion cross power spectra）。

Result: 暗光子质量（dark photon mass）明确控制信号功率谱的形状（即多极依赖关系），而动力学混合参数（kinetic mixing parameter）决定信号的总体振幅。基于Planck数据对最小暗光子模型给出的约束仅略弱于COBE/FIRAS数据在平均（单极）畸变上的约束。红移大于2×10^6处的转换可能引入等曲率型扰动（iso-curvature type perturbations）。

Conclusion: 暗光子参数空间中的质量与动力学混合参数分别控制信号功率谱的形状和振幅，CMB各向异性谱畸变可提供对暗光子模型的互补约束，且在畸变各向异性热化（thermalize）的 regimes 中可能产生新的约束条件。

Abstract: Dark photons are a gauge boson of a hypothetical dark sector, representing one of the most-studied minimal extensions of the Standard Model, with wide-ranging theoretical and observational implications. Here, we consider scenarios in which an initially unpopulated dark photon sector is populated via resonant photon to dark photon conversions. This process leads to observable spectral distortions in the cosmic microwave background (CMB), that can be used to constrain these models. We extend previous spectral distortion studies of the monopole spectrum to anisotropic spectral distortions, using the newly developed Frequency Hierarchy (FH) framework of CosmoTherm. We illustrate the physics by presenting detailed computations of the photon transfer functions and distortion cross power spectra throughout the dark photon parameter space. We find that the dark photon mass explicitly controls the shape (i.e., multipole-dependence) of the signal power spectra, while the overall amplitude of the signal is determined by the kinetic mixing parameter of the model. Using these results, we place complementary limits on the minimal dark photon model using data from Planck, finding that the constraints are only marginally weaker than those obtained with COBE/FIRAS data for the average (monopole) distortion. In addition, we compute the corrections to the standard temperature field, arguing that conversions at redshifts larger than $2\times 10^6$ may add iso-curvature type perturbations, which could lead to novel constraints in regimes where distortion anisotropies thermalize.

</details>


### [139] [Pantheon+ supernovae corrected for progenitor age indicate the universe is decelerating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09650)
*Animesh Sah,Mohamed Rameez,Subir Sarkar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae）的前身星年龄依赖的光度演化对减速参数（deceleration parameter）$q_0$宇宙学测量（cosmographic measurement）的影响。通过对Pantheon+星表施加红移依赖的前身星年龄修正，发现$q_0$的单极分量（monopole component）向正值（即减速）偏移，而局部偶极分量（dipole component）基本不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前红移断层析分析（redshift tomographic analysis）表明，局部$q_0$存在一个大致与体流（bulk flow）方向一致的强偶极各向异性（dipole anisotropy），而距离超过数百Mpc时仅余微小单极分量。本文旨在检验前身星年龄依赖的光度演化对这一结果的影响。

Method: 对Pantheon+星表（Pantheon+ catalogue）施加红移依赖（redshift-dependent）的前身星年龄修正（progenitor age corrections），重新分析减速参数$q_0$的单极与偶极分量。

Result: 引入前身星年龄修正后，$q_0$的单极分量从负值（加速）转变为正值（减速），而局部偶极分量基本保持不变。

Conclusion: Ia型超新星的前身星年龄效应主要影响$q_0$的单极分量测量，对局部偶极各向异性的影响可忽略，表明该偶极信号可能源自其他物理机制。

Abstract: We examine the impact of progenitor age-dependent luminosity evolution of Type Ia supernovae on a cosmographic measurement of the deceleration parameter $q_0$. Our recent redshift tomographic analysis showed that locally $q_0$ has a strong dipole anisotropy aligned approximately with the bulk flow, and only a small monopole component remains at distances exceeding a few hundred Mpc. Applying redshift-dependent corrections for progenitor age to the Pantheon+ catalogue, we find that this shifts the monopole component of $q_0$ to positive values (i.e. deceleration), while leaving the local dipole component essentially unchanged.

### [140] [Stochastic constant-roll inflation beyond the hilltop with the spectral method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09690)
*Eemeli Tomberg*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文采用随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）框架，通过谱方法（spectral method）求解二次山顶势（quadratic hilltop potential）对应的常数滚动暴胀（constant-roll inflation）中的扰动分布，发现越过山顶并被反射边界捕获的罕见轨迹主导了平均首达时间（mean first-passage time），因此主张用中位数（median）而非均值描述暴胀背景，并计算出粗粒化ΔN分布呈现先平坦后形成峰值的复杂结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机暴胀可用于研究大幅暴胀扰动，但先前对常数滚动暴胀（constant-roll inflation）的随机研究未能考虑越过山顶并受反射边界束缚的轨迹路径，而这些罕见轨迹可能对统计描述产生重要影响。

Method: 采用谱方法（spectral method）求解福克-普朗克算符（Fokker-Planck operator）的本征值和本征函数，从而得到二次山顶势（quadratic hilltop potential）下常数滚动暴胀（constant-roll inflation）的扰动分布解析解。

Result: 越过山顶并被另一侧反射边界捕获的罕见轨迹，其缓慢隧穿行为由最低本征解（lowest eigensolution）支配，且这些罕见轨迹反而主导了平均首达时间（mean first-passage time）；粗粒化ΔN分布呈现先平坦后形成峰值的结构。

Conclusion: 均值不能恰当描述暴胀背景，应采用中位数（median）替代；类似复杂性也可能出现在原初黑洞（primordial black hole）模型中。

Abstract: Stochastic inflation can be used to study large inflationary perturbations. This paper presents such a study for a quadratic hilltop potential, corresponding to constant-roll inflation. I solve the perturbation distribution using the spectral method, with detailed solutions of the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions of the Fokker-Planck operator. Contrary to previous studies of stochastic constant-roll inflation, the solution allows trajectories that cross the hilltop and get stuck near a reflecting boundary on the other side, tunneling out slowly in a way dictated by the lowest eigensolution. Despite their rarity, these trajectories turn out to dominate the mean first-passage time. For this reason, I argue the mean does not properly describe the inflationary background. Using the median instead, I compute the distribution of the coarse-grained $ΔN$ distribution and show that its well-known exponential tail first flattens out and then forms a peak near a maximal $ΔN$ value. I argue similar intricacies arise in primordial black hole models.

</details>


### [141] [Universal Suppression of Gravitational Waves from Black Hole Evaporation Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09804)
*Xin-Chen He,Xiao-Han Ma,Misao Sasaki,Volodymyr Takhistov*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 蒸发黑洞会在引力波背景上留下独特印记。具有有限宽度质量分布的黑洞种群表现出由蒸发动力学支配的普适晚期演化行为，导致诱导引力波出现特征性的幂律抑制。该研究将渐近引力波谱与黑洞蒸发定律直接联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示蒸发黑洞在引力波背景上留下的印记，并探索黑洞种群质量分布的普适演化行为及其对诱导引力波的影响。

Method: 通过分析具有有限宽度质量分布的黑洞种群的晚期演化，研究其在原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）场景中的行为，并考察早期宇宙物质主导时期（matter-dominated era）下的广义质量函数。

Result: 发现黑洞种群的晚期演化由蒸发动力学（evaporation dynamics）支配，而非初始质量分布的细节，导致诱导引力波出现特征性的幂律抑制（power law suppression）。临界坍缩分布（critical collapse distributions）下PBH诱导引力波的抑制是该普适现象的一个特例。

Conclusion: 建立了渐近引力波谱（asymptotic GW spectrum）与黑洞蒸发定律之间的直接联系，表明蒸发黑洞产生的引力波信号可作为一种普适探针。

Abstract: Evaporating black holes can leave distinct imprints on gravitational wave (GW) backgrounds. We show that black hole populations with finite width mass distributions exhibit a universal late time evolution governed by the evaporation dynamics rather than the details of the initial mass distribution, leading to a characteristic power law suppression of the induced GWs. We demonstrate this for a broad class of mass functions in primordial black hole (PBH) scenarios featuring an early Universe matter-dominated era, and identify the suppression of PBH-induced GWs found for critical collapse distributions as a manifestation of this general phenomenon. Our results establish a direct connection between the asymptotic GW spectrum and the underlying law of black hole evaporation.

</details>


### [142] [Inflationary interpretation of the gravitational-wave signal in the European Pulsar Timing Array DR2 with constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09810)
*Philippe Turgeon,Chiara Caprini,Anton Chudaykin,Martin Kunz,Delphine Perrodin,Ismael Cognard,Lucas Guillemot,Gilles Theureau*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于欧洲脉冲星计时阵列（EPTA）第二次数据发布的引力波背景信号，探索了暴胀（inflationary）宇宙学解释，通过引入张量标量比、张量谱指数、再加热温度和截止频率等参数，结合多种宇宙学观测约束，给出了参数空间的可行区域，发现再加热温度必须极低，这在理论上难以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EPTA合作第二次数据发布提供了引力波背景存在的证据，本文旨在检验这一信号是否可能源自暴胀（inflation）时期的原初引力波，从而探索其宇宙学起源。

Method: 将张量功率谱（tensor power spectrum）参数化为张量标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r$、张量谱指数（tensor spectral index）$n_t$、再加热温度（reheating temperature）$T_{\text{rh}}$和截止频率（cut-off frequency）$f_{\text{end}}$，并纳入宇宙微波背景（CMB）、大爆炸核合成（BBN）和LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测等所有相关观测约束进行参数空间分析。

Result: 在95%置信水平下，约束后的参数范围为：$-11.66 \lesssim \log_{10}r \lesssim -1.45$，$1.32 \lesssim n_t \lesssim 2.47$，$1.78\text{ MeV} \lesssim T_{\text{rh}} \lesssim 28.2\text{ GeV}$，$75.86\text{ nHz} \lesssim f_{\text{end}} \lesssim 14.45\text{ Hz}$。这倾向于EPTA频段的引力波谱来源于辐射主导时期（radiation-dominated era）重新进入哈勃半径（Hubble radius）的张量模（tensor modes），允许更高的$r$和更平坦的谱。

Conclusion: 该暴胀解释要求再加热温度极低（$T_{\text{rh}}$低至MeV量级），这在理论上难以得到合理的物理解释，表明该解释面临严峻的理论挑战。

Abstract: The second data release of the European Pulsar Timing Array (EPTA) collaboration provides evidence for the presence of a gravitational-wave (GW) background. In this work, we explore a potential cosmological interpretation of this signal in terms of inflationary scenarios. We parametrize the tensor power spectrum in terms of the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, the tensor spectral index $n_t$, the reheating temperature $T_{\text{rh}}$, and the cut-off frequency $f_{\text{end}}$. We incorporate all relevant observational constraints, including those from the Cosmic Microwave Background, Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, and LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observations. We demonstrate that imposing these constraints consistently reduces the region of parameter space that provides a viable interpretation of the EPTA signal, to $-11.66 \lesssim \log_{10}r \lesssim -1.45$, $1.32 \lesssim n_t \lesssim 2.47$, $1.78\text{ MeV} \lesssim T_{\text{rh}} \lesssim 28.2\text{ GeV}$, and $75.86\text{ nHz} \lesssim f_{\text{end}} \lesssim 14.45\text{ Hz}$ at the 95% confidence level. This favours the scenario in which the GW spectrum in the EPTA frequency band originates from tensor modes that re-entered the Hubble radius during the radiation-dominated era, allowing for a higher $r$ and a flatter spectrum. However, $T_{\text{rh}}$ must take very low values, which are challenging to explain theoretically.

</details>

### [143] [Constraint residuals, graph posteriors, and determinant-corrected full-space targets in Bayesian inverse problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09594)
*Jonathon Cottom,Emilia Olsson*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 该论文指出，在贝叶斯逆问题中，全参数-状态空间（full parameter-state space）的残差惩罚方法与状态消去后的降阶空间（reduced space）方法在后验测度（posterior measure）上并不自动等价，并通过理论推导证明了二者之间存在由状态雅可比（state Jacobian）行列式因子造成的差异，进而提出了保持等价性的行列式修正方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在等式约束贝叶斯逆问题中，研究者常通过在完整参数-状态空间中对残差（residual）施加惩罚来采样，而非在消去状态变量后的降阶空间中采样。该论文的动机在于揭示这两种形式在后验测度上并不自动等价的这一被忽视的问题，并澄清可行集（feasible set）等价与后验校准（posterior calibration）之间的关键区别。

Method: 论文假设约束方程 \(c(θ,u)=0\) 存在唯一解 \(u=G(θ)\) 且状态雅可比 \(\D_u c\) 非奇异，针对有限维离散化情形，定义了降阶后验（reduced posterior）、其图提升后验（graph-lifted posterior）以及零噪声残差后验（zero-noise residual posterior）三种分布，并通过局部变量变换（local change of variables）推导出未经修正的高斯残差惩罚在边缘化（marginalisation）后收敛于乘以 \(\abs{\det \D_u c(θ,G(θ))}^{-1}\) 的降阶密度。进一步推导了针对未加权、加权及重缩放残差惩罚的行列式修正项，使得修正后的惩罚方法以图提升降阶后验作为硬约束极限。

Result: 代数上等价的残差可以定义相同的可行集，但收敛到不同的极限后验分布；未修正的残差惩罚在边缘化后会产生一个由状态雅可比行列式因子偏斜的分布；通过引入相应的行列式修正，可以使残差惩罚方法正确收敛到图提升的降阶后验。

Conclusion: 仅将残差驱动到零并不能保证对图提升降阶后验的精确采样，除非采样或校正步骤针对相应的修正后密度（corrected density）进行。这分离了可行性与后验校准两个概念，强调了在等式约束贝叶斯逆问题中正确校正残差惩罚的重要性。

Abstract: Bayesian inverse problems constrained by state equations are often sampled in a full parameter-state space by penalising the residual, rather than in a reduced space where the state is eliminated. We show that these formulations are not automatically equivalent as posterior measures. For finite-dimensional discretisations of equality-constrained inverse problems, assume the state equation \(c(θ,u)=0\) has a unique solution \(u=G(θ)\) and nonsingular state Jacobian \(\D_u c\). The reduced posterior, its graph lift, and the zero-noise residual posterior are then distinct. A local change of variables shows that an uncorrected Gaussian residual penalty converges, after marginalisation over \(u\), to the reduced density multiplied by \(\abs{\det \D_u c(θ,G(θ))}^{-1}\). Thus algebraically equivalent residuals can define the same feasible set but different limiting posteriors. We derive determinant corrections for unweighted, weighted, and rescaled residual penalties that have the graph-lifted reduced posterior as their hard-constraint limit. The result separates feasibility from posterior calibration: driving the residual to zero is not sufficient for exact sampling of the graph-lifted reduced posterior unless the sampling or correction step targets the corresponding corrected density.

</details>

### [144] [Markovian dynamics of single-rebit open quantum systems with applications to colour perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08117)
*Michel Berthier,Gabriel Niebel,Edoardo Provenzi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文对定义在实数域上的开放二态量子系统（rebit）的马尔可夫动力学进行了研究，完成了马尔可夫rebit量子信道（即作用于rebit态空间上的完全正迹保持（CPTP）单参数半群）的完整分类，并将该分类应用于颜色感知建模，展示了非中性光照引起的色差可通过马尔可夫rebit信道模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推动开放量子系统在实数域上的理论分类，并探索其跨学科应用——将rebit马尔可夫动力学（Markovian dynamics）引入颜色视觉建模，以弥补现有模型在描述色觉现象方面的不足。

Method: 基于GKSL方程（Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad equation）刻画rebit量子信道，识别对应的Lindblad生成元（Lindblad generators）及完全正性（complete positivity）条件，完成所有马尔可夫rebit量子信道的分类；利用Lüders测量（Lüders measurements）模型，将色适应过程建模为马尔可夫rebit信道。

Result: 完成了马尔可夫rebit量子信道的完整分类，并展示了非中性光照导致的色度失真可由一个逐渐降低颜色可区分度的马尔可夫rebit信道表示；还指出其他类型的信道可用于研究色觉缺陷，并通过数字图像模拟验证了模型的有效性。

Conclusion: rebit马尔可夫动力学为颜色视觉建模提供了一个新的理论框架，不仅能够模拟非中性光照下的色适应过程，还有潜力用于研究色觉缺陷；分类结果为开放量子系统在实数域上的进一步应用奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: This paper investigates the Markovian dynamics of open two-state quantum systems defined over the real numbers (rebits). Two main objectives are pursued. First, we present a comprehensive classification of Markovian rebit quantum channels, i.e. one-parameter semigroups of completely positive, trace-preserving (CPTP) maps acting on the rebit state space. We show that a full characterisation of their action can be achieved and that describing these channels as solutions of the GKSL equation allows us to explicitly identify the associated Lindblad generators and conditions for complete positivity. Second, we present an original application of this classification to colour perception. Using a recent model in which perceived colours arise from Lüders measurements on the rebit state space, we show how chromatic distortion induced by a non-neutral illuminant can be modelled by a Markovian rebit channel that progressively diminishes colour distinguishability. Other types of channels could be used to study colour vision deficiencies. These phenomena are illustrated by simulations on digital images, highlighting the relevance of rebit Markovian dynamics in modelling colour vision.

</details>


### [145] [Entanglement in the Quantum Volunteer's Dilemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08227)
*Noah Dane Hebdon,Dax Enshan Koh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein框架下推广了量子志愿者困境（Quantum Volunteer's Dilemma），引入可调纠缠参数γ，分析了对称纳什均衡（symmetric Nash equilibrium）对纠缠水平依赖的条件，发现最大纠缠并非必要，而是存在一个与系统规模相关的阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典志愿者困境模型已推广至量子版本，但现有分析均假设最大纠缠（maximal entanglement）。为探究真实量子设备中有限纠缠资源对均衡行为的影响，作者引入可调纠缠参数，系统研究了纠缠水平如何影响对称纳什均衡的存在条件。

Method: 基于Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein量子博弈框架，定义广义量子志愿者困境模型。通过推导纠缠参数γ、玩家数量n与策略之间的显式条件，分析两种典型策略剖面（canonical strategy profile）：一种适用于2 ≤ n ≤ 9，另一种适用于偶数n。对称纳什均衡的存在阈值通过解析计算获得。

Result: 最大纠缠并非维持对称纳什均衡的必要条件；均衡行为在纠缠参数超过某一解析可计算的阈值后即可持续存在；该阈值直接依赖于系统规模（玩家数量n）。

Conclusion: 该阈值特征对于在资源受限的量子设备上实现量子志愿者困境具有直接指导意义，因为这些设备中的纠缠程度天生有限。

Abstract: A well-known model in game theory, the Volunteer's Dilemma describes a group of $n$ players who decide whether to volunteer for a collective benefit at a personal cost, or to abstain and risk forfeiting the benefit altogether. A quantum version of this dilemma, developed within the Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein framework, allows each player to manipulate one qubit of a shared entangled state, leading to symmetric Nash equilibria with higher expected payoffs than in the classical game. Existing analyses, however, assume maximal entanglement. Within the same framework, we introduce a generalized Quantum Volunteer's Dilemma with a tunable entanglement parameter $γ$ and study the extent to which equilibrium behavior depends on the level of entanglement. We derive explicit conditions relating $γ$, the number of players, and the players' strategies under which symmetric Nash equilibria exist, focusing on two canonical strategy profiles: one for $2\leq n\leq 9$, and one for even $n$. We find that maximal entanglement is not required to sustain symmetric equilibria. Instead, equilibrium behavior persists above a threshold value, which we compute analytically in both cases. We also demonstrate that the threshold value directly depends on system size. This characterization is directly relevant for implementations on resource-constrained quantum devices, where entanglement is inherently limited.

</details>


### [146] [Quantum algorithms for stochastic nonlinear differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08349)
*Sergey Bravyi,Adam Byrne,Mykhaylo Zayats,Sergiy Zhuk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对耗散且具有二次漂移的高维随机微分方程（stochastic differential equation, SDE）的量子算法，能够在强非线性、全连接相互作用系统中实现对低阶关联函数期望值的高效近似，计算代价为 $\log(N)$ 的多项式级别且随演化时间线性增长，主要技术突破是以 polylogarithmic 代价模拟 $N$ 个相互作用量子谐振子辅助系统，并将湍流模型（如 Navier-Stokes 和阻尼 Euler 方程）纳入该框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工程与计算物理中许多模型基于随机非线性动力学，但其高维精确模拟在经典计算中仍然困难；现有量子算法仅适用于弱非线性和稀疏系统，无法处理强非线性与全连接相互作用。

Method: 构造一个辅助系统，由 $N$ 个相互作用的量子谐振子（quantum harmonic oscillators）组成，并以 polylogarithmic 代价对其进行模拟；利用该子程序实现原随机微分方程的动态模拟，并基于严格的误差界（rigorous error bounds）逼近低阶关联函数（correlation functions）的期望值。

Result: 所提方法在保范漂移（norm-preserving drifts）条件下——该条件适用于关键的流体动力学离散化——以 $\log(N)$ 多项式级计算代价和线性时间代价逼近低阶关联函数的期望值，且具有严格的误差界。

Conclusion: 该算法将量子模拟的范围从弱非线性稀疏系统扩展到强非线性全连接系统，并建立了湍流模型（Navier-Stokes 和阻尼 Euler 方程）在该框架下的表述，从而为量子模拟强非线性随机微分方程（如湍流和非线性波动动力学）开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Stochastic nonlinear dynamics underlie many models in engineering and computational physics, yet accurate high-dimensional simulation remains challenging. We present a quantum algorithm for a broad class of $N$-dimensional stochastic differential equations with dissipation and quadratic drift. The algorithm applies to strongly nonlinear systems with all-to-all interactions, thereby extending the scope of previously known quantum algorithms that were limited to weak nonlinearity and sparse systems. For norm-preserving drifts, a condition satisfied by key fluid dynamics discretizations, our method approximates expectation values of low-order correlation functions with rigorous error bounds at a cost polynomial in $\log{(N)}$ and linear in the evolution time. Our main technical advance is a subroutine for simulating an auxiliary system of $N$ interacting quantum harmonic oscillators with cost polylogarithmic in $N$. Finally, we formulate turbulence models, including Navier-Stokes and damped Euler equations, within this framework, opening a route to quantum simulation of strongly nonlinear SDEs governing turbulence and nonlinear wave dynamics.

### [147] [Another Legacy of Andrzej Kossakowski: A Self-Contained Derivation of the GKLS Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08579)
*Gen Kimura*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为纪念GKLS方程提出50周年而作，旨在以自洽的方式重建一条通往GKLS生成元的逻辑路径，重点强调Kossakowski的结构性洞见：马尔可夫性（Markovianity）、完全正性（complete positivity）、迹保持性（trace preservation）以及量子动力学半群（quantum dynamical semigroups）的无穷小结构自然导出了该生成元的著名形式，并附有对Kossakowski的个人回忆。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为OSID期刊纪念Gorini–Kossakowski–Lindblad–Sudarshan（GKLS）方程50周年特刊撰稿，旨在从逻辑角度而非历史综述角度，揭示GKLS生成元（GKLS generator）的内在推导路径。

Method: 采用自洽的逻辑重构方法，聚焦于Kossakowski的结构性洞见：将马尔可夫性（Markovianity）、完全正性（complete positivity）、迹保持性（trace preservation）以及量子动力学半群（quantum dynamical semigroups）的无穷小结构相结合，系统性推导GKLS生成元的标准形式。

Result: 通过逻辑重构展示了上述四个条件如何自然地导出GKLS生成元的著名形式，确认了Kossakowski在该推导中核心的结构性贡献。

Conclusion: GKLS生成元的形式并非偶然的数学构造，而是马尔可夫性、完全正性、迹保持性与半群无穷小结构之间的必然逻辑结果；此外，作者还通过个人回忆缅怀了Kossakowski的指导作用。

Abstract: This note is written for the special issue of OSID dedicated to the 50th anniversary of the Gorini--Kossakowski--Lindblad--Sudarshan equation. Its purpose is not to give a comprehensive historical review, but rather to reconstruct, in a self-contained way, one logical route leading to the GKLS generator. The emphasis is placed on Kossakowski's structural insight: the combination of Markovianity, complete positivity, trace preservation, and the infinitesimal structure of quantum dynamical semigroups naturally leads to the celebrated form of the generator. I also include a few personal recollections of Andrzej Kossakowski, under whose guidance I spent one year as a postdoctoral researcher in 2003--2004.

</details>


### [148] [Is Exact Markovianity Fundamental Once Time Is Relational?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08595)
*Partha Nandi,Francesco Petruccione*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过有限精度量子钟（finite-resolution quantum clocks）的关系性框架，将马尔可夫开放量子理论（Markovian open quantum theory）推广到相对论性量子开放系统，证明精确的马尔可夫演化是有效而非基础的，只有在关系性粗粒化（relational coarse-graining）后才会出现Gorini-Kossakowski-Lindblad-Sudarshan（GKLS）结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马尔可夫开放量子理论预设了一个外部经典时间参数，但相对论物理学中并不存在根本性的优先时间概念（preferred notion of time）。论文旨在通过关系性方法解决这一张力，使开放量子动力学与相对论框架自洽。

Method: 利用Schwinger-Tomonaga形式体系（Schwinger-Tomonaga formalism），在时空超曲面（spacetime hypersurfaces）上推导协变主方程（covariant master equation）。通过有限精度量子钟实现关系性描述，并分析环境关联（environmental correlations）与时钟涨落（clock fluctuations）对动力学的影响。

Result: 所得到的约化动力学（reduced dynamics）即使在局部相互作用下也普遍是非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的。环境关联和时钟涨落共同生成记忆核（memory kernel）；GKLS结构仅出现在关系性粗粒化之后。在锐时钟极限（sharp-clock limit）下，该形式体系退化为Anastopoulos-Hu引力退相干方程（gravitational decoherence equation）。

Conclusion: 精确的马尔可夫演化是有效而非基础的，其出现依赖于关系性粗粒化过程。该工作为将开放量子系统理论纳入相对论性框架提供了形式化基础。

Abstract: Markovian open quantum theory assumes evolution with respect to an external classical time parameter, yet no preferred notion of time exists fundamentally in relativistic physics. We resolve this tension by formulating relativistic open quantum dynamics relationally through finite-resolution quantum clocks. Using the Schwinger-Tomonaga formalism, we derive a covariant master equation directly on spacetime hypersurfaces and show that the resulting reduced dynamics is generically non-Markovian even for local interactions. Environmental correlations and clock fluctuations jointly generate the memory kernel, while the Gorini-Kossakowski-Lindblad-Sudarshan (GKLS) structure emerges only after relational coarse-graining, implying that exact Markovian evolution is effective rather than fundamental. In the sharp-clock limit, the formalism reduces to the Anastopoulos-Hu gravitational decoherence equation.

</details>


### [149] [Hidden Conformal Boundary Data in Finite-Temperature Stabilizer Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08606)
*Reyhaneh Khasseh,M. A. Rajabpour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究开放临界量子自旋链的有限温度稳定子Rényi熵（finite-temperature stabilizer Rényi entropy），通过将其约化为单个Pfaffian（Pfaffian）并揭示其块Toeplitz–Hankel结构，在多个温度区间提取了大规模标度行为，发现该熵的标度函数为八级eta商（level-eight eta quotient），揭示了隐藏的类缺陷共形数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限温度下开放临界量子自旋链中稳定子Rényi熵的性质，该可观测量在Rényi指数为二分之一时可探测热Pauli弦期望值的分布，并可通过有限温关联矩阵（correlation matrix）的平方子式绝对值之和表示，但其指数级求和需要精确约化方法才能进一步分析标度行为。

Method: 将稳定子Rényi熵的指数级求和精确约化为单个Pfaffian，利用Pfaffian表示揭示出块Toeplitz–Hankel结构，从而在多个热区间提取大尺度标度行为；在逆温度与系统尺寸成比例的交叉窗口中，将稳定子熵分解为饱和广延贡献和普适有限尺寸标度函数。

Result: 该标度函数是八级eta商，而非通常的自由边界Majorana热因子（ordinary free-boundary Majorana thermal factor）。这一偏差在低温下指数级隐藏，但在高温交叉区起主导作用，给出了Pauli弦期望值权重谱的Cardy-like渐近行为。

Conclusion: 有限温度稳定子熵揭示了普通热力学探针无法探测到的隐藏类缺陷共形数据，表明稳定子熵是一种超越常规热力学量的信息理论诊断工具。

Abstract: We study the finite-temperature stabilizer Rényi entropy of the open critical quantum spin chains. At Rényi index one half, this observable probes the distribution of thermal Pauli-string expectation values and can be written as a sum over absolute values of all square minors of a finite-temperature correlation matrix for the transverse-field Ising chain. We show that this exponentially large sum is exactly reducible to a single Pfaffian. The Pfaffian representation reveals a block Toeplitz--Hankel structure and allows us to extract the large-size scaling in several thermal regimes. In the crossover window where the inverse temperature is proportional to the system size, the stabilizer entropy factorizes into a saturated extensive contribution and a universal finite-size scaling function. We find that this scaling function is a level-eight eta quotient, rather than the ordinary free-boundary Majorana thermal factor. The deviation is exponentially hidden at low temperature but controls the high-temperature crossover, where it gives a Cardy-like asymptotic for the Pauli-string expectation-weight spectrum. These results show that finite-temperature stabilizer entropy reveals hidden defect-like conformal data invisible to ordinary thermodynamic probes.

</details>


### [150] [Relativistic Effects in Spin Correlations Induced by QED Scattering and Wigner Rotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08995)
*Juan D. Fonseca,B. Hiller,I. G. da Paz,M. Sampaio*

Main category: quant-ph

Method: 在质心系（center-of-mass frame）以及洛伦兹推动系（Lorentz-boosted frame，其中出现Wigner旋转）中，分别对e⁻e⁻→e⁻e⁻和e⁻e⁻C→e⁻e⁻C过程进行分析；通过对散射振幅进行非相对论近似，提取出偶极-偶极和电流-偶极相互作用；利用von Neumann熵（von Neumann entropy）的变化来表征自旋关联的演化。

Abstract: We study the relativistic nature of the interactions that, at tree level, generate spin correlations between two electrons in Møller scattering, as well as in an extended process involving a witness particle $C$. The corresponding processes, $e^{-}e^{-}\rightarrow e^{-}e^{-}$ and $e^{-}e^{-}C\rightarrow e^{-}e^{-}C$, are analyzed both in the center-of-mass frame and, for the former process, in a Lorentz-boosted frame where Wigner rotations arise. It is found that, through a nonrelativistic approximation of the scattering amplitudes, dipole-dipole and current-dipole interactions are responsible for the emergence of these correlations. In Wigner rotations, the invariance of entropy under local unitary transformations is maintained at the expense of the emergence of quantum coherence in the density matrix at large rapidities. As a consequence, the final states of both particles are evaluated and shown to encode information about the scattering process through their spin expectation values. This framework is then used to comment on the correlations in the inelastic process $e^{-}e^{+}\rightarrowμ^{-}μ^{+}$, for which some research has reported differing results.

Abstract: Metastability in many-body quantum systems and its associated exponentially-long timescales have been the subject of considerable recent interest. Examples include boundary-driven interacting spin chains, bosonic lattice models and driven-dissipative collective spin models.
