<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索参数驱动纵向耦合超导量子比特系统中纠缠动力学的非平凡机制，特别是超越标准旋波近似（rotating-wave approximation）的纠缠产生与操控方式。

Method: 采用Floquet理论（Floquet theory）与精确数值模拟分析系统时间演化，并运用广义Van Vleck近简并微扰论（generalized Van Vleck near-degenerate perturbation theory）推导有效解析描述。

Result: 发现纠缠产生机制源于多光子共振条件下周期驱动混合了两个初始可分离的本征态；持续纠缠源于与初始基态重叠最大的主导Floquet态（Floquet states）的杂化；纠缠度可通过驱动振幅有效调控，特定振幅下纠缠完全被抑制，即相干纠缠破坏。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical generation of entanglement in a system of two superconducting qubits coupled through a parametrically driven longitudinal interaction. Using Floquet theory and exact numerical simulations, we analyze the time evolution of the system initialized in a separable ground state. Our results reveal a nontrivial mechanism for entanglement generation, fundamentally distinct from the conventional resonant excitation to an entangled eigenstate. We show that this mechanism emerges when two initially separable eigenstates are mixed by the periodic driving under multiphoton resonance conditions. Since the effect cannot be captured within a standard rotating-wave approximation, we employ generalized Van Vleck near-degenerate perturbation theory to derive an effective analytical description. Within this framework, we demonstrate that the sustained entanglement originates from the hybridization of the dominant Floquet states, namely those with the largest overlap with the initial ground state. Furthermore, the degree of entanglement can be efficiently controlled through the driving amplitude. In particular, for specific amplitudes, the entanglement is fully suppressed. We term this phenomenon as coherent destruction of entanglement.

### [154] [Quantum resource localizability transitions in deep thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08756)
*Xiaozhou Feng,Chang Liu,Zihan Cheng,Wen Wei Ho,Matteo Ippoliti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究量子资源约束如何影响“深热化”（deep thermalization）现象——即对量子多体态进行部分测量后产生的普适局域波函数分布。通过建立基于量子资源理论（QRT）的统一框架，发现了两类QRT：平滑局域化（SL）QRT与阈值局域化（TL）QRT，并将这一二分性归因于“块锐化”（block sharpening）的信息论机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子资源（如非稳定化能力（non-stabilizerness）、相干性（coherence）、不对称性（asymmetry）、虚数性（imaginarity）和非高斯性（non-Gaussianity））对量子信息处理至关重要，但其全局丰度的约束如何重塑深热化中的局域波函数分布这一问题尚未被系统理解。

Method: 在一般量子资源理论框架下发展了一个统一的深热化分析框架；将每种QRT解释为希尔伯特空间中不同“块”之间的相干性（coherence），进而提出“块锐化”机制来解释局域资源含量的行为。

Result: QRT可划分为两类：SL QRT中局域后测量态的资源含量随全局资源密度连续变化，产生连续可调的波函数分布；TL QRT中局域资源含量在临界全局资源阈值处从不连续地跃变为近最大值，产生从无资源“深遍历性破缺”分布到资源ful最大随机分布的尖锐相变。该理论定量预测了所有研究QRT的相边界，并通过大量数值模拟验证。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了零速率量子纠错码中新的“魔法”（magic）相变——此前被认为仅在有限速率下发生，并为基于后测量态系综的量子资源认证协议提供了新的启示。

Abstract: We investigate how quantum resource constraints affect deep thermalization, the emergence of universal local wavefunction distributions from partial measurements of a quantum many-body state. Quantum resources, such as non-stabilizerness (magic), coherence, asymmetry, imaginarity, and non-Gaussianity, are essential for quantum information processing, and constraints on their global abundance can reshape these emergent distributions. To address this question, we develop a unified framework for deep thermalization within general quantum resource theories (QRTs). Our central result is that QRTs fall into two classes: ``smoothly localizable'' (SL) QRTs, where the resource content of local post-measurement states changes continuously with the global resource density, set by the initial state and measurement basis, yielding continuously tunable wavefunction distributions; and ``threshold localizable'' (TL) QRTs, where the local resource content jumps discontinuously from minimal to near-maximal past a critical global resource threshold, producing a sharp transition between a resourceless, ``deep-ergodicity breaking'' distribution and a resourceful, maximally random one. We trace this SL-TL dichotomy to an information-theoretic mechanism, block sharpening: by viewing each QRT as coherence between blocks in Hilbert space, we show that the local resource content depends on the measurement's ability to collapse an initial superposition into a single resourceless block. Our theory is analytically tractable and quantitatively predicts the phase boundaries across all studied QRTs, which we validate with extensive numerical simulations. Finally, we highlight two consequences: a novel magic transition in zero-rate quantum error-correcting codes--previously believed to occur only at finite rates--and new implications for quantum resource certification protocols based on post-measurement state ensembles.

### [155] [Graph Neural Networks for Fast Operator Selection in Adaptive VQE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08794)
*Javad Vahedi,Hadi H. Arefi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出GNN-VQE方法，利用图神经网络（graph neural network）替代传统ADAPT-VQE中耗时的全池梯度扫描，通过预测纠缠算符实现自适应变分量子算法的加速，在保持能量精度的同时大幅降低经典计算开销，并验证了其在自旋链和分子基准上的可迁移性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ADAPT-VQE等自适应变分量子算法虽能避免过大的参数空间，但每步迭代需扫描整个算子池（operator pool），其经典计算成本与池大小呈线性关系（scales linearly with pool size），成为处理长程相互作用系统或大规模算子集时的主要瓶颈。

Method: 将自适应算子选择重新表述为基于图的决策问题（graph-based decision problem），引入图神经网络（GNN）策略，直接从相互作用图（interaction graph）和状态依赖可观测量（state-dependent observables）预测下一个纠缠算符。训练数据来自无序长程自旋链的精确模拟，以梯度大小（gradient magnitudes）作为监督信号。

Result: GNN策略准确复现了基于贪心梯度选择规则的主导结构，显著优于仅依赖相互作用强度的启发式方法。集成到VQE工作流后，GNN-VQE的能量误差接近标准ADAPT-VQE，同时大幅减少全池梯度评估次数。在分子基准（LiH和BeH₂）上，GNN作为候选短列表生成器（shortlist generator）效果显著：仅对少数GNN提名候选进行精确重评分（exact rescoring），即可在仅搜索极小部分算子池的情况下获得接近oracle的卷展行为（rollout behavior）。

Abstract: Adaptive variational quantum algorithms like ADAPT-VQE construct tailored ansätze by iteratively selecting operators from a pool using gradient-based criteria. While this avoids oversized parameter spaces, repeatedly scanning the full pool incurs a classical cost that scales linearly with pool size-a major bottleneck for systems with long-range interactions or large operator sets. Here, we reformulate adaptive operator selection as a graph-based decision problem and introduce a graph neural network (GNN) policy that predicts the next entangling operator directly from the interaction graph and state-dependent observables. Training data are generated from exact simulations of disordered long-range spin chains, using gradient magnitudes as supervision signals. The learned policy accurately reproduces the dominant structure of the greedy gradient-based selection rule, significantly outperforming heuristics based solely on interaction strength. Integrated into a variational quantum eigensolver (VQE) workflow, this GNN-VQE approach achieves energy errors close to standard ADAPT-VQE while drastically reducing full-pool gradient evaluations. To test transferability beyond spin models, we evaluate the policy on small active-space molecular benchmarks (LiH and BeH_$2$). We find the GNN is highly effective as a shortlist generator: exact rescoring over just a few GNN-proposed candidates recovers near-oracle rollout behavior while searching only a small fraction of the pool. These results demonstrate that adaptive circuit construction contains learnable structure that can be exploited to accelerate variational quantum algorithms.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 硬件-算法协同仿真能够有效识别硅量子点处理器在VQE任务中的噪声容忍边界。基于含噪能量估计完整分布的统计后处理（statistical post-processing）有望进一步提升计算精度，为近量子器件的噪声缓解策略提供理论指导。

Abstract: Quantum computers offer a route to outperform classical methods in tasks such as molecular simulation, motivating hybrid algorithms like the Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) for near-term devices. Silicon spin qubits are a promising platform for scalable quantum computation, but their performance is limited by hardware imperfections -- most notably charge-noise-induced potential fluctuations and static miscalibration of gate-electrode voltages -- which degrade quantum gate fidelities and, ultimately, algorithmic accuracy. Here we develop a hardware-algorithm co-simulation framework for silicon quantum-dot processors that links 3D electrostatics to effective $g$-factors and exchange couplings, and propagates voltage-level noise through realistic control pulses. Using VQE for $\mathrm{H}_2$ ground-state energy estimation as a circuit-level testbed, we study both static scaling/offset errors on the gate-electrode voltages and stochastic fluctuations modeled as random-telegraph noise with tunable amplitudes and switching times. At the gate level, we show that exchange-based two-qubit gates are roughly an order of magnitude more sensitive to these types of noise than ESR-driven single-qubit rotations. Quantum process tomography and Kraus-operator analysis further distinguish coherent and incoherent contributions and quantify the fraction of error that is, in principle, correctable by a compensating unitary. Embedding these noise models into the VQE circuit, we identify regimes of miscalibration strength and noise switching time compatible with chemically accurate energy estimates, and discuss how statistical post-processing based on the full distribution of noisy energy estimates could further improve accuracy.

### [157] [Sambe Approach to Floquet-Lindblad Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09727)
*Andriani Keliri,Marco Schirò*

TL;DR: 本文研究了由时间周期性Lindblad主方程描述的受驱开放量子系统，通过Floquet理论在扩展的Sambe-Liouville空间中构建了与时间无关的有效Floquet Lindbladian，并提出矩阵连分式方法非微扰地求和多光子过程，进而用于计算关联函数、共振荧光谱及量子点器件的电流-电压特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在闭合系统中，时间周期性驱动可由与时间无关的有效Floquet哈密顿量（Floquet Hamiltonian）描述，这是Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）的基础。然而在开放量子系统中，由于演化非酉性（non-unitary），有效时间无关Floquet Lindbladian的存在性并不显然，因此需要严格构造方法。

Method: 利用Floquet理论（Floquet theory），在扩展的Sambe-Liouville空间（extended Sambe-Liouville space）中构造了定义良好的时间无关Floquet Lindbladian，将时间依赖问题转化为静态非厄米本征值问题。针对谐振驱动情形，引入矩阵连分式方法（matrix continued fraction method），非微扰地求和多光子过程，构建仅作用于物理Liouville空间的有效Floquet Lindbladian。利用解折展开形式（resolvent formalism）给出开放量子系统关联函数的谱Floquet表示。

Result: 该方法相比于其他高频展开（high-frequency expansions）的优势在于能一次性给出整无穷级数展开。应用方面，计算了线性极化场中耗散二能级系统的共振荧光谱（resonance fluorescence spectrum），以及含泵浦与损耗的参数驱动量子点（parametrically driven quantum dot）的谱函数和电流-电压特性曲线（current-voltage characteristics）。

Conclusion: 该工作为时间周期性驱动开放量子系统提供了一套系统的非微扰理论框架，能够高效构造有效Floquet Lindbladian并计算多种可观测量的谱性质，拓展了Floquet工程在耗散系统中的应用范围。

Abstract: We study driven and open quantum systems described by a time-periodic Lindblad master equation. In closed systems, the stroboscopic dynamics can always be described by an effective time-independent Floquet Hamiltonian; this idea is the basis of Floquet engineering. However, in the presence of dissipation, the existence of an effective time-independent Floquet Lindbladian is not guaranteed due to the non-unitary nature of the evolution. Using Floquet theory, we construct a well-defined time-independent Floquet Lindbladian in an extended Sambe-Liouville space, transforming the initial time-dependent problem to a static and non-Hermitian eigenvalue problem. For harmonic driving, we introduce a matrix continued fraction method to nonperturbatively resum multiphoton processes and construct an effective Floquet Lindbladian acting only on the physical Liouville space. Compared to other high-frequency expansions, this method has the advantage of providing the whole infinite series expansion at once. Using a resolvent formalism, we show how to obtain a spectral Floquet representation of correlation functions of an open quantum system. As an application, we consider a dissipating two-level system in a linearly polarized field and calculate its resonance fluorescence spectrum. Furthermore, we consider a parametrically driven quantum dot with pump and loss for which we calculate its spectral function and current-voltage characteristics.

</details>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [158] [Jet Bundles as Higher-Order Polarised $k$-Contact Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09263)
*Javier de Lucas*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于纤维化流形 $π:E\to Q$，其 $r$ 阶射流丛 $J^rπ$ 上的Cartan分布 $C^r_π$ 是一个 $N^r_π$-接触分布（$N^r_π$-contact distribution），其中 $N^r_π=m\binom{n+r-1}{r-1}$，并基于此建立了极化的 $k$-接触几何与有限阶射流几何之间的等价性，给出了射流空间（jet geometry）的统一几何框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 射流几何（jet geometry）中许多构造（如Bäcklund变换）在传统的单一射流坐标表示下表述笨拙，缺乏统一的几何语言；同时，$k$-接触几何（$k$-contact geometry）与射流丛Cartan分布之间的内在联系尚未被系统揭示，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过自然局部构造 $N^r_π$-接触形式，证明Cartan分布为 $N^r_π$-接触分布；引入新的极化的 $k$-接触分布类别，定义“射流型极化”（polarisation of jet type），并证明极化 $k$-接触流形与有限阶射流丛局部等价的充要条件是其极化为射流型。

Result: 建立了极化 $k$-接触几何与有限阶射流几何的等价性：最高阶垂直极化、符号空间（symbol spaces）、垂直与水平微分、完整子流形（holonomic submanifolds）、PDE初值条件等均可通过 $k$-接触几何重建；解对应极化Legendre子流形（polarised Legendrian submanifolds），射流延拓对应极化Legendre延拓，适配坐标为 $k$-接触Darboux坐标。

Conclusion: 该形式化为射流几何提供了更深层的几何理解与统一的本质语言，简化了Bäcklund变换等复杂构造，将射流理论推广至新问题，并为PDE提供通用的约化方法，可应用于数学物理相关PDE。

Abstract: Let $π:E\to Q$ be a fibred manifold, with $\dim Q=n$ and rank $m$. We prove that the Cartan distribution $C^r_π$ on $J^rπ$ is an $N^r_π$-contact distribution, where $N^r_π=m\binom{n+r-1}{r-1}$, by giving a natural local construction of an $N^r_π$-contact form. This recovers the canonical structure of $J^rπ$ and the Spencer contractions, among other structures. It also yields a natural local Hamiltonian structure on $J^rπ$, recovering and extending the standard theory of characteristics to general Lie symmetries of the Cartan distribution.
  We introduce new classes of polarisations for $k$-contact distributions. This leads to our main recognition theorem, which shows that a polarised $k$-contact manifold is locally equivalent to a finite-order jet bundle with its Cartan distribution precisely when its polarisation is of jet type. This characterises finite-order jet geometry as polarised $N_π^r$-contact geometry of jet type. Moreover, the highest-order vertical polarisation, the symbol spaces, the vertical and horizontal differentials, holonomic submanifolds, and initial conditions for differential equations are reconstructed via $k$-contact geometry. For instance, adapted coordinates become $k$-contact Darboux coordinates, solutions of PDEs are treated as polarised Legendrian submanifolds, jet prolongations are recovered as polarised Legendrian prolongations, and so on.
  The resulting formalism gives a deeper geometric understanding of several parts of jet geometry, provides a uniform intrinsic language for constructions that are awkward in a single fixed jet presentation, such as Bäcklund transformations, and allows jet theory to be extended to new problems. In particular, our techniques provide very general reduction methods for PDEs. The results are applied to PDEs with mathematical and physical relevance.

</details>

### [159] [Long-term laser frequency stabilization with an FPGA-controlled scanning cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09720)
*R. Forti,R. Panza,A. Muzi Falconi,S. Sbernardori,A. Vardé,M. Marinelli,A. Carini,F. Scazza*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于FPGA的扫描转移腔锁定（STCL）方案，利用连续扫描的法布里-珀罗腔（Fabry-Perot cavity）实现对多台激光器相对于单台参考激光器的同步频率稳定，并通过AOM快速扫描技术实现亚百kHz级长期稳定性。该系统在PB原子磁光阱中验证了亚MHz级的绝对频率稳定度，具有模块化、低成本、开源等优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扫描转移腔锁定（STCL）方案在同时稳定多台激光器时存在延迟高、扩展性差的问题；标准压电陶瓷（piezo）驱动的腔长扫描方案锁定带宽有限、本征噪声较高。本文旨在利用FPGA架构的低延迟特性解决上述瓶颈，并探索基于声光调制器（AOM）频率调制的快速扫描新方法。

Method: 采用FPGA架构在同一器件内同时执行腔体扫描（cavity scanning）、峰值检测（peak detection）和反馈驱动（feedback actuation），为多台激光器提供独立控制回路；引入基于AOM频率调制的快速扫描方案，替代传统的压电陶瓷腔长扫描，以降低检测延迟、提高有效锁定带宽（locking bandwidth）。系统基于开源PyRPL固件包，运行于STEMlab Red Pitaya平台。

Result: 通过外差测量（heterodyne measurements）分析了从短时间（<1秒）到长时间（约20小时）的锁定性能；在镱原子磁光阱（magneto-optical trap）中通过原子光谱（atomic spectroscopy）验证了端到端锁定性能，实现了在可见光波段约150 nm跨度上的亚MHz绝对频率稳定度（sub-MHz absolute frequency stability），持续数小时。基于AOM快速扫描的方案实现了亚100 kHz长期稳定性。

Conclusion: 该FPGA-STCL架构以模块化、低成本和易实现的特点，为现有STCL和锁定腔方案提供了一种紧凑灵活的替代方案；在不依赖任何原子参考（atomic reference）的情况下，即可支持现代冷原子实验的激光稳定需求。

Abstract: We present an FPGA-based implementation of a scanning transfer cavity lock (STCL) for laser frequency stabilization, allowing for the simultaneous stabilization of multiple laser sources with respect to a single reference laser by means of a continuously scanned Fabry-Perot cavity. By exploiting the FPGA architecture to simultaneously perform cavity scanning, peak detection, and feedback actuation, we minimize latency and allow independent control loops for several lasers within a single device, offering direct scalability. The system performance is analyzed through heterodyne measurements from short ($<1\,$s) to long ($\sim20\,$hours) timescales. The end-to-end locking performance is validated through atomic spectroscopy of ytterbium atoms in a magneto-optical trap, demonstrating sub-MHz absolute frequency stability over several hours for the stability transfer across $\sim 150\,$nm in the visible-wavelength range. Importantly, we demonstrate a novel fast-scanning approach based on acousto-optic modulator (AOM) frequency modulation, enabled by the low detection latency of our FPGA implementation. This increases significantly the effective locking bandwidth and reduces the intrinsic noise of the system with respect to standard piezo-actuated scanning of the cavity length, allowing to reach sub-$100\,$kHz long-term stability and offering perspectives for laser-line narrowing. Owing to its modularity, low cost and ease of implementation within the open-source PyRPL firmware package for the STEMlab Red Pitaya platform, our architecture offers a compact and flexible alternative to existing STCL and locked-cavity implementations, providing a practical approach to the operation of a state-of-the-art cold-atom experiment without relying on any atomic references for laser stabilization.

### [160] [Moduli spaces of type II twists](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07737)
*Fabian Hahner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对平坦背景下的IIA型超引力（type IIA supergravity）中的扭转超荷（twisting supercharges）进行了完整分类，通过与IIB型结果的结合完成了II型超引力扭转模空间（moduli space of twists）的描述，并探讨了这些扭转的十一维降维起源、世界sheet（worldsheet）对应以及T-对偶（T-duality）关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在II型超引力中，扭转超荷的分类尚不完整，IIA型的情况尤其缺乏系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，为II型超引力的扭转模空间提供完整描述，并建立其与超弦理论（superstring theory）中世界sheet扭转及T-对偶的关联。

Method: 通过确定十维(1,1)超庞加莱代数（super Poincaré algebra）中在旋量群（Spin group）作用下平方为零的元素的轨道（orbits），对平坦背景下的IIA型超引力扭转超荷进行完全分类。结合IIB型的已有结果完成II型超引力扭转模空间的整体描述，并利用超弦的纯旋量形式（pure spinor formulation）将靶空间（target space）分类与世界sheet扭转相联系。

Result: 给出了IIA型超引力中扭转超荷的完整分类，完成了II型超引力扭转模空间的描述。识别了混合A/B模型（mixed A/B models）的超引力对应物，并给出了联系IIA与IIB型扭转的T-对偶作用。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了IIA与IIB型超引力扭转之间的系统联系，并为从超弦理论到超引力的扭转结构提供了统一框架，深化了对II型超引力与超弦理论中扭转现象的理解。

Abstract: We provide a complete classification of twisting supercharges for type IIA supergravity in a flat background by determining the orbits of square-zero elements in the (1,1) super Poincaré algebra in ten dimensions under the action of the Spin group. Together with recent results for type IIB, this completes the description of the moduli space of twists for type II supergravities. Further, we discuss the origins of these twists as dimensional reductions from eleven dimensions. Using the pure spinor formulation of the superstring, we relate the target space classification to worldsheet twists and identify supergravity counterparts of mixed A/B models. Finally, we work out the action of T-duality that relates twists of type IIA with those of type IIB.

### [161] [New Exotic Operators in the Spectrum of Wilson Lines in General Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07738)
*Daniele Artico,Carlo Meneghelli,Michele Savi,Rudolfs Treilis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现，在足够丰富的表示（representation）中，Wilson 线（Wilson lines）支持一类新的算符插入（operator insertions）。对于 $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 中的半 BPS 线，许多此类算符具有位移超多重态（displacement supermultiplet）的量子数，其维度为 1 的超原初算符（superprimary）定义了缺陷理论（defect theory）的自然形变。通过分析相应的贝塔函数（beta function）并关联至特定的 OPE 系数，证明这些形变是边缘相关的（marginally relevant），并通过弱耦合四点函数计算加以佐证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wilson 线是规范理论（gauge theories）的基本探针，但此前对其上可支持的算符插入类型的认识可能尚不充分，特别是在表示足够丰富时的情形。

Method: 分析半 BPS Wilson 线上新算符插入的量子数与位移超多重态的对应关系；通过计算关联的贝塔函数并将其与特定 OPE 系数建立联系，判断形变的重整化群（renormalization group）行为；对任意规范群（gauge group）和表示进行弱耦合（weak-coupling）四点函数计算以验证结论。

Result: 对于足够丰富的表示，Wilson 线支持一类新算符插入；这些形变是边缘相关的（marginally relevant）；弱耦合四点函数计算结果支持这一发现。

Conclusion: 在足够丰富的表示下，Wilson 线上的新算符诱导的缺陷形变是边缘相关的，这一结论通过弱耦合计算得到了验证。

Abstract: Wilson lines are fundamental probes of gauge theories. We show that, in sufficiently rich representations, they support a large new class of operator insertions. For half-BPS lines in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM many of these operators have the quantum numbers of the displacement supermultiplet. Their dimension-one superprimaries define natural deformations of the defect theory. By analyzing the associated beta functions, and relating them to specific OPE coefficients, we show that the deformations are marginally relevant. We support our finding with a weak-coupling computation of the four-point function of these operators for any gauge group and representation.

</details>


### [162] [Non-uniqueness of boundary-value problems in Renormalization Group flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07868)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Zois Gyftopoulos,Aaron Held*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了重整化群（renormalization group）流中的边值问题（boundary-value problems），发现当β函数的雅可比矩阵（Jacobian matrix）具有复数本征值时，边值问题可能不具备唯一解，并提供了相应的诊断工具及两个物理实例（标准模型和渐进安全量子引力中的爱因斯坦-希尔伯特截断）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上重整化群（renormalization group）流被视为初值问题（initial-value problem），而实际物理情境中不同耦合常数（couplings）可能在不同能标上受到约束，因此需要研究RG流中的边值问题（boundary-value problems）及其解的存在性与唯一性。

Method: 将重整化群（renormalization group）流从初值问题框架拓展为边值问题（boundary-value problem）框架，分析β函数的雅可比矩阵（Jacobian matrix）本征值对解唯一性的影响，并开发了一种适用于多耦合系统的非唯一性（non-uniqueness）诊断工具。

Result: 与提供n个耦合的n个条件的初值问题不同，提供n个耦合的n个条件的边值问题并不总是具有唯一解。当雅可比矩阵（Jacobian matrix）存在复数本征值（complex eigenvalues）时，边值问题可能出现非唯一性（non-uniqueness）。

Conclusion: 提供了诊断重整化群（renormalization group）边值问题非唯一性的工具，并给出了两个可能具有物理相关性的实例：标准模型（Standard Model）中的情形，以及渐进安全量子引力（asymptotically safe quantum gravity）中爱因斯坦-希尔伯特截断（Einstein-Hilbert truncation）内的情形。

Abstract: The Renormalization Group flow connects microscopic to macroscopic descriptions of a system and is therefore typically considered as an initial-value problem. Motivated by situations in which different couplings within a system of Renormalization Group equations are constrained at different scales, we instead consider boundary-value problems in Renormalization Group flows. We find that, unlike initial-value problems which provide $n$ conditions for $n$ couplings, boundary-value problems which provide $n$ conditions for $n$ couplings do not always have a unique solution. When the Jacobian matrix, i.e., the matrix of first derivatives of beta functions, has complex eigenvalues, boundary-value problems may be non-unique. We provide a diagnostic tool for non-uniqueness in systems with many couplings. We also provide two examples with potential relevance for physics, namely within the Standard Model as well as within the Einstein-Hilbert truncation of asymptotically safe quantum gravity.

</details>


### [163] [Spin-charge deconfinement and emergent $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ structure from a self-consistent dressing of Fierz-complete $(1+1)$d Dirac fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07955)
*L. Haddad,K. Gonzales,J. Kahanek,M. Kolding,J. Maguire,V. Palombi,H. Truelson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在(1+1)维配对狄拉克费米子的自旋-电荷分离理论基础上，构建了Fierz完备四费米子模型的自洽 dressing 形式，证明了一个平凡化定理（trivialization theorem），统一了自旋-电荷分离、半无限Wilson线 dressing 和平坦联络的holonomy三种非微扰构造。模型中的手征-双费米子转变被识别为退禁闭转变，并建立了与AdS₃/CFT₂对偶的结构对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已有的(1+1)维配对狄拉克费米子自旋-电荷分离（spin-charge separation）推导基础上，将该结果推广至Fierz完备的四费米子模型，并更详细地解析手征-双费米子相结构（chiral-difermion phase structure）。

Method: 采用自洽 dressing 变换 ψ(x) = U(x)χ(x)，构造复合联络（composite connection）A_μ^{dress} = i(∂_μU)U^{-1}，该联络编码狄拉克算符局域平凡化的障碍程度；在此基础上证明平凡化定理（trivialization theorem），并利用闭boost扇区Wilson圈（Wilson loops）诊断退禁闭转变。

Result: 三个非微扰构造（自旋-电荷分离、半无限Wilson线 dressing、平坦联络的holonomy）被统一证明；模型的手征、双费米子和中间三个区域由 emergent sl(2,R) 规范场联系；手征-双费米子转变是自旋与电荷自由度的退禁闭转变（deconfinement transition），并计算了手征相中Wilson圈的弦张力（string tension）；序参量流形呈双曲形式 ρ² - |Δ|² = σ²，推广为AdS₃。

Conclusion: 该模型为Faddeev–Niemi关于自旋-电荷分离与禁闭之间联系的猜想提供了具体实现；dressed模型与AdS₃/CFT₂对偶的运动学阶段存在明确的结构匹配，提出该模型可能实现AdS₃ sigma模型的逆Pohlmeyer约化（inverse Pohlmeyer reduction）。

Abstract: Building on a recent derivation of spin-charge separation in $(1+1)$d paired Dirac fermions~\cite{Haddad2024}, we develop a self-consistent dressing $ψ(x) = U(x)χ(x)$ for the full Fierz-complete four-fermion model, extending that result and providing a more detailed resolution of the chiral-difermion phase structure. A key feature of this approach is that the composite connection $A_μ^{\rm dress} = i(\partial_μU)U^{-1}$ encodes obstructions to local trivialization of the Dirac operator, i.e., the degree to which the background can be absorbed into the dressing. Using this fact, we prove a trivialization theorem under which three nonperturbative constructions are unified: spin-charge separation in correlated fermion systems, half-infinite Wilson-line dressing in gauge theory, and the holonomy of flat connections. Our approach shows that the three regimes of our model (chiral, difermion, intermediate), are then tied together by an emergent $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ gauge field that binds the spin and charge degrees of freedom. In particular, the chiral-difermion transition is a deconfinement transition for these degrees of freedom, diagnosed by closed boost-sector Wilson loops that develop an area law in the chiral phase for which we compute the associated string tension. This provides a concrete realization of the conjectured Faddeev--Niemi link between spin-charge separation and confinement. We close with a unifying geometric picture in which the order-parameter manifold takes hyperbolic form $ρ^2 - |Δ|^2 = σ^2$, promoted to $\mathrm{AdS}_3 \cong \mathrm{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$ on inclusion of the charge and difermion phases. The structural matching to the kinematic stage of $\mathrm{AdS}_3/\mathrm{CFT}_2$ is identified explicitly, with the conjecture that the dressed model realizes the inverse Pohlmeyer reduction of the $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ sigma model.

### [164] [Weyl conformal geometry vs Riemannian geometry of Weyl invariant dressed metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08080)
*D. M. Ghilencea,V. -M. Mandric*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文论证了Weyl共形几何（Weyl conformal geometry）作为Weyl群（膨胀与庞加莱对称性）规范理论（如Weyl二次引力及Weyl-Dirac-Born-Infeld作用量）的自然底层几何，并通过膨胀Wilson线（Wilson line of dilatations）将Weyl规范对称性映射到黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）中非局域穿 dressed 度规（dressed metric）的视角，揭示了两种几何在对称相下的非局域等价性，以及在规范场退耦后爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）的恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Weyl共形几何作为量子引力候选理论（如Weyl二次引力与WDBI作用量）的底层几何结构，这些理论是无Weyl反常（Weyl-anomaly-free）的；同时，从更熟悉的黎曼几何角度理解Weyl规范对称性，并澄清两种几何之间的映射关系。

Method: 通过膨胀Wilson线构建Weyl规范不变的非局域 dressed 场，从而将Weyl几何视为非局域 dressed 度规（$g_{μν}^*$）的黎曼几何；利用该非局域映射，将Weyl二次引力与WDBI作用量在对称相下用黎曼几何语言重写。

Result: Weyl二次引力与WDBI作用量在$d$维下保持Weyl规范不变，并在非局域 dressed 度规定义的黎曼几何中具有相同表达式；Weyl规范场（$ω_μ$）的运动方程与度规的 dressing 不对易；当$ω_μ$获得质量并退耦（破缺相）后，对易性与爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量得以恢复。

Conclusion: Weyl共形几何与黎曼几何之间通过非局域 dressing 映射在对称相下等价，且该框架在规范场退耦后自然回归到标准广义相对论；这为无反常量子引力提供了自洽的几何基础。

Abstract: Weyl conformal geometry is the natural underlying geometry of gauge theories of the Weyl group (of dilatations and Poincaré symmetry), such as Weyl quadratic gravity and its generalisation, Weyl-Dirac-Born-Infeld action (WDBI). These gauge theories are Weyl-anomaly-free candidates for quantum gravity. We describe Weyl gauge symmetry from a more familiar Riemannian view of Weyl gauge invariant dressed fields by the Wilson line of dilatations. Weyl geometry can then be seen as Riemannian geometry of non-local dressed metric ($g_{μν}^*$), at the cost of non-commutativity in the UV, also induced by the Wilson line. Then Weyl quadratic gravity and WDBI actions of Weyl geometry, which are Weyl gauge invariant in $d$ dimensions, have the same expression in Riemannian geometry defined by $g^*_{μν}$. This is a non-local map between the two geometries and actions in the symmetric phase. Unlike for the metric, the equation of motion of the Weyl gauge field ($ω_μ$) does not commute with the dressing of the metric. When $ω_μ$ becomes massive and decouples (broken phase), commutativity and Einstein-Hilbert action are recovered.

Once the factor $i$ of the $e^{iS}$ normalization is removed, the contribution is real for real external momentum, which follows from the pairing of complex conjugate terms in the loop integral. Abstract: We study conserved worldsheet charges associated with spacetime supersymmetry in heterotic pure-spinor superstrings on curved ten-dimensional superspace backgrounds. ### [168] [Stochastic Survival near Swampland Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08244)
*Omer Guleryuz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于随机生存理论的框架，将沼泽地（swampland）与紧致化（compactification）数据转化为模场（moduli）在宇宙学时间尺度上的随机生存问题，并通过Doob变换构建条件化漂移，从而在量子引力控制数据与保留在景观侧的历史之间建立随机生存界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沼泽地及紧致化数据指明了有效场论（EFT）控制可能失效的边界，而随机宇宙学则追问哪些历史能在该边界附近存活。本文的目标是将该问题形式化为模场在宇宙学时间尺度上的随机生存问题。

Method: 定义由硬损失面（hard loss surfaces）、软退化轮廓（soft degradation profiles）、有限视界（finite horizons）和随机生成元（stochastic generator）构成的生存概率，其对数为生存作用量（survival action）；运用Doob变换将对数生存代价转换为条件化系综的漂移；通过逆映射检验条件化漂移是否与标量操作损失面（scalar operational loss surface）兼容，并重建其边界法向Doob类。

Result: 在具有非零法向扩散的规则硬边界附近，结果具有普适性：幸存历史产生一个仅由固有距离（proper distance）和法向扩散决定的内向壁响应（inward wall response）。塔/物种截断、弱耦合极限、弦和Kaluza-Klein阈值以及基于势的诊断由此获得随机边界层，而无需引入微观力。

Conclusion: 该构造在量子引力控制数据与保留在控制侧（景观侧）的历史之间建立了一个随机生存界面，为连接沼泽地约束与宇宙学历史提供了形式化工具。

Abstract: Swampland and compactification data tell us where EFT control can fail; stochastic cosmology asks which histories survive near that edge. We turn this question into a survival problem for fluctuating moduli over cosmological time scales. Hard loss surfaces, soft degradation profiles, finite horizons, and a stochastic generator define a survival probability, whose logarithm is the survival action. The Doob transform then converts this logarithmic survival cost into the drift of the ensemble conditioned to remain on the controlled side. Near a regular hard boundary with nonzero normal diffusion, the answer is universal: surviving histories develop an inward wall response fixed only by proper distance and normal diffusion. In this way, tower/species cutoffs, weak-coupling limits, string and Kaluza-Klein thresholds, and potential-based diagnostics acquire stochastic boundary layers without becoming microscopic forces. The inverse map tests when a conditioned drift is compatible with a scalar operational loss surface and reconstructs its boundary-normal Doob class. The construction therefore gives a stochastic survival interface between quantum-gravity control data and the histories that remain on the landscape side of control.

### [170] [An elliptic approach to Reid's fantasy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08427)
*Lara Anderson,James Gray,Richard Nally,Washington Taylor*

Method: 本文在两类最大的已知卡拉比-丘三折叠类（环面超曲面（toric hypersurfaces）和射影空间乘积中的完全交集（complete intersections in products of projective spaces））中，通过收缩纤维化几何中的一个单除数（single divisor）这类简单的几何过渡（geometric transitions），将所有非纤维化卡拉比-丘三折叠连接到纤维化卡拉比-丘三折叠。

Abstract: It is a long-standing problem to prove that the number of distinct topological types of Calabi-Yau threefolds is finite. A related proposition, Reid's fantasy, conjectures that all Calabi-Yau threefolds are connected in a single moduli space through extremal transitions. Finiteness of topological types has been proven for the class of elliptic and genus one fibered Calabi-Yau threefolds, which recently have been shown to constitute the vast majority of known Calabi-Yau threefolds; the moduli space of elliptic CY3's is connected. In this letter, we demonstrate that all non-fibered Calabi-Yau threefolds in two of the largest known classes (toric hypersurfaces and complete intersections in products of projective spaces) are connected to fibered Calabi-Yau threefolds through a simple class of geometric transitions involving the shrinking of a single divisor from a fibered geometry. This suggests that non-fibered Calabi-Yau threefolds are rare special cases that are reached by simplifying fibered Calabi-Yau threefolds, and points to a natural path towards proving finiteness and Reid's fantasy for Calabi-Yau threefolds.

### [171] [Semi-universality of conformal higher-derivative and conformal higher-spin fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08461)

TL;DR: 本文研究自由奇异共形场论（exotic conformal field theories）在半普适极限（semi-universal limit）下的热配分函数（thermal partition function），发现该极限下会出现普适极点及依赖理论的留数函数，并证明该极限可作为探测负扭曲态（negative-twist states）的有效工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we study thermal partition functions of free exotic conformal field theories, focusing on conformal higher-derivative and conformal higher-spin fields, in the semi-universal limit $|ω_i|\rightarrow 1$. It was recently conjectured in \cite{Anand:2025mfh} that, in this limit, the thermal partition function develops universal poles in $(1-|ω_i|)$, while the corresponding residue functions are theory-dependent. We analyze conformal higher-derivative scalar, fermionic, and vector fields in the semi-universal limit. We then extend the study to the Weyl graviton, the Weyl gravitino, and conformal higher-spin fields (CHS) on $S^1_β\times S^3$, using both spectral mode-sum and operator-counting methods. In all cases, we find the expected pole structure, with residue functions whose behavior depends on the presence or absence of negative-twist states. For four-dimensional conformal higher-spin fields, we further reproduce the same residue-pole structure from the one-loop partition function of massless higher-spin fields in thermal AdS$_5$. Finally, we show that the semi-universal limit provides a useful diagnostic of negative-twist states, which indicate violations of ANEC-type bounds in these theories, whereas the traditional high-temperature expansion is insensitive to them.

### [172] [Soft Algebra for ${\cal N}=4$ SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08582)
*Luis F. Alday,Andrew Strominger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为平面 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论（planar N=4 super Yang-Mills）中的散射振幅（scattering amplitude）定义了一种全阶（all-orders）因子化方案，将红外（IR）发散部分和红外有限部分分离，并证明红外有限部分满足未修正的树图级软定理（tree-level soft theorem）以及未变形的树图级 S-代数（S-algebra）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非阿贝尔规范理论（nonabelian gauge theories）中 n 粒子散射振幅存在一个普遍因子化形式，其中红外有限部分编码了更高圈修正。本文旨在为平面 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论给出该因子化的具体全阶定义，并研究红外有限部分的结构与性质。

Method: 论文基于 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论的若干常用假设，包括 BDS 单圈指数化（BDS one-loop exponentiation）的分裂函数（splitting function）以及振幅/威尔逊圈对偶（amplitude/Wilson-loop duality），具体指定了一种全阶因子化定义。

Result: 得到的红外有限部分（A_n^{hard}）满足未经修正的树图级软定理（uncorrected tree-level soft theorem），并且能够表示由软胶子（soft gluon）塔生成的未变形树图级 S-代数（undeformed tree-level S-algebra）。

Conclusion: 该因子化定义在平面 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论中是自洽的，红外有限部分具有树图级的简单行为，表明该体系中软胶子结构在高阶微扰修正下保持未变形的形式。

Abstract: Scattering amplitudes of $n$ particles in nonabelian gauge theories admit factorizations of the general form $\mathcal{A}_n \;=\; \mathcal{A}^{\rm soft}_n \times \mathcal{A}^{\rm hard}_n$, where $\mathcal{A}^{\rm soft}_n$ is IR divergent, while $\mathcal{A}^{\rm hard}_n$ is IR finite and encodes the higher loop corrections to scattering. We specify a particular all-orders definition of this factorization for planar ${\cal N}=4$ super Yang-Mills (SYM) and argue that the resulting $\mathcal{A}_n^{\rm hard}$ obeys an uncorrected tree-level soft theorem. Moreover it furnishes a representation of the undeformed tree-level $\cal S$-algebra generated by a tower of soft gluons. The results follow from several commonly invoked assumptions for ${\cal N}=4$ SYM, including BDS one-loop exponentiation of the splitting function and amplitude/Wilson-loop duality.

### [173] [Self-Gravitating Magnetic Monopoles and Dyons in String-Inspired Models: Structure and Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08603)
*Nick E. Mavromatos,Sarben Sarkar,Dionysios P. Theodosopoulos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在引力背景下，提出由整体单极子（global monopole）诱导的磁单极子（magnetic monopole）与戴恩（dyon）的经典解。通过两种场景——质量less dilaton 场耦合电磁（EM）部门，以及非平凡的Kalb-Ramond（KR）轴子场（axion field）与质量less dilaton场耦合KR与EM部门——实现了这些构型。电磁部门采用Born-Infeld电动力学（Born-Infeld electrodynamics），确保场在核心处的正则性与有限自能。所得解具有确定核心、正ADM质量，并满足所有标准能量条件。此外，在零质量磁单极子极限下证明了最小非零磁荷存在性，并论证了机械稳定性与线性电磁扰动稳定性，戴恩解表现出轴子诱导的双折射螺旋度结构（birefringent helicity structure）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦论启发模型中，整体单极子可诱导磁单极子与戴恩解；已有模型依赖非阿贝尔规范场，而本文探索在引力背景下通过质量less dilaton场与Kalb-Ramond轴子场实现此类构型，并采用Born-Infeld电动力学解决核心奇异性和自能发散问题。

Method: 将质量less dilaton场耦合电磁部门（场景一），或同时引入Kalb-Ramond轴子场与质量less dilaton场耦合KR与电磁部门（场景二），电磁部门采用Born-Infeld电动力学。构型源于全局O(3)对称性自发破缺产生的整体单极子。

Result: 所得解为粒子状构型，具有确定核心、正ADM质量，满足所有标准能量条件；零质量极限下存在最小非零磁荷；机械稳定性满足总力分量有界且径向分量向外；在Gervalle-Volkov框架下，自引力Born-Infeld磁单极子与戴恩解在外部区域对电磁扰动线性稳定，戴恩因轴子诱导混合表现出双折射螺旋度结构。

Conclusion: 文中提出的磁单极子与戴恩解具有良好稳定性与物理合理性，为弦论启发模型中的孤立子（soliton）构型提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We present classical solutions for magnetic monopoles and dyons induced by global monopoles for string-inspired models, in the presence of gravity. Two distinct scenarios are analyzed. In the first, magnetic monopoles arise from the coupling of a non-trivial massless dilaton field to the electromagnetic (EM) sector. In the second, dyonic solutions emerge in the presence of a non-trivial Kalb-Ramond (KR) axion field and a massless dilaton field, which couples the KR and EM sectors. In both models, the monopole and dyon configurations originate from a global monopole associated with the spontaneous breaking of a global O(3) symmetry. The EM sector is described by Born-Infeld electrodynamics, ensuring regularity of the fields at the core of the monopole and a finite self-energy. The resulting solutions represent particle-like configurations with a well-defined core and positive ADM (Arnowitt-Deser-Misner) mass, and are shown to satisfy all standard energy conditions. We also demonstrate the existence of a minimum nonzero magnetic charge in the limiting case of a magnetic monopole with vanishing mass. We also discuss stability criteria for our magnetic-monopole and dyon solutions. We first demonstrate that the mechanical-stability criteria for these solutions are satisified. These require the finiteness of the total force components and also the outward-pointing nature of the radial component, which indicates the avoidance of collapse. Next we analyse the dynamical (linear perturbative) stability of the self-gravitating Born-Infeld monopole and dyon solutions within Einstein-Born--Infeld-dilaton-axion theory in the Gervalle-Volkov framework, and demonstrate that both monopole and dyonic configurations are linearly stable against electromagnetic perturbations in the exterior region, with dyons exhibiting a birefringent helicity structure due to axion-induced mixing.

### [174] [A Lorentzian Gribov no-pole condition for Yang-Mills theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08697)
*M. S. Guimaraes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出闵可夫斯基时空下Gribov无极点条件的替代表述：将Faddeev-Popov算子从欧氏椭圓型问题重新表述为双曲型波动方程的实时间边界值问题，并揭示了静电场势与静磁场背景在到达Gribov视界时的不同频率行为，同时指出Gribov-Zwanziger作用量的局域实时间延拓存在根本困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Gribov无极点条件（no-pole condition）在欧氏空间（Euclidean space）中依赖Faddeev-Popov算子的椭圓性质，但该条件在物理闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中因算子变为双曲型（hyperbolic）而失效，亟需一个洛伦兹协变的替代表述。

Method: 将问题重新表述为实时间边界值问题（real-time boundary-value problem）：要求Faddeev-Popov波动方程在Feynman边界条件下无源自由解；利用经典鬼散射映射（ghost scattering map）的负频块单射性，以及Wronskian恒等式对稳定自伴时变通道进行分析。

Result: 静态色磁背景（chromomagnetic backgrounds）再现了熟悉的零频率视界穿越（horizon crossing），而静态色电势（chromoelectric potentials）在有限非零频率处到达视界，这是$A_0$与鬼场时间导数直接耦合所导致的独特洛伦兹现象；此外，纯频率混合在稳定自伴时变通道中被证明是结构受保护的，不会单独产生阻塞。

Conclusion: 该条件可写成Fredholm形式，其精确限制是一个泛函行列式（functional determinant），而Gribov-Zwanziger作用量的朴素局域延拓无法复现该结果，构造真正的局域实时间作用量是待解决的核心问题。

Abstract: For over four decades, Gribov's no-pole condition has been almost exclusively explored in Euclidean space, where the elliptic nature of the Faddeev-Popov operator provides a clear spectral boundary. In physical Minkowski spacetime, however, this operator becomes a hyperbolic wave operator, and the Euclidean positivity criterion collapses. We show that the natural Lorentzian replacement is a real-time boundary-value problem: a gauge configuration remains inside the first Gribov region as long as the Faddeev-Popov wave equation admits no source-free solutions obeying the Feynman boundary condition. For backgrounds localized in time, this condition translates to the injectivity of the negative-frequency block of the classical ghost scattering map. For stationary backgrounds, it becomes a spatial bound-state or threshold-resonance problem under Fourier transformation. Using a Wronskian identity, we prove that pure frequency mixing in stable self-adjoint time-dependent channels is structurally protected and cannot by itself produce the obstruction. While static chromomagnetic backgrounds reproduce the familiar zero-frequency horizon crossing, static chromoelectric potentials reach the horizon at finite, non-vanishing frequency - a uniquely Lorentzian phenomenon arising because $A_0$ couples directly to the ghost time derivative. We also cast the condition in Fredholm form and show that the exact restriction is a functional determinant, which the naive local continuation of the Gribov-Zwanziger action fails to reproduce, leaving the construction of a genuine local real-time action as the central open problem.

</details>


### [175] [Fire at the Tip of the Throat: Hagedorn Phase after brane-antibrane inflation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08767)
*Dibya Chakraborty,Ahmed Rakin Kamal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究微扰模稳定膜-反膜暴胀模型（brane-antibrane inflation）中暴胀后开放弦哈格多恩相（open-string Hagedorn phase）的物理后果，发现若标准模型膜位于同一收缩喉（throat）中，湮灭释放能量足以进入哈格多恩相并压制暗辐射的有效相对论性物种数（ΔN_eff）至观测限以下；若位于不同喉中，则取决于喉间能量转移效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决膜-反膜暴胀模型中暴胀结束后能量释放能否驱动可见区（visible sector）进入开放弦哈格多恩相（open-string Hagedorn phase），并评估该过程对暗辐射（dark radiation）以及有效相对论性物种数ΔN_eff的影响，以检验模型是否与宇宙学观测一致。

Method: 基于微扰模稳定膜-反膜暴胀模型（perturbatively moduli stabilized brane-antibrane inflation）进行理论分析，该模型通过微扰修正（perturbative corrections）稳定体积模（volume modulus），避免标准η-问题（η-problem）。分析暴胀结束时通过快子凝聚（tachyon condensation）与膜-反膜湮灭释放的能量，并考察该能量能否将可见区驱动至哈格多恩相，同时区分标准模型膜位于同喉或异喉两种情形，以及不同喉间能量转移（inter-throat energy transfer）的时间尺度效应。

Result: 当标准模型膜与湮灭发生在同一喉（throat）中时，仅需湮灭释放能量中的一小部分沉积到幸存的可见开放弦上，即可进入哈格多恩相（Hagedorn regime），并将ΔN_eff压制到当前观测上限以下。若标准模型位于不同喉中，则结果取决于喉间能量转移是即时（prompt）还是延迟（delayed）——两种情形仍可能产生可见哈格多恩相。机制效率最高的条件是标准模型喉中的局域弦尺度（local string scale）低于或相当于湮灭喉中的局域弦尺度。

Conclusion: 在微扰模稳定的膜-反膜暴胀模型中，暴胀后开放弦哈格多恩相可以有效抑制暗辐射，使ΔN_eff满足观测约束；模型的可行性依赖于标准模型膜所在喉的位置以及喉间能量转移特性。

Abstract: We study the post-inflationary open-string Hagedorn phase in perturbatively moduli stabilized brane-antibrane inflation. In this class of models, the volume modulus is stabilized by perturbative corrections rather than by non-perturbative effects to the superpotential, thereby avoiding the standard brane-antibrane $η$-problem. Since inflation ends through tachyon condensation and brane-antibrane annihilation, the endpoint is intrinsically stringy and need not be described immediately by an ordinary radiation bath. We analyze whether the energy released at annihilation can drive the visible sector into an open-string Hagedorn phase, and study the consequences for dark radiation. If the Standard Model (SM) branes lie in the same throat as where the annihilation occurs, we find that a modest fraction of the released energy deposited into surviving visible open strings is sufficient to enter the Hagedorn regime and can suppress the effective number of relativistic species $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ below current observational bounds. If the SM lies in a different throat, the result depends on inter-throat energy transfer: prompt or delayed transfer can still yield a visible Hagedorn phase. However, the mechanism is most efficient when the local string scale in the SM throat is lower than or comparable to that in the annihilation throat.

### [176] [Exact Four-Parameter Rotating NS--NS Vacuum in Double Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08889)
*Hun Jang,Minkyoo Kim,Jeong-Hyuck Park*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过构造NS-NS扇区（Neveu-Schwarz–Neveu-Schwarz sector）的精确旋转真空解（即双场理论真空），首次给出了纯NS-NS真空方程中所有三个场——度规（metric）、Kalb-Ramond场（gauge field）和胀子（dilaton）——的解析旋转解。该解具有四个独立参数，其静态极限表现出非球形的轴向Zipoy–Voorhees分支，携带H-通量（H-flux），且旋转关闭后仍保留扁椭球变形，这种几何记忆效应在纯广义相对论和Einstein–Maxwell–dilaton–axion理论中不存在。在Kerr视界处解出现曲率奇异性，但在特定条件下旋转轴处的逆度规有限而黎曼度规分量发散，为双场理论中的非黎曼几何提供了可能场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NS-NS真空缺乏明确的旋转解析解，且静态解的空间结构尚未被充分探索。本文旨在通过构造精确旋转NS-NS真空解，揭示旋转消除后残存的几何记忆效应，并探讨双场理论（Double Field Theory）框架下非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）的潜在实现。

Method: 将紧致$\mathbf{SO}(2)$ S-对偶性（S-duality）应用于旋转的Einstein–标量种子（rotating Einstein–scalar seed），从而构造出NS-NS扇区（即双场理论真空）的精确旋转解。该解包含四个独立参数$\{\mathfrak{m},j,\mathfrak{q},ζ\}$，分别为质量参数、旋转参数、标量电荷参数和附加标度参数。

Result: 该解是首个所有三个NS-NS场$\{g,B,φ\}$均被解析确定的纯NS-NS真空旋转解，具有独立的胀子和H-通量（H-flux）荷，且不包含Maxwell场。静态极限$j\to 0$下几何不是Burgess–Myers–Quevedo球对称解，而是携带H-通量的轴向Zipoy–Voorhees分支，旋转关闭后扁椭球变形仍保留。在Kerr视界处外壳通常存在曲率奇异性；当$|\mathfrak{q}|>\sqrt{\mathfrak{m}^{2}-j^{2}}$时，极向测地线被向外排斥，旋转轴处逆度规$g^{μν}$有限而黎曼度规分量发散，轴外则逆度规本身发散。

Conclusion: 两个静态分支在$\ell=0$参数化后牛顿（parametrized post-Newtonian, PPN）数据上相同，但在$\ell=2$处简并解除，表明相同单极荷下存在不等价的NS-NS几何。轴上的逆度规有限而黎曼度规发散的奇异性表明，在双场理论中$\mathbf{O}(D,D)$变量$\{d,\mathcal{H}_{AB}\}$可能依然良好定义，为非黎曼几何提供了潜在研究平台。

Abstract: We construct an exact rotating vacuum of the NS--NS sector, equivalently a Double Field Theory vacuum. The construction applies compact $\mathbf{SO}(2)$ S-duality to a rotating Einstein--scalar seed. The solution has four independent parameters $\{\mathfrak{m},j,\mathfrak{q},ζ\}$. To our knowledge, this is the first explicit rotating solution of the pure NS--NS vacuum equations with all three NS--NS fields $\{g,B,φ\}$ determined analytically, independent dilaton and $H$-flux charges, and no Maxwell sector. The static limit is obtained by taking the rotation parameter $j\to 0$. In this limit the geometry is not the spherical Burgess--Myers--Quevedo solution. Instead, it is an axial Zipoy--Voorhees branch carrying $H$-flux, so an oblate deformation remains after rotation is switched off. This geometric memory is absent in pure general relativity and in Einstein--Maxwell--dilaton--axion. The two static branches nevertheless share the same $\ell=0$ parametrized post-Newtonian data $\{MG,β_{\mathrm{PPN}},γ_{\mathrm{PPN}},h\}$. They give two inequivalent NS--NS geometries at identical monopole charges, with the degeneracy lifted at $\ell=2$. At the Kerr horizon locus the outer shell is generically singular in curvature. Above the threshold $|\mathfrak{q}|>\sqrt{\mathfrak{m}^{2}-j^{2}}$, polar geodesics are repelled outward and the rotation axis becomes regular in curvature at the shell. On that axis the inverse metric $g^{μν}$ stays finite while the lower-index Riemannian metric components diverge, whereas off the axis the inverse metric itself diverges. This axis-local degeneracy may offer a setting for non-Riemannian geometry in Double Field Theory, where $g_{μν}$ is not fundamental and the $\mathbf{O}(D,D)$ variables $\{d,\mathcal{H}_{AB}\}$ remain well defined.

### [177] [Post-Newtonian analysis of the quantum signatures of gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09119)
*Tuhin Chatterjee,Soham Sen,Sunandan Gangopadhyay*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在已有量子引力探测方案（基于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体）的基础上，引入了领先阶后牛顿修正，发现非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）仍仅源于量子引力效应，但后牛顿修正会轻微压低信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作指出，仅量子引力（quantum gravity）而非经典引力会在哈密顿量中产生非二次算符，导致可探测的非高斯性。但之前的分析未考虑实际引力环境中的后牛顿（post-Newtonian）修正。本文旨在检验后牛顿修正对该探测方案的影响，使模型更贴近现实。

Method: 采用与 PRX QUANTUM 2 (2021) 010325 相同的探测模型：将玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）囚禁于谐波陷阱势（harmonic trap potential）中，作为量子引力产生非高斯性的探测器。在分析中引入领先阶后牛顿修正，并利用 BEC 中可调谐的 Feshbach 共振（Feshbach resonances）将电磁相互作用强度置零，以区分量子引力与电磁相互作用引起的非高斯性。

Result: 引入后牛顿修正后，非高斯性仍然仅由量子引力部分产生，经典引力不会导致非二次算符。然而，后牛顿效应会使得信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）相比原始方案出现轻微压低。

Conclusion: 后牛顿修正虽然对信号产生一定阻尼作用，但不改变非高斯性作为量子引力探测判据的有效性。该方案在更现实的引力框架下仍具有区分量子引力与经典引力的能力。

Abstract: In a recent work \href{https://doi.org/10.1103/PRXQuantum.2.010325}{PRX QUANTUM 2 (2021) 010325}, a new way of investigating quantum gravity signatures using quantum information theoretic techniques, have been proposed. The primary result of this analysis revealed that non-Gaussianity can arise only through the consideration of a quantum model for the gravity part. Compared to classical gravity, only quantum gravity can result in non-quadratic operators in the Hamiltonian which leads to the non-Gaussian behavior. In our current analysis, we have considered a more realistic scenario taking into effect leading order post-Newtonian corrections in the analysis. We have stayed with the same model of a Bose-Einstein condensate placed inside a harmonic trap potential which indeed works as the detector of the non-Gaussianity generated due to quantum gravitational effects. Bose-Einstein condensates are experimentally well studied; apart from being a single quantum system, they include Feshbach resonances, which helps tuning the strength of the electromagnetic interactions which in principle can be set to zero. This is important since it can help distinguish quantum gravity from electromagnetic interactions without affecting gravitational interactions, and any non-Gaussianity can then be solely attributed to quantum gravity. We observe that the signal to noise ratio gets slightly damped due to the post-Newtonian effects taken under consideration.

### [178] [Stress Tensor Deformations in dS/CFT: Mixed Boundary Conditions, Spectrum Flow and Pseudo Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09170)
*Feng Hao,Hao Ouyang,Xi-Yang Ran*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在dS/CFT对应（dS/CFT correspondence）框架下提出半经典应力张量变形字典（semiclassical stress tensor deformation dictionary），将边界理论中的应力张量变形全息地编码为未来无穷远（future infinity）处体度规的混合边界条件。在Kerr-dS$_3$/CFT$_2$中通过守恒荷与场论谱的精确匹配验证了该字典，并计算了$T\bar{T}$与根-$T\bar{T}$（root-$T\bar{T}$）变形下的全息赝熵（pseudo entropy）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用度量流（metric-flow）表述，将边界应力张量变形全息地编码为未来无穷远处体度规的混合边界条件（mixed boundary conditions）。耦合的流方程（coupled flow equations）决定了形变后的边界度规和应力张量，从而指定形变边界理论的源-响应关系（source-response relation）。

Result: 在Kerr-dS$_3$/CFT$_2$中，由全息边界应力张量构造的守恒荷与从场论流方程（field-theoretic flow equation）得到的边界谱精确一致，验证了字典的有效性。进一步应用该字典计算了$T\bar{T}$变形和根-$T\bar{T}$变形下边界区间的全息赝熵。

Conclusion: 本文提出的应力张量变形字典在超越AdS/CFT（AdS/CFT correspondence）的dS/CFT框架下是自洽且可检验的，为研究德西特时空中的全息可积变形提供了统一工具。

Abstract: We formulate a semiclassical stress tensor deformation dictionary in the context of the dS/CFT correspondence. Using the metric-flow formulation, we propose that stress tensor deformations of the putative boundary theory are encoded holographically as mixed boundary conditions for the bulk metric at future infinity. The coupled flow equations determine the deformed boundary metric and stress tensor, thereby specifying the source--response relation of the deformed boundary theory. We test the proposal in Kerr-dS$_3$/CFT$_2$, where the conserved charges constructed from the holographic boundary stress tensor agree exactly with the boundary spectrum obtained from the field-theoretic flow equation, providing a nontrivial consistency check of the dictionary. As an application, we compute the holographic pseudo entropy of boundary intervals from complexified geodesic saddles in the deformed Kerr-dS$_3$ geometry, and present explicit results for the $T\bar{T}$ and root-$T\bar{T}$ deformations.

### [179] [Asymptotic Algebras and Holography of Information in CGHS Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09346)
*Waheed A. Dar,Nirmalya Kajuri,Rinkesh Panigrahi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究CGHS模型中信息全息性（Holography of Information, HoI）与岛屿公式（island formula）在代数结构上的差异，证明在通常假设下CGHS模型的右传播模量子态可从未来类光无穷远的任意小邻域恢复，并提出若左右传播模的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）因子化成立，则岛屿熵（island entropy）不能等同于任何单边渐近代数的冯·诺伊曼熵（von Neumann entropy），这构成CGHS/RST模型的因子化问题（factorization problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决黑洞信息丢失悖论（black hole information loss paradox）的两种新兴方法——HoI与岛屿公式——给出了不同的佩奇曲线（Page curve），已有研究认为该差异源于各自关注的代数结构。本文旨在通过CGHS模型具体考察这两种方法背后的候选代数，厘清差异根源。

Method: 在CGHS模型耦合无质量标量场的框架下，沿用HoI文献中的常规假设，通过构造辐射相空间（radiative phase space）和未来类光无穷远处的渐近代数（asymptotic algebras）来建立HoI；在此基础上分析左右传播模的希尔伯特空间因子化性质，并探讨岛屿熵与单边渐近代数的关系。

Result: 证明了右传播模的量子态可从右未来类光无穷远的任意小邻域恢复；论证了若左右传播模的希尔伯特空间因子化在CGHS量子理论中成立，则岛屿熵不能等同于任何单边渐近代数的冯·诺伊曼熵，这种不匹配构成了CGHS/RST模型的因子化问题。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了HoI与岛屿公式在CGHS模型代数结构上的可能区分，指出了因子化问题是理解两种方法差异的关键。

Abstract: Holography of Information (HoI) and the island formula are two recent approaches to the black hole information loss paradox that yield different Page curves. The difference between the Page curves has been argued to be rooted in the algebra that each approach focuses on. In this paper, we study the candidate algebras for the CGHS model. Making the usual assumptions that are made in HoI literature, we establish HoI for the CGHS model coupled to a massless scalar by constructing the radiative phase space and asymptotic algebras at future null infinity. We prove that the quantum state of the right-moving modes can be recovered from an arbitrarily small neighbourhood of the right future null infinity. We then argue that if the Hilbert space factorization between left- and right-moving modes holds in the quantum theory of CGHS, then the island entropy cannot be identified with the von Neumann entropy of any one-sided asymptotic algebra, and that this mismatch constitutes a version of the factorization problem for CGHS/RST models. We discuss the possible distinction between the HoI and island approaches for the CGHS model.

</details>


### [180] [Eight-dimensional Manin triples, Yang-Baxter deformations and solutions of Supergravity Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09349)

Method: 从半阿贝尔（semi-Abelian）Manin三元组对应的1+3维平坦背景出发，通过Poisson-Lie T-对偶性变换，识别构成同一Drinfeld双不同分解的Manin三元组，从而生成新解。部分变换被解释为齐次Yang-Baxter变形（homogeneous Yang-Baxter deformations）。

Result: 除平坦背景和平面平行波（plane-parallel waves）解外，Poisson-Lie T-对偶性还产生了带挠率（torsion）的弯曲背景，满足（广义）超引力方程。非幺模（non-unimodular）变形特别给出了广义超引力方程的解。

Conclusion: 4+4维Manin三元组的系统列表为通过Poisson-Lie T-对偶性构造超引力新解提供了有效工具，其中非幺模变形在通向广义超引力解的过程中具有特殊重要性。

Abstract: Extensive list of 4+4-dimensional Manin triples that was presented recently can be used to find new solutions of supergravity equations via Poisson-Lie T-plurality. To get the solutions we start with 1+3-dimensional flat backgrounds on Poisson-Lie groups corresponding to semi-Abelian Manin triples. For application of the Poisson-Lie T-plurality we identify Manin triples that form various decompositions of the same Drinfeld double. Beside flat backgrounds and plane-parallel waves solving supergravity equations, plurality transformation also produces curved backgrounds with torsion satisfying (generalized) supergravity equations. Many of the Poisson-Lie transformations can be understood as homogeneous Yang-Baxter deformations. Of special interest are the non-unimodular deformations leading to solutions of generalized supergravity equations.

Method: 在热力学变量的奇数维接触流形（contact manifold）上首次引入一种度量，其拉回（pull-back）到横截于Reeb场的等熵辛子流形（isoentropic symplectic submanifolds）上成为Kähler度量；进一步拉回到作为Lagrangian子流形的平衡态上则给出Fisher Hessian。利用紧致交换结构（compact abelian structures）理论和特殊Kähler几何（Special Kähler Geometry）对Calabi-Vesentini流形进行编码，显式积分得到配分函数（partition function）。通过非零Casimir函数均值实现等距群的部分对称性破缺，类似于铁磁体中的自发磁化。

Result: 得到了一类新的精确Gibbs分布，该分布是Cartan神经网络在弯曲几何背景下的类比，对应传统机器学习中平空间所用的高斯概率分布。Casimir函数的非零均值提供了部分破缺等距群对称性的机制。

Conclusion: 本文建立的几何框架统一了几何热力学与信息几何，并推广了Souriau热力学，新的Gibbs分布为神经网络中的概率建模提供了基于弯曲几何（Kähler流形）的替代方案。

Abstract: In this paper we clarify the relation between Geometric Thermodynamics and Information Geometry based on the Fisher matrix. On the macroscopic odd-dimensional contact manifold of thermodynamic variables, we introduce for the first time a metric, whose pull-back on the isoentropic symplectic submanifolds transverse to the Reeb field is Kählerian. The pull-back of such metric on equilibrium states, that are lagrangian submanifolds, is the Fisher Hessian. Then we consider the Souriau-like Thermodynamics that uses Calabi-Vesentini (CV) manifolds as Kaehlerian microscopic event manifolds and the Killing moment maps as observable functions. A systematic use of the theory of compact abelian structures and the setup of Special Kähler Geometry in which CV manifolds are encoded allows us to perform the explicit integration defining the partition function for any entry in the CV Tits Satake universality class. The additional actions completing the abelian structure are non linear Casimir functions of the Killing moment-maps and suggest a generalization of Souriau thermodynamics that partially breaks the isometry group symmetry by means of the non vanishing mean values of the Casimir functions in a manner similar to the spontaneous magnetization in ferromagnetism. Our new exact Gibbs distributions provide the analogue for Cartan Neural Networks of the Gaussian probability distributions in flat space used in conventional Machine Learning.

### [182] [Perturbative study of Supercritical Crossover in Noncommutative-corrected Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09443)
*Ankit Anand,Shoucheng Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文解析研究了非对易带电AdS黑洞的Widm线及超临界交叉行为。通过将非对易参数α作为微扰处理，在正则系综和扩展系综中计算热力学量和标度方差Ω，利用Ω极值定义Widm线。Landau展开推导出两条对称交叉分支L±，其标度关系符合平均场普适类（β=1/2, γ=1），非对易参数仅改变次主导振幅而不改变普适类。数值验证和完整超临界相图进一步确认了非对易修正保持黑洞超临界性的平均场普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非对易几何效应对黑洞超临界区域热力学行为的影响，特别是Widm线（Widom line）与超临界交叉（supercritical crossover）的标度关系是否偏离平均场普适类。

Method: 采用微扰方法处理非对易参数α，在正则系综（canonical ensemble）和扩展系综（extended ensemble）中计算热力学量与标度方差Ω，以Ω极值识别Widm线；利用近临界点的Landau展开（Landau expansion）推导交叉分支的标度律，并结合数值模拟验证。

Result: 在正则系综中，Widm线交叉分支满足δT∼|ΔQ|^{β+γ}、δS∼|ΔQ|^β；在扩展系综中满足δP∼|ΔT|^{β+γ}、δρ∼|ΔT|^β。标度指数符合平均场普适类（β=1/2, γ=1），非对易参数仅改变次主导振幅。数值结果与超临界相图支持理论分析。

Conclusion: 非对易修正不改变黑洞超临界性的平均场普适性（mean-field universality），表明非对易几何效应在超临界区域仅产生定量而非定性的影响。

Abstract: We analytically study the Widom line and supercritical crossover of noncommutative charged AdS black holes. Treating the noncommutative parameter $α$ perturbatively, we compute thermodynamic quantities and the scaled variance $Ω$ in both canonical and extended ensembles. The Widom line is identified as the extremum of $Ω$. Using a Landau expansion near the critical point, we derive the two symmetric crossover branches $L^{\pm}$, which obey $δT\sim \left|ΔQ\right|^{β+γ}$, $δS\sim \left|ΔQ \right|^β$ in the canonical ensemble and $δP\sim \left|ΔT\right|^{β+γ}$, $δρ\sim \left|ΔT\right|^β$ in the extended ensemble. These scaling relations conform to the mean-field universality class ($β=1/2$, $γ=1$), and the noncommutative parameter only shifts subleading amplitudes without altering the universality class. Numerical verification and complete supercritical phase diagrams are also presented using supercritical crossover lines. Our results show that noncommutative corrections preserve the mean-field universality of black hole supercriticality.

### [183] [Effective scalaron--photon interaction in $f(R)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09510)
*Yuri Shtanov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视了f(R)引力中标量场（scalaron）与规范场的有效耦合，重点分析标量场衰变为两个光子的过程。通过Fujikawa方法推导出由迹反常（trace anomaly）贡献的有效相互作用，并指出在特定质量极限下，图解贡献与反常诱导项相互抵消，导致有效耦合消失，从而澄清了文献中关于标量场有效耦合不一致的来源及其对暗物质现象学的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将标量场视为Jordan框架度规（Jordan-frame metric）的内禀分量，利用Fujikawa方法（Fujikawa's method）推导与物质场在Jordan框架与Einstein框架之间变换相关的反常诱导贡献。先针对QED（量子电动力学）进行分析，再推广至完整标准模型（Standard Model）。

Abstract: We revisit the effective coupling of the scalaron to gauge fields in $f(R)$ gravity minimally coupled to the Standard Model, focusing on the scalaron decay into two photons. Treating the scalaron as an intrinsic component of the Jordan-frame metric, we analyse quantum effects arising from its coupling to the energy--momentum tensor. In this framework, the trace anomaly contributes to the scalaron--gauge boson interaction.
  Using Fujikawa's method, we derive the anomaly-induced contribution, associated with the transformation of matter fields between the Jordan and Einstein frames, first in QED and then in the full Standard Model. The resulting effective scalaron--photon interaction agrees with direct perturbative calculations that include the trace anomaly and differs from the result obtained when only the classical trace of the energy--momentum tensor is taken into account. In the limit where the scalaron mass is much smaller than the masses of particles circulating in the loop, the diagrammatic contribution cancels the anomaly-induced term, leading to a vanishing effective coupling and a strong suppression of the scalaron decay rate into photons.
  These results clarify the origin of discrepancies in the literature concerning the effective scalaron coupling to massless gauge fields. The discrepancies arise from inequivalent prescriptions for implementing quantum loop effects in $f(R)$ gravity, leading to different scalaron--gauge field interactions with direct implications for scalaron dark-matter phenomenology.

*Denjoe O'Connor,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有U(N)规范对称性的玻色d矩阵谐振子的SO(d)和O(d)不变扇区，通过配对公式推导了微正则简并度，发现了微正则热容由负转正的“热量折叠”（caloric fold）现象，并将其与反德西特空间中的黑洞热力学建立联系。

Conclusion: SO(d)和O(d)不变扇区的d矩阵量子力学是捕获黑洞热力学对偶描述关键特征的可处理矩阵系统，为研究黑洞热力学提供了新的理论工具。

This pairing formula is derived by counting invariant words in multi-matrix variables $X^i_{j,a}$, using properties of Clebsch-Gordan multiplicities (Kronecker coefficients) for the symmetric group $S_k$, Schur-Weyl duality and harmonic analysis on the homogeneous space $U(d)/SO(d)$. Data from the pairing formula is well fitted by $k_{\rm crit} \sim { N^2 \over 4 }$ for small values of $d$. A derivation of this large $N$ formula is given using a matrix model approximation and semi-classical analysis of the eigenvalue density. The large $N,d$ limit of the degeneracies reveals a key role for ribbon graph combinatorics. The caloric fold is also notably a property of black hole thermodynamics in anti-de-Sitter spaces. We propose the spherically symmetric \(SO(d)\) and \(O(d)\) invariant sectors of \(d\)-matrix quantum mechanics as tractable matrix systems for capturing key features of dual descriptions of black-hole thermodynamics.

Abstract: We construct the double-current deformations of two-dimensional quantum field theories whose partition functions have background gauge-field anomalies. The deformed partition function then has the same anomaly as the undeformed one.

*A. A. Saharian,E. L. Karapetyan,G. V. Mirzoyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个通用理论框架，用于研究翘曲几何背景中拓扑缺陷对量子标量场局部特性的影响。通过将场方程分离为径向、角度和翘曲坐标三个独立部分，获得了任意角度亏损参数下的归一化模函数，并将该形式化方法应用于共形平坦翘曲时空、广义宇宙弦、整体单极子和反德西特型翘曲几何等具体情形，最终在反德西特时空的整体单极子背景中计算了Hadamard两点函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑缺陷（如宇宙弦、整体单极子）在弯曲时空量子场论中具有重要物理意义，但现有研究对翘曲几何背景中缺陷如何影响量子标量场的局部特性缺乏统一的处理框架。本文旨在建立一套通用形式化方法，以系统分析这一相互作用。

Method: 首先将Ricci张量和曲率标量分解为翘曲因子、径向几何和角度缺陷结构三部分贡献。对于任意曲率耦合参数，将场方程分离为径向、角度和翘曲坐标三个独立方程。通过求解分离后的方程，获得一般角度亏损参数下的完整归一化模函数集。

Result: 成功建立了针对翘曲几何中拓扑缺陷影响量子标量场的通用框架，获得了任意角度亏损参数下的归一化模函数。将该形式化方法应用于共形平坦翘曲时空、广义宇宙弦、整体单极子和反德西特型翘曲几何等多个具体情形，并在反德西特时空的整体单极子背景下利用所得模函数计算了Hadamard两点函数。

Conclusion: 本文提供的通用框架为研究翘曲几何中拓扑缺陷对量子场局部特性的影响奠定了数学基础，可推广至更广泛的翘曲几何与缺陷构型。该工作有助于深入理解量子场在非平凡拓扑和几何背景下的行为。

Abstract: We develop a general framework for investigating the influence of topological defects on the local characteristics of a quantum scalar field in a warped geometry background. The Ricci tensor and curvature scalar are decomposed into contributions from the warp factor, the radial geometry and the angular defect structure. For an arbitrary curvature coupling parameter, the field equation is separated into independent radial, angular and warp-coordinate parts. A complete set of normalized mode functions is obtained for general values of the angular deficit parameters. The general formalism is applied to several specific cases, such as conformally flat warped spacetimes, generalized cosmic strings, global monopoles and anti-de Sitter (AdS)-type warped geometries. The Hadamard two-point function is then evaluated for a global monopole in AdS spacetime using the obtained mode functions.

</details>

### [188] [Inverse supersymmetry in finite temperature Bose-Fermi mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07784)
*Zachary Gazzillo,Carlos A. R. Sá de Melo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文研究近简并玻色-费米混合物，指出广义超对称（gSUSY）的破缺会产生最多四味的费米型戈德斯延模（Goldstino modes），并区分了典型超对称（SUSY）与逆超对称（iSUSY）两种情形，最后提出通过射频或微波谱学实验来探测这些模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索近简并玻色-费米混合物中广义超对称（gSUSY）破缺的物理后果，并区分典型超对称（SUSY）与逆超对称（iSUSY）两种不同情形下的戈德斯延模（Goldstino mode）行为。

Method: 基于理论分析，研究最多两种内态（internal states）的玻色-费米混合物中广义超对称破缺导致的戈德斯延模，并对比典型超对称与逆超对称下戈德斯延模的赝自旋（pseudospin）承载粒子差异；类比凝聚态物理中的动量（角）分辨光电子谱（photoemission），提出射频（radio-frequency）或微波（microwave）谱学实验方案。

Result: 广义超对称破缺可产生最多四味的费米型戈德斯延模；典型超对称下戈德斯延模的赝自旋由费米子承载，而逆超对称下由玻色子承载；两种情形对玻色和费米原子谱函数（spectral functions）的影响不同。

Conclusion: 通过射频或微波谱学实验可测量赝自旋依赖的谱函数，从而在$^{39}$K与$^{40}$K混合物中探测戈德斯延模的出现。

Abstract: We investigate nearly degenerate Bose-Fermi mixtures and show that the breaking of generalized supersymmetry (gSUSY) between bosons and fermions, with up to two internal states, manifests itself through the emergence of fermionic Goldstino modes with up to four flavors. In particular, we draw a distinction between typical supersymmetry (SUSY), where bosons have pseudospin 0 and fermions have pseudospin 1/2, and inverse supersymmetry (iSUSY), where bosons have pseudospin 1/2 and fermions have pseudospin 0. In such systems, we highlight that the Goldstino pseudospin is carried by either its constituent fermion (SUSY) or boson (iSUSY). We then distinguish between these two cases by depicting their differing effects on the spectral functions of the bosonic and fermionic atomic species. Lastly, we propose radio-frequency- or microwave-spectroscopy experiments, analogous to momentum (angular) resolved photoemission in condensed matter physics, to measure the pseudospin-dependent spectral functions and detect the emergence of Goldstino modes in mixtures of $^{39}$K and $^{40}$K.

</details>


### [189] [Ultracold Amplification Proposal for Parity Violation in Chiral Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08717)
*Daniel Martínez-Gil,Pedro Bargueño,Salvador Miret-Artés*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种理论机制，通过超冷气体中宏观对映体过量（enantiomeric excess）间接探测手性对映体之间微小的宇称破坏能量差（PVED）。该机制利用超冷碰撞共振形成手性分子，并借助玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）内的集体动力学将微观不对称放大为全局布居失衡，从而在现实条件下实现完全对映体过量，为探测尚未实验确认的分子宇称破坏（parity violation）提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性对映体之间的宇称破坏能量差（PVED）是一种极小的弱相互作用效应，至今尚未被实验直接探测到。本文旨在通过超冷系统中的宏观对映体过量间接检测这一微小不对称性，从而提供一种可行的实验探测路径。

Method: 本文提出了一个理论机制：将手性分子通过非手性双原子分子的超冷碰撞共振形成，PVED导致左、右手性构型共振能量产生微小不对称；此后手性分子在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中演化，包含非线性相互作用、对映体间隧穿、内在PVED及热转化率；利用耦合速率方程（coupled rate equations）描述这些集体动力学如何将微观偏差放大为宏观布居失衡。

Result: 在现实参数条件下，即使内在不对称性极其微小，该机制仍能实现完全的对映体过量。以HSOH、H₂Se₂、H₂Te₂为具体分子示例，预测了在可行的实验条件下可观测的对映体过量。此外，还分析了电场、磁场及热涨落等非PVED效应同样可能被该机制放大。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，超冷物理学（ultracold physics）可能为探测分子宇称破坏（molecular parity violation）提供一条新的途径，该效应作为基本的弱相互作用效应至今尚未被实验确认。

Abstract: We propose a theoretical mechanism to indirectly detect the small parity-violating energy difference (PVED) between chiral enantiomers through a macroscopic enantiomeric excess observed in an ultracold gas. We consider that chiral molecules are formed resonantly via ultracold collisions of achiral diatomic molecules, with PVED inducing a slight asymmetry in the resonance energies of right- and left-handed configurations. After formation, chiral molecules evolve within a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC), incorporating nonlinear interactions, tunneling between enantiomeric states, intrinsic PVED, and thermal conversion rates. These collective dynamics enable amplification of the microscopic bias into a global population imbalance. Using coupled rate equations, we show that, under realistic regimes, a complete enantiomeric excess can be achieved even for extremely small intrinsic asymmetries. We illustrate the model with concrete examples (HSOH, H$_2$Se$_2$, H$_2$Te$_2$), predicting observable enantiomeric excesses under plausible experimental conditions. We also consider non-PVED effects that could be amplified under the proposed mechanism, including electric and magnetic fields as well as thermal fluctuations, the latter being illustrated through the aforementioned molecular examples. Overall, our results suggest that ultracold physics could provide a new pathway to probe molecular parity violation, a fundamental weak effect that remains experimentally undetected.

</details>


### [190] [The Map of Parameter Space in Double Microwave Shielding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09636)
*Hubert J. Jóźwiak,Ian Stevenson,Sebastian Will,Tijs Karman*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过利用散射问题的普适性，系统映射了双微波屏蔽（double microwave shielding）的四维参数空间，定义了最优工作区间（无场关联束缚态、充分抑制两体损耗），并评估了候选分子种类，发现重、强偶极分子在中等场强下即可实现极致的损耗抑制与相互作用可调性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管双微波屏蔽技术已成功实现分子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate）和自束缚液滴（self-bound droplet），但该屏蔽机制的最优工作区间尚未被充分探索。

Method: 利用散射问题的普适性，系统扫描由两个微波场的失谐量（detuning）和强度（intensity）构成的四维参数空间；通过排除场关联束缚态（field-linked bound state）并确保两体损耗低于超冷样品典型寿命，界定最优工作区间；在该区间内计算弹性与非弹性碰撞比（elastic-to-inelastic collision ratio），并调查候选分子种类。

Result: 确定了严格无场关联束缚态且充分抑制两体损耗的最优工作区间；在该区间内评估了有效偶极相互作用（effective dipolar interaction）的可调范围及蒸发冷却所需碰撞比；发现重、强偶极分子在中等场强下可实现极致的损耗抑制与稳健的相互作用可调性。

Conclusion: 重、强偶极分子是未来量子模拟实验（quantum simulation）最具前景的平台。

Abstract: Double microwave shielding employs $σ^{+}$- and $π$-polarized microwave fields, tuned close to the lowest rotational transition, to engineer a long-range repulsive barrier between polar molecules. By preventing molecules from reaching the short range, this technique suppresses detrimental two-body losses and recently enabled the realization of molecular Bose-Einstein condensates and self-bound droplets. Yet, the optimal operating regimes of the shielding mechanism remain largely unexplored. Here, by leveraging the underlying universality of the scattering problem, we systematically map the four-dimensional microwave parameter space-spanned by the detunings and intensities of the two fields-to identify configurations that maximize both shielding efficiency and interaction tunability. We define optimal operating regimes as configurations that are strictly free of field-linked bound states while sufficiently suppressing two-body losses to exceed typical lifetimes of ultracold samples. In these regimes, we evaluate the elastic-to-inelastic collision ratios required for efficient evaporative cooling and explore the accessible tuning range of the effective dipolar interactions. Finally, to identify the best platforms for future quantum simulation experiments, we conduct a global survey of candidate molecular species under realistic field constraints. We identify heavy, strongly dipolar molecules as the most promising candidates, demonstrating that they can achieve extreme loss suppression alongside robust interaction tunability using only moderate field strengths.

</details>


### [191] [Analog quantum simulation of chiral magnetic dynamics using optical superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09708)
*Sabhyata Gupta,Luis Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出利用超冷原子在光学超晶格（optical superlattice）中进行手征磁性动力学（chiral magnetic dynamics）的类比量子模拟（analog quantum simulation）。通过将零规范耦合极限下的施温格模型（massive Schwinger model）映射为Rice-Mele模型，用超晶格参数编码费米子质量和拓扑角，研究两种淬火协议下的矢量流实时动力学。模拟结果表明，电流动力学表现出清晰的质量依赖性，且对实验噪声具有鲁棒性，矢量流可通过单键分辨探测直接测量，从而将冷原子超晶格确立为探测非平衡手征现象的有效平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在冷原子量子模拟平台上实现手征磁性动力学（chiral magnetic dynamics）的类比量子模拟（analog quantum simulation），为研究非平衡手征现象提供新的实验途径。

Method: 将零规范耦合极限下的施温格模型（massive Schwinger model）映射到Rice-Mele模型，通过超晶格（superlattice）参数编码费米子质量和拓扑角；设计连续手征注入（chirality injection）和手征弛豫（chirality relaxation）两种淬火协议，模拟矢量流（vector current）的实时动力学。

Result: 在具有真实超晶格参数和实验噪声的模拟中，两种淬火协议下的矢量流动力学均表现出清晰的质量依赖性，且该结果对实验不完美性具有鲁棒性（robust）。

Conclusion: 矢量流可通过单键分辨探测（single-bond-resolved detection）直接测量，冷原子超晶格可成为探测非平衡手征现象的可行实验平台。

Abstract: We propose an analog quantum simulation of chiral magnetic dynamics using ultracold atoms in an optical superlattice. The massive Schwinger model in the zero gauge coupling limit maps onto the Rice-Mele model, with the fermion mass and topological angle encoded in the superlattice parameters. We study the real-time dynamics of the vector current following two quench protocols that drive continuous chirality injection and chirality relaxation. Simulations with realistic superlattice parameters and experimental noise demonstrates clear mass dependence of the current dynamics in both protocols, robust against experimental imperfections. The vector current may be directly measurable via single-bond-resolved detection, establishing cold atom superlattices as a viable platform for probing non-equilibrium chiral phenomena.

### [192] [All-electron Dynamical Bethe-Salpeter Equation for Extended Systems with Atom-centered Orbital Basis Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08350)
*Ruiyi Zhou,Songrui Liu,Jianhang Xu,Yi Yao,Yosuke Kanai*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文将基于平面波的有效介电函数方法推广到以原子中心轨道为基函数的动态BSE计算中，并在全电子数值原子中心轨道（NAO）框架下实现了动态BSE@GW方法，通过对萘分子晶体的动态BSE@G0W0计算验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于格林函数（Green's function）的多体理论中，Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）是描述电子激发中粒子-空穴（激子）相互作用的常用方法。传统BSE计算采用静态近似，但当激子结合能较大时，动力学屏蔽效应变得不可忽略，静态近似不再可靠。同时，求解动态BSE在扩展体系中面临巨大的计算成本挑战。

Method: 将基于平面波的有效介电函数方法（effective dielectric function method）重新表述为以原子中心轨道为基函数的动态BSE计算形式；在已有的全电子数值原子中心轨道（numerical atom-centered orbital, NAO）实现的BSE@GW框架中实现了该动态BSE方法；采用动态BSE@G0W0计算对萘（naphthalene）分子晶体进行实际应用验证。

Result: 成功在全电子NAO框架下实现了动态BSE方法，并通过萘分子晶体的动态BSE@G0W0计算验证了该实现的正确性与实际应用能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于NAO基组的动态BSE方法为扩展体系中考虑动力学屏蔽效应的激子计算提供了可行的实现路径，克服了静态近似在强激子体系中的局限性。

Abstract: Solving Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE) for the two-particle Green's function is the most widely used approach for taking into account the particle-hole (exciton) interaction in electronic excitation in the context of the many-body theory based on Green's function. In BSE calculations, the static approximation to the screened Coulomb interaction kernel is commonly employed. However, when the excitonic character is significant as typically indicated by a large exciton binding energy, dynamical screening effects become non-negligible, rendering the static approximation questionable. Because of the large computational cost due to the dense Brillouin zone integration necessary for convergence, solving the dynamical BSE for extended systems remains a significant challenge, especially when combined with GW calculation for the calculation of quasi-particle energies. In this work, we formulate the plane-wave based effective dielectric function method [Zhang, et al., Phys. Rev. B 107, 235205 (2023)] for the dynamical BSE calculation using atom-centered orbitals as basis functions. We implement this approach in our recently developed all-electron numerical atom-centered orbital (NAO) implementation of BSE@GW [Zhou, et. al. J. Chem. Theory Comput. 21, 291 (2025)] for extended systems. We validate our all-electron NAO-based implementation of the dynamical BSE method, and we then discuss its realistic application to molecular crystal of naphthalene by performing the dynamical BSE@G0W0 calculation.

</details>


### [193] [Revealing Wavelength- and Size-Dependent CO2 Reduction Selectivity via Operando Scanning Photo-Electrochemical Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09612)
*Fatemeh Kiani,Milad Sabzehparvar,Priscila Vensaus,Elif Nur Dayi,Olga D'Anania,Tarique Anwar,Nuria Lopez,Ravishankar Sundararaman,Giulia Tagliabue*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究利用定量原位扫描光电化学显微镜（photo-SECM）直接证明，在等离子体Au/p-GaN光阴极上，通过调控光子能量可以切换CO2还原反应（CO2R）的选择性：带间激发（460-560 nm）促进CO生成，而带内激发（640-800 nm）则有利于析氢。结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算和热载流子输运分析，揭示了电子能量驱动的选择性机制，并指出纳米结构几何尺寸（<100 nm vs. ~300 nm）通过热载流子输运效应进一步调控选择性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离子体催化中产物选择性的控制，尤其是CO2还原（CO2R）的选择性调控，是当前尚未解决的核心挑战，对光驱动燃料与化学合成具有直接影响。

Method: 采用定量原位扫描光电化学显微镜（photo-SECM）直接观测选择性切换；通过控制不同波长下吸收功率恒定并验证线性功率依赖关系，隔离热载流子能量（hot-carrier energy）的光子效应和光热效应；结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算和第一性原理热载流子输运计算。

Result: 带间激发（460-560 nm）驱动选择性CO生成，带内激发（640-800 nm）促进析氢反应（H2 evolution）；DFT计算表明更高能量的带间激发逐步增加热电子可达态与CO生成中间体的重叠，从而选择性促进CO而非甲酸盐（formate）；纳米结构尺寸方面，亚100 nm结构维持CO2R活性，而约300 nm纳米圆盘因热载流子输运损失抑制了活性。

Conclusion: 光子能量、载流子输运和纳米结构几何构型是耦合的等离子体CO2R选择性设计参数；解决了关于等离子体驱动选择性效应起源的长期争议，并将photo-SECM定位为光（电）催化领域广泛适用的原位（operando）研究平台。

Abstract: Controlling product selectivity in plasmonic catalysis, particularly in CO2 reduction (CO2R), remains a central unsolved challenge with direct implications for light-driven fuel and chemical synthesis. Here, we deploy quantitative operando scanning photoelectrochemical microscopy (photo-SECM) to provide a direct demonstration that tuning photon energy switches CO2R selectivity through an electronically driven pathway. On plasmonic Au/p-GaN photocathodes, interband excitation (460-560 nm) drives selective CO production while intraband excitation (640-800 nm) favors H2 evolution. By maintaining constant absorbed power across wavelengths and confirming linear power dependence, we isolate the role of hot-carrier energy from photonic and photothermal contributions. Density functional theory calculations reveal that higher-energy interband excitation progressively increases the overlap between hot-electron-accessible states and the CO-producing intermediate, selectively promoting CO over formate, in excellent agreement with experiment. We further show that selectivity is geometrically gated by hot-carrier transport: sub-100 nm nanostructures sustain CO2R activity, while ~300 nm nanodisks suffer transport losses that suppress it, consistent with ab initio hot-carrier transport calculations. Together, these results establish photon energy, carrier transport, and nanostructure geometry as coupled design parameters for plasmonic CO2R selectivity, resolve a longstanding debate on the origin of plasmon-driven selectivity effects, and position photo-SECM as a broadly applicable operando platform for photo(electro)catalysis.

</details>
