### [194] [Neutrino monitoring of explosions for excluding fission yield](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09571)
*O. Benevides Rodrigues,N. S. Bowden,R. Carr,A. Conant,M. Foxe,D. Hornback,P. Huber,A. Irani,L. Lebanowski,V. A. Li,J. M. Link,B. R. Littlejohn,F. Machado,M. P. Mendenhall,H. P. Mumm,J. Newby,I. D. Olusola,G. D. Orebi Gann,T. Papatyi,L. Pickard,X. Zhang*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨利用中微子（neutrino）信号缺失来限制化学爆炸中的核裂变（nuclear fission）成分，量化了通过反β衰变（inverse beta decay）探测器在不同距离和背景条件下所需探测器质量，并评估了其在核试验场监测中的适用性与局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核裂变会释放中微子，因此通过检测中微子信号的缺失，可以限制爆炸中的裂变成分。该能力可用于前核试验场，向监管机构、国际监测方或其他观察者保证化学爆炸活动中的核裂变含量不超过指定限值。

Method: 本文量化了在源到探测器距离（source-to-detector distance）达100公里时，通过反β衰变（inverse beta decay）检测并在现实背景水平下，所需的中微子探测器质量，以设定裂变产量限值（fission yield limit）。

Result: 分析表明，活性质量（active mass）在吨级至数万吨级的探测器可对内华达国家安全场区（Nevada National Security Site）大型化学爆炸的裂变产量设定潜在有用的限值。然而，反β衰变探测器不适用于在更远距离或某些试验场在停止核爆炸试验后发生的亚临界核实验（subcritical nuclear experiments）中排除裂变产量。

Conclusion: 中微子探测器在一定距离和场景下可用于监测化学爆炸中的核裂变成分，但其适用范围受限于探测距离和实验类型。

Abstract: Nuclear fission produces neutrinos, so the absence of a neutrino signal can be used to set a limit on the fission content of an explosion. This capability could be employed on former nuclear test sites to assure regulators, international monitors, or other observers that activities involving chemical explosions do not exceed a designated limit for nuclear fission. This paper quantifies the neutrino detector masses that would be required to set fission yield limits at source-to-detector distances up to 100 km, assuming detection by inverse beta decay with realistic background levels. The analysis indicates that detectors with active mass in the ton- to tens-of-kiloton range can set potentially useful limits on the fission yield of large chemical explosions at the Nevada National Security Site. In contrast, inverse beta decay detectors are not well suited to excluding fission yield at longer range or in the subcritical nuclear experiments that have occurred at some test sites following the cessation of explosive nuclear testing.

</details>

### [195] [Considerations for an Integrated Detector Design at FCC-ee: A Human-AI Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07564)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 集成探测器设计（integrated detector design）从初始起点到AI助手的修订“偏见”探测器概念经历了实质性演变。讨论覆盖了从束流管（beam pipe）到亮度监测器（luminosity monitor）的整个探测器，特别关注子系统选择之间的相互影响以及校准（calibration）、稳定性（stability）和操作简便性（operational simplicity）等实际考量。

Conclusion: 报告重点聚焦于设计过程本身，以阐明人类-AI协作在实验物理设计中的潜力与局限性；文中各“偏见”探测器概念的物理性能仍待后续探索。

Abstract: This report explores detector design considerations for the Future Circular Collider in its electron-positron mode (FCC-ee) through an extended dialogue between a physicist and an AI assistant. Starting from initial "prejudice" detector concepts proposed by the AI assistant without explicit physicist input, each subsystem is examined in detail, with the AI's assumptions challenged and revised through the exchange. The discussion covers the full detector from beam pipe to luminosity monitor, with particular attention to the interplay between subsystem choices and the practical considerations - calibration, stability, and operational simplicity - that are essential for a fifteen-year precision physics program. The narrative documents how the integrated detector design evolved substantially from the starting point to revised "prejudice" detector concepts of the AI assistant. The focus of this report is on the process to illustrate both the potential and the limitations of human-AI collaboration in experimental physics design, and the physics capabilities of any of the "prejudice" detector concepts remain to be explored.

</details>


### [196] [Investigation of Thick-GEM detectors fabricated in India for muography application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08664)
*Saikat Ghosh,Promita Roy,Subhendu Das,Shubhabrata Dutta,Nilanjan Biswas,Supratik Mukhopadhyay,Nayana Majumdar*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文研究了厚型气体电子倍增器（Thick-GEM）探测器在缪子成像（muography）中的应用潜力。通过制作多个原型探测器并测试其增益特性、缪子探测效率和空间分辨率，验证了该探测器在基于多次库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering）的材料识别缪子成像系统中的适用性。实验表明，该探测器在单级和双级配置下均能达到99.5%的最高缪子探测效率和30 μm的最佳空间分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缪子成像（muography）是一种利用宇宙射线缪子（cosmic-ray muons）对大型静态或不可达物体进行无损成像的技术。为了实现基于缪子在物质中多次库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering）的材料识别，需要高性能的缪子追踪探测器。厚型气体电子倍增器（Thick-GEM）因其机械坚固性、成本效益和出色的位置探测能力而成为候选，因此需要系统评估其在缪子成像应用中的性能。

Method: 研究采用本地制造的多个尺寸为40 mm × 48 mm的厚型气体电子倍增器（Thick-GEM）原型探测器，设计参数有所变化。在完成探测器调理（conditioning）后，系统测量了单级和双级配置下不同电压设定中的增益变化，并使用缪子源和准直Fe⁵⁵源分别测量了缪子探测效率（muon detection efficiency）和空间分辨率（spatial resolution）。

Result: 在单级和双级配置中，缪子探测效率在整个工作范围内均达到最高99.5%。使用准直Fe⁵⁵源测得的最佳空间分辨率为30 μm，单级与双级配置结果一致。

Conclusion: 厚型气体电子倍增器（Thick-GEM）探测器在缪子成像（muography）应用中展现出优异的性能，包括高缪子探测效率和精细的空间分辨率，验证了其作为缪子追踪装置（muon tracking device）的可行性。

Abstract: Muography, commonly known as muon tomography, is a passive, non-destructive imaging technique that utilizes naturally occurring cosmic-ray muons to visualize the internal density structures of large, static, or inaccessible objects. In course of developing a small prototype muography system for material identification that relies upon the multiple Coulomb scattering of muons in matter, we explored the possible use of Thick-GEM detector as muon tracking device. It is a 5-20 fold scaled-up version of traditional GEM technology, that has become increasingly popular in recent years, owing to its mechanical robustness, cost-effective production, and excellent position sensing capabilities. A few prototypes of this detector of dimension $40\,\mathrm{mm} \times 48\,\mathrm{mm}$ with variation in other design parameters, were manufactured from a local industry. Subsequent to conditioning, detailed characterization of the detectors was performed to validate their suitability in muography applications. To identify the optimal operating region, gain variation was studied under various voltage configurations for both single and double-stage configurations. Experimental measurement of muon detection efficiency across the entire operating range yielded a maximum efficiency of 99.5\% in both cases. Using a collimated Fe$^{55}$-source, the best spatial resolution was determined to be 30 $μ$m for both single and double-stage operation.

</details>


### [197] [Study on the shielding efficiency of water, HDPE, and boron-loaded HDPE for neutron background of plastic scintillator neutrino detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08968)
*D. X. Lu,Y. H. Liu,X. S. Zhang,F. P. An,G. Luo,W. Wang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文针对ALARM（阵列式反中微子反应堆监测实验）的屏蔽设计，实验测试了水、HDPE和掺硼HDPE三种材料对快中子和热中子的屏蔽性能。30 cm厚的掺硼HDPE对两类中子的屏蔽效率均超过95%，Monte Carlo模拟结果与实验数据一致，并给出了完整屏蔽组件的模拟性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地表反应堆反中微子实验受宇宙射线诱导中子本底影响严重，尤其是浅覆盖条件下。ALARM实验部署深度仅9.6米，快中子本底显著，因此需要有效的屏蔽系统来保障反应堆功率监测的灵敏度。

Method: 采用基于EJ426闪烁体的热中子探测器，以Am-Be源为中子源，实验测量了水、高密度聚乙烯（HDPE）和40%硼掺杂高密度聚乙烯（BHDPE）三种材料在不同厚度下的屏蔽效率。同时开展了Monte Carlo模拟，并将模拟结果与实验数据进行比对。

Result: 30 cm厚度的硼掺杂高密度聚乙烯（BHDPE）对快中子和热中子的屏蔽效率均超过95%。Monte Carlo模拟结果与EJ426实验装置的测量数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: BHDPE被验证为ALARM实验的有效屏蔽材料，30 cm厚度即可满足高屏蔽需求；模拟与实验的一致性表明Monte Carlo方法可用于全尺寸屏蔽组件的性能预测。

Abstract: Surface-level reactor antineutrino experiments usually have substantial cosmic ray induced neutron backgrounds, particularly with shallow overburden. The Array of Lattice for Anti-neutrino Reactor Monitoring (ALARM) is a plastic scintillator based experiment designed for reactor power monitoring. It will be deployed about 44 m from the core of a reactor at the Taishan Nuclear Power Plant. Placed at a depth of 9.6 meters below the surface, cosmic ray induced fast neutrons constitute a significant background, making an effective neutron shielding system essential for the experiment. For the shielding design of ALARM, we tested the shielding performance of three materials water, HDPE, and 40\% boron-doped HDPE (BHDPE) against both fast and thermal neutrons. A thermal neutron detector composed of an EJ426 scintillator setup was first used to measure the shielding efficiency of these materials at various thicknesses using neutrons from an Am-Be source. A 30-cm thickness of BHDPE achieved a shielding efficiency exceeding 95\% for both fast and thermal neutrons. Monte Carlo simulations of the EJ426 setup yielded results consistent with the experimental data. Simulation results for the shielding performance of the full ALARM shielding assembly are also presented.

</details>


### [198] [A Polarization-Decomposed Method for Simulating Inhomogeneous Birefringence in Laser-Interferometric Gravitational-Wave Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08943)
*Haoyu Wang,Yuta Michimura,Keiko Kokeyama,Daniel Brown,Yoichi Aso,Marc Eisenmann,Matteo Leonardi,Yutaro Enomoto,Takafumi Ushiba,Hiroaki Yamamoto,Masaki Ando,Kentaro Somiya*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需修改现有仿真框架即可模拟测试质量基底中非均匀双折射（birefringence）的一般性方法，通过等效三-马赫-曾德尔（triple-Mach-Zehnder）构造耦合两个偏振分量的独立标量场，并使用KAGRA蓝宝石输入测试质量的实际双折射图进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试质量基底中的双折射正成为当前及未来激光干涉引力波探测器（gravitational-wave detectors）的新兴限制因素，尤其随着探测器向更高循环功率、低温运行和晶体光学材料发展；空间变化的双折射会改变腔内场的偏振态与空间模式，降低干涉对比度并耦合到长度和对准控制信号中。

Method: 该方法将两个偏振分量表示为独立的标量场，并通过一个等效的三-马赫-曾德尔构造引入它们之间的耦合，该构造再现了双折射介质的琼斯矩阵（Jones matrix）。该方法兼容任何频域干涉仪模型，无需修改现有模拟框架。

Result: 使用KAGRA蓝宝石输入测试质量的实际双折射图展示了该方法的可行性；该技术能够高效支持下一代引力波探测器的双折射研究。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法是一种实用且通用的模拟非均匀双折射的方案，适用于任何频域干涉仪模型，且无需修改现有仿真工具，为未来引力波探测器中的双折射效应研究提供了高效工具。

Abstract: Birefringence in test mass substrates is an emerging limitation for current and future laser-interferometric gravitational-wave detectors, particularly as detectors move toward higher circulating power, cryogenic operation, and crystalline optical materials. Spatially varying birefringence alters both the polarization state and spatial mode content of the intracavity field, reducing interference contrast and coupling into length and alignment control signals. Accurate modeling of these effects is complicated by the fact that most frequency-domain simulation tools employ scalar modal propagation and lack native support for polarization and two-dimensional substrate maps. In this work, we present a practical and general method for simulating inhomogeneous birefringence without modifying existing simulation frameworks. The approach represents the two polarization components as independent scalar fields and introduces their coupling through an equivalent triple-Mach-Zehnder construction that reproduces the Jones matrix of a birefringent medium. We demonstrate the method using realistic birefringence maps of the KAGRA sapphire input test masses. The technique is compatible with any frequency-domain interferometer model and enables efficient birefringence studies for next-generation gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>


### [199] [High-Efficiency Broadband Mid-Infrared Absorption in Asymmetrically Matched Metallic Meanders: Development of Ti40V60 Alloy based LEKIDs for Mid-Far IR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09309)
*Shilpam Sharma,Shekhar Chandra Pandey,Anudeep Singh,Shankar Lal,R. S. Saini,M. K. Chattopadhyay*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无背腔（backshort-free）的LEKID（集总元件动能电感探测器，Lumped Element Kinetic Inductance Detector）吸收器架构，通过匹配超导Ti-V合金曲折线的方块电阻与硅衬底的波阻抗，并结合亚波长周期结构对传播透射的倏逝波抑制，在中远红外（MIR-FIR）12.5–30微米波段实现了50%–90%的宽带吸收效率，避免了传统λ/4背腔结构的窄带和光机械挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中远红外至远红外波段需要快速、高灵敏度且宽带工作的探测器，以支持天体物理学及基于红外自由电子激光（IR-FEL）设施的时间分辨光谱学等应用。传统LEKID依赖窄带谐振λ/4背腔，在MIR-FIR波段面临光机械设计困难且带宽受限的问题，亟需一种宽带、结构简单的吸收器方案。

Method: 采用无背腔LEKID吸收器架构，使用超导Ti40V60合金制成密集曲折线。通过从硅衬底背面照明、将曲折线方块电阻匹配至硅衬底波阻抗以抑制前表面反射，同时利用亚波长周期曲折线产生倏逝波约束（evanescent wave confinement）抑制向自由空间的传播透射，从而在金属曲折线内实现高效的欧姆耗散（Ohmic dissipation）。

Result: 实验表征表明，在12.5–30微米波长范围内，该无背腔LEKID吸收器的吸收效率达50%–90%。此外，基于Ti40V60合金制备了测试LEKID谐振器，并对其作为有源超导探测器材料的适用性进行了实验表征。

Conclusion: 无背腔设计极大简化了焦平面阵列（focal plane array）的制造工艺，同时提供下一代探测器所需的宽带响应。Ti40V60合金被验证可作为有源超导探测器材料用于LEKID谐振器。

Abstract: Fast, highly sensitive, and broadband detectors operating in the mid-to-far-infrared (MIR-FIR) spectral region are essential for applications ranging from astrophysics to time-resolved spectroscopy using laboratory-based sources and beamlines at Infrared Free-Electron Laser (IR-FEL) facilities. Conventional Lumped Element Kinetic Inductance Detectors (LEKID) achieve high optical efficiency using resonant quarter wavelength (λ/4) backshort cavities. However, this cavity-based approach is inherently narrowband and becomes optomechanically challenging at the mid to far infrared (MIR-FIR) wavelengths. Here, we present a completely backshort-free LEKID absorber architecture that achieves broadband absorption exceeding 50%. The meander absorbers were fabricated from a superconducting Ti-V alloy and characterized using IR radiation from the IR-FEL at RRCAT, India. By illuminating through the silicon substrate and matching the meander's sheet resistance to the silicon substrate's wave impedance, the front-side reflection is strongly suppressed. Simultaneously, the sub-wavelength periodicity of the dense meander inhibits propagating transmission into free space via evanescent wave confinement. This combined mechanism drives efficient Ohmic dissipation within the metallic meander, yielding an experimental absorption efficiency ranging from 50% to 90% across the 12.5-30 micrometer wavelength range. The cavity-free design greatly simplifies the fabrication of the focal plane array while providing the broadband response required for next-generation detectors. To assess the suitability of the Ti40V60 alloy as an active superconducting detector material, a test LEKID resonator was also designed, fabricated, and experimentally characterized.

</details>

# math.CT [[Back]](#toc)

### [200] [The Degeneracy of the Centre Comonad Model and the Precomposition Obstruction for Quantum Modalities on Presheaf Topoi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09467)
*Joey Woo*

Main category: math.CT

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了中心余单子（centre comonad）模型在非交换代数上的退化性：量子模态（quantum modality）湮灭所有非交换代数，线性逻辑（linear logic）坍缩为经典笛卡尔逻辑。作者定位了退化的结构根源——经典核的对偶与笛卡尔幺半范畴等价，并指出构建非退化量子模态必须避免预复合（precomposition）构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Schreiber提出的开放性难题——中心余单子模型虽提供了首个具体的黏性线性$\infty$-拓扑斯（cohesive linear $\infty$-topos），但其量子模态将所有非交换代数映射为零，导致线性逻辑退化为经典笛卡尔逻辑。需要从数学上诊断这一退化的完整原因。

Method: 通过证明中心余单子将简单非交换代数的可表层（representable sheaf）发送为空预层（empty presheaf），且其状态空间为空；进一步证明经典核（classical core）上的Day卷积（Day convolution）是笛卡尔的，迫使Seely同构平凡成立从而导致线性逻辑坍缩。最后提炼出退化的一般充分条件：经典核的对偶与笛卡尔幺半范畴幺半等价时，任何余反射预复合余单子都会呈现相同退化。

Result: 中心余单子模型对非交换代数退化的严格数学证明；识别出退化由经典核的对偶与笛卡尔幺半范畴的幺半等价这一结构原因导致。

Conclusion: 非退化的量子模态不能通过预复合构造实现，必须探索其他构造方向；本文为后续构建非退化量子模态提供了理论约束。

Abstract: The centre comonad model provided the first concrete cohesive linear $\infty$-topos, settling an open problem of Schreiber. However, the model is degenerate: the quantum modality annihilates all non-commutative algebras, and the associated linear logic collapses to classical cartesian logic. In this paper we give a complete mathematical diagnosis of this degeneracy. We prove that the centre comonad sends the representable sheaf of a simple non-commutative algebra to the empty presheaf, and that the state space of any such algebra is empty. We then prove that the Day convolution on the classical core is cartesian, forcing the Seely isomorphism to hold trivially and collapsing the linear logic. We isolate the structural reason behind this collapse: whenever the opposite of the classical core is monoidally equivalent to a cartesian monoidal category, any coreflective precomposition comonad will exhibit the same degeneracy. We conclude that a non-degenerate quantum modality must be constructed without precomposition, and we briefly discuss possible directions.

</details>

### [201] [Experimental observation of hyperbolic spacetime dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09501)
*Jonas Himmel,Coraline Bacq,Krishna Chand Maurya,Max Ehrhardt,Matthias Heinrich,Tom A. W. Wolterink,Pablo Basteiro,Rathindra Nath Das,René Meyer,Tobias Huber-Loyola,Andreas Pfenning,Sven Höfling,Johanna Erdmenger,Alexander Szameit*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用光子平台首次实验模拟了洛伦兹签名反德西特（Anti-de-Sitter, AdS）时空中的费米子波包动力学，通过将弯曲时空中的狄拉克方程映射到波导阵列中光传播，直接观测了引力束缚、测地线振荡和颤动（Zitterbewegung）效应，并揭示了曲率对相对论量子动力学的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弯曲时空中的量子动力学是量子力学与引力交叉领域的核心难题；尽管反德西特/共形场论（AdS/CFT）对应关系具有重要意义，但此前缺乏对洛伦兹签名AdS时空中动力学量子现象的直接实验观测手段。

Method: 通过将弯曲时空中的狄拉克方程映射到工程化波导阵列中的光传播，利用光子平台实验模拟洛伦兹签名AdS₂时空中的费米子波包动力学。

Result: 直接观测到相对论性波包的引力束缚效应及其质心运动；识别出由时空曲率决定的慢速测地线振荡和由相对论粒子-反粒子干涉引起的快速颤动（Zitterbewegung）这两种特征叠加模式；发现测地线频率与费米子质量无关，而颤动频率同时依赖于质量和曲率，揭示了曲率诱导的相对论量子动力学修正。

Conclusion: 该工作首次提供了对模拟洛伦兹签名AdS₂时空中费米子体动力学（bulk dynamics）的定量实验观测，建立了一个可扩展的模拟平台，有望用于探索全息原理（holography）的动力学方面。

Abstract: Understanding quantum dynamics in curved spacetime is a central challenge at the intersection of quantum mechanics and gravity. Anti-de-Sitter (AdS) spacetime plays a pivotal role in the context of the AdS/CFT correspondence, which relates gravitational dynamics in the AdS bulk to a conformal field theory (CFT) living on its boundary. Despite its foundational importance, direct experimental access to dynamical quantum phenomena in Lorentzian AdS spacetime has so far remained out of reach. Here, we report the first experimental emulation of fermionic wave packet dynamics in Lorentzian AdS spacetime using a photonic platform. By mapping the Dirac equation in curved spacetime onto the propagation of light in engineered wave\-guide arrays, we directly observe gravitational confinement of relativistic wave packets and resolve their center-of-mass motion in real time. We identify a characteristic superposition of slow geodesic oscillations governed solely by spacetime curvature and fast Zitterbewegung arising from relativistic particle--antiparticle interference. While the geodesic frequency is independent of fermion mass, the Zitterbewegung frequency exhibits a distinct joint dependence on mass and curvature, revealing a curvature-induced modification of relativistic quantum dynamics. Our results provide the first quantitative experimental access to fermionic bulk dynamics in emulated AdS$_2$ spacetime with Lorentzian signature. This establishes a scalable analog platform that may potentially be used for exploring dynamical aspects of holography.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一种工程化超宽禁带（UWBG）半导体器件的策略，为其在极端条件下的可靠运行提供了路径，可满足工业过程控制、热力与核能发电以及航空航天等领域的新兴需求。

Abstract: Semiconductor photodetectors are conventionally optimized for sensing weak optical signals, and they typically saturate at low-to-moderate light intensity. Here, we demonstrate sub-bandgap AlN photodetectors that exhibit non-saturating linear response to ultra-bright blue light exceeding 40 $\mathrm{W/cm^2}$. The photodetector further shows undistorted linear response at elevated temperature, up to at least 300 $\mathrm{^\circ C}$. This exceptional performance originates from photoresponse mediated by point defects with energy deep in the bandgap ("deep levels") at the metal-AlN Schottky junction. Through dopant design and contact engineering, we demonstrate that a narrow space charge region is essential for enabling ultra-bright light detection and accurate measurement. These results establish a strategy for engineering ultra-wide bandgap (UWBG) semiconductor devices for reliable operation in extreme conditions to meet emerging needs in industrial process control, thermal and nuclear power generation, and aeronautics and spaceflight.

### [203] [Machine-learning surrogate model for one-dimensional GaAs/Al$_{0.3}$Ga$_{0.7}$As distributed Bragg reflector spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08108)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯过程（Gaussian process, GP）的代理模型，用于替代传统的传输矩阵法（transfer-matrix method, TMM）模拟一维GaAs/Al0.3Ga0.7分布式布拉格反射镜（distributed Bragg reflector, DBR）的正入射反射谱。通过主成分分析（principal component analysis, PCA）降维后拟合26个GP，该模型在保持合理精度的同时实现了约70倍的推理加速，但预测误差仍高于随机森林基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DBR设计空间探索传统上依赖TMM仿真，但TMM计算成本较高，限制了大规模参数扫描的效率。因此需要一种快速且可靠的代理模型来加速设计空间的搜索和优化。

Method: 采用拉丁超立方采样生成了1500组TMM仿真数据集。使用主成分分析（PCA）将光谱输出降至26个主成分，对每个主成分分别拟合一个高斯过程（GP）回归模型。以随机森林（Random Forest）作为对比基线。

Result: 在测试集上，GP模型的RMSE为0.085，R²为0.276；随机森林基线RMSE为0.065，R²为0.572。GP推理每光谱耗时4.4毫秒，TMM约为308毫秒，实现了约70倍加速。GP的95%预测区间覆盖了98.9%的测试残差。

Conclusion: GP代理模型能够大幅加速DBR反射谱的预测，适合快速设计空间探索；但当前精度低于随机森林，仍有改进空间。不确定性校准结果表明GP的置信区间是可靠且偏保守的。

Abstract: We present a Gaussian-process (GP) surrogate model for the normal-incidence reflectance spectrum of one-dimensional GaAs/Al$_{0.3}$Ga$_{0.7}$ distributed Bragg reflectors (DBRs). A Latin-hypercube dataset of 1500 transfer-matrix-method (TMM) simulations is used to train and evaluate the model. Principal component analysis reduces the spectral output to 26 components; one GP is fitted per component. On a held-out test set the GP achieves RMSE=0.085 and $R^2=0.276$, while a Random Forest baseline reaches RMSE=0.065 and $R^2=0.572$. GP inference is 4.4 ms per spectrum compared with ~308 ms for TMM, yielding a ~70x speedup. Uncertainty calibration shows that the GP 95% prediction band covers 98.9% of test residuals. These results establish a rapid surrogate for DBR design-space exploration.

Abstract: Plasmon-exciton hybrids, or plexcitons, offer deeply subwavelength light-matter interactions with versatile pathways for energy redistribution. Incorporating chirality into such systems is particularly compelling, enabling spin-sensitive optical functionality that can operate on ultrafast timescales and within ultracompact volumes. Despite recent progress in chiral plexcitonic systems, how structural chirality and plasmon-exciton coupling determine chiroptical spectra and ultrafast energy flow remains elusive. Here we realize chiral plexcitons by functionalizing intrinsically chiral gold helicoid nanoparticles with molecular J-aggregates. Within a non-Hermitian framework, we trace the microscopic origin of the helicoid chiroptical response and its coupling to the excitonic transition, revealing how the helicity of light selectively addresses distinct hybrid responses. At the spatiotemporal extreme, we find that the gap-localized response not only enhances polarization-sensitive contrast but also strengthens the local hybrid interaction, leading to accelerated ultrafast relaxation. Together, these space-, time-, and polarization-resolved measurements provide a physically grounded and experimentally benchmarked picture of chiral plexcitonic coupling, identifying chirality as a practical control parameter for selectively steering nanoscale energy pathways and dynamics.

### [205] [Single plasmon transport in one dimensional nanowire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09523)
*A. A. Dıaz-Valles,B. Rousseaux,S. Guérin,H. Jauslin,A. Leray,G. Colas des Francs*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的单等离激元（single-plasmon）输运理论框架，将量子化电磁格林张量（Green's tensor）形式与非厄米有效哈密顿量模型相连接，分析了单等离激元脉冲在原子链耦合色散纳米线中的时空动力学，并展示了多发射器系统在等离激元调制和耦合损耗方面的显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将量子化电磁格林张量形式与非厄米有效哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）模型统一；使用Löwdin正交化（Löwdin orthogonalization）程序处理多发射器系统中的集体相互作用。

Result: 单量子发射器耦合银纳米线时，在通信波段（telecom wavelengths）及实际条件下预测单等离激元透射率（transmittivity）低至7%，原子量子比特（qubit）布居数为12%；优化放置五个发射器可增强等离激元调制，透射率达2%，并将耦合损耗降至单发射器情况的三分之一。

Conclusion: 该统一理论框架为分析和设计等离激元波导量子电动力学系统提供了坚实基础，证明了优化多发射器系统在等离激元调控和降低损耗方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: We introduce a unified theoretical framework for single-plasmon transport in one-dimensional nanowires, bridging the quantized electromagnetic Green's tensor formalism with effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian models. This approach naturally incorporates propagating surface plasmon polaritons, high-order modes dissipative channels, and intrinsic losses. We investigate both the stationary regime and the spatio-temporal dynamics of a single-plasmon pulse travelling through an atomic chain coupled to a dispersive nanowire. We analyze modal contributions to reflection and transmission spectra for quantum emitter coupled to a silver nanowire, a configuration proposed as a single-plasmon transistor, and we demonstrate that optimized multi-emitter systems offer significant advantages. Extension to multi-emitter systems using a Löwdin orthogonalization procedure enables a consistent treatment of collective interactions. We show that optimized positioning with just five emitters enhances plasmon modulation, achieving a transmittivity of 2\% but also reduces coupling losses to one-third compared to the single-emitter case. Our results establish a robust foundation for analyzing and designing plasmonic waveguide quantum electrodynamics systems.

*Shihao Zhou,Junming Wu,Jiazhen Li,Qing Gu,Wei Zhang*

Abstract: We study a Mach-Zehnder interferometer (MZI)-based optoelectronic magnonic parametric oscillator (OEMPO) incorporating a YIG-loaded magnonic branch and a tunable phase-shifter branch, enabling systematic investigation of adaptive interferometric oscillator dynamics under distributed phase perturbations. Through analysis of nondegenerate OEPO mode pairs and frequency-pulling behavior, the loop free spectral range (FSR) and effective delay time were quantitatively extracted. Despite the nominally frequency-pinned parametric operation, weak frequency pulling and OEPO mode softening were observed, revealing an additional adaptive interferometric degree of freedom introduced by the MZI architecture. By comparing local and global sampling configurations, we demonstrate that the YIG branch behaves predominantly as a local dispersive resonant subsystem governed by the complex magnonic susceptibility, whereas the phase-shifter branch primarily controls the global interferometric redistribution geometry. Nevertheless, coherent recombination and adaptive regeneration within the loop produce finite cross-coupling between the two branches, resulting in partially synchronized interferometric dynamics and branch-dependent adaptive redistribution. Quantitative complex-Lorentzian analysis further reveals substantial phase-to-amplitude conversion and distinct differences between the OEO and OEPO regimes: the phase-pinned OEPO favors strongly dispersive local YIG response, while the frequency-adaptive OEO exhibits more mixed absorptive--dispersive behavior due to spectral relaxation through frequency pulling. Broadly, the present platform establishes a versatile framework for exploring adaptive nonlinear interferometric physics, coherent phase redistribution, and branch-dependent synchronization phenomena in hybrid magnonic-photonic oscillator systems.

### [207] [Natural Selection in the Wake of Catastrophe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09040)
*Jesse Young Lin,Omer Granek,Joshua Sodicoff,Seppe Kuehn,David Pincus,Vincenzo Vitelli*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文在灾难后自然选择的背景下提出了一个数据验证的理论，揭示平均适应度（mean fitness）随时间倒数弛豫的简单定律，其前置因子与灾难后环境耦合的性状数量成正比。通过大肠杆菌（E. coli）抗生素实验验证，发现平均性状适应并非遵循适应度景观（fitness landscape）上的梯度上升，而是一种Levenberg-Marquardt优化算法；在适应度峰值附近，进化轨迹偏向反贪婪，即灾难后选择是乐观的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在理解当环境灾难摧毁生态位多样性（niche diversity）后，自然选择如何驱动生物快速适应。已有理论主要关注稳态适应，对灾难后突然适应（sudden adaptation）的定量规律缺乏统一解释。

Method: 作者提出了一个数据验证的理论模型，利用大肠杆菌在抗生素给药后的实验适应度景观（fitness landscape）进行验证。通过比较平均性状适应（mean trait adaptation）的实际轨迹与梯度上升（gradient ascent）及Levenberg-Marquardt优化算法的预测，检验理论的准确性。

Result: 研究发现灾难后平均适应度随时间倒数弛豫，前置因子与耦合性状数量成正比。实验数据表明，平均性状适应不符合适应度景观上的梯度上升，而是遵循Levenberg-Marquardt优化算法；在适应度峰值附近，进化轨迹表现出反贪婪（biased against greediness）特性，即灾难后选择是乐观的。

Conclusion: 灾难后的自然选择遵循一个简洁的时序定律，且其优化机制与经典梯度上升不同，呈现出一种偏向乐观的Levenberg-Marquardt算法。该结论为理解生物在环境剧变后的快速适应提供了可检验的理论框架。

Abstract: Living organisms, from bacteria to humans, are more likely to survive if their traits enhance fitness. In populations well adapted to their environmental niches, natural selection proceeds via rarely beneficial mutations. But when a catastrophe wipes out niche diversity, sudden adaptation often follows. Here, we present a data-validated theory of natural selection in the wake of catastrophe and unveil a simple law that emerges during recovery: the mean fitness relaxes inversely with time, with a prefactor proportional to the number of traits coupled to the post-catastrophe environment. We put our approach to test using experimental fitness landscapes measured following antibiotic administration to E. coli. The resulting mean trait adaptation is not described by gradient ascent on a fitness landscape, instead it follows an algorithm known as Levenberg-Marquardt optimization. Near fitness peaks, evolutionary trajectories are biased against greediness - from an optimization perspective, post-catastrophic selection is optimistic.

</details>


### [208] [Percolation and clustering in ecological communities: A dynamical theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09494)
*Dario Sergo,Cédric Koller,Vittorio Erba,Lenka Zdeborová*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文针对具有结构化相互作用的生态群落中出现的渗流（percolation）和聚类（clustering）等集体现象，提出了一种基于随机相互作用图（random interaction graph）的动力学理论。通过引入广义Lotka-Volterra模型（generalized Lotka-Volterra model）的离散版本，该框架在保留连续生态动力学关键宏观特征的同时实现解析处理，揭示了动力学可达性（dynamical accessibility）如何控制聚类与渗流的涌现，从而补充了经典Lotka-Volterra理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管实验与模拟已证实结构化相互作用的生态群落中存在渗流和聚类等集体现象，但系统的解析理解仍然有限，亟需一个理论框架来从动力学角度阐明这些现象的涌现机制。

Method: 本文采用随机相互作用图（random interaction graph）上的竞争性生态系统为模型，引入广义Lotka-Volterra模型（generalized Lotka-Volterra model）的离散版本，该版本在保留连续生态动力学关键宏观特征的同时允许解析处理。

Result: 该框架刻画了渗流簇（percolating clusters）的涌现以及存活位点（surviving sites）的空间组织，揭示了动力学可达性（dynamical accessibility）如何决定哪些平衡态（equilibrium）能被动力学过程达到，并进而控制聚类和渗流的产生。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为结构化群落的集体组织提供了动力学视角，补充了经典Lotka-Volterra理论（classical Lotka-Volterra theory）在群落集体现象解析分析上的不足。

Abstract: Ecological communities with structured interactions exhibit collective phenomena such as percolation and clustering of occupied sites. While these effects have been documented in experiments and simulations, systematic analytical understanding has remained limited. In this paper, we develop a dynamical theory of these phenomena for competitive ecological systems defined on random interaction graphs. We introduce a discrete version of the generalized Lotka-Volterra model that preserves key macroscopic features of continuous ecological dynamics while enabling analytical treatment. Within this framework, we characterize the emergence of percolating clusters and describe the spatial organization of surviving sites. Our analysis uncovers which equilibria can be reached by the dynamics and shows how this dynamical accessibility governs the onset of clustering and percolation. In doing so, our framework complements classical Lotka-Volterra theory by providing a dynamical perspective on the collective organization of structured communities.

### [209] [REM universality and Poisson-Dirichlet Gibbs weights for linear random energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07757)
*Francesco Concetti,Simone Franchini*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类Ising自旋哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）在独立稀疏采样下的能级统计，证明了其点过程在适当中心化后弱收敛到具有指数强度的泊松点过程（Poisson point process），从而在能级结构上实现随机能量模型（Random Energy Model, REM）的普适性（universality）。此外，还确定了Gibbs权重的极限分布（泊松-狄利克雷律，Poisson–Dirichlet law）以及淬火自由能（quenched free energy）在β=λ̃处的冻结相变（freezing transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作仅对能量涨落量级为e^{-O(n)}或随机选取e^{o(√n)}个构型的情形建立了该模型的REM普适性。本文旨在将REM普适性推广到指数数量级e^{O(n)}的构型稀疏采样情形，从而显著扩大已有结论的适用范围。

Method: 考虑哈密顿量H_n(h,σ)=∑_{i=1}^n h_i(σ_i-m)，其中h_i为独立同分布（i.i.d.）实随机变量，σ_i为独立同分布Ising自旋。对构型空间进行独立稀疏化（independent thinning），仅保留指数数量e^{O(n)}个构型。通过依赖于h_i的中心化（centering）操作，证明能级点过程在分布意义下收敛到具有指数强度的泊松点过程。

Result: 在指数级稀疏采样下，能级点过程弱收敛到指数强度泊松点过程，即能级渐近结构等同于REM。Gibbs权重的极限分布为泊松-狄利克雷律。淬火自由能在β=λ̃处出现冻结相变。

Conclusion: 本研究将REM普适性从亚指数构型采样规模大幅扩展到指数级构型采样规模，证实了该模型在更一般的稀疏采样条件下仍具有REM型能级统计特性；同时揭示了Gibbs权重与自由能的临界行为。

Abstract: We study the Hamiltonian $H_n(h,σ)=\sum_{i=1}^n h_i(σ_i-m), $ where $(h_i)$ are i.i.d.\ real random variables and $(σ_i)$ are i.i.d.\ Ising spins. We consider the energy levels obtained after an independent thinning that retains an exponential number of configurations ($e^{O(n)}$). We prove that, after an $(h_i)$-dependent centering, the resulting point process converges in distribution to a Poisson point process with exponential intensity. Thus, the energy levels asymptotically has the one of the Random Energy Model (REM). Our results extend previous ones, where REM universality for this model was established only either for energy fluctuations of order $e^{-O(n)}$ or for $e^{o(\sqrt n)}$ randomly selected configurations. We also identify the limiting Gibbs weights, which converge to a Poisson--Dirichlet law, and the quenched free energy, which exhibits a freezing transition at $β=\tildeλ$. The proofs are presented here in compressed form; full details are given in the companion preprint.

</details>


### [210] [Pointwise Complexity for Gaussian Fields: Upper Envelopes, Algorithmic Lower Bounds, and Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07931)
*Yunbei Xu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个面向中心化高斯过程的方差感知逐点控制测度定理，推广了经典泛链（generic chaining）理论；同时基于交互式Fano/数据处理原理给出了贝叶斯算法下界，并通过一个加权基示例揭示了各复杂度度量之间的分离关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典泛链理论（generic chaining）仅刻画了高斯过程的期望上确界$\mathbb E\sup_{x\in T}X_x$，缺乏同时高概率的逐点（pointwise）控制；同时，传统极小极大风险在过参数化（overparameterized）环境中要么过于粗糙，要么依赖不可知的预言（oracle），需要更精细的局部几何复杂度度量。

Method: 证明了一个方差感知的逐点控制测度定理（variance-aware pointwise majorizing-measure theorem），通过逐点Fernique-Talagrand泛函$Φ_μ(x):=\int_0^{4σ(x)}\sqrt{\log\frac{1}{μ(B_d(x,\varepsilon))}}\,d\varepsilon$结合高斯尾部项给出全场的高概率包络（envelope）。此外，基于交互式Fano/数据处理原理（interactive Fano/data-processing principle），利用精确的鬼小弹球质量（ghost small-ball mass）$\mathbb E_{Y\sim Q}π(B_d(\widehat t(Y),Δ))$导出贝叶斯算法下界，并在高斯定位实验（Gaussian location experiments）中通过比较解码器（comparison decoders）建立联系。

Result: 得到了高斯过程中经典泛链的可重用场级精炼（field-level refinement），以及深度神经网络点态经验过程界的对应物。构造了一个加权基（weighted-basis）示例，展示了固定先验下的通常Fano松弛、贝叶斯算法下界、选定子图集上的点态高斯包络以及全类极小极大风险/全局高斯尺度之间的分离。

Conclusion: 算法下界（algorithmic lower bounds）在过参数化环境（overparameterized ambient classes）中为固定估计量提供了点态复杂度的局部几何证书（local-geometric certificates），恰好填补了经典极小极大理论过于粗糙或依赖预言的空白区域。

Abstract: We prove a variance-aware pointwise majorizing-measure theorem for centered Gaussian processes. Classical generic chaining characterizes the scalar quantity $\mathbb E\sup_{x\in T}X_x$; the theorem here gives a simultaneous high-probability envelope for the entire field. For an ambient prior $μ$, the envelope at $x$ is governed by a pointwise Fernique-Talagrand functional \[Φ_μ(x):=\int_0^{4σ(x)}\sqrt{\log\frac{1}{μ(B_d(x,\varepsilon))}}\,d\varepsilon,\] together with the corresponding Gaussian tail term. The theorem provides a reusable field-level refinement of classical generic chaining and a Gaussian-process counterpart of pointwise empirical-process bounds for deep neural networks.
  We also record a Bayesian algorithmic lower envelope from the interactive Fano/data-processing principle. For a known prior $π$, an observation channel, and a concrete estimator $\widehat t(Y)$, the lower bound is expressed through the exact ghost small-ball mass $\mathbb E_{Y\sim Q}π(B_d(\widehat t(Y),Δ))$, rather than a worst-case covering number. In Gaussian location experiments, comparison decoders convert Bayes location error into lower bounds on decision-aligned Gaussian ranges. We then construct an elementary weighted-basis example separating the usual Fano relaxation for a fixed prior, the Bayesian algorithmic lower envelope, the pointwise Gaussian envelope on the selected subatlas, and the full-class minimax risk/global Gaussian scale. Together, these results show that algorithmic lower bounds provide local-geometric certificates of pointwise complexity for fixed estimators in overparameterized ambient classes, precisely in regimes where classical minimax theory becomes either too coarse or oracle-dependent.

</details>

### [211] [Multicriticality and Scaling: Mellin Spectral Theory, and the Decoupling of Geometric and Spectral Exponents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07644)
*Laurence A. Jacobs,Alejandro Frank*

Main category: math.GM

TL;DR: 本文发展了乘法半直线上的标度不变算子（scale-invariant operators）的谱理论，证明其核（kernel）必然因子化为幂律包络与形状函数的乘积，并揭示了几何指数（geometric exponent）与谱指数（spectral exponent）之间的解耦（decoupling），为多重临界性（multicriticality）提供了精确的数学刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标度不变算子（scale-invariant operators）在重整化群（renormalization group）和多体物理中扮演核心角色，但其谱结构（spectral structure）和不同指数之间的独立关系缺乏严格的数学理解，尤其是多重临界性（multicriticality）的起源尚不清晰。

Method: 利用梅林变换（Mellin transform）对角化乘法半直线$(\mathbb{R}_+, dx/x)$上的标度不变算子；通过对称性约束将核因子化为$(xy)^{-a/2}F(x/y)$形式；对具体核$F(t)=c\rho^{|\ln t|}$计算梅林乘子（Mellin multiplier）的洛伦兹型（Lorentzian）谱；通过有限维截断（finite-dimensional truncation）分析有限尺寸修正。

Result: 几何指数$a$由幂律包络$(xy)^{-a/2}$决定，谱指数$b$由形状函数的梅林变换$\tilde{F}(\omega)$决定，二者一般不等；离散自相似性（discrete self-similarity）导致本征向量（eigenvector）在格点上的坍缩；有限尺寸修正（finite-size corrections）通过数值量化得到。

Conclusion: 指数$a=b$对应重整化群（renormalization group）的简单临界不动点（simple critical fixed point），而$a\neq b$标志着存在多个独立标度维度（independent scaling dimensions），从而为多重临界性（multicriticality）提供了严格的谱理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a spectral theory of scale-invariant operators on the multiplicative half-line $(\mathbb{R}_+, dx/x)$. A symmetric kernel $M(x, y)$ satisfying $M(kx, ky) = k^{-a}M(x, y)$ necessarily factorizes as $(xy)^{-a/2}F(x/y)$, where the shape function $F$ depends only on the ratio of its arguments. The Mellin transform diagonalizes such operators: the generalized eigenfunctions are $ψ_ω(x) = x^{-a/2+iω}$, and the eigenvalues are the Mellin multiplier $\tilde{F}(ω)$. This structure reveals a fundamental decoupling of two exponents. The geometric exponent $a$, carried by the power-law envelope $(xy)^{-a/2}$, governs the matrix scaling under dilation. The spectral exponent $b$, measured from the eigenvalue decay of the finite-dimensional truncation, is an effective quantity determined by the shape of $\tilde{F}(ω)$. For the explicit kernel $F(t) = c ρ^{|\ln t|}$, the Mellin multiplier is a Lorentzian of width $σ= -\ln ρ$, not a power law -- so $b$ is generically distinct from $a$. This decoupling provides a precise mathematical characterization of multicriticality: the equality $a = b$ corresponds to a simple critical fixed point of the Renormalization Group, while $a \neq b$ signals the presence of multiple independent scaling dimensions. We prove that the discrete self-similarity condition forces eigenvector collapse on the lattice, motivating the continuum formulation. Finite-size corrections from lattice sampling are quantified numerically.

</details>

### [212] [B-model Categorical Enumerative Invariants and holomorphic anomaly equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07960)
*Yefeng Shen,Junwu Tu*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究光滑射影卡拉比-丘三折叠（Calabi-Yau 3-folds）上相干层导出范畴（derived categories of coherent sheaves）的B-模型范畴枚举不变量（CEI）。文章首先在一般框架下证明了CEI的胀子方程（dilaton equation）、弦方程（string equation）和除子方程（divisor equation），随后利用这些方程与Givental量子化公式（Givental quantization formula），证明了任意小万有族（miniversal family）光滑射影Calabi-Yau三折叠上的B-模型CEI满足Bershadsky-Cecotti-Ooguri-Vafa提出的全纯异常方程（holomorphic anomaly equations）。这为将CEI作为B-模型拓扑弦配分函数（B-model topological string partition function）的严格数学定义提供了有力证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为B-模型拓扑弦理论（B-model topological string theory）提供一个严格的数学基础，寻找能够满足全纯异常方程的数学对象，从而将范畴枚举不变量与物理中的拓扑弦配分函数联系起来。

Method: 首先在一般上下文中证明CEI的胀子方程、弦方程和除子方程；然后结合这些方程与Givental量子化公式，推导CEI满足全纯异常方程。

Result: 证明了B-模型CEI满足Bershadsky-Cecotti-Ooguri-Vafa提出的全纯异常方程。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，范畴枚举不变量（CEI）可被视为B-模型拓扑弦配分函数（B-model topological string partition function）的严格数学定义。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the B-model categorical enumerative invariants (CEI) associated with derived categories of coherent sheaves on smooth projective Calabi-Yau $3$-folds. We first prove the analogs of the dilaton, string, and divisor equations of CEI in a general context. Then we use these equations and the Givental quantization formula to prove that the B-model CEI for any miniversal family of smooth projective Calabi-Yau $3$-folds satisfies the holomorphic anomaly equations introduced by Bershadsky-Cecotti-Ooguri-Vafa. This provides strong evidence that CEI may be taken as a rigorous mathematical definition of the B-model topological string partition function.

### [213] [Cocompletions for non-abelian vertex tensor categories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07987)
*Robert McRae,Cris Negron*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文证明顶点算子代数（vertex operator algebra）$C_1$-余有限模（$C_1$-cofinite module）范畴的辫子幺半结构（braided monoidal structure）可唯一扩展到该范畴在滤余极限（filtered colimit）完备化上的顶点代数自然辫子幺半结构，并在抽象范畴论层面建立了一类稠密包含（dense inclusion）下幺半结构扩展的存在唯一性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Huang 最近证明了任意顶点算子代数的 $C_1$-余有限模范畴具有自然的辫子幺半结构。本文旨在证明该结构可进一步扩展到该范畴的滤余极限完备化中，从而为顶点算子代数扩张（vertex operator algebra extension）的表象理论提供统一的代数框架。

Method: 不使用 $C_1$-余有限模范畴是阿贝尔范畴（abelian）或 $C_1$-余有限模在余完备化中紧致（compact）的假定，而是利用稠密包含 $\mathscr{C}_0 \to \mathscr{C}$ 这一抽象的范畴论工具，将具体的顶点代数问题提炼为一般幺半范畴中幺半结构沿稠密包含扩展的存在唯一性问题。

Result: 在一般广义 $V$-模（generalized $V$-module）构成的背景范畴内，$C_1$-余有限 $V$-模范畴的滤余极限完备化上存在唯一的、顶点代数自然（vertex algebraically natural）的辫子幺半结构。作为推广，建立了抽象的幺半范畴中，幺半结构沿稠密包含扩展的存在唯一性定理。

Conclusion: 该结果适用于许多可被实现为若干顶点算子子代数的 $C_1$-余有限模范畴滤余极限完备化中对象的顶点算子代数，从而在顶点算子代数扩张的表象理论中具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: It was recently shown by Huang that the category of $C_1$-cofinite modules for any vertex operator algebra $V$ admits a natural braided monoidal structure. Here, we show that this structure extends uniquely to a vertex algebraically natural braided monoidal structure on the completion of the category of $C_1$-cofinite $V$-modules under filtered colimits, within the ambient category of all generalized $V$-modules. A critical point here is that we do not assume the category of $C_1$-cofinite $V$-modules is abelian or that $C_1$-cofinite modules are compact in the cocompletion, since these properties are not known to hold in general. Our results have many applications in the representation theory of vertex operator algebra extensions, since many vertex operator algebras can be realized as objects in the filtered colimit completion of the category of $C_1$-cofinite modules for a vertex operator subalgebra. Generalizing from the specific vertex algebraic setting, we also establish existence and uniqueness for extensions of monoidal structures along a dense inclusion $\mathscr{C}_0 \to \mathscr{C}$ from an abstract, essentially small monoidal category into a well-structured cocomplete target.

### [214] [Exact Boundary Enforcement Along Implicit Geometries for Physics-Informed, Deep Learning Problems in Continuum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07579)
*Cody Rucker,Brittany A. Erickson*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了物理信息神经网络（PINN）在连续介质力学初边值问题中，软边界强制与硬边界强制策略对模型精度和训练时长的影响，发现一阶平面应变问题下PINN精度更高，且存在精度与运行时间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续介质力学中适定问题的解连续依赖于边界条件，边界数据执行方式的变化会影响依赖高效正演模型的反演技术的可靠性，因此需要理解不同边界实现技术对前向模型性能的影响。

Method: 通过在隐式边界表示上插值边界数据，测量物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural network, PINN）在软边界强制（soft boundary enforcement）和硬边界强制（hard boundary enforcement）不同配置下的性能。针对弹性动力学平面应变问题，提出了在任意隐式定义域边界上对牵引条件进行硬强制的方法，考虑了控制方程的一阶和二阶两种形式。

Result: PINN在求解一阶平面应变问题时获得了更高的相对精度；软边界强制与硬边界强制之间存在权衡：全部采用软强制时精度更高但运行时间更长，全部采用硬强制时精度较低但运行时间更短。

Conclusion: 边界强制策略的选择对PINN求解连续介质力学问题有显著影响，精度与运行时间之间的权衡由软硬边界的数量比例决定，研究者可根据实际需求选择合适的边界实施方式。

Abstract: Solutions to well-posed problems in continuum mechanics are continuously dependent upon prescribed boundary conditions. Because of this, variations in the enforcement of boundary data can impact the reliability of inversion techniques that rely on efficient and accurate forward models. To this end, it is necessary to understand how specific boundary implementation techniques can affect the performance of a given forward model. Our work focuses on the impact that key modeling decisions have on physics-informed neural network (PINN) solutions for initial boundary value problems in continuum mechanics. By interpolating boundary data over implicit boundary representations, we measure the performance of a physics-informed neural network across different configurations of soft and hard boundary enforcement. We target the problem of elastodynamic plane-strain and present a method of hard-enforcement of traction conditions over arbitrary, implicitly-defined, domain boundaries considering both first and second order formulations of the governing equations. We show that PINNs achieve a higher relative accuracy when solving the first-order plane strain problem and we observe a tradeoff between the final relative error and the total run time to complete training. This tradeoff is characterized by the number of hard and soft boundaries where, in the extremes, all soft-enforcement results in greater accuracy with a longer run time, while all hard-enforcement leads to lesser accuracy and a shorter run time.

</details>


### [215] [PDE-Agents: An LLM-Orchestrated Multi-Agent Framework for Automated Finite Element Simulations with Knowledge Graph-Augmented Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07850)
*Sayan Adhikari,Gulshan Noorsumar,Øyvind Jensen*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了PDE-Agents，一个基于多智能体（multi-agent）架构的自然语言交互系统，可自动完成偏微分方程（PDE）/有限元方法（FEM）仿真的完整生命周期。系统由三个大语言模型（LLM）智能体（Simulation、Analytics、Database）通过LangGraph监督器协调运行，并集成GraphRAG知识库。实验表明，知识图谱（KG）的集成模式（而非内容）是决定GraphRAG增强效果的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PDE/FEM仿真自动化工具缺乏端到端自然语言交互能力，且知识库（knowledge base）对大语言模型智能体的增强机制尚未明确。本文旨在验证多智能体架构能否通过图检索增强生成（GraphRAG）显著提升仿真任务的成功率与输出质量。

Method: 提出PDE-Agents生态系统，包含三个LLM智能体（Simulation、Analytics、Database），由LangGraph监督器统一编排；采用本地开源LLM栈（Qwen3-Coder-Next、Llama 4 Scout）运行于双NVIDIA RTX PRO 6000 GPU；构建GraphRAG知识库（Neo4j图数据库+768维向量嵌入）存储材料属性、失效模式与历史运行记录。通过三项消融实验（KG On、KG Off、KG Smart）、新颖材料测试、100任务知识库增长实验等进行评估。

Result: 热方程求解器验证确认了二阶空间收敛性（O(h²)）；50任务消融实验中KG Smart模式（KG Smart）达到100%成功率，物理一致性（physics）得分0.933（KG Off为0.853）、材料属性保真度（MPF）0.926（KG Off为0.796）；虚构新材料实验中KG Smart的MPF达到1.00，而KG Off基线仅为0.34；1,369次生产运行实现97.8%成功率、57.6%首次尝试成功率；100任务增长实验中困难任务MPF提升8.8%。

Conclusion: GraphRAG增强的效果取决于集成模式（integration pattern）而非知识内容本身；智能的检索模式选择（KG Smart）可显著提升仿真任务的成功率与输出质量。

Abstract: We present PDE-Agents, a multi-agent ecosystem that automates the full lifecycle of partial differential equation (PDE) / finite element method (FEM) simulations through natural-language interaction. Three specialist large language model (LLM) agents (Simulation, Analytics, Database) are orchestrated via a LangGraph supervisor, with a local open-source LLM stack (Qwen3-Coder-Next, Llama 4 Scout) on dual NVIDIA RTX PRO 6000 GPUs. The architecture is model-agnostic, validated across two LLM generations. A GraphRAG knowledge base (Neo4j, 768-d vector embeddings) encodes curated material properties, known failure patterns, and prior run lineage. We report seven contributions: (i) a verification and validation (V&V) study confirming second-order spatial convergence (O(h^2)) on the heat-equation solver; (ii) a three-way ablation over 50 tasks with a frozen KG (KG On, KG Off, KG Smart), where KG Smart reaches 100% success and the highest output quality (physics 0.933 vs. 0.853 for KG Off; MPF 0.926 vs. 0.796); (iii) a novel-material experiment with three fictional materials known only to the KG, where KG Smart attains near-perfect material property fidelity (MPF = 1.00) versus 0.34 for the KG-free baseline; (iv) a failure analysis tracing KG On's three failures to budget exhaustion and timeout, establishing warm-start injection as the dominant reliability factor; (v) an adaptive framework selecting the optimal retrieval mode per task; (vi) production metrics from 1,369 runs (97.8% success, 57.6% first-try); and (vii) a 100-task KG growth experiment showing a difficulty-dependent gain, with hard-task MPF improving 8.8% while easy/novel tasks stay at ceiling. All code, models, and evaluation artifacts are released openly. Our findings show that integration pattern, not knowledge content, determines whether GraphRAG augmentation helps or hinders LLM agents.

</details>

### [216] [MatMind: A Structure-Activity Knowledge-Driven Generative Foundation Model for Materials Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07712)
*Zhan'ao Yao,Boxuan Zhang,Jingyuan Shu,Xiaoyu Wu,Rongyan Wang,Linjing Li,Dajun Zeng,Yudong Yao,Tingwei Chen,Youwei Wang,Xiaolin Zhao,Jiahui Shi,Jianjun Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出MatMind，一种面向晶体材料科学的生成式基础模型（generative foundation model），通过结构-活性知识注入、双头架构（dual-head architecture）与多目标物理信息强化学习（multi-objective physics-informed reinforcement learning）的统一范式，在能量凸包高度、体模量、带隙预测以及无条件/条件晶体生成任务上超越或匹敌传统窄域专家模型，证明了大语言模型（LLM）范式可作为晶体材料科学的统一骨干。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI驱动晶体材料科学依赖为特定任务设计的窄域架构（narrow architectures），如图神经网络（graph neural networks）用于性质预测、扩散模型（diffusion models）用于晶体生成，这些模型各自在自身领域表现出色，但无法作为跨全谱材料问题的共享骨干。生成式大语言模型（generative large language models）虽能统一结构表征、定量预测与构效推理，但该范式在实际材料学任务中尚未达到与窄域专家模型竞争的水平。

Method: MatMind采用渐进式训练框架（progressive training framework），包含三个核心机制：（1）结构-活性知识注入（structure-activity knowledge injection）；（2）双头架构（dual-head architecture），在共享表征空间内联合训练语言推理与数值回归；（3）多目标物理信息强化学习（multi-objective physics-informed reinforcement learning），优化稳定性、新颖性与结构多样性。

Result: 在能量凸包高度（energy above hull）、体模量（bulk modulus）和带隙（band gap）预测上达到最低平均绝对误差（mean absolute error），超越专用图神经网络预测器；无条件晶体生成（unconditional crystal generation）的S.U.N.率达到65.3%；在磁化密度条件生成（magnetization-density-conditioned generation）任务中，于60万以上训练样本里仅有21个正样本的情况下，实现了可比的多倍改进。

Conclusion: MatMind在匹配或超越窄域专家模型自身优势任务的同时，以单一统一模型运行，证明基于大语言模型（LLM）的范式能够作为晶体材料科学未来发展的可行骨干（viable backbone）。

Abstract: Progress in AI-driven crystal materials science has so far been carried by narrow architectures purpose-built for individual tasks -- graph neural networks for property prediction, diffusion and flow-matching models for crystal generation -- each excelling within its niche yet unable to act as a shared backbone across the full spectrum of materials problems. Generative large language models offer a fundamentally different paradigm, in which structural representation, quantitative prediction, and structure-activity reasoning can be unified within one model, but the materials community has yet to see this paradigm realized at a level competitive with established narrow specialists. Here we present MatMind, a generative foundation model purpose-built for crystal materials science under this paradigm, developed through the coordinated activation of structure-activity knowledge and physics-informed feedback within a progressive training framework -- combining structure-activity knowledge injection, a dual-head architecture that jointly trains language reasoning and numerical regression in a shared representation space, and multi-objective physics-informed reinforcement learning over stability, novelty, and structural diversity. Across three task families, MatMind attains the lowest mean absolute error on energy above hull, bulk modulus, and band gap -- surpassing graph neural network predictors purpose-built for these tasks -- reaches an S.U.N. rate of 65.3% on unconditional crystal generation, and achieves a comparable multiplicative improvement on magnetization-density-conditioned generation, where only 21 positive samples exist within over 600000 training entries. By matching or surpassing narrow specialists on their own ground while operating within a single unified model, MatMind shows that the LLM-based paradigm can serve as a viable backbone for crystal materials science going forward.

</details>


### [217] [Machine learning assisted molecular dynamics of charge-transfer mechanisms at Li/Ga-doped Li$_7$La$_3$Zr$_2$O$_{12}$ (LLZO) interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07772)
*Arseniy S. Burov,Artem M. Abakumov,Dmitry A. Aksyonov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过训练鎓矩张量势（moment tensor potentials, MTPs）并结合机器学习分子动力学（machine-learning molecular dynamics, MLMD）模拟，系统研究了Li/LLZO固态电解质界面的电荷转移动力学，发现Li/Ga-LLZO界面的电荷转移活化能很低（167 meV），表明其并非电池性能的限速步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统密度泛函理论（DFT）和微动弹性带（nudged elastic band, NEB）方法忽略了多体关联和有限温度效应，可能导致活化能垒计算不准确。因此需要更精确的方法来评估固态电解质（solid electrolytes, SEs）与锂金属之间界面电荷转移的真实动力学行为。

Method: 针对石榴石型LLZO体系（t-LLZO、c-LLZO、Ga-LLZO）和锂金属训练了鎓矩张量势（MTPs），进而执行机器学习分子动力学（MLMD）模拟，研究Li⁺在体相和Li/SE界面的扩散行为；同时引入停留时间窗方法（residence-time window method）以滤除离子震颤（rattling）并分离出真实的电荷转移事件。

Result: Li/Ga-LLZO界面的电荷转移活化能为167 meV，Ga-LLZO体相为200 meV，对应的界面电阻约为~10⁻⁵ Ω·cm²。这些结果表明Li/Ga-LLZO的本征电荷转移并非限速步骤。

Conclusion: Li/LLZO体系具有快速的界面动力学，所提出的MTP-MLMD结合停留时间窗方法可用于进一步优化固态电池中的界面设计。

Abstract: Interfacial charge transfer between solid electrolytes (SEs) and Li metal is a key factor limiting all-solid-state battery performance. Conventional density functional theory and nudged elastic band calculations neglect many-body correlations and finite-temperature effects, which can lead to inaccurate activation barriers. Here, we trained moment tensor potentials (MTPs) for garnet LLZO systems (t-LLZO, c-LLZO, and Ga-LLZO) and Li metal, enabling machine-learning molecular dynamics (MLMD) simulations of Li$^+$ diffusion in the bulk and at Li/SE interfaces. We also introduce a residence-time window method that filters out ion rattling and isolates genuine charge-transfer events. The resulting charge-transfer activation energies are low: 167 meV at the Li/Ga-LLZO interface and 200 meV in Ga-LLZO, corresponding to resistances of $\sim \, 10^{-5} \, Ω\,\mathrm{cm}^{2}$. These results indicate that intrinsic Li/Ga-LLZO charge transfer is not rate-limiting. Overall, our findings clarify the fast interfacial kinetics in Li/LLZO systems, and the proposed methodology can aid further interface optimization in solid-state batteries.

</details>


### [218] [Redox-Active Halide Materials for Cathode Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07815)
*Zhuohan Li,Gerbrand Ceder*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）系统研究了Li-M-Cl（M = 3d过渡金属）三元电化学活性卤化物（eREAL）材料的相稳定性与电化学活性，发现金属-氯键的高离子性提升了阳离子氧化还原电位但易引发Cl氧化与Cl-Cl二聚化，阴离子替代可有效调控电位窗口，而该类材料平缓的电压曲线可能带来电化学兼容性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电化学活性卤化物（eREAL）材料是一类兼具高锂离子电导率与过渡金属氧化还原活性的新兴材料，有望作为氧化还原活性阴极电解液（catholyte）大幅提升固态电池的能量密度。然而，其稳定性和电化学活性的理论基础尚不完善，亟需系统性的理论分析来指导材料设计与优化。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），针对Li-M-Cl（M = 3d过渡金属）三元体系，系统考察了不同金属-氯比例、过渡金属种类、氧化态（oxidation state）及阴离子骨架（anion framework）下eREAL结构的相稳定性，并计算了阳离子和阴离子的氧化还原电位（redox potential）。

Result: 研究发现，金属-氯键的高离子性（ionicity）使得阳离子氧化还原电位高于传统氧化物正极材料，但同时也促进了高电压下的Cl氧化和Cl-Cl二聚化（dimerization），可能限制材料稳定性。阴离子替代可有效调控阴阳离子氧化还原电位，其中F替代是扩展可逆电压窗口的可行途径。此外，eREAL化合物普遍呈现平缓的电压曲线（flat voltage profiles），这可能在与不同电压范围工作的活性材料配对时产生电化学兼容性挑战。

Conclusion: 本研究为eREAL材料的氧化还原行为提供了综合分析，为其在下一代电池应用中的合理设计与优化奠定了基础。

Abstract: Electrochemically redox-active halide (eREAL) materials are an emerging class of materials that combine high Li-ion conductivity with transition-metal redox activity, making them promising candidates for cathode or catholyte applications. As a redox-active catholyte, they could significantly increase the energy density of solid-state batteries. In this work, we perform first-principles calculations on Li-M-Cl (M = 3d transition metals) ternaries to establish such a theoretical foundation for their stability and electrochemical activity. We map the phase stability of eREAL structures with varying metal-to-Cl ratio, transition-metal species, oxidation states, and anion frameworks, and compute cation and anion redox potentials. We find that the high ionicity of metal-Cl bonds elevates cation redox potentials above those of conventional oxide cathodes, but also will promote Cl oxidation and Cl-Cl dimerization at high voltages, which may limit the stability of these materials. Anion substitution effectively tunes both cation and anion redox potentials, with F substitution standing out as a viable route to extend the reversible voltage window. Beyond the anion redox issue, eREAL compounds generally exhibit flat voltage profiles, which potentially poses an electrochemical compatibility challenge when paired with active materials that operate at different voltage values or over wider voltage ranges. Collectively, our study provides a comprehensive analysis for redox behavior of eREAL materials, paving the way for their rational design and optimization in next-generation battery applications.

</details>


### [219] [Agentic multi-fidelity learning of quasiparticle and excitonic properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07836)
*Arnab Neogi,Aaron Forde,Christopher A. Lane,Sergei Tretiak,Jian-Xin Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种智能体引导的多保真度框架，用于修正GW-Bethe-Salpeter激发态计算中的数值不稳定性与收敛失败。该框架通过结构智能体评估计算置信度、结合高斯过程校正，在MoS2-WS2双层体系中显著提升了准粒子能隙和激子结合能的预测准确性，并证明了激发态材料代理学习必须诊断数值脆弱性，而非直接内插原始第一性原理数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体GW-Bethe-Salpeter方程计算对现代低维纳米材料的电子结构和光学性质模拟至关重要，但其计算成本高昂，且在高通量工作流中难以检测局域数值不稳定性或收敛失败。现有方法缺乏系统性地识别和修正这些数值伪影的机制，亟需一种可靠且可迁移的校正框架。

Method: 提出一种智能体引导的多保真度框架（agent-guided multi-fidelity framework）。该框架包含：(1) 一个结构智能体（structural agent），通过分配置信权重并选择性使用少量高精度参考点来评估各计算任务；(2) 机器学习模型跨相关系统传递信息；(3) 高斯过程校正（Gaussian process corrections）恢复改进的准粒子能隙（quasiparticle gaps）和激子结合能（exciton binding energies），并给出校准的不确定性估计。

Result: 该框架能够识别出尖峰状偏离、近零能隙崩塌和跨保真度不一致性（与脆性长波长介电屏蔽相关）。校正后的结果在不消除物理应变依赖性的前提下，有效修正了数值引入的伪影，相较于无智能体基线方案，与高保真度参考值的一致性显著提高。

Conclusion: 激发态材料的可靠代理学习（surrogate learning）需要明确诊断数值脆弱性（numerical fragility），而非直接对原始第一性原理数据点进行内插。该框架易于迁移至其他具有强量子限域效应的光电子纳米材料，如量子点（quantum dots）、纳米带（nanoribbons）、层状二维半导体及杂化钙钛矿纳米结构。

Abstract: Many-body GW-Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations are essential for accurate simulations of electronic structure and optical properties in modern low-dimensional nanomaterials. However, these methods are computationally demanding and can exhibit localized numerical instabilities or convergence failures that are difficult to detect within high-throughput workflows. We introduce an agent-guided multi-fidelity framework for correcting GW-Bethe-Salpeter excited-state landscapes in strained MoS2-WS2 bilayers. Across stacking registries, strain branches and reciprocal-space samplings, the workflow identifies spike-like excursions, near-zero-gap collapse and cross-fidelity inconsistencies associated with fragile long-wavelength dielectric screening. A structural agent evaluates calculations by assigning confidence weights and selectively using a small number of high-accuracy reference points. Machine learning models then transfer information across related systems and apply Gaussian process corrections to recover improved quasiparticle gaps and exciton binding energies, with calibrated uncertainty estimates. The approach corrects numerically induced artifacts without erasing physical strain dependence and substantially improves agreement with higher-fidelity references relative to a no-agent baseline. These results show that reliable surrogate learning for excited-state materials requires explicit diagnosis of numerical fragility, not direct interpolation of raw first-principles data points. The proposed framework is readily transferable to other optoelectronic nanomaterials characterized by strong quantum confinement, such as quantum dots, nanoribbons, layered two-dimensional semiconductors, and hybrid perovskite nanostructures.

</details>


### [220] [Crystallizing Substrates Drag Supported Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07862)
*Cheng-Yu Chen,Duncan Burns,Peter W. Voorhees,Eric A. Stach*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过原位透射电镜（in situ TEM）统计追踪 Pt 纳米颗粒运动，并结合时间分辨衍射和 4D-STEM 表征，实验证明了非晶 AlO$_x$ 薄膜中的晶化前沿（crystallization front）能够主动拖拽（drag）支撑其上的 Pt 纳米颗粒进行长距离迁移；相场模拟（phase-field simulation）揭示颗粒-基底界面能（interfacial energy）的不对称性是驱动该运动的唯一机制，表明任何传播的表面能边界均可成为支撑纳米颗粒迁移的确定性驱动力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体基底发生晶化时，移动的非晶-晶态转变前沿会分隔出不同表面能的区域，形成动态界面能边界（interfacial energy boundary）。支撑于该边界上的纳米颗粒会遭遇不对称的颗粒-基底界面能环境，这构成了横向热力学驱动力（lateral thermodynamic driving force）。然而，这一机制是否普遍成立以及背后的动力学细节尚待验证。

Method: 采用原位透射电镜（in situ TEM）统计追踪 Pt 纳米颗粒的运动；结合时间分辨衍射（time-resolved diffraction）和四维扫描透射电镜（4D-STEM）表征基底晶化过程；通过 4D-STEM 虚拟结晶度图（virtual crystallinity maps）建立晶化前沿与颗粒迁移的时间关联；利用相场模拟（phase-field simulations）验证界面能差异驱动颗粒迁移的机制。

Result: 晶化前沿的启动与 Pt 纳米颗粒的快速迁移在时间上相关；4D-STEM 虚拟结晶度图证实晶化前沿驱动了颗粒运动；相场模拟表明，仅凭颗粒-基底间的界面能对比（interfacial energy contrast）即可维持颗粒拖拽（particle drag）；模拟进一步识别出颗粒表面曲率梯度（curvature gradients）是前沿重新分配质量并推动颗粒位移的微观机制。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了支撑纳米颗粒迁移的一个通用机制：任何基底上的传播性表面能边界（propagating surface-energy boundary）均可作为支撑纳米颗粒输运的确定性驱动器（deterministic driver）。

Abstract: When a solid support undergoes crystallization, the advancing amorphous-to-crystalline transformation front separates regions of distinct surface energy, creating a moving interfacial energy boundary. A supported nanoparticle straddling such a boundary experiences an asymmetric particle-substrate interfacial energy environment that constitutes a lateral thermodynamic driving force for migration. Here, using in situ transmission electron microscopy to track Pt nanoparticle motion statistically, paired with time-resolved diffraction and 4D-STEM analysis to characterize support crystallization, we demonstrate that propagating crystallization fronts in amorphous AlO$_x$ thin films actively drag supported Pt nanoparticles over long distances. Temporal correlation between the onsets of support crystallization and rapid particle migration, together with 4D-STEM virtual crystallinity maps, establishes that the front drives particle motion. Phase-field simulations confirm that particle-substrate interfacial energy contrast alone sustains particle drag, and identify curvature gradients along the particle surface as the mechanism by which the advancing front redistributes mass and displaces the particle. These results establish a general mechanism by which any propagating surface-energy boundary on a substrate can act as a deterministic driver of supported nanoparticle transport.

</details>


### [221] [Elusive Exciton Insulator States in 1T-HfTe2: Exciton softening, and Symmetry Breaking by Ab Initio Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07863)
*Hong Tang,Niraj Pangeni,Daniel D. Rivera,Adrienn Ruzsinszky*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过meta GGA计算和Bethe-Salpeter方程方法，结合结构与电子对称性破缺分析，研究了单层、双层、三层及块体1T HfTe₂中的激子绝缘体态。结果显示单层和双层具有负激子能量，可自发形成束缚激子与激子绝缘体（EI）态，而三层和块体则不支持EI态。研究还发现结构对称性破缺导致的Hf原子面内位移很小，且单层的电子对称性破缺计算结果与实验高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验已在1T HfTe₂中发现激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator, EI）态的证据，但该材料体系在不同维度（单层、双层、三层及块体）下的EI行为尚待系统的理论研究，以阐明其形成条件与机理。

Method: 采用先进的meta广义梯度近似（meta GGA）计算以及模型Bethe-Salpeter方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation, BSE）方法，并结合结构对称性破缺（structural symmetry breaking）与电子对称性破缺（electronic symmetry breaking）分析。

Result: 单层和双层1T HfTe₂表现出负激子能量（negative exciton energy），可自发形成束缚激子与EI态；三层和块体则呈现正激子能量，不支持EI态。结构对称性破缺计算显示Hf原子面内位移极小。单层电子对称性破缺计算在M点出现明显的展开价带特征，在Gamma点费米能级附近无展开导带态，与实验一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持低维1T HfTe₂中存在EI态，且所建立的方法可推广至其他相关量子材料体系中EI行为的研究。

Abstract: Recent experiments have provided evidence for excitonic insulator (EI) states in 1T HfTe2. In this work, we investigate EI states in monolayer, bilayer, trilayer, and bulk 1T HfTe2 using advanced meta generalized gradient approximation (meta GGA) calculations and a model Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE) approach, together with structural and electronic symmetry breaking analyses. Our results show that both the monolayer and bilayer exhibit negative exciton energies, leading to the spontaneous formation of bound excitons and EI states, whereas the trilayer and bulk display positive exciton energies and do not support EI states. Structural symmetry-breaking calculations show very small in-plane displacements of the Hf atoms from their symmetric positions in the monolayer and multilayers, consistent with experimental observations. Interestingly, electronic symmetry-breaking calculations for the monolayer, performed using a symmetric structure and a hybrid functional, show a pronounced unfolded valence-band feature at the M point and no unfolded conduction-band states near the Fermi level at Gamma, in good agreement with experimental results. Overall, our findings support the existence of EI states in low dimensional 1T HfTe2. The methodology developed here can be readily extended to investigate EI behavior in other related quantum material systems.

</details>


### [222] [Post Annealing Crystallization behavior of RF Sputtered Yttrium Iron Garnet thin films on Si/SiO2 patterned substrates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07886)
*Maria Roman,Tito Busani,Aleem Siddiqui*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过射频溅射（RF sputtering）在带有SiO2缓冲层的Si衬底上沉积钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜，并结合后退火结晶的制造路线，目标是为实现可悬浮的YIG磁子（magnonic）器件奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: YIG因高铁磁性和长程磁子传播能力而广泛应用于磁子器件（magnonic devices），但现有制备工艺在实现可悬浮或可转移的YIG器件方面仍存在不足，需要探索可行的制造路线。

Method: 在Si衬底上生长240 nm厚的SiO2缓冲层，然后通过低真空射频溅射沉积390 nm厚的YIG薄膜。设置两组样品：一组在SiO2上通过氟刻蚀制备图案化孔对（patterned hole pairs）作为晶种形核点（seed nucleation points）；另一组为无图案的均匀沉积。随后在O2气氛、750–850°C水平炉中进行后退火再结晶。

Result: 图案化的SiO2缓冲层可作为YIG结晶的形核点，有助于研究结晶行为。通过该路线成功实现了YIG薄膜的沉积和后退火结晶，初步验证了可悬浮器件的制造可行性。但化学计量比（stoichiometry）仍需进一步优化。

Conclusion: 建立了一条通过SiO2缓冲层图案化、射频溅射沉积YIG和后退火结晶的器件制造路线。若能实现精确的成分控制，将有望实现完全悬浮与释放的YIG器件，并转移到其他衬底上。

Abstract: Yttrium Iron Garnet YIG (Y3Fe5O12), is a commonly used material for magnonic devices due to its crystal and chemical structure, which makes the material highly ferromagnetic and enables long-range magnon propagation. Magnonic devices were fabricated by depositing a 390 nm thick thin film of YIG, using low vacuum RF sputtering, on Si substrates with a 240 nm buffer layer of SiO2. Two sets of devices were used to study the effect of the Si/SiO2 interface on the YIG. The first set features patterned hole pairs on the SiO2, which was created using fluorine etching. Patterned samples were used as seed nucleation points to study the crystallization behavior. The second set was a non-patterned Si/SiO2 with YIG deposited uniformly on the top. Post-deposition recrystallization of the YIG film was accomplished in a horizontal furnace under O2 atmosphere, between 750 degrees C and 850 degrees C. By patterning devices with a SiO2 buffer layer, depositing YIG via RF sputtering, and subsequently crystallizing the films in a furnace, we establish a fabrication route toward devices that can be suspended. Although further optimization of stoichiometry is required, achieving precise compositional control would enable the realization of fully suspended and released YIG devices that can be transferred onto alternative substrates.

</details>


### [223] [Wafer-scale Demonstration of High-voltage beta-Ga2O3 MOSFETs with Excellent Uniformity and over 3kV Breakdown Voltages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07973)
*Ningtao Liu,Hengrui Zhang,Shujun Zhu,Zhihao Yan,Dongyang Han,Shen Hu,Li Ji,Ning Xia,Jichun Ye,Wenrui Zhang*

TL;DR: 该研究展示了2英寸掺硅β-Ga₂O₃(100)外延晶圆（epitaxial wafer）的晶圆级生长，并实现了均匀、高压横向β-Ga₂O₃ MOSFET阵列。MOCVD生长的外延膜具有优异的晶圆级均匀性，所制备的MOSFET击穿电压超过3 kV，开关比高于1E9，且全晶圆统计分布显示出良好的器件一致性。

Conclusion: 首次证明利用2英寸β-Ga₂O₃外延晶圆可实现晶圆级性能均匀的高压β-Ga₂O₃ MOSFET，为该材料体系在下一代功率器件中的实用化提供了关键验证。

Abstract: This study demonstrates a wafer-scale growth of a 2-inch Si-doped $β$-Ga2O3 (100) epitaxial wafer and the realization of uniform, high-voltage lateral $β$-Ga2O3 MOSFET arrays. The 2-inch homoepitaxial $β$-Ga2O3 (100) film grown by MOCVD exhibit excellent crystalline uniformity with an average rocking curve FWHM of ~27.0 arcsec and a low surface roughness less than 1 nm, alongside a uniform net doping concentration on the value of 4.60 $\times$ 1E17 cm-3. Statistical analysis across the entire wafer presents good device uniformity, with threshold voltages ranging from -28 V to -36 V, output current densities of 60-75 mA/mm, and a breakdown voltage over 3 kV. These results provide the demonstration using the 2-inch $β$-Ga2O3 epitaxial wafer to realize high-voltage $β$-Ga2O3 MOSFETs with wafer-scale performance uniformity for next-generation power device application.

### [224] [Steering Selective Formation and 2D Crystallization of [4]Radialenes on Au(111) via [1+1+1+1] Cycloaddition of Isocyanides and Enantioselective Molecular Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08111)
*Jian-Wei Liu,Ying Wang,Cui-Ping Wu,Jia-Xin Li,Li-Xia Kang,Jian-Hui Fu,Wen-Wen Gong,Pei-Nian Liu,Deng-Yuan Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了在金(111)表面上通过异腈（isocyanide）的[1+1+1+1]环加成反应，实现高化学选择性和立体选择性（stereoselectivity）地生成四氮杂[4]轮烯（tetraaza[4]radialene），并通过对映选择性分子识别（enantioselective molecular recognition）驱动其长程有序二维（2D）同手性分子结晶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共轭碳环（conjugated carbon rings）是有机功能材料的基本骨架，但如何在表面实现其高化学选择性和立体选择性的形成与二维结晶仍是一个重大挑战。

Method: 采用渐进退火（progressive annealing）方法；结合扫描隧道显微镜/谱学（STM/STS）和非接触原子力显微镜（nc-AFM）确定原子结构与分子轨道；利用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算揭示反应机理与选择性来源。

Result: 室温下异腈与金吸附原子形成双轴对称的异腈-金-异腈配合物；升高退火温度诱导配合物转化并发生共价聚合，选择性生成同向构型（homotactic configuration）的四氮杂[4]轮烯；四氮杂[4]轮烯通过多重C-H···Cl氢键相互作用组装为二维同手性分子晶体；四元环呈平面几何结构，具有定域的最低未占分子轨道（LUMO）；[1+1+1+1]环加成涉及C-C键的逐步形成，高选择性源于空间位阻效应。

Abstract: Conjugated carbon rings are fundamental skeletons of organic functional materials, and their selective formation is of paramount importance in molecular materials engineering. However, steering the formation and 2D crystallization of conjugated carbon rings on the surface with high chemo- and stereoselectivities remains a great challenge. Here, we report a highly chemoselective [1+1+1+1] cycloaddition of isocyanides on the Au(111) surface, which affords the stereospecific tetraaza[4]radialene products and further enables their long-range-ordered 2D crystallization via enantioselective molecular recognition. Using the progressive annealing method, we found that at room temperature, isocyanides undergo a coordination reaction with Au adatoms to form two-fold symmetric isocyanide-Au-isocyanide complexes. In contrast, gradually increasing the annealing temperature induces the transformation of these complexes and subsequent covalent polymerization, leading to the selective generation of tetraaza[4]radialenes with homotactic configurations. The tetraaza[4]radialenes further assemble into 2D homochiral molecular crystals through enantioselective molecular recognition driven by multiple C-H -- Cl hydrogen-bonding interactions. By combining scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy and non-contact atomic force microscopy, we determined the atomic structure and molecular orbitals of tetraaza[4]radialene, confirming that its four-membered ring adopts a planar geometry with a localized lowest unoccupied molecular orbital. Density functional theory calculations suggest that the [1+1+1+1] cycloaddition process involves stepwise formation of C-C bonds and its high selectivity arises from the spatial steric hindrance. Our findings provide new insights into the selective formation of conjugated rings on surfaces and have implications for engineering 2D homochiral molecular crystallization.

### [225] [Inverse design of bespoke interatomic potentials via active learning by information-matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08148)
*Yonatan Kurniawan,Logan D. Williams,Amit Samanta,Ilia Nikiforov,Daniel Schwalbe-Koda,Mark K. Transtrum,Ellad B. Tadmor,Vincenzo Lordi,Vasily V. Bulatov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文应用信息匹配（information-matching, IM）方法，通过间接目标策略（针对与强度相关的低成本中间量）构建定制化的原子间势（interatomic potentials, IPs），以预测金属的塑性强度，并探讨了后验不确定性膨胀修正对模型误差的缓解作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统主动学习（active learning, AL）框架在构建原子间势（IPs）时虽能降低参数不确定性，但未明确考虑待预测的具体材料属性。为解决这一问题，作者引入信息匹配（IM）方法，以在选定训练数据中提供足够的参数空间信息，从而实现对感兴趣量（quantities of interest, QoIs）的预定不确定性目标。

Method: 采用间接信息匹配（indirect IM）策略，避免直接模拟高计算代价的塑性强度，转而选择与强度相关且计算成本较低的中间感兴趣量（intermediate QoIs）作为目标；训练数据基于IM准则筛选，确保对参数空间施加精确约束。

Result: IM方法能够在极少量训练数据下实现对参数空间的精确约束，进而对中间QoIs和塑性强度均给出精确预测。然而，模型误差（model error）仍是关键限制因素，后验不确定性膨胀修正（post hoc uncertainty inflation correction）可有效缓解该问题。

Conclusion: 不确定性感知的主动学习（uncertainty-aware AL）在预测复杂材料属性方面具有潜力，但也存在固有局限（如模型误差）；后验修正策略为提升预测可靠性提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Interatomic potentials (IPs) enable large-scale atomistic simulations beyond the reach of first-principles methods, but their predictive reliability depends critically on the selection of training data, quantified uncertainty, and model expressiveness. Active learning (AL) provides a principled framework for constructing efficient and accurate IPs, yet most strategies reduce parameter uncertainty without explicitly accounting for the specific material properties being predicted. The information-matching (IM) approach addresses this limitation by requiring that the selected training data provide at least as much parameter space information as needed to achieve prescribed uncertainty targets for selected quantities of interest (QoIs). Here, we apply IM to develop bespoke IPs specifically tailored for predicting plastic strength in metals. Due to the high computational cost of simulating plastic strength, we employ an indirect IM strategy that targets inexpensive intermediate QoIs that correlate with strength. The IM method enables precise parameter constraints with minimal training data, yielding precise predictions for both the intermediate QoIs and plastic strength. Yet, model error remains a key limitation, and a post hoc uncertainty inflation correction provides a viable means to mitigate this limitation. These findings illustrate both the promise and limits of uncertainty-aware AL for predicting complex material properties.

Method: 采用相同的工程化铁电栅堆叠（8 nm HZO / 3 nm Al2O3 / 8 nm HZO）和混合覆盖层（3 nm HfO2 + 3 nm Al2O3），分别以掺Ga的InO（IGO）和掺W的InO（IWO）为沟道材料，在不同退火温度和时间下进行实验；结合电学分析和掠入射X射线衍射（GIXRD）表征。

Abstract: In this work, we report a systematic study of the impact of high-temperature post-capping thermal annealing on the memory characteristics of Oxide-semiconductor channel ferroelectric field-effect transistors (OS-FeFETs). Using an identical engineered ferroelectric gate stack 8nm Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 (HZO) / 3 nm Al2O3 / 8 nm HZO (8/3/8) and a hybrid capping layer (3 nm HfO2 + 3 nm Al2O3), 10 percent Ga doped InO (IGO) channel and 4 percent W doped InO (IWO) channel FeFETs remain functional after annealing at temperatures up to 650 C for durations of up to 30 min and 10 min, respectively; further annealing results in irreversible loss of conduction and device failure. Detailed electrical analysis reveals that the MW enhancement originates from a preferential positive shift in the erased-state threshold voltage, while the programmed-state threshold voltage remains comparatively stable. Grazing-incidence X-ray diffraction measurements further indicate structural evolution in the IWO and IGO oxide channels with increasing annealing temperature, supporting the observed electrical trends.

### [227] [First-Principles Insights into Surface and Ligand Effects in Stoichiometric HgTe Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08399)
*Raagya Arora,Patrick J. Lohr,Dibyajyoti Ghosh,Jennifer Hollingsworth,Sergei Tretiak*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: HgTe quantum dots are promising mid-infrared nanomaterials owing to their exceptional bandgap tunability, yet their electronic structure is strongly influenced by surface coordination and ligand passivation at ultrasmall sizes. Here, we employ atomistic simulations to systematically investigate stoichiometric HgTe nanoclusters with sizes 0.86 to 1.85 nm. The in silico exploration uncovers a transition from confinement-dominated electronic structures with delocalized frontier states in small self-passivated clusters to surface influenced characteristics in larger nanoclusters. Increased coordination and bond-length inhomogeneity in the larger nanoclusters generate localized near-gap states centered on undercoordinated surface atoms. At intermediate sizes, the band edge states become spatially separated on different regions of the cluster without forming deep gap states, marking the onset of surface induced electronic asymmetry. In larger clusters (1.8 nm), common neutral ligands like amines, thiols, phosphines, and alcohols effectively eliminate surface-derived localized states by restoring local coordination and altering the band edge electronic structure through ligand surface hybridization. The sensitivity of the bandgap to ligand identity and binding site underscores the interplay between surface coordination and ligand chemistry in shaping the electronic structure of these nanoclusters. These insights provide an atomistic understanding of size-dependent electronic structures in ultrasmall HgTe clusters. The study further establishes neutral ligands as powerful chemical handles for engineering frontier electronic states relevant to infrared optoelectronic functionality.

### [228] [Dimensionality-Driven Charge Stabilization of Group-IV Color Centers in Diamond Ultrathin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08550)
*Jijun Huang,Bing Huang,Song Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算证明，在金刚石薄膜（diamane）中利用维度限制（dimensional confinement）——包括量子限域（quantum confinement）和表面钝化（surface termination）——可以在无需有意掺杂的条件下，稳定IV族空位中心（group-IV vacancy centers）的中性电荷态，并系统调控其电子结构、零场分裂（zero-field splitting）和自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），从而为固态量子缺陷的电荷、光学与自旋性质工程提供通用策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中性IV族空位（XV, X=Si, Ge, Sn, Pb）中心是新兴的固态自旋-光子界面（spin-photon interface），具有优异的自旋相干性和反演对称性保护的光学跃迁。然而，稳定中性电荷态通常需要在高纯度硼掺杂钻石中进行严苛的费米能级工程（Fermi-level engineering），这带来了显著的材料生长挑战。因此，亟需寻找一种无需有意掺杂即可稳定电荷态的替代方案。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究金刚石薄膜（diamane）中的维度限制效应——包括量子限域和表面钝化——对IV族空位中心电荷态稳定性的影响，并分析厚度和表面终止基团对电子结构、零场分裂及自旋-轨道耦合的调控作用。

Result: 量子限域与表面钝化协同调谐了宿主材料的带隙，并将占据的缺陷态从价带边缘向上移动，从而扩大了中性电荷态的热力学稳定窗口，同时抑制了价带辅助的激发路径。改变金刚石薄膜的厚度和表面终止基团可以实现对XV中心电子结构、零场分裂和自旋-轨道耦合的系统性调控，同时其光学跃迁能量基本保持不变。在所有结构中，氢化金刚石薄膜在电荷态稳定性与磁光性能之间取得了最优平衡。

Conclusion: 维度限制被证明是一种无需有意掺杂即可工程化调控固态量子缺陷的电荷、光学和自旋性质的通用策略。该发现为克服传统钻石中电荷态稳定所需严苛材料条件提供了新的思路，并为设计高性能固态自旋-光子界面奠定了基础。

Abstract: Neutral group-IV vacancy (XV, X = Si, Ge, Sn, and Pb) centers in diamond are emerging solid-state spin-photon interfaces because of their favorable spin coherence and inversion symmetry-protected optical transitions. However, stabilizing their neutral charge state typically requires stringent Fermi-level engineering in high purity boron-doped diamond, which poses significant materials-growth challenges. Here, we demonstrate that dimensional confinement in diamane provides an alternative route to charge-state stabilization without intentional doping. Using first-principles calculations, we show that quantum confinement and surface termination cooperatively tune the host band gap and shift the occupied defect states upward from the valence-band edge, thereby enlarging the thermodynamic stability window of the neutral charge state and suppressing valence-band assisted excitation pathways. We further reveal that the thickness and surface termination of diamane enable systematic tuning of the electronic structure, zero-field splitting, and spin-orbit coupling of XV centers while largely preserving their optical transition energies. Among the structures considered, hydrogenated diamane offers the most favorable balance between charge-state stability and magneto-optical performance. More broadly, our findings establish dimensional confinement as a general strategy for engineering the charge, optical, and spin properties of solid-state quantum defects.
