### [229] [V-Doped Niobate Nanosheets for Enhanced Photocatalytic Activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08567)
*M. Tuğrul Avcu,Uğur Ünal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过固相反应、质子化及四丁基铵离子剥离制备了V掺杂的[Ca₂Nb₃₋ₓVₓO₁₀]⁻纳米片，发现V掺杂降低了带隙（从3.54 eV降至2.60-2.88 eV），并在全光谱氙灯下，[Ca₂Nb₂.₇V₀.₃O₁₀]⁻纳米片实现了11.3 mmol/g/h的产氢速率，产氢量达到未掺杂纳米片的4.7倍；负载Pt作为助催化剂后，产氢量达到未掺杂Pt负载纳米片的2.9倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维纳米片（2D nanosheets）因其小厚度可降低电子-空穴复合（electron-hole recombination）且具有较大比表面积以增加光催化活性位点，有望提升光催化性能；通过V掺杂（V-doping）进一步缩小宽带隙（band gap），以增强可见光吸收与光催化活性。

Method: 先通过固相反应（solid state reaction）合成V掺杂钙铌酸盐前驱体，再经质子化（protonation）和四丁基铵离子（tetrabutylammonium ions）剥离（exfoliation）获得[Ca₂Nb₃₋ₓVₓO₁₀]⁻纳米片（x = 0, 0.15, 0.3, 0.6, 0.75）。在析氢反应（hydrogen evolution reactions）中使用10 vol%甲醇作为空穴牺牲剂（hole scavenger），并在纳米片上沉积3 wt% Pt作为助催化剂（co-catalyst），以全光谱氙灯（full-spectrum Xe light）测试光催化产氢性能。

Result: 未掺杂纳米片的宽带隙为3.54 eV，V掺杂后带隙降至2.60-2.88 eV范围。在全光谱氙灯下，[Ca₂Nb₂.₇V₀.₃O₁₀]⁻纳米片产氢率达11.3 mmol/g/h，产氢量为未掺杂纳米片的4.7倍；负载Pt后，该组成产氢量达到未掺杂Pt负载纳米片的2.9倍。

Conclusion: V掺杂能有效减小[Ca₂Nb₃O₁₀]⁻纳米片的带隙并显著提升光催化产氢性能，其中x = 0.3的组成表现出最佳活性；Pt助催化剂可进一步促进产氢效率。

Abstract: V-doped [Ca$_{2}$Nb$_{3-x}$V$_{x}$O$_{10}$]$^{-}$ (x = 0, 0.15, 0.3, 0.6, 0.75) nanosheets were produced by solid state reaction followed by protonation and exfoliation by tetrabutylammonium ions. 2D nanosheets have improved photocatalytic activity due to their small thickness that reduces electron-hole recombination, larger surface area that increases photocatalytic sites, and decreased band gap from added V. V-doping has caused the wide band gap of 3.54 eV of undoped nanosheets to decrease to 2.60-2.88 eV range. 10 vol% methanol was used as a hole scavenger in the hydrogen evolution reactions, and 3 wt% Pt was deposited on nanosheets as a co-catalyst. Under a full-spectrum Xe light, [Ca$_{2}$Nb$_{2.7}$V$_{0.3}$O$_{10}$]$^{-}$ has produced 4.7 times the H$_{2}$ yield as undoped nanosheets with a 11.3 mmol/g/h production rate, [Ca$_{2}$Nb$_{2.7}$V$_{0.3}$O$_{10}$]$^{-}$ with Pt co-catalyst has produced 2.9 times the H$_{2}$ yield as undoped Pt-loaded nanosheets.

</details>


### [230] [Divergent Coherent Phonon Responses Across the Metal-Insulator Crossover](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08608)
*Felix Hoff,Timo Veslin,Tim Bartsch,Carl-Friedrich Schön,Dante M. Kennes,Matthias Wuttig*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过激光注量诱导的声子软化与相干反射振荡振幅两个实验可及响应函数，系统比较了不同材料对超快光激发的响应强度，发现只有Sb、GeTe、Bi₂Te₃等少数材料表现出显著响应。这些响应在中间电导率区间（约10²–10⁴ S/cm）达到峰值，对应局域化与退局域化电子态的交叉区域。研究提出该类材料采用一种独特的成键机制——元价键合（metavalent bonding），并基于冻结声子密度泛函理论（DFT）计算表明，强注量依赖性源于Peierls型不稳定性导致的大形变势与非谐振双阱势。该工作将元价键合确立为增强相干声子控制的设计原则，并提供了识别具有超快响应材料的定量框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions）是实现超快激光调控材料性能的基础，但不同材料对超快光激发的响应强度差异巨大，缺乏统一的定量比较框架与设计原则。

Method: 采用激光注量诱导的声子软化（phonon softening）与相干反射振荡振幅（coherent reflectance oscillations）两个实验可测响应函数，跨材料对比光激发响应；结合冻结声子DFT计算（frozen-phonon DFT calculations）分析注量依赖性的微观起源。

Result: 仅Sb、GeTe、Bi₂Te₃等少数材料表现出声子软化的显著增强与反射振荡幅度的巨大增长；响应峰值出现在约10²–10⁴ S/cm的中间电导率区间，即局域化与退局域化电子态的交叉区域；该材料类别还表现出高介电常数、增强的Born有效电荷（Born effective charges）、超过8-N规则的配位数等非常规性质。

Conclusion: 上述材料的非凡响应源于一种独特的成键机制——元价键合（metavalent bonding），其导致Peierls型不稳定性与大形变势及非谐振双阱势。元价键合可作为增强相干声子控制（coherent phonon control）的设计原则，研究同时给出了定量识别超快响应材料的框架。

Abstract: Ultrafast laser control of material properties hinges on understanding light-matter interactions. We use two experimentally accessible response functions, laser fluence induced phonon softening and the amplitude of coherent reflectance oscillations, to compare how strongly different materials respond to ultrafast photoexcitation. Comparing a diverse set of materials, we find that only a narrow class, including Sb, GeTe, and Bi2Te3, shows exceptional responses such as pronounced phonon softening and a giant increase of reflectance oscillations with increasing fluence. These response functions peak in an intermediate conductivity regime of about 102 - 104 S/cm, at the crossover between localized and delocalized electronic states. The corresponding class of solids also shows other unconventional properties including high dielectric constants, enhanced Born effective charges, coordination numbers exceeding the 8-N rule and uncommon bond rupture. This suggests that these materials employ a unique bonding mechanism, coined metavalent bonding. Frozen-phonon DFT calculations show that the strong fluence dependence arises from Peierls-like instabilities, leading to large deformation potentials and anharmonic double-well potentials. These findings identify metavalent bonding as a design principle for enhanced coherent phonon control and provide a quantitative framework for identifying materials with exceptional ultrafast responses.

### [231] [Nonperturbative isotope effect on light-matter interaction in boron arsenide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08639)
*Huan Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种非微扰（nonperturbative）方法，用于描述强同位素无序（strong isotope disorder）下硼化砷（boron arsenide）中光与物质的相互作用，揭示了非微扰同位素效应对介电函数、表面声子极化激元（surface phonon polariton）以及近场辐射传热（near-field radiative heat transfer）的影响，并实现了对辐射热通量的两倍调控。该工作建立了从微扰到非微扰区域的统一理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强同位素无序条件下，传统量子微扰理论（quantum perturbation theory）失效，但缺乏一个能够同时涵盖微扰与非微扰区域的统一理论框架。硼化砷中两种稳定硼同位素之间的巨大质量差为这一挑战提供了典型范例。

Method: 发展了一种非微扰方法（nonperturbative approach），用于捕捉硼化砷中同位素无序对光-物质相互作用的影响。

Result: 揭示了在非微扰区域下，两种硼同位素之间相干混合振动会重塑介电函数（dielectric function）；非微扰同位素相互作用决定了耦合表面声子极化激元（coupled surface phonon polaritons）的性质以及近场辐射传热；通过同位素工程调控表面声子极化激元共振，实现了对辐射热通量的两倍调控（two-fold tuning）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个连接微扰（perturbative）与非微扰极限的统一框架，能够在从弱无序到强无序的整个区间内进行定量预测。

Abstract: The interaction of light and matter under strong isotope disorder gives rise to unconventional physics that goes beyond the quantum perturbation theory. In boron arsenide, the large mass difference between the two stable boron isotopes presents a paradigmatic case where perturbation theory fails, yet a unified theoretical framework across the perturbative and nonperturbative regime has remained elusive. Here, we develop a nonperturbative approach to capture isotope-disorder effect in boron arsenide, which fundamentally alters light-matter interactions. We reveal that coherently mixed vibrations between two boron isotopes reshape the dielectric function in the nonperturbative regime. The nonperturbative isotope interactions dictate the properties of coupled surface phonon polaritons and near-field radiative heat transfer. Two-fold tuning of radiative heat flux is achieved by modulating the surface phonon polariton resonance via isotope engineering. This work establishes a unified framework connecting the perturbative and nonperturbative limits, enabling quantitative predictions across weak to strong disorder regime.

### [232] [Information Entropy Based Crystal Structure Prediction of Chemically Disordered Alloys via Graph Convolutional Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08686)
*Suman Chabri,Gautam Anand*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于信息论（information theory）的方法，用于化学无序合金（chemically disordered alloys）的相预测（phase prediction）。该方法结合了基于图卷积神经网络（Graph Convolutional Neural Network）的炼金蒙特卡洛采样（alchemical Monte Carlo sampling）与信息熵（information entropy）度量，并对比了键失衡量（Bond Disproportion Vector, BDV）与平滑重叠原子位置（Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions, SOAP）描述符的性能，在二元至五元合金体系中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学无序合金（包括高熵合金）由于组合复杂性（combinatorial complexity），其相预测面临巨大的计算挑战。现有方法难以高效探索此类复杂材料的势能面（potential energy landscape），且缺乏有效的量化指标来指导相预测。

Method: 提出一种信息论方法，利用基于图卷积神经网络（Graph Convolutional Neural Network）的高效机器学习模型进行炼金蒙特卡洛采样（alchemical Monte Carlo sampling）。同时采用键失衡量（Bond Disproportion Vector, BDV）作为低计算成本描述符，并与先进的平滑重叠原子位置（Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions, SOAP）描述符进行基准对比，最终引入基于信息熵（information entropy）的度量指标实现相预测。

Result: 该方法在二元（CoNi、MoW、FeNi、TaW）、三元（CoCrNi、CrFeNi）、四元（CoCrFeNi）及五元（Alₓ(CoCrFeNi)₁₋ₓ）合金体系中验证了信息熵基相预测的适用性。基于信息熵的方法能够在传统方法不可行的挑战性场景下发挥作用。

Conclusion: 基于信息熵的相预测方法为化学无序合金的相预测提供了一种新的高效途径，尤其适用于传统方法难以处理的复杂合金体系。

Abstract: The phase prediction of chemically disordered alloys poses a significant computational challenge due to the combinatorial complexity of such materials. The high-throughput compositional exploration of chemically disordered alloys, including high-entropy alloys, requires an approach to efficiently explore the potential energy landscape of such complex materials. Additionally, a metric to quantify the potential energy landscape explored for phase prediction of the compositions needs to be defined. We propose an information-theoretic approach to phase prediction in chemically disordered alloys in the present work. We demonstrate the applicability of alchemical Monte Carlo sampling using an efficient Graph Convolutional Neural Network-Based machine learning model. We additionally demonstrate the applicability and limitations of the Bond Disproportion Vector (BDV) as a low-computational-cost descriptor and benchmark it against the state-of-the-art Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions (SOAP) descriptor. We show the applicability of an information entropy-based metric for the phase prediction of binary (CoNi, MoW, FeNi and TaW), ternary (CoCrNi, CrFeNi), quaternary (CoCrFeNi) and quinary ($\mathrm{Al_x(CoCrFeNi)_{1-x}}$) alloys. Information entropy-based phase prediction can be applicable in challenging cases where conventional approaches are not feasible.

### [233] [Chiral-Angle-Controlled Altermagnetic Spin Splitting in Nanotubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08757)
*Ersoy Sasioglu,Tom. G. Saunderson,Börge Göbel,Ingrid Mertig,Samir Lounis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究表明，将二维 d 波交变磁体（altermagnet）卷成纳米管后，动量依赖的自旋劈裂会通过维度投影（dimensional projection）转化为手性角度控制的一维自旋劈裂，其遵循 cos(2θ) 依赖关系，且该机制对多种二维交变磁体衍生的纳米管具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）虽具有零净磁化强度却表现出动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting），如何将这种体相中的动量空间自旋劈裂传递至低维系统（如一维纳米管）是一个尚未解决的关键问题。

Method: 采用最小紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），分析二维 d 波交变磁体卷曲成纳米管后的电子结构变化，系统研究维度投影对自旋劈裂行为的影响。

Result: 纳米管中的自旋劈裂呈现出特征性的 cos(2θ) 依赖关系：当纳米管取向为节线方向（nodal orientations）时自旋劈裂消失，反节线方向（antinodal orientations）时达到极值。该机制对多种二维交变磁体衍生的纳米管保持稳健。

Conclusion: 维度投影是将动量依赖的交变磁自旋劈裂传递到一维系统的通用路径，为在低维磁性材料中工程化自旋劈裂量子态提供了理论基础和设计框架。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting despite having zero net magnetization. Here, we show that rolling a two-dimensional (2D) $d$-wave altermagnet into a nanotube transforms this momentum-dependent spin splitting into chiral-angle-controlled one-dimensional (1D) spin splitting through dimensional projection. Using a minimal tight-binding model and first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that the nanotube spin splitting follows a characteristic $\cos(2θ)$ dependence, vanishing for nodal orientations and reaching extrema for antinodal orientations. The mechanism remains robust across a broad class of nanotubes derived from 2D altermagnets. Our results establish dimensional projection as a general route for transferring momentum-dependent altermagnetic spin splitting into 1D systems and provide a framework for engineering spin-split quantum states in low-dimensional magnetic materials.

### [234] [Chiral Surface Phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08820)
*Mike Pols,Nicola A. Spaldin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过对称性论证与密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）证明，所有晶体材料的表面都天然存在手性表面声子（chiral surface phonons）。以高对称性AB岩盐（rocksalt）化合物为模型系统，发现表面局域声子的原子位移呈现手性运动，并进一步展示这些手性表面声子会在表面产生面内磁性（in-plane magnetism）。研究揭示，表面或界面处的对称性降低是手性声子普遍存在的根源，从而将表面确立为手性声子及其相关磁矩的一个重要但此前被忽视的来源，对多种表面敏感测量可能具有影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索晶体材料表面是否普遍存在手性声子（chiral phonons），并揭示其来源与物理效应，填补关于手性声子表面产生机制的研究空白。

Method: 采用对称性论证（symmetry arguments）结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行计算分析，以高对称性AB岩盐（rocksalt）化合物的平板（slab）模型为研究对象。

Result: 发现所有晶体材料表面均存在表面局域的手性声子，其原子位移呈现手性运动；该手性表面声子可在表面生成面内磁性（in-plane magnetism）层。

Conclusion: 手性声子可普遍存在于所有晶体材料中，起因于表面或界面处的对称性降低。表面是此前被忽视的手性声子及其磁矩的来源，可能对广泛的表面敏感测量有重要意义。

Abstract: We use symmetry arguments combined with density functional theory to demonstrate that all surfaces of crystalline materials host surface phonons that are chiral. As model system, we study slabs of highly symmetric AB rocksalt compounds, and find surface-localized phonons whose atomic displacements exhibit chiral motion. We further show that these chiral surface phonons generate sheets of in-plane magnetism at the surface. Our results reveal that chiral phonons can emerge in all crystalline materials as a result of reduced symmetry at surfaces or interfaces. These findings establish surfaces as a previously overlooked source of chiral phonons and their associated magnetic moments, which could play a role in a broad range of surface-sensitive measurements.

</details>


### [235] [Local electronic structure and dynamics of hydrogen in $\text{CeO}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08915)
*A. Koda,T. U. Ito,M. Hiraishi,H. Okabe,R. Kadono*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合μSR实验与第一性原理DFT计算，探究了高质量单晶二氧化铈（CeO₂）中作为氢同位素的μ子（Mu）的局域电子态。实验在约10 K以下观测到顺磁态（Mu⁰）和抗磁态（Mu*），并通过磁场依赖性与DFT结果证实了极化子（polaron）态的形成，即Mu与配位氧成键，同时一个4f电子局域在附近的Ce位。Mu⁰信号的晶体取向依赖性揭示了自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致的4f电子强各向异性。温度高于约10 K时，Mu⁰转变为另一种表现为抗磁响应的Mu⁰态（即Mu*），并在约30 K以上消失，表明高温下4f电子和/或Mu（以及H）存在快速扩散运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用μ子作为氢的同位素探针，结合μSR技术与第一性原理DFT计算，研究高质量单晶二氧化铈中氢的局域电子态与极化子行为，以揭示其微观电子结构与动力学机制。

Method: 采用μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（muon spin rotation/relaxation, μSR）实验与第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算相结合的方法，对高质量单晶CeO₂中植入的正μ子进行表征。

Result: 在约10 K以下同时观测到顺磁态（Mu⁰）和抗磁态（Mu*）。磁场依赖性与DFT结果表明形成了极化子（polaron）态：Mu与配位氧成键，一个4f电子局域在邻近Ce位。Mu⁰信号的晶体取向依赖性证实了因自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）引起的4f电子强各向异性。温度高于约10 K时，Mu⁰转变为另一种表现为抗磁响应的Mu⁰态（即Mu*），并在约30 K以上消失。

Conclusion: 上述发现表明，在较高温度下，4f电子和/或Mu（以及H）存在快速的扩散运动。

Abstract: The local electronic states of muon (Mu) as an isotope of hydrogen (H) in high-quality single-crystalline ceria (CeO$_2$) are investigated using muon spin rotation/relaxation ($μ\text{SR}$) and first-principles density functional theory (DFT) calculations. Upon positive muon implantation, both paramagnetic (Mu$^0$) and diamagnetic (Mu$^*$) states are observed below $\approx$10 K. Magnetic field dependence of the Mu$^0$ signals combined with DFT results provides evidence for the formation of a polaron state, consisting of Mu bonded to a ligand oxygen and a $4f$ electron localized on a nearby Ce site. The crystal-orientation dependence of the Mu$^0$ signal suggests strong anisotropy of the $4f$ electron due to the spin-orbit coupling with lifted degeneracy. Furthermore, the Mu$^0$ state exhibits transition to the Mu$^*$ state that corresponds to another Mu$^0$ state (exhibiting a diamagnetic response due to fast spin/charge fluctuations) at temperatures above $\approx$10 K, before disappearing above $\approx$30 K. These findings suggest rapid diffusive motion of the $4f$ electrons and/or Mu (as well as H) at higher temperatures.

### [236] [Chemical tuning of magnetic ordering and cryogenic magnetocaloric response in zircon-type Gd1-xErxVO4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08916)
*Ming Zeng,Muqing Su,Liang Ming,Xiaolong Yang,Wang Chen,Lingwei Li,Hai-Feng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了多晶锆石型Gd1-xErxVO4（x=0, 0.1, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75）系列化合物的结构演化、磁学性质与磁热效应，发现少量Er替代（x=0.1）可抑制磁有序温度、削弱磁反常并显著提升低温磁热性能，最大磁熵变达45.1 J kg⁻¹ K⁻¹（μ₀ΔH=7 T），为开发高效低温制冷材料提供了调控策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学替代是调控稀土氧化物中磁有序与磁热性能（magnetocaloric performance）的有效途径，旨在为低温制冷（cryogenic refrigeration）探索性能更优的材料体系。

Method: 采用固相反应法合成多晶锆石型Gd1-xErxVO4系列样品（x=0, 0.1, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75），通过粉末X射线衍射（XRD）确认相纯度与晶体结构，利用磁化测量系统研究磁性质与磁热效应。

Result: 所有样品均为四方锆石结构（tetragonal zircon structure），无杂相；Er³⁺替代Gd³⁺导致晶格收缩。磁有序温度从GdVO4的3.65(2) K降至Gd0.9Er0.1VO4的2.76(2) K，同时自旋翻转类（spin-flop-like）场致磁反常减弱。Gd0.9Er0.1VO4在μ₀ΔH=7 T下获得最大磁熵变45.1 J kg⁻¹ K⁻¹。

Conclusion: 少量Er替代可有效调控交换作用、偶极耦合与磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）之间的竞争，在磁有序与可用自旋熵（spin entropy）之间实现优化平衡，这对开发高效低温制冷材料至关重要。

Abstract: Chemical substitution offers an effective route to tune magnetic ordering and magnetocaloric performance in rare-earth oxides for cryogenic refrigeration. Here we investigate the structural evo lution, magnetic properties, and magnetocaloric effect of polycrystalline zircon-type Gd1-xErxVO4 (x=0, 0.1, 0.25, 0.5, and 0.75). Powder X-ray diffraction confirms that all samples crystallize in the tetragonal zircon structure without detectable impurity phases. Substitution of Gd3+ by the smaller Er3+ ion produces a systematic lattice contraction and modifies the magnetic behavior of the rare-earth sublattice. In particular, the magnetic ordering temperature is suppressed from 3.65(2) K in GdVO4 to 2.76(2) K in Gd0.9Er0.1VO4 , accompanied by a weakening of the spin-flop-like field-induced anomaly observed in the parent compound. A low Er concentration correspondingly improves the low-temperature magnetocaloric performance, with Gd0.9Er0.1VO4 exhibiting a max imum magnetic entropy change of 45.1 J kg-1 K-1 for mu_0 Delta H=7T. These results demonstrate that weak Er substitution effectively tunes the competition among exchange interactions, dipolar coupling, and magnetic anisotropy, optimizing the balance between magnetic ordering and available spin entropy in zircon-type rare-earth vanadates, which is crucial for developing efficient cryogenic refrigeration materials.

### [237] [Precipitate phase selection and grain boundary morphology in Cu-Ni-Si-Mn alloys: A machine-learning interatomic potential study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09023)
*Aadil Fayaz Wani,Il-Seok Jeong,Haekwan Jeon,Jaesun Kim,SuDong Park,Eun-Ae Choi,Seung Zeon Han,Seungwu Han,Byungki Ryu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential, MLIP）计算，揭示了Cu-Ni-Si合金中Mn添加如何通过改变界面原子结构，促使沉淀相从不规则形状的Ni₂Si转变为薄膜状Mn₆Ni₁₆Si₇（G相），从而改善力学性能的原子尺度机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cu-Ni-Si合金中Mn添加显著改变了晶界（grain boundary, GB）析出行为：无Mn合金中稳定Ni₂Si的GB析出与力学性能下降相关，而Mn添加则促进薄膜状Mn₆Ni₁₆Si₇（G相）析出并改善性能。然而，这种截然不同的GB相选择与形貌的原子起源尚不清楚。

Method: 采用机器学习原子间势（MLIP）计算，可靠复现了DFT级别的界面键合与微观结构构型能量学，并结合大尺度原子界面计算以及实验观测进行验证。

Conclusion: 界面原子结构是决定Cu-Ni-Si合金中GB析出相选择与形貌的关键因素：Ni₂Si的共格界面导致应变积累与排斥效应，形成不规则形貌；而G相的非共格界面能量适中且无排斥区，促进薄膜状连续析出，从而解释了Mn添加改善力学性能的原子尺度起源。

Abstract: Alloys inevitably contain interphase boundaries, whose energetics govern nucleation processes and precipitate morphology. In Cu-Ni-Si alloys, Mn addition markedly changes grain boundary (GB) precipitation behavior. While GB precipitation of stable Ni$_2$Si in Mn-free alloys is associated with degraded mechanical properties, Mn addition instead promotes film-shaped Mn$_6$Ni$_{16}$Si$_7$ (G-phase) precipitation, which is correlated improved mechanical properties. However, the atomic origin of the contrasting GB phase selection and morphology remains unclear. Here we perform machine-learning interatomic potential (MLIP) calculations to investigate the effect of interphase-boundary atomic structure on GB precipitates in Cu-Ni-Si alloys with and without Mn. The MLIP calculations reliably reproduce DFT-level energetics for interfacial bonding and microstructural configurations, and further predict that Mn addition favors GB precipitation of Mn$_6$Ni$_{16}$Si$_7$ rather than Ni$_2$Si. Experimentally, Mn-free alloys are observed to exhibit irregularly-shaped Ni$_2$Si precipitates with open-boundary-like Cu/Ni$_2$Si interfaces, whereas Mn-added alloys exhibit film-like G-phase at GBs. Large-scale atomistic interface calculations reveal that the coherent interface structure between Cu and Ni$_2$Si favors the formation of plate-like strained Ni$_2$Si precipitates in the matrix. Upon coarsening and stress release, an out-of-phase coherent-like interface can form at GBs, generating a local repulsive region that gives rise to surface-like open-boundary structures and explains the irregular morphology of GB stable Ni$_2$Si precipitates. In contrast, Cu/Mn$_6$Ni$_{16}$Si$_7$ interfaces remain predominantly incoherent with moderate boundary energies and no pronounced repulsive regime, thereby stabilizing continuous interfacial contact and explaining film-shaped GB precipitation.

The resulting film contains face-centred cubic (FCC), body-centred cubic (BCC), hexagonal close-packed (HCP), and amorphous regions. Analysis of the radial distribution function (RDF) was used to determine nearest-neighbour distances and estimate lattice parameters for the crystalline phases. The simulated phase composition and structural parameters are in good agreement with available experimental data.

### [241] [BSE+ calculations for 2D materials: a unified description of excitons and plasmons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09192)
*Amalie H. Svaneborg,and Kristian S. Thygesen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文详细介绍了BSE+方法，该方法通过结合四点BSE型方程和两点Dyson方程，在保持低能激子特征的同时正确描述高能等离激元结构，有效抑制了BSE中因忽略高能跃迁而产生的虚假等离激元峰，并在过渡金属二硫族化物单层体系中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Bethe-Salpeter方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation, BSE）虽然能精确描述强激子效应下的低能光学谱，但其高计算成本限制了所包含的电子-空穴跃迁数量，忽略高能跃迁会导致介电函数实部被低估，并在电子能量损失谱（electron energy loss spectrum, EELS）中产生虚假的等离激元（plasmon）峰。

Method: BSE+方法将用于不可极化率的四点BSE型方程与包含高能跃迁的两点Dyson方程相结合，其中高能跃迁在随机相位近似（Random Phase Approximation, RPA）层次处理。本文将该方法推广至二维材料，并在GPAW代码中实现。

Result: 在过渡金属二硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenide）单层体系中，BSE+在低能区域保留了BSE的激子特征，在高能区域再现了RPA的等离激元结构，有效抑制了虚假等离激元峰，在全能量范围内与实验EELS数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: BSE+方法相比标准BSE在电子-空穴基组大小上收敛更快，计算成本相当，能够同时准确描述低能激子效应和高能等离激元行为。

Abstract: The Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE) accurately describes low-energy optical spectra in materials with strong excitonic effects, but its high computational cost limits the number of electron-hole transitions that can be included. Neglecting high-energy transitions leads to an underestimation of the real part of the dielectric function, often producing a spurious plasmon peak in the BSE electron energy loss spectrum (EELS). The recently introduced BSE+ method addresses this by combining a four-point BSE-like equation for the irreducible polarisability with a two-point Dyson equation that includes the high-energy transitions at the Random Phase Approximation (RPA) level. Here, we present a detailed account of the method, extend it to two-dimensional materials, and apply it to a set of transition metal dichalcogenide monolayers. BSE+ preserves the excitonic features of the BSE at low energies while reproducing the plasmonic structure of the RPA at higher energies, yielding good agreement with experimental EELS data across the full energy range and strongly suppressing the spurious plasmon. BSE+ converges much faster than BSE with respect to the electron-hole basis size, at a comparable computational cost, and is implemented in the GPAW code.

Method: 采用混合密度泛函理论（hybrid density functional theory）进行计算，考虑非晶态和晶态Ga₂O₃相下的Ga-O-rich、As-rich和As-O-rich三种界面化学计量条件。

The efficiency of these devices depends strongly on the band alignment between the two materials, however both type-I and type-II alignment have been reported in the literature for these heterostructures. To address this ambiguity, we use hybrid density functional theory to systematically investigate the band alignment at GaAs/Ga$_2$O$_3$ interfaces, focusing on the role of interface chemistry. By considering Ga-O-, As-, and As-O-rich interfaces both in amorphous and crystalline Ga$_2$O$_3$ phases, we demonstrate that interface stoichiometry determines the alignment type: Ga-O-rich interfaces exhibit type-II alignment with large valence band offsets (~3.1 eV), while As-rich and As-O-rich interfaces favor type-I alignment with reduced offsets (~2.3-2.6 eV). Our findings provide insight into the relationship between chemistry and band alignment in GaAs/Ga$_2$O$_3$ heterostructures, enabling targeted optimization for specific device applications.

Motivation: 探索呼吸型kagome晶格（breathing kagome lattice）中内禀对称性破缺如何产生电极化表面，以及层间堆叠序（如反铁电AB堆叠）如何通过层奇偶性（layer parity）控制表面极化，并进一步验证这些极化结构能否用于调控范德华界面的激子（exciton）和光电器件响应。

Method: 采用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy）的开尔文探针力显微镜（Kelvin probe force microscopy, KPFM）模式，直接可视化剥离的Nb₃Cl₈薄片中层依赖的极化态，并测量表面静电势。通过构建Nb₃Cl₈与单层MoSe₂的异质结，研究极化纹理对激子发射的调控。

Result: 观测到表面静电势（surface electrostatic potential）的奇偶层数振荡（odd-even oscillation）；识别出层内极性畴（intralayer polar domains），其中呼吸型kagome网络的局域原子重构可翻转表面层的面外电偶极子，形成类铁电堆叠构型；在Nb₃Cl₈/MoSe₂界面实现了极化依赖的激子发射调制。

Conclusion: Nb₃Cl₈是一种内禀的层极化范德华（van der Waals）平台，层奇偶性为编程范德华界面处的激子和光电器件响应提供了强大的结构自由度。

Abstract: The intrinsic symmetry breaking in the breathing kagome lattice of layered Nb$_3$Cl$_8$ provides a unique mechanism for realizing electrically polar surfaces. In each monolayer, the trimerization of Nb atoms breaks inversion and mirror symmetries, generating an out-of-plane electric dipole. The AB-stacked $α$ phase arranges adjacent layer dipoles antiferroelectrically, leaving the uncompensated surface polarization strictly governed by layer parity. Here, using atomic force microscopy operated in Kelvin probe force microscopy mode, we directly visualize layer-dependent polarization states in exfoliated Nb$_3$Cl$_8$ flakes and resolve a pronounced odd-even oscillation of the surface electrostatic potential. Beyond this parity-locked antiferroelectric order, we further identify intralayer polar domains in which local atomic reconstructions of the breathing kagome network reverse the out-of-plane dipole of the surface layer, producing ferroelectric-like stacking configurations. By interfacing monolayer MoSe$_2$ with Nb$_3$Cl$_8$, we demonstrate that these surface-polarization textures effectively modulate adjacent excitonic emission through domain-dependent interfacial band alignment and charge transfer. Our findings establish Nb$_3$Cl$_8$ as an intrinsic layer-polarized van der Waals platform and show that layer parity provides powerful structural degree of freedom for programming excitonic and optoelectronic responses at van der Waals interfaces.

### [245] [Crystal Shape and Lattice Deformation in Powder Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09319)
*Matteo Leoni,Alberto Leonardi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于傅里叶（Fourier）的广义框架，将晶域形状变形、晶格变形及形状-晶格相对取向作为独立可精修的张量操作统一处理，实现了对衍射峰形的高精度建模与微观结构参数的同时恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从纳米晶材料的粉末衍射数据中准确提取微观结构信息（如晶粒尺寸、形状）需要精确的衍射峰形（diffraction peak shape）建模，但现有的通用体积函数（common-volume functions）仅对少数理想几何形状具有解析表达式，限制了复杂实际体系的适用性。

Method: 构建了一个基于傅里叶变换的广义框架，将晶域形状变形（shape deformation）、晶格变形（lattice deformation）和形状-晶格相对取向（relative shape-lattice misorientation）作为独立可精修的张量操作（tensor operations），在统一形式论中进行处理。该方法在连续仿射变换（affine transformations）下保持方向傅里叶系数（directional Fourier coefficients）的解析求值，支持单个衍射峰、全粉末衍射图谱及全散射（total-scattering）形状校正。

Result: 在虚拟散射实验数据的验证中表明，该方法能够同时以高精度恢复晶粒尺寸、形状、晶格变形及形状-晶格相对取向等微观结构参数。

Conclusion: 该框架克服了传统粉末衍射线形分析方法无法处理复杂形状-晶格耦合变换的局限，为纳米晶材料的微观结构表征提供了一种统一且灵活的建模工具。

Abstract: Accurate modelling of diffraction peak shapes is essential for extracting microstructural information from nanocrystalline materials. Common-volume functions are widely used to describe finite-size and shape broadening in powder diffraction, but analytical expressions are available only for a limited set of ideal geometries. Here, we introduce a generalized Fourier-based framework in which crystal-domain shape deformation, lattice deformation, and relative shape-lattice misorientation are treated as independently refinable tensor operations within a unified formalism. The approach enables continuous affine transformations of both crystal shape and lattice base while preserving analytical evaluation of directional Fourier coefficients. As a result, complex particle shapes, anisotropic deformations, and arbitrary relative orientations between shape and lattice can be modelled within a single reciprocal- and real-space framework, including coupled shape-lattice transformations not accessible using conventional powder diffraction line-profile methods. The formalism can be applied to individual diffraction peaks, full powder patterns, and total-scattering shape corrections. Validation against virtual scattering experiment data demonstrates that crystal size, shape, lattice deformation, and relative shape-lattice orientation can be simultaneously recovered with high accuracy.

Abstract: Although Raman scattering in magnetic materials exhibits rich experimental phenomena, the symmetry constraints on Raman tensors have not been fully elucidated. In this work, we use Onsager reciprocity relation, other than the conventional corepresentation method, to deal with the mathematical structures of Raman tensors in magnetic groups. Using this approach, we generate Raman tensor tables for all magnetic point groups, and present a comprehensive understanding of the Raman selection rules in magnetic materials with direct product representations method. Our theoretical and numerical results match previous experiments well, and resolve a puzzle in the Raman spectroscopy of CrSBr. Moreover, we identify a common but overlooked phenomenon: the magneto-Raman vector can be orthogonal to the magnetic moment direction. Our method and associated Raman tensor tables will be helpful for the Raman studies in both experimental and theoretical domains.

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is rapidly advancing materials characterization, yet most applications in electron microscopy rely solely on image contrast, overlooking the chemical and experimental context that shapes image formation. Here we develop a context-aware learning framework that integrates image-derived contrast with metadata describing composition, beam energy, and detector geometry. However, this shift has relocated the bottleneck to the human dimension: time-consuming mechanical processes, such as input preparation and data analysis, now dominate the research lifecycle. We introduce Paimon, a Platform for Agentic Integration in Materials Optimization and Nanoscale-simulations. Through hundreds of trials on an expert-level liquid electrolyte simulation, we show that Paimon substantially improves the reliability of agentic workflows by suppressing silent errors: plausible yet physically incorrect results. We further demonstrate that Paimon can cooperate with an external scientific agent and autonomously reproduce simulation methodologies from the literature. As an agent harness for atomistic simulations, Paimon affords researchers a continuous, science-centric workflow throughout the entire simulation lifecycle.

Method: 该方法基于Kramers-Heisenberg公式表述双微分截面，其中跃迁矩阵元由多体微扰理论中的Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）计算得到；为扩展至时域，引入了由实时含时密度泛函理论（RT-TDDFT）获得的非平衡载流子分布，并推广了RIXS实现中对任意极化方向的适用性。

To extend this approach to the time domain, we incorporate non-equilibrium charge-carrier distributions obtained from real-time, time-dependent density-functional theory (RT-TDDFT). Generalizing the RIXS implementation with respect to arbitrary polarizations, allows us to consider different orientations of incoming and outgoing light. TL;DR: 提出了一种基于神经网络的分子材料性质预测方法，通过将分子结构编码为数值向量并输入反向传播神经网络，在多种热力学、物理和物理化学性质上实现了0.2-8.1%的平均精度，并提出了“计算合成”（computational synthesis）作为材料设计的新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从化学结构出发高效预测分子基材料（molecular-based materials）的各类性质，为材料设计提供定量结构-性质关系（quantitative structure property relationships, QSPR）的计算工具。

Method: 利用简单算法将有机分子的结构与组成直接编码为数值向量，作为反向传播（backpropagation）型神经网络的输入，从而将数值输入与目标性质关联。

Result: 针对碳氢化合物、氢氟碳化合物和冠醚系列，在热容、焓、蒸发热、沸点、密度、折射率、稳定常数等性质上平均精度达0.2-8.1%，最大偏差16-20%；对聚合物材料的部分物理及力学性质也进行了估计，并与回归分析进行了比较。

Conclusion: 神经网络能够建立准确的定量结构-性质关系，基于此提出了“计算合成”（computational synthesis）方法，用于实现材料设计（materials design）。

Abstract: A computational scheme, which utilizes neural networks, was developed to predict properties of molecular-based materials from chemical structures. The method uses a set of simple algorithms to encode the structure and composition of organic molecules directly into numerical vectors, which is used as input for neural networks. Backpropagation type neural networks are then used to correlate these numeric inputs with a set of desired properties. Calculated results for a series of hydrocarbons, hydrofluorocarbons, and crown ethers demonstrate average accuracies of 0.2-8.1% with maximum deviations of 16-20% for a broad range of thermodynamic, physical, and physical-chemical characteristics (heat capacity, enthalpy, heat of evaporation, boiling point, density, refractive index, stability constants, etc.). In addition, a number of physical and mechanical properties were estimated for polymeric materials and compared with regression analysis. Based on the neural network capabilities of formulating accurate quantitative structure property relationships, a technique called computational synthesis is suggested for performing materials design.

### [253] [Stoichiometric Epitaxial Strontium Titanate Thin Films on Silicon by High-Temperature Sr Segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09574)
*Andries Boelen,Marina Baryshnikova,Maxim Korytov,Sean R. C. McMitchell,Felix Cahyadi,Christian Haffner,Clement Merckling*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究在硅(001)衬底上生长的富锶钛酸锶（SrTiO₃, STO）薄膜通过氧气氛后退火（post-growth annealing）实现化学计量比（stoichiometry）调控的机制与效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅基STO薄膜需要精确的化学计量比和单晶有序性以充分发挥其功能特性，但氧化分子束外延（oxide molecular beam epitaxy）存在源氧化导致的通量不稳定问题，仅能提供狭窄的阳离子化学计量比控制窗口。

Method: 在氧气氛中对故意富Sr的外延STO薄膜进行后退火处理，并在较宽温度范围内系统研究其Sr偏析（segregation）行为与化学计量比演变。

Result: 发现两种不同的Sr偏析机制：低于800 °C时，过量Sr向表面偏析形成SrO析出物，并在更高温度下逐渐升华；高于800 °C时，Sr在STO/硅界面的SiO₂层中累积。两种机制共同将过量Sr从STO晶格中移除，获得更接近化学计量比的钙钛矿（perovskite）层。

Conclusion: 先生长轻微富Sr的STO模板再进行可控后退火，是一种改善晶体质量的实用方法，为在硅衬底上实现高质量STO集成提供了可扩展策略。

Abstract: Thin-film strontium titanate (SrTiO$_3$, STO) layers grown on silicon require accurate stoichiometry and single-crystalline order to exploit their functional properties optimally. Oxide molecular beam epitaxy can provide an epitaxial interface, but suffers from source oxidation and resulting flux instabilities, yielding only a narrow growth process window for cationic stoichiometry control. Here, we investigate post-growth annealing in oxygen as a pathway to drive the STO layer toward stoichiometry in intentionally Sr-rich epitaxial STO films on silicon (001). Annealing over a broad temperature range revealed two distinct Sr-segregation mechanisms. Below 800 °C, excess Sr segregates toward the surface, forming SrO outgrowths that progressively sublimate at elevated temperatures. Above 800 °C, a second mechanism dominates: Sr accumulates within the interfacial SiO$_2$ layer formed by oxygen diffusion at the STO/Si interface. Together, these mechanisms effectively remove excess Sr from the STO lattice, yielding a more stoichiometric perovskite layer. Our results demonstrate that growing slightly Sr-rich STO templates followed by controlled annealing provides a practical route to improve crystalline quality, offering a scalable strategy for high-quality STO integration on silicon.

</details>


### [254] [k-Means Clustering in Fingerprint-Based Configuration Selection for Fitting Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09575)
*Miroslav Lebeda,Jan Drahokoupil,Ludvík Löbel,Petr Vlčák*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于k-means聚类和原子配置指纹（CrystalNN模型结合径向分布函数RDF）的方法，从大数据集中选择少量代表性原子构型用于拟合经典分子动力学势函数。以钛的嵌入原子法（EAM）势拟合为例，证明该方法在仅需约30个构型时即可达到与1800个构型相当的能量与力预测精度，优于随机选择。t-SNE可视化揭示了构型间的信息冗余，进一步验证了k-means聚类在消除冗余方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典分子动力学（molecular dynamics）势函数拟合中，从密度泛函理论（DFT）数据中选择代表性原子构型是关键步骤。随机选择效率低，需要大量构型才能达到较好精度，因此需要一种能自动选择多样化且信息丰富的构型子集的方法，以降低数据需求并提高拟合效率。

Method: 首先基于CrystalNN模型和径向分布函数（RDF）生成原子构型的指纹特征（fingerprints），然后对指纹特征应用k-means聚类（k-means clustering），从每个聚类中选取代表性构型构成训练子集。同时使用t分布随机邻域嵌入（t-SNE）将高维指纹降至二维空间，用于可视化分析构型间的重叠与冗余关系。

Result: 基于1800个初始构型，k-means聚类方法在能量和力的预测精度上均优于随机选择，且仅需约30个构型即可达到与全部构型相当的表现。t-SNE可视化显示含钛空位（Ti vacancy）与不含空位的构型子集在二维空间存在重叠，表明其原子环境相似；k-means聚类保留了这种相似性，而随机选择无法捕捉。排除重叠构型后，测试集的预测精度仍保持稳定，验证了重叠构型存在信息冗余。

Conclusion: 基于k-means聚类的构型选择方法能够以远少于随机选择的构型数量实现高精度势函数拟合，其有效性源于对原子构型信息冗余的识别与消除。原子环境相似性导致的构型重叠是信息冗余的来源，而聚类方法能自动处理这一问题。

Abstract: In this study, we present a method for selecting an arbitrary number of distinct configurations from a larger data set by applying k-means clustering to atomistic configuration fingerprints based on the CrystalNN model and radial distribution function (RDF). This approach improves the accuracy of fitting classical molecular dynamics interatomic potentials to density functional theory (DFT) data for both energies and forces while requiring fewer configurations than random selection. We demonstrate this improvement by fitting an embedded-atom method (EAM) potential for titanium, using various configurational sizes from an initial set of 1800 configurations. The k-means clustering consistently achieves better precision and lower standard deviations for a smaller number of configurations than random selection. The results also suggest that only about 30 configurations are sufficient to obtain an EAM model that describes well the full set of 1800 configurations in terms of energies and forces. Additionally, t-distributed stochastic neighbor embedding (t-SNE) method was used to reduce the configuration fingerprints into 2D space, and it revealed an overlap between two configuration subsets with and without Ti vacancy, indicating similar atomic environments. This similarity is captured by k-means clustering but not by random selection. Furthermore, when the overlapping configurations with vacancies were excluded from the k-means algorithm and used only as a test set, their energy and force predictions showed similar precision to those when they were included. This indicates that the overlapping configurations in the 2D t-SNE space indeed imply potential information redundancy among the atomistic configurations.

</details>


### [255] [Lattice genome: representation and analysis of heterogeneous crystalline microstructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09611)
*Jiayang Wang,Mathieu Calvat,J. C. Stinville,Marat I. Latypov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 受广义材料基因概念启发，本文提出晶体材料的“晶格基因（lattice gene）”与“晶格基因组（lattice genome）”概念：通过变分自编码器（variational autoencoder）编码菊池衍射花样（Kikuchi diffraction patterns），得到局部晶体结构的紧致表示（compact representation）；该表示满足材料基因的关键准则（紧凑性、实验可及性、存在反映结构相似性的距离度量、以及足以重构原始衍射花样的信息含量）；晶格基因组则是在电子背散射衍射（EBSD）映射的代表性区域上空间分辨地收集晶格基因，捕获控制材料性能的介观尺度异质性（mesoscale heterogeneity）。进一步在增材制造与锻造镍基高温合金的微观结构上验证了三个应用：潜变量组分图（latent component maps）、基于潜空间距离与角度的域分割（domain segmentation）、以及核与域潜向量展宽（kernel and domain latent vector spreads）以量化晶粒内部异质性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受广义材料基因（generalized materials genome）概念启发，旨在为晶体材料构建一种既能紧凑表示局部晶体结构、又具备实验可及性和结构可比性的“材料基因”表示，以弥合微观结构与宏观性能之间的表征鸿沟。

Method: 利用变分自编码器（variational autoencoder）对菊池衍射花样（Kikuchi diffraction patterns）进行编码，获得局部晶体结构的紧致表示——晶格基因（lattice gene）；将电子背散射衍射（EBSD）映射的代表性区域内所有晶格基因空间分辨地收集，构成晶格基因组（lattice genome）。

Result: 晶格基因表示满足紧凑性、实验可及性、结构相似性距离度量以及足够的信息含量（可重构原始衍射花样）等关键准则。在增材制造与锻造镍基高温合金微观结构上，成功验证了三个应用：潜变量组分图、基于潜空间度量的域分割、以及核与域潜向量展宽对晶粒内部异质性的定量刻画。

Conclusion: 本文提出的晶格基因与晶格基因组是一种有效的材料基因框架，能够通过实验可及的潜空间表示揭示从晶粒尺度到晶粒内部的介观异质性，为晶体材料的微观结构表征与性能预测提供新工具。

Abstract: Inspired by the concept of a generalized materials genome, we introduce the notions of lattice gene and lattice genome for crystalline materials. A lattice gene is a compact representation of the local crystalline structure obtained by encoding the Kikuchi diffraction patterns with a variational autoencoder. We show that this representation satisfies key criteria for a materials gene: compactness, experimental accessibility, existence of a distance metric reflecting structural similarity, and sufficient information content for reconstructing the original diffraction patterns. The lattice genome is the spatially resolved collection of lattice genes across a representative area mapped by electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD), which captures mesoscale heterogeneity that ultimately controls properties. We demonstrate three applications of the lattice genome: (i) latent component maps that visualize grain-scale and intra-grain heterogeneities, (ii) domain segmentation based on distance and angle metrics in the latent space, and (iii) kernel and domain latent vector spreads that quantify intragranular heterogeneity as high-dimensional analogs of kernel average misorientation and grain orientation spread. All three tools are validated on microstructures of additively manufactured and wrought Ni-base superalloys in as-built and recrystallized conditions.

</details>


### [256] [Ab initio parametrization of distributed polarizable force fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09647)
*Felix Post,Jean-Philip Filling,Toulik Maitra,Falk May,Michael Wand,Denis Andrienko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出通过将原子极化率（atomic polarizability）分配给单个原子而非原子类型，并采用原子极化率张量（atomic polarizability tensor）替代标量值，显著提升了极化力场（polarizable force field）的精度。研究基于第一性原理（first-principles）参数化流程，并利用消息传递图神经网络（message-passing graph neural network）预测极化率参数，在不增加模拟计算成本的前提下实现了高效可扩展的参数化，同时提供了清晰的诊断标准以识别力场模型失效的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化力场相比经典力场具有更好的可迁移性和精度，并能获取折射率、电子态密度等电子响应性质。然而，现有方法在描述阳离子、阴离子及激发态时仍存在局限性，需要对原子极化率的分配方式进行根本性改进以提升其准确性。

Method: 方法包含两个改进：(1) 将原子极化率赋予单个原子而非基于原子类型（atom type）进行分组；(2) 使用原子极化率张量（tensor）代替标量（scalar）。研究提出了基于第一性原理的参数化流程，并在含共轭单元的小有机分子数据集上进行了验证。为克服第一性原理计算的高成本，训练了一种消息传递图神经网络来预测极化率参数。

Result: 改进后的极化力场在应用于小有机分子时表现出更高的准确性，能够适用于阳离子、阴离子和激发态，并对中性分子提供更精确的描述。图神经网络预测的极化率参数在不增加额外计算开销的前提下，实现了高效可扩展的参数化。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种改进极化力场准确性的有效策略，并建立了清晰的诊断标准（diagnostic criterion），用于识别极化力场模型无法准确描述分子极化率的情形。该方法在模拟过程中不引入额外计算成本，具有良好的实际应用前景。

Abstract: Polarizable force fields offer superior transferability and accuracy compared to classical force fields, enabling access to electronic response properties such as refractive index and electronic density of states. Here, we demonstrate two key improvements that significantly enhance their accuracy: (1) assigning atomic polarizability to individual atoms rather than atom types, and (2) employing atomic polarizability tensors instead of scalar values. These modifications extend the applicability of polarizable force fields to cations, anions, and excited states, while also providing more accurate descriptions of neutral molecules. We propose a first-principles-based parameterization procedure for atomic polarizability tensors and scalars, validated on a set of small organic molecules with conjugated building blocks. To overcome the computational cost of ab initio calculations, we train a message-passing graph neural network to predict polarizability parameters, enabling efficient and scalable parameterization. Crucially, this approach imposes no additional computational cost during simulations and provides a clear diagnostic criterion for identifying cases where polarizable force field models fail to accurately describe molecular polarizability.

</details>


### [257] [Crystallography of periodic nanotextures in a strained Mott insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09685)
*Benjamin Z. Gregory,Yorick A. Birkhölzer,Noah Schnitzer,Ziming Shao,Jeff Hodgson,Suchismita Sarker,Jacob P. Ruff,Berit H. Goodge,David A. Muller,Kyle M. Shen,Darrell G. Schlom,Andrej Singer*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大体积X射线倒空间映射（large-volume X-ray reciprocal-space mapping），测量24个对称不等价布拉格反射（Bragg reflections）周围的卫星图案强度，并结合卫星消光分析（satellite-extinction analysis）进行晶体学表征。

Conclusion: 经典不变平面应变晶体学（classical invariant-plane-strain crystallography）可描述这一莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）中磁、电子和晶格序相互纠缠的纳米尺度畴几何，暗示应变工程可调控强关联体系中的相分离行为。

Abstract: Here we investigate stripes of alternating structural phases spontaneously forming in epitaxially strained $Ca_2RuO_4$ thin films below the metal-insulator transition. Using large-volume X-ray reciprocal-space mapping, we show that satellite-pattern intensities across 24 symmetry-inequivalent Bragg reflections collapse onto a single parameter-free curve. The collapse identifies a coherent martensitic laminate of few-nm-wide domains separated by ${012}$ interfaces, with displacements along $\left\langle01\bar{2}\right\rangle$. Satellite-extinction analysis demonstrates that both coexisting phases retain the bulk orthorhombic space group despite the pseudocubic $LaAlO_3$ substrate, biaxial epitaxial strain, and intrinsic strain at the interfaces. Classical invariant-plane-strain crystallography thus governs the nanoscale domain geometry of a Mott insulator with intertwined magnetic, electronic, and lattice order.

### [258] [Bi-S network origin of cation-disorder stability and dispersive band edges in AgBiS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09704)
*Han-Pu Liang,Songyuan Geng,Heng Kang,Chen Qiu,Xiao-Ping Yao,Qing'an Li,Bozhao Zhang,Lechuan Sun,Yuxuan Chen,Shan Zhang,Su-Huai Wei,Peng-Fei Guan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）和深度学习哈密顿量（deep-learning Hamiltonian）相结合的方法，揭示了阳离子无序的AgBiS2中三维Bi-S网络是决定无序稳定性和带边电子态的核心结构基元，澄清了有序相的结构争议，建立了非等价半导体合金中无序稳定与光电响应的统一物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AgBiS2是一种有前景的无铅光电材料，但其有序结构及优异电子性质的微观起源仍存在争议。理论上提出由四面体AgS4和八面体BiS6单元构成的混合配位倾向，而实验主要报道八面体配位的有序和阳离子无序相以及局域阳离子偏心位移。亟需在较大尺度上解析其结构与电子演化的耦合机制。

Method: 本文结合机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）和深度学习哈密顿量（deep-learning Hamiltonian），在较大长度尺度上对AgBiS2的结构与电子演化进行耦合研究。

Result: 在弱无序条件下，Ag/Bi交换与Ag亚晶格的偏心倾向竞争，产生强扭曲局域环境和复杂的衍射特征，阻碍有序相的识别。随着无序程度增加，BiS6类单元连接形成连续的Bi-S网络，稳定了岩盐类无序相。AgBiS2保持清晰的半导体类带色散（band dispersion）并形成直接带隙；Bi-S网络支持的Bi:p-S:p态保留了色散的导带底和较小的电子有效质量，而可移动的Ag破坏了Ag-S键的长程周期性，导致强局域化的价带态。

Conclusion: 研究明确将三维Bi-S网络识别为决定无序稳定性和带边电子态的核心结构基元，澄清了有序AgBiS2的结构争议，建立了非等价半导体合金（nonisovalent semiconductor alloys）中无序稳定与光电响应的统一物理图像。

Abstract: Cation-disordered AgBiS2 is a promising lead-free optoelectronic material, but both its ordered structure and the microscopic origin of its favorable electronic properties remain debated. Theory has proposed a mixed-coordination tendency with tetrahedral AgS4 and octahedral BiS6 units, whereas experiments mainly report octahedrally coordinated ordered and cation-disordered phases, together with local cation off-centering. Here, we combine a machine-learning interatomic potential with a deep-learning Hamiltonian to resolve the coupled structural and electronic evolution of AgBiS2 at large length scales. We identify the three-dimensional Bi-S network as the central structural motif governing both disorder stability and band-edge electronic states. At weak disorder, Ag/Bi exchange competes with the off-centering tendency of the Ag sublattice, producing strongly distorted local environments and convoluted diffraction signatures that hinder the identification of the ordered phase. With increasing disorder, BiS6-like units connect into a continuous Bi-S network, which stabilizes the rocksalt-like disordered phase. Despite strong cation disorder, AgBiS2 retains clear semiconductor-like band dispersion and develops a direct band gap. The connected Bi:p-S:p states supported by the Bi-S network preserve a dispersive conduction-band edge and a small electron effective mass. In contrast, mobile Ag disrupts the long-range periodicity of Ag-S bonding, leading to strongly localized valence states. These results clarify the structural controversy in ordered AgBiS2 and establish a unified physical picture of disorder stability and optoelectronic response in nonisovalent semiconductor alloys.

</details>

### [259] [Inverse scattering for the focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation with elliptic background and full soliton gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08321)
*Tamara Grava,Robert Jenkins,Xiaofan Zhang,Zechuan Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对三次聚焦非线性薛定谔方程（cubic focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation），发展了一类初始条件渐近于具不同相位的椭圆行波（elliptic travelling wave）的正反散射问题（direct and inverse scattering problem），并证明了该初始数据类与全孤子气体（full soliton gas）初始数据存在非零交集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有散射理论多处理背景为常数的初始数据，而实际物理系统常出现周期性或准周期性背景，例如椭圆行波。本文旨在将散射理论推广至这类更一般背景下的初始条件。

Method: 发展三次聚焦非线性薛定谔方程在椭圆行波背景上的正反散射方法，重点处理谱带（spectral bands）与实轴相交的情形。

Result: 证明了所考虑的初始数据类与全孤子气体（full soliton gas）初始数据存在非零交集。

Conclusion: 该工作为研究椭圆背景上非线性薛定谔方程的散射理论及孤子气体（soliton gas）提供了新的理论基础和分析框架。

Abstract: In this manuscript we develop the direct and inverse scattering problem for the cubic focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation and for initial data that are asymptotic to an elliptic travelling wave with distinct phase at $\pm \infty$. We consider the case in which the spectral bands intersect the real axis. We then show that this class of initial data has non zero intersection with the full soliton gas initial data.

</details>


### [260] [Finite-Scale One-Component Regularity via Harmonic Pressure for the 3D Navier-Stokes Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08352)
*Runlong Yu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程（Navier-Stokes equations）的合适弱解，提出了一个有限尺度（finite-scale）单分量正则性机制（one-component regularity mechanism），包含无条件和条件性（对数与幂次）三个层次的结果，分别通过二维半极限类（two-and-a-half-dimensional limiting class）、对数阴影比较（logarithmic shadow comparison）和松弛阴影比较（relaxed shadowing comparison）实现紧致模量（compactness modulus）的量化升级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维Navier-Stokes方程的正则性理论（regularity theory）中，如何利用单一速度分量的小性获得完整的局部正则性半径（local regularity radius）下界，是一个核心问题。现有Caffarelli–Kohn–Nirenberg（CKN）理论需要全速度场的尺度不变小性，而本文试图将条件弱化为仅对竖直分量提出小性要求，并同时探索紧致性论证（compactness argument）的定量化（quantitative）极限。

Method: 第一层采用无条件论证：在尺度不变局部界Φ(1) ≤ M下，利用竖直分量C_3(1)小性，通过近似为二维半极限类（two-and-a-half-dimensional limiting class）转化为CKN型小性。压力近似在空间调和函数（spatially harmonic functions）的商空间中度量。第二层引入对数阴影比较包（logarithmic shadow comparison），将抽象紧致模量替换为对数模量（logarithmic modulus），得到对数型有限尺度衰减。第三层采用松弛阴影比较（relaxed shadowing comparison），将比较类扩展为光滑无拉伸水平流（smooth no-stretching horizontal flows）V=(v_h,0)，允许比较压力满足∂_3π ≠ 0，通过竖直残余（vertical residual）在相对能量恒等式（relative-energy identity）中配对，得到幂次型松弛调和近似（power-type relaxed harmonic approximation）和幂次型有限尺度衰减。

Result: 无条件层：在Φ(1) ≤ M条件下，竖直分量小性保证以原点为中心的局部正则性半径存在一个仅依赖于M的正下界。条件性对数层：紧致模量被替换为对数模量，获得对数型有限尺度衰减。条件性幂次层：在缓冲强流（buffered strong-flow）和局部化松弛稳定（localized relaxed stability）输入下，获得幂次型松弛调和近似和幂次型有限尺度衰减。三个层次将无条件的紧致性结论与对数/幂次型定量假设分离开来。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个从单分量小性出发的三层正则性机制，揭示了竖直分量的控制能力及压力拓扑的特殊障碍——依赖于时间的调和压力（time-dependent harmonic pressures）可能具有有界的尺度不变L^{3/2}振荡，而逐点梯度超出了现有尺度不变量的控制范围。后两个条件性层次明确了将紧致模量升级为对数或幂次型定量衰减所需的稳定性机制（stability mechanisms）。

Abstract: We study a finite-scale one-component regularity mechanism for suitable weak solutions of the three-dimensional incompressible Navier--Stokes equations. The results are organized in three layers. The first layer is unconditional. Under a fixed scale-invariant local bound Phi(1)=A(1)+E(1)+C(1)+D(1) <= M, smallness of the critical vertical-component quantity C_3(1)=int_{Q_1} |u_3|^3 dx dt yields a positive lower bound, depending only on M, for the local regularity radius at the origin. The proof converts one-component smallness into approximation by the two-and-a-half-dimensional limiting class and then into Caffarelli--Kohn--Nirenberg smallness at a smaller scale. The pressure approximation is measured in a quotient by spatially harmonic functions. This pressure topology reflects a genuine obstruction: time-dependent harmonic pressures may have bounded scale-invariant L^{3/2}-oscillation while their pointwise gradients lie beyond the control provided by the available scale-invariant quantities. The second layer is a conditional logarithmic refinement. A prepared two-shadow comparison package replaces the abstract compactness modulus by a logarithmic modulus and gives a logarithmic finite-scale decay. The third layer is a conditional relaxed-shadowing refinement. The comparison class is enlarged to smooth no-stretching horizontal flows V=(v_h,0), with the comparison pressure allowed to have partial_3 pi not equal to 0. The resulting vertical residual pairs with the small component u_3 in the relative-energy identity. Under the buffered strong-flow and localized relaxed stability inputs stated below, this gives a power-type relaxed harmonic approximation and a power-type finite-scale decay. The unconditional theorem is separated from the logarithmic and power-type assumptions; the latter two layers identify the quantitative stability mechanisms needed to upgrade the compactness modulus.

</details>

### [261] [Searches for GeV-Scale ALPs at RHIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07739)
*Kaori Fuyuto,Claudio Andrea Manzari,Hitoshi Murayama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用相对论重离子对撞机（RHIC）上的超周边Au+Au碰撞数据，通过共振过程γγ→a→γγ搜寻与光子耦合的轴子似粒子（ALP），基于现有PHENIX实验1.9 nb⁻¹的数据，预计可探测ALP质量2–5 GeV、耦合强度≥4×10⁻⁴ GeV⁻¹尚未被探索的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子似粒子（axion-like particle, ALP）是与光子存在耦合的假想粒子，现有参数空间中仍存在未探测的区域。利用重离子对撞中受Z⁴增强的双光子（γγ）光度和RHIC的低光子能量阈值，可开辟一条新的ALP搜寻途径。

Method: 基于RHIC（运行于2000–2026年）的超周边Au+Au碰撞数据，通过共振过程γγ→a→γγ进行ALP搜寻。模拟信号与主要背景过程（轻子-轻子散射（light-by-light scattering）、强子共振产生及误识别的e⁺e⁻对），并假设利用PHENIX实验已采集的1.9 nb⁻¹数据估计ALP-光子耦合强度g_{aγγ}的上限。

Result: 研究发现，该方法对ALP质量在2 GeV ≲ m_a ≲ 5 GeV范围、耦合强度g_{aγγ} ≳ 4×10⁻⁴ GeV⁻¹的区域具有探测灵敏度，可探测此前未被探索的参数空间。

Conclusion: 更大亮度的数据集可显著扩展该搜寻的灵敏度，应推动对RHIC上PHENIX及其他实验采集的超周边碰撞数据进行专门分析。

Abstract: We point out that ultra-peripheral Au+Au collision data collected at the Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider, operational during 2000-2026, can be used to search for axion-like particles coupled to photons via the resonant process $γγ\to a \to γγ$. Exploiting the $Z^4$ enhancement of the two-photon luminosity in heavy-ion collisions and the low photon energy thresholds achievable at RHIC, we simulate signal and background processes, the latter dominated by light-by-light scattering, hadronic resonance production, and misidentified $e^+e^-$ pairs, and estimate upper limits on the ALP-photon coupling $g_{aγγ}$ assuming $1.9~\text{nb}^{-1}$ of existing data collected by the PHENIX experiment. We find sensitivity to ALP masses in the range $2~\text{GeV} \lesssim m_a \lesssim 5~\text{GeV}$ with couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 4\times 10^{-4}~\text{GeV}^{-1}$, probing previously unexplored regions of parameter space. Access to larger luminosity datasets could substantially extend the sensitivity of this search, motivating a dedicated analysis of ultra-peripheral collision data collected at RHIC by PHENIX as well as other experiments.

</details>


### [262] [Impact of $N^*$ and $Λ^*$ resonances on $CP$ violation in $Λ_b^0$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08248)
*Yu-Kuo Hsiao,Kai-Lei Wang,Juan Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在组分夸克模型（constituent quark model）框架下，系统研究了四体衰变 Λ_b^0 → pK⁻π⁺π⁻ 中激发核子（N^*）和超子（Λ^*）共振态的贡献，首次建立了量化激发重子共振态对多体美重子衰变（multi-body beauty-baryon decays）影响的完整框架，并成功解释了实验上首次观测到的重子 CP 破坏（baryonic CP violation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四体衰变 Λ_b^0 → pK⁻π⁺π⁻ 已观测到首个重子 CP 破坏信号，但其底层的两体子过程 Λ_b^0 → N^* M 和 Λ_b^0 → Λ^* M 以及激发核子（N^*）与超子（Λ^*）共振态的具体作用尚未被充分探索。

Method: 在组分夸克模型（constituent quark model）框架下，识别出对两体中间过程有贡献的相关共振态，包括 N(1535)、N(1520)、Λ(1670)、Λ(1690) 以及其余 1P 波重子态（1P-wave baryon states）。

Result: 计算得到共振分支比 B(Λ_b^0 → pK⁻π⁺π⁻) = (30.0^{+2.8+4.0}_{-1.3-3.4} ± 1.8) × 10⁻⁶，以及 CP 不对称参量 A_CP(Λ_b^0 → pK⁻π⁺π⁻) = (3.18 ± 0.11 ± 0.13 ± 0.11)%，该结果自然解释了首次观测到的重子 CP 不对称性（baryonic CP asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 建立了首个量化激发重子共振态（excited baryon resonances）对多体美重子衰变（multi-body beauty-baryon decays）影响的完整框架，其关联机制可推广应用于其他重子 CP 不对称（baryonic CP asymmetries）过程。

Abstract: The four-body decay $Λ_b^0\to pK^-π^+π^-$ has led to the first observation of baryonic $CP$ violation. However, the underlying subprocesses $Λ_b^0\to N^* M$ and $Λ_b^0\to Λ^* M$, as well as the roles of excited nucleon ($N^*$) and hyperon ($Λ^*$) resonances, remain largely unexplored. Within the constituent quark model, we identify the relevant resonant states contributing to these underlying two-body transitions, including $N(1535)$, $N(1520)$, $Λ(1670)$, $Λ(1690)$, together with the remaining $1P$-wave baryon states. We obtain the resonant branching fraction ${\cal B}(Λ_b^0\to pK^-π^+π^-) =(30.0^{+2.8+4.0}_{-1.3-3.4}\pm1.8)\times10^{-6}$, while the resulting ${\cal A}_{CP}(Λ_b^0\to pK^-π^+π^-)=(3.18\pm0.11\pm0.13\pm0.11)\%$ provides a natural interpretation of the first observed baryonic $CP$ asymmetry. Our analysis establishes the first comprehensive framework for quantifying the impact of excited baryon resonances in multi-body beauty-baryon decays, with the associated mechanism generally applicable to baryonic $CP$ asymmetries.

</details>


### [263] [Meson-Nucleus Bound States with Neural-Network Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09254)
*Wei-Lin Wu,Liang-Zhen Wen,Shi-Lin Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于HAL QCD介子-核子势，利用神经网络变分蒙特卡洛（neural-network variational Monte Carlo）方法求解(A+1)体薛定谔方程，系统计算了φ、η_c和J/ψ与原子核（A≤12）形成的基态束缚态。研究发现φ-核系统束缚最强（达数十MeV），而粲偶素（charmonium）系统束缚较弱（J/ψ数MeV，η_c亚MeV量级）。φ-核系统的每核子结合能随质量数A呈非单调变化，在⁴He处达到峰值，体现了短程强吸引的φN相互作用特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立从格点QCD（lattice QCD）介子-核子相互作用到介子-核束缚态多体现象的定量桥梁，为未来实验搜索提供理论预测。

Method: 采用HAL QCD方法在接近物理点（near-physical point）计算的介子-核子势，利用推广了介子自由度的神经网络变分蒙特卡洛（neural-network variational Monte Carlo, NN-VMC）框架求解(A+1)体薛定谔方程。

Result: 轻核（²H至¹²C）基准测试的基态能与实验一致。φ-核束缚态在A≥2时出现，J/ψ-核在A≥4，η_c-核在A≥6。φ-核结合能最强（数十MeV），J/ψ-核（数MeV）和η_c-核（亚MeV）较弱。φ-核每核子结合能呈非单调行为，在⁴He处峰值；粲偶素系统则近线性随A加深。介子压缩核子分布，随A增大从晕（halo）构型演化为嵌入核内。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从格点QCD介子-核子相互作用到介子-核多体束缚态现象的定量桥梁，为未来实验搜索提供了具体预测。

Abstract: We present the first systematic calculations of $φ$-, $η_c$-, and $J/ψ$-nucleus ground states up to mass number $A{=}12$ based on the HAL QCD meson-nucleon potentials at near-physical point. The $(A{+}1)$-body Schrödinger equation is solved with a neural-network variational Monte Carlo framework, generalized to incorporate mesonic degrees of freedom. Benchmarking on light nuclei from $^2$H to $^{12}$C yields ground-state energies consistent with experiment. Meson-nucleus bound states emerge at $A\ge2$ for $φ$, $A\ge4$ for $J/ψ$, and $A\ge6$ for $η_c$. The $φ$-nucleus systems exhibit the strongest binding, with binding energies reaching tens of MeV. The $J/ψ$-nucleus and $η_c$-nucleus systems are weakly bound at the few-MeV and sub-MeV scale, respectively. The binding energy per nucleon deepens nearly linearly with $A$ for charmonium systems, whereas the $φ$-nucleus system exhibits a non-monotonic behavior peaking at $^4$He -- a distinctive hallmark of the short-range and strongly attractive $φN$ interaction. The meson compresses the nucleon distribution relative to the parent nucleus, and evolves from a halo configuration to one embedded inside the nucleus with increasing $A$. Our results provide predictions for future experimental searches, and establish a quantitative bridge between lattice QCD meson-nucleon interactions and the emergent many-body phenomena in meson-nucleus bound states.

</details>


### [264] [Space- and time-like electromagnetic form factors of the $\mathbfΩ$ baryon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09324)
*L. Albino,B. Almeida-Zamora,A. Bashir,J. J. Cobos-Martínez,K. Raya,J. Segovia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用基于矢量-矢量接触相互作用的对称性保持框架，通过彩虹-阶梯截断的戴森-施温格方程（Dyson-Schwinger equations）结合庞加莱协变的法捷耶夫方程（Faddeev equation），计算了仅由奇异夸克构成的Ω重子在类空区和类时区的弹性电磁形状因子（electromagnetic form factors），并分析了夸克质量和SU(3)味对称性对重子结构的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ω重子仅由奇异夸克组成，为研究夸克质量与SU(3)味对称性在重子结构形成中的作用提供了纯净环境，但此前对其弹性电磁形状因子在类空和类时区的系统计算尚不充分。

Method: 采用矢量-矢量接触相互作用（vector⊗vector contact interaction）的对称性保持框架，在QCD戴森-施温格方程的彩虹-阶梯截断（rainbow-ladder truncation）下，结合庞加莱协变的三夸克束缚态法捷耶夫方程进行计算。电磁流（electromagnetic current）的构建与沃德-高桥恒等式（Ward-Takahashi identity）一致，得到电单极、磁偶极、电四极和磁八极矩对应的四个独立形状因子。类时区形状因子通过类空解的渐近解析延拓（asymptotic analytic continuation）获得。

Result: 计算得到的静态电磁矩和多极形状因子对戴斯夸克反常磁矩（dressed-quark anomalous magnetic moment）表现出明显敏感性，尤其在磁性和高阶多极扇区。通过解析延拓构建了有效形状因子（effective form factor），并与现有实验数据和近期唯象分析结果进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该框架能够可靠地描述Ω重子在类空和类时区的电磁结构，夸克反常磁矩对高阶多极矩有显著贡献，类时区结果与实验及唯象分析具有可比性。

Abstract: We present predictions for the elastic electromagnetic form factors of the $Ω$ baryon in both space-like and time-like regions, computed within a confining, symmetry-preserving framework based on a vector$\,\otimes\,$vector contact interaction. The calculation is performed in the rainbow-ladder truncation of QCD's Dyson-Schwinger equations, combined with a Poincaré-covariant Faddeev equation for the three-quark bound state. The $Ω$ baryon, composed solely of strange quarks, provides a particularly clean environment in which to investigate the role of quark mass and SU(3)-flavor symmetry in shaping baryon structure. Within this approach, the electromagnetic current is constructed consistently with the Ward-Takahashi identity, yielding four independent form factors associated with the electric monopole, magnetic dipole, electric quadrupole, and magnetic octupole moments. We compute these form factors over a broad kinematic domain and analyze their behavior in both space-like and time-like regions. The resulting static electromagnetic moments and multipole form factors of the $Ω$ baryon exhibit a visible sensitivity to the dressed-quark anomalous magnetic moment, particularly in the magnetic and higher-order multipole sectors. The time-like form factors are obtained through asymptotic analytic continuation of the corresponding space-like solutions, allowing the construction of the effective form factor and its comparison with available experimental data and recent phenomenological analyses.

</details>


### [265] ["Hadron-in-fat-jet'' AI Tagging to Detect Rare Decays Such as $W^{\pm}\toπ^{\pm}γ$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09458)
*Linrui Chen,Tianyi Yang,Zixun Kou,Zijian Wang,Youpeng Wu,Leyun Gao,Qiang Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出"强子-在大喷注中"（hadron-in-fat-jet）新范式，通过将预训练的Sophon AI模型与BDT（Boosted Decision Tree）和软drop质量（soft-drop-mass）形状拟合相结合，在LHC（Large Hadron Collider）上搜索稀有或半独占地衰变到可识别强子或夸克偶素（quarkonium）态的增能喷注（boosted jet）信号，并对W±→π±γ衰变分支比给出了预期的95%置信度上限。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统增能喷注研究主要关注多部分子（multi-prong partonic）亚结构，而忽略了强子或夸克偶素嵌入喷注内部的混合构型（hybrid configuration），如W±→π±γ。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索一种基于"强子-在大喷注中"范式的稀有衰变搜索新方法。

Method: 针对大半径喷注优化预训练的Sophon AI模型；结合事例级BDT（Boosted Decision Tree）和软drop质量形状拟合（soft-drop-mass shape fit）进行联合分析；将该方法应用于W±→π±γ信号搜索，构建完整的统计推断流程。

Result: 在标称设置下，对于450 fb⁻¹的积分亮度，预期在95%置信水平（CL）上给出W±→π±γ分支比的上限为ℬ(W±→π±γ) < 2.78×10⁻⁵。

Conclusion: 该研究首次原理验证了"hadron-in-fat-jet"范式；通过改进触发策略、增加产生道和专用标记器（tagger）可显著提升灵敏度；该方法论广泛适用于当前及未来对撞机实验中多种稀有标准模型过程及轻质量或奇异共振态（exotic resonance）的搜索。

Abstract: We investigate a novel class of boosted-object signatures at the LHC, where a high-$p_{\text{T}}$ fat-jet contains an identifiable hadron or quarkonium state originating from rare or semi-exclusive decays. Unlike conventional boosted jet studies, which focus on multi-prong partonic substructure, our approach probes hybrid configurations such as $W^{\pm}\toπ^{\pm}γ$, where a localized hadronic or quarkonium signal is embedded within a collimated jet. By fine-tuning the signature-oriented, pre-trained Sophon AI model optimized for large-radius jets, and combining it with an event-level BDT and a soft-drop-mass shape fit, we obtain an expected 95\% CL upper limit of ${\cal B}(W^{\pm}\toπ^{\pm}γ)<2.78\times10^{-5}$ for $450\,\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ in our nominal setup. This study serves as a first proof-of-principle demonstration of the ``hadron-in-fat-jet'' paradigm; substantial gains in sensitivity are expected from improved trigger strategies, additional production channels, and dedicated taggers, while the methodology itself is broadly applicable to a wide range of rare Standard Model processes and searches for light or exotic resonances at present and future collider experiments.

</details>


### [266] [Dispersive analysis of the $\boldsymbol{J/ψ\to γπ^0 π^0}$ process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09768)
*Bai-Long Hoid,Igor Danilkin,Anna Testa,Marc Vanderhaeghen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于BESIII实验的强度与相位数据，对$J/ψ\toγπ^0π^0$衰变中低能$π^0π^0$系统进行了色散振幅分析，采用耦合道Muskhelishvili-Omnès表示描述$S$波和$D$波的强末态相互作用，并解决了$0^{++}-2^{++}$ $E1$相位歧义问题，最终标定振幅绝对尺度，为引力形状因子中双π贡献的色散研究提供输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是利用BESIII实验提供的$J/ψ\toγπ^0π^0$衰变中$0^{++}$和$2^{++}$强度、总谱及$E1$相位差等高质量数据，通过色散振幅分析方法系统描述低能$π^0π^0$系统的强相互作用动力学，并解决实验相位歧义问题，为后续引力形状因子（gravitational form factors）中双π贡献的色散研究提供可靠的振幅输入。

Method: 采用色散振幅分析（dispersive amplitude analysis）方法：$S$波使用耦合道$ππ/K\bar K$ Muskhelishvili-Omnès表示，以描述$f_0(500)$和$f_0(980)$相关的强末态相互作用（final-state interactions）；$D$波采用单道$ππ$ Muskhelishvili-Omnès表示，并在变换到实验$E1$、$M2$、$E3$多极子（multipoles）之前识别螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）的所有运动学约束；短距离产生效应通过减除多项式（subtraction polynomials）参数化，左-hand割（left-hand-cut）效应被估计并确定为数值上次主导；利用产生振幅的模-$π$自由度（modulo-$π$ freedom）解决$0^{++}-2^{++}$ $E1$相位歧义，并归一化BESIII强度以固定振幅绝对尺度。

Result: 识别出BESIII $0^{++}-2^{++}$ $E1$相位歧义中的负解是与幺正性约束（unitarity constraints）兼容的相位解，表明实验测量的相位信息可以通过Omnès相位运动（Omnès phase motion）容纳，无需引入额外的大相位；通过提取的分支比（branching fraction）归一化BESIII强度，确定了拟合振幅的绝对标度。

Conclusion: 该色散振幅分析成功描述了$J/ψ\toγπ^0π^0$衰变中的低能$π^0π^0$系统，解决了相位歧义并标定了振幅绝对尺度，所得振幅可作为未来双π贡献对引力形状因子色散研究的标准输入。

Abstract: We present a dispersive amplitude analysis of the low-energy $π^0π^0$ system in the radiative decay $J/ψ\toγπ^0π^0$, using the mass-independent BESIII $0^{++}$ and $2^{++}$ intensities, the total spectrum, and the measured $0^{++}-2^{++}$ $E1$ phase difference. The isoscalar $S$-wave is described by a coupled-channel $ππ/K\bar K$ Muskhelishvili-Omnès representation, which implements the strong final-state interactions associated with the $f_0(500)$ and $f_0(980)$. The $D$-wave is treated with a single-channel $ππ$ Muskhelishvili-Omnès representation, where we identify all kinematic constraints of helicity amplitudes before transforming them to the experimental $E1$, $M2$, and $E3$ multipoles. Smooth short-distance production of a pseudoscalar-meson pair is encoded in subtraction polynomials, while left-hand-cut effects are estimated and found to be numerically subleading. We identify the negative solution of the BESIII $0^{++}-2^{++}$ $E1$ phase ambiguity, after using the modulo-$π$ freedom of production amplitudes, as the phase solution compatible with unitarity constraints, showing that the measured phase information can be accommodated with the Omnès phase motion without requiring large additional phases. By normalizing the BESIII intensities with the extracted branching fraction, we fix the absolute scale of the fitted amplitudes, making them suitable as input for future dispersive studies of two-pion contributions to gravitational form factors.

</details>


### [267] [A New Route to the Annihilation of Multi-Wall String Topological Configurations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08142)
*Utsav Atta,Tathagata Ghosh,Sudip Manna*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种新的宇宙弦-畴壁网络湮灭机制：在包含全局U(1)对称性的超出标准模型粒子物理中，引力效应会将对称性破缺为离散子群，从而形成附着多畴壁的宇宙弦；若与对称性破缺标量场耦合的费米子具有微小裸质量项，辐射修正可产生温度依赖的偏置（bias），触发畴壁网络湮灭，从而规避宇宙学畴壁问题。以包含右手中微子微小裸质量项的主要子（majoron）框架为例进行验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超出标准模型的粒子物理模型常引入全局对称性来解决未解问题，但这类对称性被认为会在普朗克尺度（Planck scale）被引力效应显式破坏。全局U(1)对称性的破缺会导致附着多畴壁的宇宙弦（cosmic strings attached to multiple domain walls）形成，而畴壁的缓慢标度行为可能主导宇宙能量密度，引发宇宙学畴壁问题（cosmological DW problem），受大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis）的强约束。本文旨在提出一种新的畴壁湮灭机制，以避免上述宇宙学困境。

Method: 方法的理论核心是：若与对称性破缺标量场耦合的费米子具有微小裸质量项（small bare mass term），则辐射校正（radiative corrections）可生成随温度变化的偏置，从而触发畴壁湮灭。作为代表性示例，选取包含带微小裸质量项的右手中微子（right-handed neutrinos）的主要子框架（majoron framework），在该框架中引力效应会导致壁-弦网络（wall-string network）出现。

Result: 在该主要子框架内，研究证明右手中微子的微小裸质量提供了偏置（bias）的来源，该偏置负责触发畴壁网络的湮灭（annihilation），从而解决了宇宙学畴壁问题。

Conclusion: 提出了一种在包含最简单连续全局对称性U(1)的理论中，存在引力效应时畴壁的新湮灭机制，为全局对称性模型在宇宙学框架下的自洽性提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Particle physics models beyond the Standard Model often contain global symmetries to address various unanswered questions. However, a common criticism of theories based on global symmetries is that such symmetries are generally expected to be explicitly violated by gravitational effects at the Planck scale. In the case of a global $U(1)$ symmetry, this explicit breaking can reduce the symmetry to a discrete subgroup of $U(1)$, leading to the formation of cosmic strings attached to multiple domain walls (DWs). These DWs are usually cosmologically problematic, since their slow scaling behavior can eventually dominate the energy density of the Universe, giving rise to the well-known cosmological DW problem, which is strongly constrained by Big Bang Nucleosynthesis. In this letter, we propose a new annihilation mechanism of such DWs in theories with the simplest continuous global symmetry, $U(1)$, in the presence of gravitational effects. The mechanism is as follows: if a fermion coupled to the symmetry-breaking scalar possesses a small bare mass term, radiative corrections can generate a temperature-dependent bias for triggering DW annihilation. As a representative example, we study a majoron framework containing right-handed neutrinos with small bare mass terms, in which a wall-string network can arise once gravitational effects are taken into account. Within this setup, we show that the small bare masses of the right-handed neutrinos provide the origin of the bias responsible for triggering the annihilation of the DW network.

### [268] [Retarded Correlators of Charge Transport in a Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08139)
*Xuan Zhao,Qiuze Sun,Yi Wang,Jin Hu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过松弛时间近似（relaxation-time approximation）下的动理学理论（kinetic theory），精确求解了磁化相对论性等离子体（magnetized relativistic plasma）中的线性化玻尔兹曼方程（linearized Boltzmann equation），获得了以贝塞尔函数（Bessel functions）表达的分布函数解析解，并由此计算了推迟流-流关联函数、验证了Ward恒等式（Ward identities）。在流体力学极限下提取了电荷扩散模，发现横扩散系数在强场下正比于1/B₀²，纵扩散则不受影响；此外还分析了非流体力学支割线，确定了其运动学阈值并识别了相应的波-粒相互作用为纵向朗道阻尼（Landau damping）和横向回旋阻尼（cyclotron damping）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁化等离子体中的电荷输运行为在相对论性天体物理（如中子星、吸积盘）和极端条件实验中有重要意义，但由于磁场对动理学过程的影响复杂，精确解析解在以往文献中仍然缺乏。

Method: 采用松弛时间近似的动理学理论，在均匀磁场中精确求解线性化玻尔兹曼方程，得到以贝塞尔函数表示的分布函数解析解，进而计算全部推迟流-流关联函数，并通过Ward恒等式验证自洽性。

Result: 在流体力学极限下提取了电荷扩散模，发现横向扩散系数在强磁场区域中随1/B₀²标度被强烈抑制，而纵向扩散系数不受影响；同时识别出非流体力学支割线（non-hydrodynamic branch cuts），其运动学阈值分别对应纵向朗道阻尼和横向回旋阻尼。

Conclusion: 该工作为磁化相对论性等离子体中的线性响应分析提供了完全解析的动理学处理框架，揭示了磁场对扩散模式的显著各向异性抑制，并将非流体力学支割线与具体的波-粒耗散机制（朗道阻尼和回旋阻尼）建立了直接对应关系。

Abstract: We study charge transport in a magnetized relativistic plasma using kinetic theory within the relaxation-time approximation. By exactly solving the linearized Boltzmann equation in a uniform magnetic field, we obtain an analytic solution for the distribution function in terms of Bessel functions. Using this solution, we compute the full set of retarded current-current correlators and verify the Ward identities. In the hydrodynamic limit, we extract the charge diffusion modes, demonstrating that the transverse diffusion coefficient is strongly suppressed by the magnetic field, scaling as $1/B_0^2$ in the strong-field regime, while the longitudinal diffusion remains unaffected. Furthermore, we analyze the non-hydrodynamic branch cuts in the complex frequency plane, determining their kinematic thresholds and identifying the underlying wave-particle interactions as longitudinal Landau damping and transverse cyclotron damping.

### [269] [Lepton $g-2$ non-universality of hadronic contributions and a sub-GeV window to New Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08329)
*Siyuan Li,Vladimir Pascalutsa,Maxim Pospelov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出线性组合 $a_{\mu-e} \equiv a_\mu - (m_\mu/m_e)^2 a_e$，其中质量比平方的缩放因子 $(m_\mu/m_e)^2$ 确保了短程贡献的精确抵消，从而改善紫外行为并规避 $a_\mu$ 或 $a_e$ 各自面临的问题。

Result: 在 $a^{\rm HVP}_{\mu-e}$ 中，强子真空极化效应及其不确定性相比 $a^{\rm HVP}_\mu$ 降低了约85%。该观测量对当前数据驱动与格点QCD评估之间的分歧具有增强的敏感性。

Conclusion: $a_{\mu-e}$ 在检验具有一定味非普适性（flavor non-universality）的新物理以及味普适（flavor-universal）的亚GeV态方面具有前景，但这依赖于电子反常磁矩 $a_e$ 和精细结构常数 $\alpha$ 实验测量的显著改进。

Abstract: We propose the linear combination of the anomalous magnetic moments of the muon and electron, $a_{μ-e} \equiv a_μ- (m_μ/m_e)^2 a_e$, as a natural low-energy window quantity, with enhanced sensitivity to the current discrepancy between the data-driven and lattice-QCD evaluations of hadronic contributions. The rescaling ensures an exact cancellations the short-range effects, thereby improving the UV behavior and bypassing a number of issues that arise in $a_μ$ or $a_e$ separately. The hadronic-vacuum-polarization effect in $a^{\rm HVP}_{μ-e}$, together with its uncertainty, is reduced as compared to $a^{\rm HVP}_μ$ by $\sim 85\%$. This is promising for tests of New Physics, conditional to significant improvements in experimental measurements of $a_e$ and $α$. One can foresee the improvements in tests of New Physics with some degree of flavor non-universality, as well as for the flavor-universal sub-GeV states.

### [270] [Detector Resolution and Observable Infrared Memory in QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08879)
*Takeshi Fukuyama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出QED中红外发散的消除虽移除了非物理的红外正则化参数，但探测分辨率尺度ω_max仍保留在可观测量中。该尺度可自然解释为硬子区域约化密度矩阵中的粗粒化尺度，使软光子重叠成为分辨率依赖的函数D_ij(ω_max)。由此，红外记忆不仅由渐近软区定义，还取决于观测与非观测红外自由度之间的分辨率尺度，衔接了传统红外安全截面与现代软光子承载红外记忆与量子信息的诠释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统QED中红外发散（infrared divergence）通过Bloch-Nordsieck机制和KLN定理（Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg theorem）在包含性可观测量中相消，但这一消去仅移除了非物理的红外正则化参数。作者强调，探测分辨率尺度ω_max依然保留在截面中，其物理意义尚需澄清。本文旨在揭示ω_max作为约化密度矩阵粗粒化尺度的自然解释，并建立传统红外安全截面（infrared-safe cross-section）与现代软光子（soft photon）作为红外记忆（infrared memory）与量子信息载体的桥梁。

Method: 本文采用理论分析的方法，将QED截面中残留的探测分辨率尺度ω_max重新解释为硬子区域（hard sector）约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）中的粗粒化尺度（coarse-graining scale）。低于ω_max的软光子被视为未被观测而实际上被求迹（traced over）的部分，由此软区重叠（soft-sector overlap）D_ij成为ω_max的函数。作者通过这一粗粒化视角，将传统截面公式与现代量子信息诠释联系起来。

Result: 该分析表明，可观测的红外记忆（infrared memory）不仅由渐近软区（asymptotic soft sector）本身定义，还取决于划分观测与非观测红外自由度的分辨率尺度ω_max。软区重叠D_ij(ω_max)因此具有分辨率依赖性，这为理解红外物理的量子信息内容提供了新视角。

Conclusion: 本文从粗粒化视角统一了QED中两个看似独立的论述——传统红外安全截面公式与现代将软光子看作红外记忆与量子信息载体的诠释。这一框架表明，红外观测结果天然依赖于实验分辨率，而该依赖性具有明确的量子信息基础。

Abstract: Infrared divergences in QED cancel in inclusive observables through the Bloch--Nordsieck and KLN mechanisms. However, this cancellation removes only the unphysical infrared regulator. The detector resolution scale $ω_{\max}$, which specifies the maximum energy of unresolved soft photons, remains in the observable cross section. We emphasize that this surviving scale has a natural interpretation as a coarse-graining scale in the reduced density matrix of the hard sector. Soft photons below $ω_{\max}$ are not observed and are effectively traced over. The corresponding soft-sector overlap therefore becomes resolution dependent, $D_{ij}=D_{ij}(ω_{\max})$. Observable infrared memory is consequently defined not only by the asymptotic soft sector itself, but also by the resolution scale separating observed and unobserved infrared degrees of freedom. This provides a bridge between the traditional infrared-safe cross-section formulation and the modern interpretation of soft photons as carriers of infrared memory and quantum information.

</details>


### [271] [Primordial Black Holes from Slow Phase Transitions with Delayed Reheating: A Peak-Theory Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09482)
*Indra Kumar Banerjee*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究慢速一级相变（first-order phase transition）结合延迟再加热（delayed reheating）产生原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）的可能性。通过峰值理论方法、蒙特卡洛模拟和环圈判据（hoop-conjecture criterion）分析，发现PBH自旋参数平均为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$，丰度对再加热效率极其敏感，并识别出能解释全部暗物质（dark matter）丰度的参数空间，同时利用PBH观测数据约束了相变与再加热性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在慢速一级相变过程中，由延迟再加热导致的早期物质主导阶段产生原初黑洞的机制，并评估其作为暗物质候选者的可行性。

Method: 基于相变产生的过密度（overdensity）的非高斯分布，发展适用于物质主导阶段的峰值理论方法；执行大规模蒙特卡洛模拟并结合环圈判据计算坍缩概率；引入潮汐力矩项（tidal-torque terms）研究PBH的初始自旋。

Result: 平均自旋参数约为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$；坍缩的过密度阈值依赖于相变性质和再加热效率；PBH丰度对再加热效率高度敏感，效率变化单位量级即可导致坍缩分数变化多个数量级；识别出可使PBH贡献全部暗物质丰度的参数空间。

Conclusion: 延迟再加热场景下慢速一级相变可以产生足够丰度的PBH以解释全部暗物质；PBH的当前（非）观测数据可用于约束相变与再加热过程的相关参数。

Abstract: We study the possibility of significant PBH production from a slow first-order phase transition with delayed reheating. Since delayed reheating results in an early matter-dominated phase between percolation and reheating, we developed a peak-theoretic approach to PBH formation during this phase based on the non-Gaussian distribution of overdensity arising from the transition. To obtain the collapse probability, we performed large-scale Monte Carlo simulations and employed the hoop-conjecture criterion. We include tidal-torque terms to investigate the initial spin of the PBHs and find that the average spin parameter is $\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$. Furthermore, we obtain an emergent overdensity threshold for collapse that depends on the phase transition properties and reheating efficiency. We find that the resulting PBH abundance is extremely sensitive to the reheating efficiency, with order-unity changes in efficiency leading to variations of many orders of magnitude in the collapse fraction. We identify regions of parameter space where the resulting PBHs can account for the entirety of the dark matter abundance. Finally, we also constrain the phase transition and reheating properties from current data on (non-)observations of PBHs.
