### [272] [Model of Flavors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09431)
*Jiri Hosek*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文复活了Weinberg-Salam关于动力学电弱对称性破缺的BCS动机思想，用强耦合的SU(3)_f量子味动力学（QFD）取代了三代费米子的Higgs部分。在QFD框架下，通过手征禁止的费米子质量生成机制，自洽地产生了三种不同的Majorana中微子质量、三种简并的Dirac质量，并实现了完整的味对称性自发破缺与电弱对称性自发破缺，最终通过Pagels-Stokar的紫外有限微扰论解释了SM费米子的味简并质量劈裂以及中微子质量的seesaw机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于BCS超导理论的启发，复活Weinberg和Salam关于动力学电弱对称性破缺（dynamical EW symmetry breaking）的早期设想，旨在用强耦合的量子味动力学（QFD）取代标准模型（SM）中基本的Higgs标量场机制，从而为费米子质量的起源和味结构提供一种无需基本标量粒子的动力学解释。

Method: 将三代费米子（家族）的手征味对称性推广为强耦合的SU(3)_f规范群（QFD），并引入每味一个电弱惰性右手neutrino $ν_R$以消除反常。通过QFD在强耦合下生成手征禁止的费米子质量（chirality-prohibited masses）：$ν_R$的Majorana质量$M_f \sim Λ$和SM费米子的简并Dirac质量$m_f$。利用$M_f$实现$SU(3)_f \times U(1)$的完全自发破缺，利用$m_f$实现$SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$到$U(1)_{em}$的自发破缺。最后采用Pagels-Stokar的紫外有限电弱动力学微扰论（UV-finite EW dynamical perturbation theory）引入电荷和质量比的修正来劈裂味简并。

Result: 1. $SU(3)_f \times U(1)$破缺导致所有味胶子（flavor gluons）获得$\sim M_f$的质量，产生$ν_R$-复合的类Goldstone Majoron和三个$0^{+}$重Higgs玻色子。2. 电弱对称性破缺使$W$、$Z$玻色子的质量由费米子质量平方和决定，定义了有效费米标度$v=246 \rm GeV$，并产生三个SM费米子复合的$0^{+}$ Higgs玻色子$h_f$。3. Pagels-Stokar微扰论通过电荷和质量比$m_f/m_{W,Z}$劈裂了SM费米子的味简并质量。4. 六个Majorana中微子质量可通过seesaw机制计算。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，用强耦合的量子味动力学完全替代基本的Higgs标量场，可以自洽地实现动力学电弱对称性破缺，为费米子质量谱的起源提供了一种无需基本标量的替代框架，并自然预言了$ν_R$-复合的标量粒子和SM费米子复合的Higgs玻色子，为超越标准模型（BSM）的味物理研究提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: The BCS-motivated idea of Weinberg and Salam on dynamical EW symmetry breaking is revived: The Higgs sector of the EW gauge model of three fermion flavors (families) is replaced with the chiral gauge $SU(3)_f$ quantum flavor dynamics (QFD) strongly coupled at a huge scale $Λ$. I. With all chiral fermions in flavor triplets the anomaly freedom demands the welcome BSM extension of the SM fermion sector by one EW-sterile neutrino $ν_R$ per flavor. II. The QFD distinguishes flavors by generating at strong coupling the chirality-prohibited (i.e. calculable) fermion masses: Three different Majorana masses $M_f \sim Λ$ of $ν_R$, and three different, arguably small Dirac masses $m_f$ of SM fermions degenerate for all species in each flavor. 1. Complete spontaneous breakdown of $SU(3)_f \times U(1)$ by $M_f$ implies: (i) All flavor gluons acquire self-consistently masses $\sim M_f$. (ii) There is the $ν_R$-composite pseudo-NG Majoron. (iii) There are three very heavy $0^{+}$ $ν_R$-composite Higgs bosons. 2. Spontaneous breakdown of the EW $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ symmetry to $U(1)_{em}$ by $m_f$, in sharp contrast with the Higgs mechanism, implies: (i) The $W$ and $Z$ bosons acquire masses $\sim g(\sum m^2_f)^{1/2}$ and $\sim (g^2+g^{'2})^{1/2}(\sum m^2_f)^{1/2}$ respectively, defining the effective Fermi scale $v=246 \rm GeV$. (ii) There are three SM-fermion-composite $0^{+}$ Higgs bosons $h_f$ at this scale. III. The UV-finite EW dynamical perturbation theory of Pagels and Stokar splits the flavor-degenerate masses of SM-fermions by their electric charges and the ratios $m_f/m_{W,Z}$. Six Majorana neutrino masses are calculable by seasaw.

</details>


### [273] [PTA-Compatible Domain Walls at LISA and Taiji: Bayesian Reconstruction and Multiband Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09713)
*Satyabrata Datta,Rome Samanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了畴壁（domain walls）作为脉冲星计时阵列（Pulsar Timing Array, PTA）数据解释方案的可行性，重点分析了其引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）谱的紫外（ultraviolet, UV）尾在mHz频段对LISA和Taiji等空间干涉仪的交叉探测潜力，并通过10维贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）评估了单独分析与联合分析的信息增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 畴壁模型能够很好地拟合脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）数据，其特殊的引力波（GW）谱紫外（UV）尾可能延伸到mHz频段，使得与LISA、Taiji等空间干涉仪的交叉探测成为可能。然而，该参数空间的重建前景以及联合分析（joint analysis）能否带来额外信息增益尚不明确，论文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用10维贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference），包含2个畴壁信号参数和8个描述仪器噪声与天体物理前景（astrophysical foregrounds）的 nuisance 参数。针对LISA单独和Taiji单独分析使用49个网格注入（grid injections），联合分析使用65个来自PTA支撑区域的注入点，并采用Clough–Tocher插值（Clough–Tocher interpolation）构建后验热力图（posterior heat maps）。

Result: LISA和Taiji能够探测到产生mHz频段紫外（UV）尾的扩展参数空间，即使存在天体物理前景（astrophysical foregrounds）干扰。在PTA支撑区域内部，真正有信息量的区域集中在高信号边缘。仅用空间探测器分析时，后验存在严重的参数简并（degeneracy），但一个主参数组合可在高信号区域被高精度重建。引入PTA先验后，额外信息增益局限于同一高信号区域，能有效抑制LISA/Taiji单独分析的简并性，但最终后验的轴比（axis ratio）往往与PTA单独分析相当。

Conclusion: 空间干涉仪LISA和Taiji有望与PTA协同探测畴壁引力波（GW）信号；联合分析（joint analysis）在PTA支撑的高信号区域具有非平凡的信息增益，能够打破空间探测器单独分析中的参数简并（degeneracy），但信息增益范围有限，最终后验约束整体仍受PTA主导。

Abstract: Domain walls provide an excellent fit to Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) data. A distinctive feature of the associated gravitational-wave (GW) spectrum is its ultraviolet (UV) tail, which can extend into the mHz band and thereby make cross-detection with space-based interferometers such as LISA and Taiji possible. In this work, we explore the PTA-compatible parameter space of domain-wall models and study both the reconstruction prospects at LISA and Taiji and the information gain achievable through joint PTA--LISA and PTA--Taiji analyses. We find that LISA and Taiji can probe an extended region of parameter space yielding an ultraviolet tail in the milli-Hz band, even in the presence of astrophysical foregrounds. Within the PTA-supported region, however, the genuinely informative regime is more restricted and concentrated toward the high-signal edge. In the space-based-detector-only analysis, the posterior is strongly degenerate in the underlying model parameters, although one principal parameter combination can be reconstructed with high precision where the signal is sufficiently strong. When PTA-informed priors are incorporated, the additional information gain is localized to the same high-signal region: there the space-based data produce a non-negligible posterior update and strongly suppress the catastrophic LISA(Taiji)-only degeneracy, while the final posterior often retains an axis ratio comparable to that of PTA alone. Our analysis is based on a 10-dimensional Bayesian inference with two domain-wall signal parameters and eight nuisance parameters describing instrumental noise and astrophysical foregrounds. We use 49 grid injections for the LISA-only and Taiji-only analyses and 65 injections from the PTA-supported region for the joint analyses, with Clough--Tocher interpolation used to construct posterior heat maps.

</details>


### [274] [Higher-dimensional operators and Polyakov loop in hot Scalar QED from the heat kernel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09779)
*Siddhartha Bandyopadhyay,Joydeep Chakrabortty,Debmalya Dey,Philipp Schicho,Tushar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文利用有限温度热核方法（finite-temperature heat kernel method）计算了高温标量量子电动力学（scalar QED）中直到维度六（dimension-six）的规范不变有效拉格朗日量（gauge-invariant effective Lagrangian），提出了两种互补的计算方法，并考察了Polyakov环（Polyakov loop）对匹配系数及宇宙学一级相变热力学的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能物理和早期宇宙研究中，有限温度下的量子场论有效描述对于理解相变动力学和引力波（gravitational-wave spectrum）产生至关重要。作者旨在发展一种系统计算有限温度下有效场论（effective field theory）的方法，特别关注规范理论中高温极限下的有效算符结构。

Method: 采用有限温度热核方法（heat kernel method）计算规范不变有效拉格朗日量；提出了两种互补途径：一是在有限温度下积分掉重模（integrating out heavy modes），二是从零温热核系数推导有限温度热核系数；并利用Coleman-Weinberg有效势（Coleman-Weinberg effective potential）处理常数背景场。

Result: 在静态极限（static limit）下，两种方法得到相同的三维有效算符；计算了常数背景场下的规范不变Coleman-Weinberg有效势；发现Polyakov环会修正匹配系数（matching coefficients），并影响高阶算符对宇宙学一级相变热力学的贡献。

Conclusion: 所发展的有限温度有效场论方法可用于规范理论中高温行为的系统分析；Polyakov环与高阶维算符对一级相变热力学和引力波谱均有不可忽视的影响，为早期宇宙相变研究提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Using the finite-temperature heat kernel method, we compute the gauge-invariant effective Lagrangian up to dimension-six for massive hot scalar QED. We propose two complementary methods: integrating out heavy modes at finite temperature, and deriving the finite-temperature heat kernel coefficients from the zero-temperature ones. We show that in the static limit, both lead to the same three-dimensional effective operators. We also compute the gauge-invariant Coleman-Weinberg effective potential for a constant background at finite temperature. We further examine how the Polyakov loop modifies the matching coefficients and assess its impact together with the higher-dimensional operators on the thermodynamics of cosmological first-order phase transitions, which in turn can affect an associated gravitational-wave spectrum.

### [275] [Finite Massless Pentaboxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09715)
*Gustavo Figueiredo,David A. Kosower,Pavel P. Novichkov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了无质量五盒费曼图（massless pentabox）的积分核分子（integrand numerators）特性，给出了生成元的紧凑表达式，并利用 HyperInt 包和五边形函数（pentagon functions）计算了最低秩核分子对应的积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高阶微扰量子场论（perturbative quantum field theory）中，费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的计算是散射振幅精确预测的关键。无质量五盒图作为一类重要的双圈拓扑结构，其核分子的局域有限性（locally finite）或消逝性（evanescent）特征尚未被系统刻画，论文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 论文通过引入适配动量基（adapted momentum basis）和格拉姆行列式（Gram determinants）给出了生成无质量五盒图局域有限或消逝核分子理想（ideal）的紧凑表达式。积分计算方面，使用 HyperInt 包进行多重对数（polylogarithms）展开，并借助五边形函数（pentagon functions）完成解析表达式。

Result: 获得了描述无质量五盒图局域有限或消逝核分子生成元的紧凑表达式，并成功计算了最低秩核分子对应的积分，结果以多重对数和五边形函数形式给出。

Conclusion: 论文为无质量五盒图提供了核分子结构的系统描述，并给出了对应积分的具体解析结果，有助于推动双圈费曼积分的计算与简化。

Abstract: We characterize the integrand numerators that give rise to locally finite or evanescent Feynman integrals for the massless pentabox. We provide compact expressions for the generators of the corresponding ideal in terms of an adapted momentum basis and also in terms of Gram determinants. We also compute the integrals corresponding to the lowest-rank numerators in terms of polylogarithms using the HyperInt package, and in terms of pentagon functions.

### [276] [Einstein-de Haas effect and induced rotation in an evolving magnetized QCD matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09760)
*Dushmanta Sahu,Captain R. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在准粒子模型（QPM）框架下研究了动态膨胀的夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中爱因斯坦-德哈斯（EdH）效应，计算了自旋对齐驱动集体旋转产生的角速度，并发现强磁场与弱磁场区域之间存在非平庸的交叉温度，标志着自旋主导区与惯性主导区之间的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将爱因斯坦-德哈斯（Einstein-de Haas, EdH）效应——即自旋排列在外磁场驱动下引发集体旋转的现象——推广到动态膨胀的夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）体系中，探索磁化QCD物质中角动量守恒的物理体现。

Method: 采用准粒子模型（quasiparticle model, QPM）描述动态膨胀的夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP），计算EdH诱导的角速度 $\omega_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ 作为温度、固有时和火球半径的函数。

Result: $\omega_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ 随固有时增大而增长，但在较高温度下受到抑制；在QGP crossover转变温度附近，$\omega_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ 达到不可忽略的显著量级；强磁场与弱磁场区域之间存在非平庸的交叉，该交叉温度将系统划分为自旋主导区（spin-dominated regime）和惯性主导区（inertia-dominated regime）。

Conclusion: EdH效应是磁化QCD物质中角动量守恒的一种表现形式，自旋排列与维持轨道运动所需能量之间的竞争决定了磁场驱动旋转的不同动力学区域。

Abstract: The Einstein-de Haas (EdH) effect describes the emergence of collective rotation driven by spin alignment under an external magnetic field. We investigate this effect in a dynamically expanding quark-gluon plasma (QGP) using a quasiparticle model (QPM). We compute the EdH-induced angular velocity $ω_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ as a function of temperature, proper time, and fireball radius. Our results show that $ω_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ grows with proper time and is consequently suppressed at higher temperatures. Near the QGP crossover temperature, $ω_{\mathrm{EdH}}$ attains a substantial, non-negligible magnitude. We identify a nontrivial crossing between the strong and weak magnetic field regimes that reflects the competition between spin alignment and the energy required to sustain orbital motion. This nontrivial crossing temperature separates a spin-dominated regime from an inertia-dominated regime of magnetic field-induced rotation. These findings establish the EdH effect as a manifestation of angular momentum conservation in magnetized QCD matter.

</details>
